40020017	And as Jesus was going up to Jerusalem , he took the twelve disciples aside , and on the way he said to them ,

40021001	Now when they drew near to Jerusalem and came to Bethphage , to the Mount of Olives , then Jesus sent two disciples ,

40021018	In the morning , as he was returning to the city , he became hungry .
40021019	And seeing a fig tree by the wayside , he went to it and found nothing on it but only leaves . And he said to it , “ May no fruit ever come from you again ! ” And the fig tree withered at once .
40021020	When the disciples saw it , they marveled , saying , “ How did the fig tree wither at once ? ”
40021021	And Jesus answered them , “ Truly , I say to you , if you have faith and do not doubt , you will not only do what has been done to the fig tree , but even if you say to this mountain , ‘ Be taken up and thrown into the sea , ’ it will happen .
40021022	And whatever you ask in prayer , you will receive , if you have faith . ”
40021023	And when he entered the temple , the chief priests and the elders of the people came up to him as he was teaching , and said , “ By what authority are you doing these things , and who gave you this authority ? ”
40021024	Jesus answered them , “ I also will ask you one question , and if you tell me the answer , then I also will tell you by what authority I do these things .
40021025	The baptism of John , from where did it come ? From heaven or from man ? ” And they discussed it among themselves , saying , “ If we say , ‘ From heaven , ’ he will say to us , ‘ Why then did you not believe him ? ’
40021026	But if we say , ‘ From man , ’ we are afraid of the crowd , for they all hold that John was a prophet . ”
40021027	So they answered Jesus , “ We do not know . ” And he said to them , “ Neither will I tell you by what authority I do these things .
40021028	“ What do you think ? A man had two sons . And he went to the first and said , ‘ Son , go and work in the vineyard today . ’
40021029	And he answered , ‘ I will not , ’ but afterward he changed his mind and went .
40021030	And he went to the other son and said the same . And he answered , ‘ I go , sir , ’ but did not go .
40021031	Which of the two did the will of his father ? ” They said , “ The first . ” Jesus said to them , “ Truly , I say to you , the tax collectors and the prostitutes go into the kingdom of God before you .
40021032	For John came to you in the way of righteousness , and you did not believe him , but the tax collectors and the prostitutes believed him . And even when you saw it , you did not afterward change your minds and believe him .
40021033	“ Hear another parable . There was a master of a house who planted a vineyard and put a fence around it and dug a winepress in it and built a tower and leased it to tenants , and went into another country .
40021034	When the season for fruit drew near , he sent his servants to the tenants to get his fruit .
40021035	And the tenants took his servants and beat one , killed another , and stoned another .
40021036	Again he sent other servants , more than the first . And they did the same to them .
40021037	Finally he sent his son to them , saying , ‘ They will respect my son . ’
40021038	But when the tenants saw the son , they said to themselves , ‘ This is the heir . Come , let us kill him and have his inheritance . ’
40021039	And they took him and threw him out of the vineyard and killed him .
40021040	When therefore the owner of the vineyard comes , what will he do to those tenants ? ”
40021041	They said to him , “ He will put those wretches to a miserable death and let out the vineyard to other tenants who will give him the fruits in their seasons . ”
40021042	Jesus said to them , “ Have you never read in the Scriptures : “ ‘ The stone that the builders rejected has become the cornerstone ; this was the Lord’s doing , and it is marvelous in our eyes ’ ?
40021043	Therefore I tell you , the kingdom of God will be taken away from you and given to a people producing its fruits .
40021044	And the one who falls on this stone will be broken to pieces ; and when it falls on anyone , it will crush him . ”
40021045	When the chief priests and the Pharisees heard his parables , they perceived that he was speaking about them .
40021046	And although they were seeking to arrest him , they feared the crowds , because they held him to be a prophet .
40022001	And again Jesus spoke to them in parables , saying ,
40022002	“ The kingdom of heaven may be compared to a king who gave a wedding feast for his son ,
40022003	and sent his servants to call those who were invited to the wedding feast , but they would not come .
40022004	Again he sent other servants , saying , ‘ Tell those who are invited , See , I have prepared my dinner , my oxen and my fat calves have been slaughtered , and everything is ready . Come to the wedding feast . ’
40022005	But they paid no attention and went off , one to his farm , another to his business ,
40022006	while the rest seized his servants , treated them shamefully , and killed them .
40022007	The king was angry , and he sent his troops and destroyed those murderers and burned their city .
40022008	Then he said to his servants , ‘ The wedding feast is ready , but those invited were not worthy .
40022009	Go therefore to the main roads and invite to the wedding feast as many as you find . ’
40022010	And those servants went out into the roads and gathered all whom they found , both bad and good . So the wedding hall was filled with guests .
40022011	“ But when the king came in to look at the guests , he saw there a man who had no wedding garment .
40022012	And he said to him , ‘ Friend , how did you get in here without a wedding garment ? ’ And he was speechless .
40022013	Then the king said to the attendants , ‘ Bind him hand and foot and cast him into the outer darkness . In that place there will be weeping and gnashing of teeth . ’
40022014	For many are called , but few are chosen . ”
40022015	Then the Pharisees went and plotted how to entangle him in his words .
40022016	And they sent their disciples to him , along with the Herodians , saying , “ Teacher , we know that you are true and teach the way of God truthfully , and you do not care about anyone’s opinion , for you are not swayed by appearances .
40022017	Tell us , then , what you think . Is it lawful to pay taxes to Caesar , or not ? ”
40022018	But Jesus , aware of their malice , said , “ Why put me to the test , you hypocrites ?
40022019	Show me the coin for the tax . ” And they brought him a denarius .
40022020	And Jesus said to them , “ Whose likeness and inscription is this ? ”
40022021	They said , “ Caesar’s . ” Then he said to them , “ Therefore render to Caesar the things that are Caesar’s , and to God the things that are God’s . ”
40022022	When they heard it , they marveled . And they left him and went away .
40022023	The same day Sadducees came to him , who say that there is no resurrection , and they asked him a question ,
40022024	saying , “ Teacher , Moses said , ‘ If a man dies having no children , his brother must marry the widow and raise up children for his brother . ’
40022025	Now there were seven brothers among us . The first married and died , and having no children left his wife to his brother .
40022026	So too the second and third , down to the seventh .
40022027	After them all , the woman died .
40022028	In the resurrection , therefore , of the seven , whose wife will she be ? For they all had her . ”
40022029	But Jesus answered them , “ You are wrong , because you know neither the Scriptures nor the power of God .
40022030	For in the resurrection they neither marry nor are given in marriage , but are like angels in heaven .
40022031	And as for the resurrection of the dead , have you not read what was said to you by God :
40022032	‘ I am the God of Abraham , and the God of Isaac , and the God of Jacob ’ ? He is not God of the dead , but of the living . ”
40022033	And when the crowd heard it , they were astonished at his teaching .
40022034	But when the Pharisees heard that he had silenced the Sadducees , they gathered together .
40022035	And one of them , a lawyer , asked him a question to test him .
40022036	“ Teacher , which is the great commandment in the Law ? ”
40022037	And he said to him , “ You shall love the Lord your God with all your heart and with all your soul and with all your mind .
40022038	This is the great and first commandment .
40022039	And a second is like it : You shall love your neighbor as yourself .
40022040	On these two commandments depend all the Law and the Prophets . ”
40022041	Now while the Pharisees were gathered together , Jesus asked them a question ,
40022042	saying , “ What do you think about the Christ ? Whose son is he ? ” They said to him , “ The son of David . ”
40022043	He said to them , “ How is it then that David , in the Spirit , calls him Lord , saying ,
40022044	“ ‘ The Lord said to my Lord , Sit at my right hand , until I put your enemies under your feet ’ ?
40022045	If then David calls him Lord , how is he his son ? ”
40022046	And no one was able to answer him a word , nor from that day did anyone dare to ask him any more questions .
40023001	Then Jesus said to the crowds and to his disciples ,
40023002	“ The scribes and the Pharisees sit on Moses ’ seat ,
40023003	so practice and observe whatever they tell you — but not what they do . For they preach , but do not practice .
40023004	They tie up heavy burdens , hard to bear , and lay them on people’s shoulders , but they themselves are not willing to move them with their finger .
40023005	They do all their deeds to be seen by others . For they make their phylacteries broad and their fringes long ,
40023006	and they love the place of honor at feasts and the best seats in the synagogues
40023007	and greetings in the marketplaces and being called rabbi by others .
40023008	But you are not to be called rabbi , for you have one teacher , and you are all brothers .
40023009	And call no man your father on earth , for you have one Father , who is in heaven .
40023010	Neither be called instructors , for you have one instructor , the Christ .
40023011	The greatest among you shall be your servant .
40023012	Whoever exalts himself will be humbled , and whoever humbles himself will be exalted .
40023013	“ But woe to you , scribes and Pharisees , hypocrites ! For you shut the kingdom of heaven in people’s faces . For you neither enter yourselves nor allow those who would enter to go in .
40023015	Woe to you , scribes and Pharisees , hypocrites ! For you travel across sea and land to make a single proselyte , and when he becomes a proselyte , you make him twice as much a child of hell as yourselves .
40023016	“ Woe to you , blind guides , who say , ‘ If anyone swears by the temple , it is nothing , but if anyone swears by the gold of the temple , he is bound by his oath . ’
40023017	You blind fools ! For which is greater , the gold or the temple that has made the gold sacred ?
40023018	And you say , ‘ If anyone swears by the altar , it is nothing , but if anyone swears by the gift that is on the altar , he is bound by his oath . ’
40023019	You blind men ! For which is greater , the gift or the altar that makes the gift sacred ?
40023020	So whoever swears by the altar swears by it and by everything on it .
40023021	And whoever swears by the temple swears by it and by him who dwells in it .
40023022	And whoever swears by heaven swears by the throne of God and by him who sits upon it .
40023023	“ Woe to you , scribes and Pharisees , hypocrites ! For you tithe mint and dill and cumin , and have neglected the weightier matters of the law : justice and mercy and faithfulness . These you ought to have done , without neglecting the others .
40023024	You blind guides , straining out a gnat and swallowing a camel !
40023025	“ Woe to you , scribes and Pharisees , hypocrites ! For you clean the outside of the cup and the plate , but inside they are full of greed and self-indulgence .
40023026	You blind Pharisee ! First clean the inside of the cup and the plate , that the outside also may be clean .
40023027	“ Woe to you , scribes and Pharisees , hypocrites ! For you are like whitewashed tombs , which outwardly appear beautiful , but within are full of dead people’s bones and all uncleanness .
40023028	So you also outwardly appear righteous to others , but within you are full of hypocrisy and lawlessness .
40023029	“ Woe to you , scribes and Pharisees , hypocrites ! For you build the tombs of the prophets and decorate the monuments of the righteous ,
40023030	saying , ‘ If we had lived in the days of our fathers , we would not have taken part with them in shedding the blood of the prophets . ’
40023031	Thus you witness against yourselves that you are sons of those who murdered the prophets .
40023032	Fill up , then , the measure of your fathers .
40023033	You serpents , you brood of vipers , how are you to escape being sentenced to hell ?
40023034	Therefore I send you prophets and wise men and scribes , some of whom you will kill and crucify , and some you will flog in your synagogues and persecute from town to town ,
40023035	so that on you may come all the righteous blood shed on earth , from the blood of innocent Abel to the blood of Zechariah the son of Barachiah , whom you murdered between the sanctuary and the altar .
40023036	Truly , I say to you , all these things will come upon this generation .
40023037	“ O Jerusalem , Jerusalem , the city that kills the prophets and stones those who are sent to it ! How often would I have gathered your children together as a hen gathers her brood under her wings , and you would not !
40023038	See , your house is left to you desolate .
40023039	For I tell you , you will not see me again , until you say , ‘ Blessed is he who comes in the name of the Lord . ’ ”
40024001	Jesus left the temple and was going away , when his disciples came to point out to him the buildings of the temple .
40024002	But he answered them , “ You see all these , do you not ? Truly , I say to you , there will not be left here one stone upon another that will not be thrown down . ”
40024003	As he sat on the Mount of Olives , the disciples came to him privately , saying , “ Tell us , when will these things be , and what will be the sign of your coming and of the close of the age ? ”

40024008	All these are but the beginning of the birth pains .

40024031	And he will send out his angels with a loud trumpet call , and they will gather his elect from the four winds , from one end of heaven to the other .
40024032	“ From the fig tree learn its lesson : as soon as its branch becomes tender and puts out its leaves , you know that summer is near .

40024040	Then two men will be in the field ; one will be taken and one left .
40024041	Two women will be grinding at the mill ; one will be taken and one left .
40024042	Therefore , stay awake , for you do not know on what day your Lord is coming .
40024043	But know this , that if the master of the house had known in what part of the night the thief was coming , he would have stayed awake and would not have let his house be broken into .
40024044	Therefore you also must be ready , for the Son of Man is coming at an hour you do not expect .
40024045	“ Who then is the faithful and wise servant , whom his master has set over his household , to give them their food at the proper time ?
40024046	Blessed is that servant whom his master will find so doing when he comes .
40024047	Truly , I say to you , he will set him over all his possessions .

40027001	When morning came , all the chief priests and the elders of the people took counsel against Jesus to put him to death .

40027006	But the chief priests , taking the pieces of silver , said , “ It is not lawful to put them into the treasury , since it is blood money . ”
40027007	So they took counsel and bought with them the potter’s field as a burial place for strangers .
40027008	Therefore that field has been called the Field of Blood to this day .
40027009	Then was fulfilled what had been spoken by the prophet Jeremiah , saying , “ And they took the thirty pieces of silver , the price of him on whom a price had been set by some of the sons of Israel ,
40027010	and they gave them for the potter’s field , as the Lord directed me . ”
40027011	Now Jesus stood before the governor , and the governor asked him , “ Are you the King of the Jews ? ” Jesus said , “ You have said so . ”
40027012	But when he was accused by the chief priests and elders , he gave no answer .
40027013	Then Pilate said to him , “ Do you not hear how many things they testify against you ? ”
40027014	But he gave him no answer , not even to a single charge , so that the governor was greatly amazed .
40027015	Now at the feast the governor was accustomed to release for the crowd any one prisoner whom they wanted .
40027016	And they had then a notorious prisoner called Barabbas .
40027017	So when they had gathered , Pilate said to them , “ Whom do you want me to release for you : Barabbas , or Jesus who is called Christ ? ”
40027018	For he knew that it was out of envy that they had delivered him up .
40027019	Besides , while he was sitting on the judgment seat , his wife sent word to him , “ Have nothing to do with that righteous man , for I have suffered much because of him today in a dream . ”
40027020	Now the chief priests and the elders persuaded the crowd to ask for Barabbas and destroy Jesus .
40027021	The governor again said to them , “ Which of the two do you want me to release for you ? ” And they said , “ Barabbas . ”
40027022	Pilate said to them , “ Then what shall I do with Jesus who is called Christ ? ” They all said , “ Let him be crucified ! ”
40027023	And he said , “ Why , what evil has he done ? ” But they shouted all the more , “ Let him be crucified ! ”
40027024	So when Pilate saw that he was gaining nothing , but rather that a riot was beginning , he took water and washed his hands before the crowd , saying , “ I am innocent of this man’s blood ; see to it yourselves . ”
40027025	And all the people answered , “ His blood be on us and on our children ! ”
40027026	Then he released for them Barabbas , and having scourged Jesus , delivered him to be crucified .
40027027	Then the soldiers of the governor took Jesus into the governor’s headquarters , and they gathered the whole battalion before him .
40027028	And they stripped him and put a scarlet robe on him ,
40027029	and twisting together a crown of thorns , they put it on his head and put a reed in his right hand . And kneeling before him , they mocked him , saying , “ Hail , King of the Jews ! ”
40027030	And they spit on him and took the reed and struck him on the head .
40027031	And when they had mocked him , they stripped him of the robe and put his own clothes on him and led him away to crucify him .
40027032	As they went out , they found a man of Cyrene , Simon by name . They compelled this man to carry his cross .
40027033	And when they came to a place called Golgotha ( which means Place of a Skull ) ,
40027034	they offered him wine to drink , mixed with gall , but when he tasted it , he would not drink it .
40027035	And when they had crucified him , they divided his garments among them by casting lots .
40027036	Then they sat down and kept watch over him there .
40027037	And over his head they put the charge against him , which read , “ This is Jesus , the King of the Jews . ”
40027038	Then two robbers were crucified with him , one on the right and one on the left .
40027039	And those who passed by derided him , wagging their heads
40027040	and saying , “ You who would destroy the temple and rebuild it in three days , save yourself ! If you are the Son of God , come down from the cross . ”
40027041	So also the chief priests , with the scribes and elders , mocked him , saying ,
40027042	“ He saved others ; he cannot save himself . He is the King of Israel ; let him come down now from the cross , and we will believe in him .
40027043	He trusts in God ; let God deliver him now , if he desires him . For he said , ‘ I am the Son of God . ’ ”
40027044	And the robbers who were crucified with him also reviled him in the same way .
40027045	Now from the sixth hour there was darkness over all the land until the ninth hour .
40027046	And about the ninth hour Jesus cried out with a loud voice , saying , “ Eli , Eli , lema sabachthani ? ” that is , “ My God , my God , why have you forsaken me ? ”
40027047	And some of the bystanders , hearing it , said , “ This man is calling Elijah . ”
40027048	And one of them at once ran and took a sponge , filled it with sour wine , and put it on a reed and gave it to him to drink .
40027049	But the others said , “ Wait , let us see whether Elijah will come to save him . ”
40027050	And Jesus cried out again with a loud voice and yielded up his spirit .
40027051	And behold , the curtain of the temple was torn in two , from top to bottom . And the earth shook , and the rocks were split .
40027052	The tombs also were opened . And many bodies of the saints who had fallen asleep were raised ,
40027053	and coming out of the tombs after his resurrection they went into the holy city and appeared to many .
40027054	When the centurion and those who were with him , keeping watch over Jesus , saw the earthquake and what took place , they were filled with awe and said , “ Truly this was the Son of God ! ”
40027055	There were also many women there , looking on from a distance , who had followed Jesus from Galilee , ministering to him ,
40027056	among whom were Mary Magdalene and Mary the mother of James and Joseph and the mother of the sons of Zebedee .
40027057	When it was evening , there came a rich man from Arimathea , named Joseph , who also was a disciple of Jesus .
40027058	He went to Pilate and asked for the body of Jesus . Then Pilate ordered it to be given to him .
40027059	And Joseph took the body and wrapped it in a clean linen shroud
40027060	and laid it in his own new tomb , which he had cut in the rock . And he rolled a great stone to the entrance of the tomb and went away .
40027061	Mary Magdalene and the other Mary were there , sitting opposite the tomb .
40027062	The next day , that is , after the day of Preparation , the chief priests and the Pharisees gathered before Pilate
40027063	and said , “ Sir , we remember how that impostor said , while he was still alive , ‘ After three days I will rise . ’
40027064	Therefore order the tomb to be made secure until the third day , lest his disciples go and steal him away and tell the people , ‘ He has risen from the dead , ’ and the last fraud will be worse than the first . ”
40027065	Pilate said to them , “ You have a guard of soldiers . Go , make it as secure as you can . ”
40027066	So they went and made the tomb secure by sealing the stone and setting a guard .
40028001	Now after the Sabbath , toward the dawn of the first day of the week , Mary Magdalene and the other Mary went to see the tomb .
40028002	And behold , there was a great earthquake , for an angel of the Lord descended from heaven and came and rolled back the stone and sat on it .
40028003	His appearance was like lightning , and his clothing white as snow .
40028004	And for fear of him the guards trembled and became like dead men .
40028005	But the angel said to the women , “ Do not be afraid , for I know that you seek Jesus who was crucified .
40028006	He is not here , for he has risen , as he said . Come , see the place where he lay .
40028007	Then go quickly and tell his disciples that he has risen from the dead , and behold , he is going before you to Galilee ; there you will see him . See , I have told you . ”
40028008	So they departed quickly from the tomb with fear and great joy , and ran to tell his disciples .
40028009	And behold , Jesus met them and said , “ Greetings ! ” And they came up and took hold of his feet and worshiped him .
40028010	Then Jesus said to them , “ Do not be afraid ; go and tell my brothers to go to Galilee , and there they will see me . ”
40028011	While they were going , behold , some of the guard went into the city and told the chief priests all that had taken place .
40028012	And when they had assembled with the elders and taken counsel , they gave a sufficient sum of money to the soldiers
40028013	and said , “ Tell people , ‘ His disciples came by night and stole him away while we were asleep . ’
40028014	And if this comes to the governor’s ears , we will satisfy him and keep you out of trouble . ”
40028015	So they took the money and did as they were directed . And this story has been spread among the Jews to this day .
40028016	Now the eleven disciples went to Galilee , to the mountain to which Jesus had directed them .
40028017	And when they saw him they worshiped him , but some doubted .
40028018	And Jesus came and said to them , “ All authority in heaven and on earth has been given to me .
40028019	Go therefore and make disciples of all nations , baptizing them in the name of the Father and of the Son and of the Holy Spirit ,
40028020	teaching them to observe all that I have commanded you . And behold , I am with you always , to the end of the age . ”
41001001	The beginning of the gospel of Jesus Christ , the Son of God .
41001002	As it is written in Isaiah the prophet , “ Behold , I send my messenger before your face , who will prepare your way ,
41001003	the voice of one crying in the wilderness : ‘ Prepare the way of the Lord , make his paths straight , ’ ”
41001004	John appeared , baptizing in the wilderness and proclaiming a baptism of repentance for the forgiveness of sins .
41001005	And all the country of Judea and all Jerusalem were going out to him and were being baptized by him in the river Jordan , confessing their sins .
41001006	Now John was clothed with camel’s hair and wore a leather belt around his waist and ate locusts and wild honey .
41001007	And he preached , saying , “ After me comes he who is mightier than I , the strap of whose sandals I am not worthy to stoop down and untie .
41001008	I have baptized you with water , but he will baptize you with the Holy Spirit . ”
41001009	In those days Jesus came from Nazareth of Galilee and was baptized by John in the Jordan .
41001010	And when he came up out of the water , immediately he saw the heavens being torn open and the Spirit descending on him like a dove .
41001011	And a voice came from heaven , “ You are my beloved Son ; with you I am well pleased . ”
41001012	The Spirit immediately drove him out into the wilderness .
41001013	And he was in the wilderness forty days , being tempted by Satan . And he was with the wild animals , and the angels were ministering to him .
41001014	Now after John was arrested , Jesus came into Galilee , proclaiming the gospel of God ,
41001015	and saying , “ The time is fulfilled , and the kingdom of God is at hand ; repent and believe in the gospel . ”
41001016	Passing alongside the Sea of Galilee , he saw Simon and Andrew the brother of Simon casting a net into the sea , for they were fishermen .
41001017	And Jesus said to them , “ Follow me , and I will make you become fishers of men . ”
41001018	And immediately they left their nets and followed him .
41001019	And going on a little farther , he saw James the son of Zebedee and John his brother , who were in their boat mending the nets .
41001020	And immediately he called them , and they left their father Zebedee in the boat with the hired servants and followed him .
41001021	And they went into Capernaum , and immediately on the Sabbath he entered the synagogue and was teaching .
41001022	And they were astonished at his teaching , for he taught them as one who had authority , and not as the scribes .
41001023	And immediately there was in their synagogue a man with an unclean spirit . And he cried out ,
41001024	“ What have you to do with us , Jesus of Nazareth ? Have you come to destroy us ? I know who you are — the Holy One of God . ”
41001025	But Jesus rebuked him , saying , “ Be silent , and come out of him ! ”
41001026	And the unclean spirit , convulsing him and crying out with a loud voice , came out of him .
41001027	And they were all amazed , so that they questioned among themselves , saying , “ What is this ? A new teaching with authority ! He commands even the unclean spirits , and they obey him . ”
41001028	And at once his fame spread everywhere throughout all the surrounding region of Galilee .
41001029	And immediately he left the synagogue and entered the house of Simon and Andrew , with James and John .
41001030	Now Simon’s mother-in-law lay ill with a fever , and immediately they told him about her .
41001031	And he came and took her by the hand and lifted her up , and the fever left her , and she began to serve them .
41001032	That evening at sundown they brought to him all who were sick or oppressed by demons .
41001033	And the whole city was gathered together at the door .
41001034	And he healed many who were sick with various diseases , and cast out many demons . And he would not permit the demons to speak , because they knew him .
41001035	And rising very early in the morning , while it was still dark , he departed and went out to a desolate place , and there he prayed .
41001036	And Simon and those who were with him searched for him ,
41001037	and they found him and said to him , “ Everyone is looking for you . ”
41001038	And he said to them , “ Let us go on to the next towns , that I may preach there also , for that is why I came out . ”
41001039	And he went throughout all Galilee , preaching in their synagogues and casting out demons .
41001040	And a leper came to him , imploring him , and kneeling said to him , “ If you will , you can make me clean . ”
41001041	Moved with pity , he stretched out his hand and touched him and said to him , “ I will ; be clean . ”
41001042	And immediately the leprosy left him , and he was made clean .
41001043	And Jesus sternly charged him and sent him away at once ,
41001044	and said to him , “ See that you say nothing to anyone , but go , show yourself to the priest and offer for your cleansing what Moses commanded , for a proof to them . ”
41001045	But he went out and began to talk freely about it , and to spread the news , so that Jesus could no longer openly enter a town , but was out in desolate places , and people were coming to him from every quarter .
41002001	And when he returned to Capernaum after some days , it was reported that he was at home .
41002002	And many were gathered together , so that there was no more room , not even at the door . And he was preaching the word to them .
41002003	And they came , bringing to him a paralytic carried by four men .
41002004	And when they could not get near him because of the crowd , they removed the roof above him , and when they had made an opening , they let down the bed on which the paralytic lay .
41002005	And when Jesus saw their faith , he said to the paralytic , “ Son , your sins are forgiven . ”
41002006	Now some of the scribes were sitting there , questioning in their hearts ,
41002007	“ Why does this man speak like that ? He is blaspheming ! Who can forgive sins but God alone ? ”
41002008	And immediately Jesus , perceiving in his spirit that they thus questioned within themselves , said to them , “ Why do you question these things in your hearts ?
41002009	Which is easier , to say to the paralytic , ‘ Your sins are forgiven , ’ or to say , ‘ Rise , take up your bed and walk ’ ?
41002010	But that you may know that the Son of Man has authority on earth to forgive sins ” — he said to the paralytic —
41002011	“ I say to you , rise , pick up your bed , and go home . ”
41002012	And he rose and immediately picked up his bed and went out before them all , so that they were all amazed and glorified God , saying , “ We never saw anything like this ! ”
41002013	He went out again beside the sea , and all the crowd was coming to him , and he was teaching them .
41002014	And as he passed by , he saw Levi the son of Alphaeus sitting at the tax booth , and he said to him , “ Follow me . ” And he rose and followed him .
41002015	And as he reclined at table in his house , many tax collectors and sinners were reclining with Jesus and his disciples , for there were many who followed him .
41002016	And the scribes of the Pharisees , when they saw that he was eating with sinners and tax collectors , said to his disciples , “ Why does he eat with tax collectors and sinners ? ”
41002017	And when Jesus heard it , he said to them , “ Those who are well have no need of a physician , but those who are sick . I came not to call the righteous , but sinners . ”
41002018	Now John’s disciples and the Pharisees were fasting . And people came and said to him , “ Why do John’s disciples and the disciples of the Pharisees fast , but your disciples do not fast ? ”
41002019	And Jesus said to them , “ Can the wedding guests fast while the bridegroom is with them ? As long as they have the bridegroom with them , they cannot fast .
41002020	The days will come when the bridegroom is taken away from them , and then they will fast in that day .
41002021	No one sews a piece of unshrunk cloth on an old garment . If he does , the patch tears away from it , the new from the old , and a worse tear is made .
41002022	And no one puts new wine into old wineskins . If he does , the wine will burst the skins — and the wine is destroyed , and so are the skins . But new wine is for fresh wineskins . ”
41002023	One Sabbath he was going through the grainfields , and as they made their way , his disciples began to pluck heads of grain .
41002024	And the Pharisees were saying to him , “ Look , why are they doing what is not lawful on the Sabbath ? ”
41002025	And he said to them , “ Have you never read what David did , when he was in need and was hungry , he and those who were with him :
41002026	how he entered the house of God , in the time of Abiathar the high priest , and ate the bread of the Presence , which it is not lawful for any but the priests to eat , and also gave it to those who were with him ? ”
41002027	And he said to them , “ The Sabbath was made for man , not man for the Sabbath .
41002028	So the Son of Man is lord even of the Sabbath . ”
41003001	Again he entered the synagogue , and a man was there with a withered hand .
41003002	And they watched Jesus , to see whether he would heal him on the Sabbath , so that they might accuse him .
41003003	And he said to the man with the withered hand , “ Come here . ”
41003004	And he said to them , “ Is it lawful on the Sabbath to do good or to do harm , to save life or to kill ? ” But they were silent .
41003005	And he looked around at them with anger , grieved at their hardness of heart , and said to the man , “ Stretch out your hand . ” He stretched it out , and his hand was restored .
41003006	The Pharisees went out and immediately held counsel with the Herodians against him , how to destroy him .
41003007	Jesus withdrew with his disciples to the sea , and a great crowd followed , from Galilee and Judea
41003008	and Jerusalem and Idumea and from beyond the Jordan and from around Tyre and Sidon . When the great crowd heard all that he was doing , they came to him .
41003009	And he told his disciples to have a boat ready for him because of the crowd , lest they crush him ,
41003010	for he had healed many , so that all who had diseases pressed around him to touch him .
41003011	And whenever the unclean spirits saw him , they fell down before him and cried out , “ You are the Son of God . ”
41003012	And he strictly ordered them not to make him known .
41003013	And he went up on the mountain and called to him those whom he desired , and they came to him .
41003014	And he appointed twelve ( whom he also named apostles
41003015	and have authority to cast out demons .
41003016	He appointed the twelve : Simon ( to whom he gave the name Peter ) ;
41003017	James the son of Zebedee and John the brother of James ( to whom he gave the name Boanerges , that is , Sons of Thunder ) ;
41003018	Andrew , and Philip , and Bartholomew , and Matthew , and Thomas , and James the son of Alphaeus , and Thaddaeus , and Simon the Cananaean ,
41003019	and Judas Iscariot , who betrayed him .
41003020	Then he went home , and the crowd gathered again , so that they could not even eat .
41003021	And when his family heard it , they went out to seize him , for they were saying , “ He is out of his mind . ”
41003022	And the scribes who came down from Jerusalem were saying , “ He is possessed by Beelzebul , ” and “ by the prince of demons he casts out the demons . ”
41003023	And he called them to him and said to them in parables , “ How can Satan cast out Satan ?
41003024	If a kingdom is divided against itself , that kingdom cannot stand .
41003025	And if a house is divided against itself , that house will not be able to stand .
41003026	And if Satan has risen up against himself and is divided , he cannot stand , but is coming to an end .
41003027	But no one can enter a strong man’s house and plunder his goods , unless he first binds the strong man . Then indeed he may plunder his house .
41003028	“ Truly , I say to you , all sins will be forgiven the children of man , and whatever blasphemies they utter ,
41003029	but whoever blasphemes against the Holy Spirit never has forgiveness , but is guilty of an eternal sin ” —
41003030	for they were saying , “ He has an unclean spirit . ”
41003031	And his mother and his brothers came , and standing outside they sent to him and called him .
41003032	And a crowd was sitting around him , and they said to him , “ Your mother and your brothers are outside , seeking you . ”
41003033	And he answered them , “ Who are my mother and my brothers ? ”
41003034	And looking about at those who sat around him , he said , “ Here are my mother and my brothers !
41003035	For whoever does the will of God , he is my brother and sister and mother . ”
41004001	Again he began to teach beside the sea . And a very large crowd gathered about him , so that he got into a boat and sat in it on the sea , and the whole crowd was beside the sea on the land .
41004002	And he was teaching them many things in parables , and in his teaching he said to them :
41004003	“ Listen ! A sower went out to sow .
41004004	And as he sowed , some seed fell along the path , and the birds came and devoured it .
41004005	Other seed fell on rocky ground , where it did not have much soil , and immediately it sprang up , since it had no depth of soil .
41004006	And when the sun rose , it was scorched , and since it had no root , it withered away .
41004007	Other seed fell among thorns , and the thorns grew up and choked it , and it yielded no grain .
41004008	And other seeds fell into good soil and produced grain , growing up and increasing and yielding thirtyfold and sixtyfold and a hundredfold . ”
41004009	And he said , “ He who has ears to hear , let him hear . ”
41004010	And when he was alone , those around him with the twelve asked him about the parables .
41004011	And he said to them , “ To you has been given the secret of the kingdom of God , but for those outside everything is in parables ,
41004012	so that “ they may indeed see but not perceive , and may indeed hear but not understand , lest they should turn and be forgiven . ”
41004013	And he said to them , “ Do you not understand this parable ? How then will you understand all the parables ?
41004014	The sower sows the word .
41004015	And these are the ones along the path , where the word is sown : when they hear , Satan immediately comes and takes away the word that is sown in them .
41004016	And these are the ones sown on rocky ground : the ones who , when they hear the word , immediately receive it with joy .
41004017	And they have no root in themselves , but endure for a while ; then , when tribulation or persecution arises on account of the word , immediately they fall away .
41004018	And others are the ones sown among thorns . They are those who hear the word ,
41004019	but the cares of the world and the deceitfulness of riches and the desires for other things enter in and choke the word , and it proves unfruitful .
41004020	But those that were sown on the good soil are the ones who hear the word and accept it and bear fruit , thirtyfold and sixtyfold and a hundredfold . ”
41004021	And he said to them , “ Is a lamp brought in to be put under a basket , or under a bed , and not on a stand ?
41004022	For nothing is hidden except to be made manifest ; nor is anything secret except to come to light .
41004023	If anyone has ears to hear , let him hear . ”
41004024	And he said to them , “ Pay attention to what you hear : with the measure you use , it will be measured to you , and still more will be added to you .
41004025	For to the one who has , more will be given , and from the one who has not , even what he has will be taken away . ”
41004026	And he said , “ The kingdom of God is as if a man should scatter seed on the ground .
41004027	He sleeps and rises night and day , and the seed sprouts and grows ; he knows not how .
41004028	The earth produces by itself , first the blade , then the ear , then the full grain in the ear .
41004029	But when the grain is ripe , at once he puts in the sickle , because the harvest has come . ”
41004030	And he said , “ With what can we compare the kingdom of God , or what parable shall we use for it ?
41004031	It is like a grain of mustard seed , which , when sown on the ground , is the smallest of all the seeds on earth ,
41004032	yet when it is sown it grows up and becomes larger than all the garden plants and puts out large branches , so that the birds of the air can make nests in its shade . ”
41004033	With many such parables he spoke the word to them , as they were able to hear it .
41004034	He did not speak to them without a parable , but privately to his own disciples he explained everything .
41004035	On that day , when evening had come , he said to them , “ Let us go across to the other side . ”
41004036	And leaving the crowd , they took him with them in the boat , just as he was . And other boats were with him .
41004037	And a great windstorm arose , and the waves were breaking into the boat , so that the boat was already filling .
41004038	But he was in the stern , asleep on the cushion . And they woke him and said to him , “ Teacher , do you not care that we are perishing ? ”
41004039	And he awoke and rebuked the wind and said to the sea , “ Peace ! Be still ! ” And the wind ceased , and there was a great calm .
41004040	He said to them , “ Why are you so afraid ? Have you still no faith ? ”
41004041	And they were filled with great fear and said to one another , “ Who then is this , that even the wind and the sea obey him ? ”
41005001	They came to the other side of the sea , to the country of the Gerasenes .
41005002	And when Jesus had stepped out of the boat , immediately there met him out of the tombs a man with an unclean spirit .
41005003	He lived among the tombs . And no one could bind him anymore , not even with a chain ,
41005004	for he had often been bound with shackles and chains , but he wrenched the chains apart , and he broke the shackles in pieces . No one had the strength to subdue him .
41005005	Night and day among the tombs and on the mountains he was always crying out and cutting himself with stones .
41005006	And when he saw Jesus from afar , he ran and fell down before him .
41005007	And crying out with a loud voice , he said , “ What have you to do with me , Jesus , Son of the Most High God ? I adjure you by God , do not torment me . ”
41005008	For he was saying to him , “ Come out of the man , you unclean spirit ! ”
41005009	And Jesus asked him , “ What is your name ? ” He replied , “ My name is Legion , for we are many . ”
41005010	And he begged him earnestly not to send them out of the country .
41005011	Now a great herd of pigs was feeding there on the hillside ,
41005012	and they begged him , saying , “ Send us to the pigs ; let us enter them . ”
41005013	So he gave them permission . And the unclean spirits came out , and entered the pigs , and the herd , numbering about two thousand , rushed down the steep bank into the sea and were drowned in the sea .
41005014	The herdsmen fled and told it in the city and in the country . And people came to see what it was that had happened .
41005015	And they came to Jesus and saw the demon-possessed man , the one who had had the legion , sitting there , clothed and in his right mind , and they were afraid .
41005016	And those who had seen it described to them what had happened to the demon-possessed man and to the pigs .
41005017	And they began to beg Jesus to depart from their region .
41005018	As he was getting into the boat , the man who had been possessed with demons begged him that he might be with him .
41005019	And he did not permit him but said to him , “ Go home to your friends and tell them how much the Lord has done for you , and how he has had mercy on you . ”
41005020	And he went away and began to proclaim in the Decapolis how much Jesus had done for him , and everyone marveled .
41005021	And when Jesus had crossed again in the boat to the other side , a great crowd gathered about him , and he was beside the sea .
41005022	Then came one of the rulers of the synagogue , Jairus by name , and seeing him , he fell at his feet
41005023	and implored him earnestly , saying , “ My little daughter is at the point of death . Come and lay your hands on her , so that she may be made well and live . ”
41005024	And he went with him . And a great crowd followed him and thronged about him .
41005025	And there was a woman who had had a discharge of blood for twelve years ,
41005026	and who had suffered much under many physicians , and had spent all that she had , and was no better but rather grew worse .
41005027	She had heard the reports about Jesus and came up behind him in the crowd and touched his garment .
41005028	For she said , “ If I touch even his garments , I will be made well . ”
41005029	And immediately the flow of blood dried up , and she felt in her body that she was healed of her disease .
41005030	And Jesus , perceiving in himself that power had gone out from him , immediately turned about in the crowd and said , “ Who touched my garments ? ”
41005031	And his disciples said to him , “ You see the crowd pressing around you , and yet you say , ‘ Who touched me ? ’ ”
41005032	And he looked around to see who had done it .
41005033	But the woman , knowing what had happened to her , came in fear and trembling and fell down before him and told him the whole truth .
41005034	And he said to her , “ Daughter , your faith has made you well ; go in peace , and be healed of your disease . ”
41005035	While he was still speaking , there came from the ruler’s house some who said , “ Your daughter is dead . Why trouble the Teacher any further ? ”
41005036	But overhearing what they said , Jesus said to the ruler of the synagogue , “ Do not fear , only believe . ”
41005037	And he allowed no one to follow him except Peter and James and John the brother of James .
41005038	They came to the house of the ruler of the synagogue , and Jesus saw a commotion , people weeping and wailing loudly .
41005039	And when he had entered , he said to them , “ Why are you making a commotion and weeping ? The child is not dead but sleeping . ”
41005040	And they laughed at him . But he put them all outside and took the child’s father and mother and those who were with him and went in where the child was .
41005041	Taking her by the hand he said to her , “ Talitha cumi , ” which means , “ Little girl , I say to you , arise . ”
41005042	And immediately the girl got up and began walking ( for she was twelve years of age ) , and they were immediately overcome with amazement .
41005043	And he strictly charged them that no one should know this , and told them to give her something to eat .
41006001	He went away from there and came to his hometown , and his disciples followed him .
41006002	And on the Sabbath he began to teach in the synagogue , and many who heard him were astonished , saying , “ Where did this man get these things ? What is the wisdom given to him ? How are such mighty works done by his hands ?
41006003	Is not this the carpenter , the son of Mary and brother of James and Joses and Judas and Simon ? And are not his sisters here with us ? ” And they took offense at him .
41006004	And Jesus said to them , “ A prophet is not without honor , except in his hometown and among his relatives and in his own household . ”
41006005	And he could do no mighty work there , except that he laid his hands on a few sick people and healed them .
41006006	And he marveled because of their unbelief . And he went about among the villages teaching .
41006007	And he called the twelve and began to send them out two by two , and gave them authority over the unclean spirits .
41006008	He charged them to take nothing for their journey except a staff — no bread , no bag , no money in their belts —
41006009	but to wear sandals and not put on two tunics .

41006011	And if any place will not receive you and they will not listen to you , when you leave , shake off the dust that is on your feet as a testimony against them . ”
41006012	So they went out and proclaimed that people should repent .

41006014	King Herod heard of it , for Jesus ’ name had become known . Some said , “ John the Baptist has been raised from the dead . That is why these miraculous powers are at work in him . ”
41006015	But others said , “ He is Elijah . ” And others said , “ He is a prophet , like one of the prophets of old . ”

41006019	And Herodias had a grudge against him and wanted to put him to death . But she could not ,
41006020	for Herod feared John , knowing that he was a righteous and holy man , and he kept him safe . When he heard him , he was greatly perplexed , and yet he heard him gladly .

41006022	For when Herodias’s daughter came in and danced , she pleased Herod and his guests . And the king said to the girl , “ Ask me for whatever you wish , and I will give it to you . ”
41006023	And he vowed to her , “ Whatever you ask me , I will give you , up to half of my kingdom . ”
41006024	And she went out and said to her mother , “ For what should I ask ? ” And she said , “ The head of John the Baptist . ”
41006025	And she came in immediately with haste to the king and asked , saying , “ I want you to give me at once the head of John the Baptist on a platter . ”
41006026	And the king was exceedingly sorry , but because of his oaths and his guests he did not want to break his word to her .
41006027	And immediately the king sent an executioner with orders to bring John’s head . He went and beheaded him in the prison
41006028	and brought his head on a platter and gave it to the girl , and the girl gave it to her mother .

41006031	And he said to them , “ Come away by yourselves to a desolate place and rest a while . ” For many were coming and going , and they had no leisure even to eat .
41006032	And they went away in the boat to a desolate place by themselves .
41006033	Now many saw them going and recognized them , and they ran there on foot from all the towns and got there ahead of them .
41006034	When he went ashore he saw a great crowd , and he had compassion on them , because they were like sheep without a shepherd . And he began to teach them many things .
41006035	And when it grew late , his disciples came to him and said , “ This is a desolate place , and the hour is now late .
41006036	Send them away to go into the surrounding countryside and villages and buy themselves something to eat . ”
41006037	But he answered them , “ You give them something to eat . ” And they said to him , “ Shall we go and buy two hundred denarii worth of bread and give it to them to eat ? ”
41006038	And he said to them , “ How many loaves do you have ? Go and see . ” And when they had found out , they said , “ Five , and two fish . ”
41006039	Then he commanded them all to sit down in groups on the green grass .
41006040	So they sat down in groups , by hundreds and by fifties .
41006041	And taking the five loaves and the two fish he looked up to heaven and said a blessing and broke the loaves and gave them to the disciples to set before the people . And he divided the two fish among them all .
41006042	And they all ate and were satisfied .
41006043	And they took up twelve baskets full of broken pieces and of the fish .
41006044	And those who ate the loaves were five thousand men .
41006045	Immediately he made his disciples get into the boat and go before him to the other side , to Bethsaida , while he dismissed the crowd .
41006046	And after he had taken leave of them , he went up on the mountain to pray .
41006047	And when evening came , the boat was out on the sea , and he was alone on the land .
41006048	And he saw that they were making headway painfully , for the wind was against them . And about the fourth watch of the night he came to them , walking on the sea . He meant to pass by them ,
41006049	but when they saw him walking on the sea they thought it was a ghost , and cried out ,
41006050	for they all saw him and were terrified . But immediately he spoke to them and said , “ Take heart ; it is I . Do not be afraid . ”
41006051	And he got into the boat with them , and the wind ceased . And they were utterly astounded ,
41006052	for they did not understand about the loaves , but their hearts were hardened .
41006053	When they had crossed over , they came to land at Gennesaret and moored to the shore .
41006054	And when they got out of the boat , the people immediately recognized him
41006055	and ran about the whole region and began to bring the sick people on their beds to wherever they heard he was .
41006056	And wherever he came , in villages , cities , or countryside , they laid the sick in the marketplaces and implored him that they might touch even the fringe of his garment . And as many as touched it were made well .
41007001	Now when the Pharisees gathered to him , with some of the scribes who had come from Jerusalem ,
41007002	they saw that some of his disciples ate with hands that were defiled , that is , unwashed .
41007003	( For the Pharisees and all the Jews do not eat unless they wash their hands , holding to the tradition of the elders ,
41007004	and when they come from the marketplace , they do not eat unless they wash . And there are many other traditions that they observe , such as the washing of cups and pots and copper vessels and dining couches .
41007005	And the Pharisees and the scribes asked him , “ Why do your disciples not walk according to the tradition of the elders , but eat with defiled hands ? ”
41007006	And he said to them , “ Well did Isaiah prophesy of you hypocrites , as it is written , “ ‘ This people honors me with their lips , but their heart is far from me ;
41007007	in vain do they worship me , teaching as doctrines the commandments of men . ’
41007008	You leave the commandment of God and hold to the tradition of men . ”
41007009	And he said to them , “ You have a fine way of rejecting the commandment of God in order to establish your tradition !
41007010	For Moses said , ‘ Honor your father and your mother ’ ; and , ‘ Whoever reviles father or mother must surely die . ’
41007011	But you say , ‘ If a man tells his father or his mother , “ Whatever you would have gained from me is Corban ” ’ ( that is , given to God ) —
41007012	then you no longer permit him to do anything for his father or mother ,
41007013	thus making void the word of God by your tradition that you have handed down . And many such things you do . ”
41007014	And he called the people to him again and said to them , “ Hear me , all of you , and understand :
41007015	There is nothing outside a person that by going into him can defile him , but the things that come out of a person are what defile him . ”
41007017	And when he had entered the house and left the people , his disciples asked him about the parable .
41007018	And he said to them , “ Then are you also without understanding ? Do you not see that whatever goes into a person from outside cannot defile him ,
41007019	since it enters not his heart but his stomach , and is expelled ? ” ( Thus he declared all foods clean .
41007020	And he said , “ What comes out of a person is what defiles him .
41007021	For from within , out of the heart of man , come evil thoughts , sexual immorality , theft , murder , adultery ,
41007022	coveting , wickedness , deceit , sensuality , envy , slander , pride , foolishness .
41007023	All these evil things come from within , and they defile a person . ”
41007024	And from there he arose and went away to the region of Tyre and Sidon . And he entered a house and did not want anyone to know , yet he could not be hidden .
41007025	But immediately a woman whose little daughter had an unclean spirit heard of him and came and fell down at his feet .
41007026	Now the woman was a Gentile , a Syrophoenician by birth . And she begged him to cast the demon out of her daughter .
41007027	And he said to her , “ Let the children be fed first , for it is not right to take the children’s bread and throw it to the dogs . ”
41007028	But she answered him , “ Yes , Lord ; yet even the dogs under the table eat the children’s crumbs . ”
41007029	And he said to her , “ For this statement you may go your way ; the demon has left your daughter . ”
41007030	And she went home and found the child lying in bed and the demon gone .
41007031	Then he returned from the region of Tyre and went through Sidon to the Sea of Galilee , in the region of the Decapolis .
41007032	And they brought to him a man who was deaf and had a speech impediment , and they begged him to lay his hand on him .
41007033	And taking him aside from the crowd privately , he put his fingers into his ears , and after spitting touched his tongue .
41007034	And looking up to heaven , he sighed and said to him , “ Ephphatha , ” that is , “ Be opened . ”
41007035	And his ears were opened , his tongue was released , and he spoke plainly .
41007036	And Jesus charged them to tell no one . But the more he charged them , the more zealously they proclaimed it .
41007037	And they were astonished beyond measure , saying , “ He has done all things well . He even makes the deaf hear and the mute speak . ”
41008001	In those days , when again a great crowd had gathered , and they had nothing to eat , he called his disciples to him and said to them ,

41009001	And he said to them , “ Truly , I say to you , there are some standing here who will not taste death until they see the kingdom of God after it has come with power . ”

41009045	And if your foot causes you to sin , cut it off . It is better for you to enter life lame than with two feet to be thrown into hell .

41009048	‘ where their worm does not die and the fire is not quenched . ’
