41010046	And they came to Jericho . And as he was leaving Jericho with his disciples and a great crowd , Bartimaeus , a blind beggar , the son of Timaeus , was sitting by the roadside .
41010047	And when he heard that it was Jesus of Nazareth , he began to cry out and say , “ Jesus , Son of David , have mercy on me ! ”
41010048	And many rebuked him , telling him to be silent . But he cried out all the more , “ Son of David , have mercy on me ! ”
41010049	And Jesus stopped and said , “ Call him . ” And they called the blind man , saying to him , “ Take heart . Get up ; he is calling you . ”
41010050	And throwing off his cloak , he sprang up and came to Jesus .
41010051	And Jesus said to him , “ What do you want me to do for you ? ” And the blind man said to him , “ Rabbi , let me recover my sight . ”
41010052	And Jesus said to him , “ Go your way ; your faith has made you well . ” And immediately he recovered his sight and followed him on the way .
41011001	Now when they drew near to Jerusalem , to Bethphage and Bethany , at the Mount of Olives , Jesus sent two of his disciples
41011002	and said to them , “ Go into the village in front of you , and immediately as you enter it you will find a colt tied , on which no one has ever sat . Untie it and bring it .
41011003	If anyone says to you , ‘ Why are you doing this ? ’ say , ‘ The Lord has need of it and will send it back here immediately . ’ ”
41011004	And they went away and found a colt tied at a door outside in the street , and they untied it .
41011005	And some of those standing there said to them , “ What are you doing , untying the colt ? ”
41011006	And they told them what Jesus had said , and they let them go .
41011007	And they brought the colt to Jesus and threw their cloaks on it , and he sat on it .
41011008	And many spread their cloaks on the road , and others spread leafy branches that they had cut from the fields .
41011009	And those who went before and those who followed were shouting , “ Hosanna ! Blessed is he who comes in the name of the Lord !
41011010	Blessed is the coming kingdom of our father David ! Hosanna in the highest ! ”
41011011	And he entered Jerusalem and went into the temple . And when he had looked around at everything , as it was already late , he went out to Bethany with the twelve .
41011012	On the following day , when they came from Bethany , he was hungry .
41011013	And seeing in the distance a fig tree in leaf , he went to see if he could find anything on it . When he came to it , he found nothing but leaves , for it was not the season for figs .
41011014	And he said to it , “ May no one ever eat fruit from you again . ” And his disciples heard it .
41011015	And they came to Jerusalem . And he entered the temple and began to drive out those who sold and those who bought in the temple , and he overturned the tables of the money-changers and the seats of those who sold pigeons .
41011016	And he would not allow anyone to carry anything through the temple .
41011017	And he was teaching them and saying to them , “ Is it not written , ‘ My house shall be called a house of prayer for all the nations ’ ? But you have made it a den of robbers . ”
41011018	And the chief priests and the scribes heard it and were seeking a way to destroy him , for they feared him , because all the crowd was astonished at his teaching .
41011019	And when evening came they went out of the city .
41011020	As they passed by in the morning , they saw the fig tree withered away to its roots .
41011021	And Peter remembered and said to him , “ Rabbi , look ! The fig tree that you cursed has withered . ”
41011022	And Jesus answered them , “ Have faith in God .
41011023	Truly , I say to you , whoever says to this mountain , ‘ Be taken up and thrown into the sea , ’ and does not doubt in his heart , but believes that what he says will come to pass , it will be done for him .
41011024	Therefore I tell you , whatever you ask in prayer , believe that you have received it , and it will be yours .
41011025	And whenever you stand praying , forgive , if you have anything against anyone , so that your Father also who is in heaven may forgive you your trespasses . ”
41011027	And they came again to Jerusalem . And as he was walking in the temple , the chief priests and the scribes and the elders came to him ,
41011028	and they said to him , “ By what authority are you doing these things , or who gave you this authority to do them ? ”
41011029	Jesus said to them , “ I will ask you one question ; answer me , and I will tell you by what authority I do these things .
41011030	Was the baptism of John from heaven or from man ? Answer me . ”
41011031	And they discussed it with one another , saying , “ If we say , ‘ From heaven , ’ he will say , ‘ Why then did you not believe him ? ’
41011032	But shall we say , ‘ From man ’ ? ” — they were afraid of the people , for they all held that John really was a prophet .
41011033	So they answered Jesus , “ We do not know . ” And Jesus said to them , “ Neither will I tell you by what authority I do these things . ”
41012001	And he began to speak to them in parables . “ A man planted a vineyard and put a fence around it and dug a pit for the winepress and built a tower , and leased it to tenants and went into another country .
41012002	When the season came , he sent a servant to the tenants to get from them some of the fruit of the vineyard .
41012003	And they took him and beat him and sent him away empty-handed .
41012004	Again he sent to them another servant , and they struck him on the head and treated him shamefully .
41012005	And he sent another , and him they killed . And so with many others : some they beat , and some they killed .
41012006	He had still one other , a beloved son . Finally he sent him to them , saying , ‘ They will respect my son . ’
41012007	But those tenants said to one another , ‘ This is the heir . Come , let us kill him , and the inheritance will be ours . ’
41012008	And they took him and killed him and threw him out of the vineyard .
41012009	What will the owner of the vineyard do ? He will come and destroy the tenants and give the vineyard to others .
41012010	Have you not read this Scripture : “ ‘ The stone that the builders rejected has become the cornerstone ;
41012011	this was the Lord’s doing , and it is marvelous in our eyes ’ ? ”
41012012	And they were seeking to arrest him but feared the people , for they perceived that he had told the parable against them . So they left him and went away .
41012013	And they sent to him some of the Pharisees and some of the Herodians , to trap him in his talk .
41012014	And they came and said to him , “ Teacher , we know that you are true and do not care about anyone’s opinion . For you are not swayed by appearances , but truly teach the way of God . Is it lawful to pay taxes to Caesar , or not ? Should we pay them , or should we not ? ”
41012015	But , knowing their hypocrisy , he said to them , “ Why put me to the test ? Bring me a denarius and let me look at it . ”
41012016	And they brought one . And he said to them , “ Whose likeness and inscription is this ? ” They said to him , “ Caesar’s . ”
41012017	Jesus said to them , “ Render to Caesar the things that are Caesar’s , and to God the things that are God’s . ” And they marveled at him .
41012018	And Sadducees came to him , who say that there is no resurrection . And they asked him a question , saying ,
41012019	“ Teacher , Moses wrote for us that if a man’s brother dies and leaves a wife , but leaves no child , the man must take the widow and raise up offspring for his brother .
41012020	There were seven brothers ; the first took a wife , and when he died left no offspring .
41012021	And the second took her , and died , leaving no offspring . And the third likewise .
41012022	And the seven left no offspring . Last of all the woman also died .
41012023	In the resurrection , when they rise again , whose wife will she be ? For the seven had her as wife . ”
41012024	Jesus said to them , “ Is this not the reason you are wrong , because you know neither the Scriptures nor the power of God ?
41012025	For when they rise from the dead , they neither marry nor are given in marriage , but are like angels in heaven .
41012026	And as for the dead being raised , have you not read in the book of Moses , in the passage about the bush , how God spoke to him , saying , ‘ I am the God of Abraham , and the God of Isaac , and the God of Jacob ’ ?
41012027	He is not God of the dead , but of the living . You are quite wrong . ”
41012028	And one of the scribes came up and heard them disputing with one another , and seeing that he answered them well , asked him , “ Which commandment is the most important of all ? ”
41012029	Jesus answered , “ The most important is , ‘ Hear , O Israel : The Lord our God , the Lord is one .
41012030	And you shall love the Lord your God with all your heart and with all your soul and with all your mind and with all your strength . ’
41012031	The second is this : ‘ You shall love your neighbor as yourself . ’ There is no other commandment greater than these . ”
41012032	And the scribe said to him , “ You are right , Teacher . You have truly said that he is one , and there is no other besides him .
41012033	And to love him with all the heart and with all the understanding and with all the strength , and to love one’s neighbor as oneself , is much more than all whole burnt offerings and sacrifices . ”
41012034	And when Jesus saw that he answered wisely , he said to him , “ You are not far from the kingdom of God . ” And after that no one dared to ask him any more questions .
41012035	And as Jesus taught in the temple , he said , “ How can the scribes say that the Christ is the son of David ?
41012036	David himself , in the Holy Spirit , declared , “ ‘ The Lord said to my Lord , Sit at my right hand , until I put your enemies under your feet . ’
41012037	David himself calls him Lord . So how is he his son ? ” And the great throng heard him gladly .
41012038	And in his teaching he said , “ Beware of the scribes , who like to walk around in long robes and like greetings in the marketplaces
41012039	and have the best seats in the synagogues and the places of honor at feasts ,
41012040	who devour widows ’ houses and for a pretense make long prayers . They will receive the greater condemnation . ”
41012041	And he sat down opposite the treasury and watched the people putting money into the offering box . Many rich people put in large sums .
41012042	And a poor widow came and put in two small copper coins , which make a penny .
41012043	And he called his disciples to him and said to them , “ Truly , I say to you , this poor widow has put in more than all those who are contributing to the offering box .
41012044	For they all contributed out of their abundance , but she out of her poverty has put in everything she had , all she had to live on . ”
41013001	And as he came out of the temple , one of his disciples said to him , “ Look , Teacher , what wonderful stones and what wonderful buildings ! ”
41013002	And Jesus said to him , “ Do you see these great buildings ? There will not be left here one stone upon another that will not be thrown down . ”
41013003	And as he sat on the Mount of Olives opposite the temple , Peter and James and John and Andrew asked him privately ,
41013004	“ Tell us , when will these things be , and what will be the sign when all these things are about to be accomplished ? ”
41013005	And Jesus began to say to them , “ See that no one leads you astray .
41013006	Many will come in my name , saying , ‘ I am he ! ’ and they will lead many astray .
41013007	And when you hear of wars and rumors of wars , do not be alarmed . This must take place , but the end is not yet .
41013008	For nation will rise against nation , and kingdom against kingdom . There will be earthquakes in various places ; there will be famines . These are but the beginning of the birth pains .
41013009	“ But be on your guard . For they will deliver you over to councils , and you will be beaten in synagogues , and you will stand before governors and kings for my sake , to bear witness before them .
41013010	And the gospel must first be proclaimed to all nations .
41013011	And when they bring you to trial and deliver you over , do not be anxious beforehand what you are to say , but say whatever is given you in that hour , for it is not you who speak , but the Holy Spirit .
41013012	And brother will deliver brother over to death , and the father his child , and children will rise against parents and have them put to death .
41013013	And you will be hated by all for my name’s sake . But the one who endures to the end will be saved .
41013014	“ But when you see the abomination of desolation standing where he ought not to be ( let the reader understand ) , then let those who are in Judea flee to the mountains .
41013015	Let the one who is on the housetop not go down , nor enter his house , to take anything out ,
41013016	and let the one who is in the field not turn back to take his cloak .
41013017	And alas for women who are pregnant and for those who are nursing infants in those days !
41013018	Pray that it may not happen in winter .
41013019	For in those days there will be such tribulation as has not been from the beginning of the creation that God created until now , and never will be .
41013020	And if the Lord had not cut short the days , no human being would be saved . But for the sake of the elect , whom he chose , he shortened the days .
41013021	And then if anyone says to you , ‘ Look , here is the Christ ! ’ or ‘ Look , there he is ! ’ do not believe it .
41013022	For false christs and false prophets will arise and perform signs and wonders , to lead astray , if possible , the elect .
41013023	But be on guard ; I have told you all things beforehand .
41013024	“ But in those days , after that tribulation , the sun will be darkened , and the moon will not give its light ,
41013025	and the stars will be falling from heaven , and the powers in the heavens will be shaken .
41013026	And then they will see the Son of Man coming in clouds with great power and glory .
41013027	And then he will send out the angels and gather his elect from the four winds , from the ends of the earth to the ends of heaven .
41013028	“ From the fig tree learn its lesson : as soon as its branch becomes tender and puts out its leaves , you know that summer is near .
41013029	So also , when you see these things taking place , you know that he is near , at the very gates .
41013030	Truly , I say to you , this generation will not pass away until all these things take place .
41013031	Heaven and earth will pass away , but my words will not pass away .
41013032	“ But concerning that day or that hour , no one knows , not even the angels in heaven , nor the Son , but only the Father .
41013033	Be on guard , keep awake . For you do not know when the time will come .
41013034	It is like a man going on a journey , when he leaves home and puts his servants in charge , each with his work , and commands the doorkeeper to stay awake .
41013035	Therefore stay awake — for you do not know when the master of the house will come , in the evening , or at midnight , or when the rooster crows , or in the morning —
41013036	lest he come suddenly and find you asleep .
41013037	And what I say to you I say to all : Stay awake . ”
41014001	It was now two days before the Passover and the Feast of Unleavened Bread . And the chief priests and the scribes were seeking how to arrest him by stealth and kill him ,
41014002	for they said , “ Not during the feast , lest there be an uproar from the people . ”
41014003	And while he was at Bethany in the house of Simon the leper , as he was reclining at table , a woman came with an alabaster flask of ointment of pure nard , very costly , and she broke the flask and poured it over his head .
41014004	There were some who said to themselves indignantly , “ Why was the ointment wasted like that ?
41014005	For this ointment could have been sold for more than three hundred denarii and given to the poor . ” And they scolded her .
41014006	But Jesus said , “ Leave her alone . Why do you trouble her ? She has done a beautiful thing to me .
41014007	For you always have the poor with you , and whenever you want , you can do good for them . But you will not always have me .
41014008	She has done what she could ; she has anointed my body beforehand for burial .
41014009	And truly , I say to you , wherever the gospel is proclaimed in the whole world , what she has done will be told in memory of her . ”
41014010	Then Judas Iscariot , who was one of the twelve , went to the chief priests in order to betray him to them .
41014011	And when they heard it , they were glad and promised to give him money . And he sought an opportunity to betray him .
41014012	And on the first day of Unleavened Bread , when they sacrificed the Passover lamb , his disciples said to him , “ Where will you have us go and prepare for you to eat the Passover ? ”
41014013	And he sent two of his disciples and said to them , “ Go into the city , and a man carrying a jar of water will meet you . Follow him ,
41014014	and wherever he enters , say to the master of the house , ‘ The Teacher says , Where is my guest room , where I may eat the Passover with my disciples ? ’
41014015	And he will show you a large upper room furnished and ready ; there prepare for us . ”
41014016	And the disciples set out and went to the city and found it just as he had told them , and they prepared the Passover .
41014017	And when it was evening , he came with the twelve .
41014018	And as they were reclining at table and eating , Jesus said , “ Truly , I say to you , one of you will betray me , one who is eating with me . ”
41014019	They began to be sorrowful and to say to him one after another , “ Is it I ? ”
41014020	He said to them , “ It is one of the twelve , one who is dipping bread into the dish with me .
41014021	For the Son of Man goes as it is written of him , but woe to that man by whom the Son of Man is betrayed ! It would have been better for that man if he had not been born . ”
41014022	And as they were eating , he took bread , and after blessing it broke it and gave it to them , and said , “ Take ; this is my body . ”
41014023	And he took a cup , and when he had given thanks he gave it to them , and they all drank of it .
41014024	And he said to them , “ This is my blood of the covenant , which is poured out for many .
41014025	Truly , I say to you , I will not drink again of the fruit of the vine until that day when I drink it new in the kingdom of God . ”
41014026	And when they had sung a hymn , they went out to the Mount of Olives .
41014027	And Jesus said to them , “ You will all fall away , for it is written , ‘ I will strike the shepherd , and the sheep will be scattered . ’
41014028	But after I am raised up , I will go before you to Galilee . ”
41014029	Peter said to him , “ Even though they all fall away , I will not . ”
41014030	And Jesus said to him , “ Truly , I tell you , this very night , before the rooster crows twice , you will deny me three times . ”
41014031	But he said emphatically , “ If I must die with you , I will not deny you . ” And they all said the same .
41014032	And they went to a place called Gethsemane . And he said to his disciples , “ Sit here while I pray . ”
41014033	And he took with him Peter and James and John , and began to be greatly distressed and troubled .
41014034	And he said to them , “ My soul is very sorrowful , even to death . Remain here and watch . ”
41014035	And going a little farther , he fell on the ground and prayed that , if it were possible , the hour might pass from him .
41014036	And he said , “ Abba , Father , all things are possible for you . Remove this cup from me . Yet not what I will , but what you will . ”
41014037	And he came and found them sleeping , and he said to Peter , “ Simon , are you asleep ? Could you not watch one hour ?
41014038	Watch and pray that you may not enter into temptation . The spirit indeed is willing , but the flesh is weak . ”
41014039	And again he went away and prayed , saying the same words .
41014040	And again he came and found them sleeping , for their eyes were very heavy , and they did not know what to answer him .
41014041	And he came the third time and said to them , “ Are you still sleeping and taking your rest ? It is enough ; the hour has come . The Son of Man is betrayed into the hands of sinners .
41014042	Rise , let us be going ; see , my betrayer is at hand . ”
41014043	And immediately , while he was still speaking , Judas came , one of the twelve , and with him a crowd with swords and clubs , from the chief priests and the scribes and the elders .
41014044	Now the betrayer had given them a sign , saying , “ The one I will kiss is the man . Seize him and lead him away under guard . ”
41014045	And when he came , he went up to him at once and said , “ Rabbi ! ” And he kissed him .
41014046	And they laid hands on him and seized him .
41014047	But one of those who stood by drew his sword and struck the servant of the high priest and cut off his ear .
41014048	And Jesus said to them , “ Have you come out as against a robber , with swords and clubs to capture me ?
41014049	Day after day I was with you in the temple teaching , and you did not seize me . But let the Scriptures be fulfilled . ”
41014050	And they all left him and fled .
41014051	And a young man followed him , with nothing but a linen cloth about his body . And they seized him ,
41014052	but he left the linen cloth and ran away naked .
41014053	And they led Jesus to the high priest . And all the chief priests and the elders and the scribes came together .
41014054	And Peter had followed him at a distance , right into the courtyard of the high priest . And he was sitting with the guards and warming himself at the fire .
41014055	Now the chief priests and the whole Council were seeking testimony against Jesus to put him to death , but they found none .
41014056	For many bore false witness against him , but their testimony did not agree .
41014057	And some stood up and bore false witness against him , saying ,
41014058	“ We heard him say , ‘ I will destroy this temple that is made with hands , and in three days I will build another , not made with hands . ’ ”
41014059	Yet even about this their testimony did not agree .
41014060	And the high priest stood up in the midst and asked Jesus , “ Have you no answer to make ? What is it that these men testify against you ? ”
41014061	But he remained silent and made no answer . Again the high priest asked him , “ Are you the Christ , the Son of the Blessed ? ”
41014062	And Jesus said , “ I am , and you will see the Son of Man seated at the right hand of Power , and coming with the clouds of heaven . ”
41014063	And the high priest tore his garments and said , “ What further witnesses do we need ?
41014064	You have heard his blasphemy . What is your decision ? ” And they all condemned him as deserving death .
41014065	And some began to spit on him and to cover his face and to strike him , saying to him , “ Prophesy ! ” And the guards received him with blows .
41014066	And as Peter was below in the courtyard , one of the servant girls of the high priest came ,
41014067	and seeing Peter warming himself , she looked at him and said , “ You also were with the Nazarene , Jesus . ”
41014068	But he denied it , saying , “ I neither know nor understand what you mean . ” And he went out into the gateway and the rooster crowed .
41014069	And the servant girl saw him and began again to say to the bystanders , “ This man is one of them . ”
41014070	But again he denied it . And after a little while the bystanders again said to Peter , “ Certainly you are one of them , for you are a Galilean . ”
41014071	But he began to invoke a curse on himself and to swear , “ I do not know this man of whom you speak . ”
41014072	And immediately the rooster crowed a second time . And Peter remembered how Jesus had said to him , “ Before the rooster crows twice , you will deny me three times . ” And he broke down and wept .
41015001	And as soon as it was morning , the chief priests held a consultation with the elders and scribes and the whole Council . And they bound Jesus and led him away and delivered him over to Pilate .
41015002	And Pilate asked him , “ Are you the King of the Jews ? ” And he answered him , “ You have said so . ”
41015003	And the chief priests accused him of many things .
41015004	And Pilate again asked him , “ Have you no answer to make ? See how many charges they bring against you . ”
41015005	But Jesus made no further answer , so that Pilate was amazed .
41015006	Now at the feast he used to release for them one prisoner for whom they asked .
41015007	And among the rebels in prison , who had committed murder in the insurrection , there was a man called Barabbas .
41015008	And the crowd came up and began to ask Pilate to do as he usually did for them .
41015009	And he answered them , saying , “ Do you want me to release for you the King of the Jews ? ”
41015010	For he perceived that it was out of envy that the chief priests had delivered him up .
41015011	But the chief priests stirred up the crowd to have him release for them Barabbas instead .
41015012	And Pilate again said to them , “ Then what shall I do with the man you call the King of the Jews ? ”
41015013	And they cried out again , “ Crucify him . ”
41015014	And Pilate said to them , “ Why , what evil has he done ? ” But they shouted all the more , “ Crucify him . ”
41015015	So Pilate , wishing to satisfy the crowd , released for them Barabbas , and having scourged Jesus , he delivered him to be crucified .
41015016	And the soldiers led him away inside the palace ( that is , the governor’s headquarters ) , and they called together the whole battalion .
41015017	And they clothed him in a purple cloak , and twisting together a crown of thorns , they put it on him .
41015018	And they began to salute him , “ Hail , King of the Jews ! ”
41015019	And they were striking his head with a reed and spitting on him and kneeling down in homage to him .
41015020	And when they had mocked him , they stripped him of the purple cloak and put his own clothes on him . And they led him out to crucify him .
41015021	And they compelled a passerby , Simon of Cyrene , who was coming in from the country , the father of Alexander and Rufus , to carry his cross .
41015022	And they brought him to the place called Golgotha ( which means Place of a Skull ) .
41015023	And they offered him wine mixed with myrrh , but he did not take it .
41015024	And they crucified him and divided his garments among them , casting lots for them , to decide what each should take .
41015025	And it was the third hour when they crucified him .
41015026	And the inscription of the charge against him read , “ The King of the Jews . ”
41015027	And with him they crucified two robbers , one on his right and one on his left .
41015029	And those who passed by derided him , wagging their heads and saying , “ Aha ! You who would destroy the temple and rebuild it in three days ,
41015030	save yourself , and come down from the cross ! ”
41015031	So also the chief priests with the scribes mocked him to one another , saying , “ He saved others ; he cannot save himself .
41015032	Let the Christ , the King of Israel , come down now from the cross that we may see and believe . ” Those who were crucified with him also reviled him .
41015033	And when the sixth hour had come , there was darkness over the whole land until the ninth hour .
41015034	And at the ninth hour Jesus cried with a loud voice , “ Eloi , Eloi , lema sabachthani ? ” which means , “ My God , my God , why have you forsaken me ? ”
41015035	And some of the bystanders hearing it said , “ Behold , he is calling Elijah . ”
41015036	And someone ran and filled a sponge with sour wine , put it on a reed and gave it to him to drink , saying , “ Wait , let us see whether Elijah will come to take him down . ”
41015037	And Jesus uttered a loud cry and breathed his last .
41015038	And the curtain of the temple was torn in two , from top to bottom .
41015039	And when the centurion , who stood facing him , saw that in this way he breathed his last , he said , “ Truly this man was the Son of God ! ”
41015040	There were also women looking on from a distance , among whom were Mary Magdalene , and Mary the mother of James the younger and of Joses , and Salome .
41015041	When he was in Galilee , they followed him and ministered to him , and there were also many other women who came up with him to Jerusalem .
41015042	And when evening had come , since it was the day of Preparation , that is , the day before the Sabbath ,
41015043	Joseph of Arimathea , a respected member of the Council , who was also himself looking for the kingdom of God , took courage and went to Pilate and asked for the body of Jesus .
41015044	Pilate was surprised to hear that he should have already died . And summoning the centurion , he asked him whether he was already dead .
41015045	And when he learned from the centurion that he was dead , he granted the corpse to Joseph .
41015046	And Joseph bought a linen shroud , and taking him down , wrapped him in the linen shroud and laid him in a tomb that had been cut out of the rock . And he rolled a stone against the entrance of the tomb .
41015047	Mary Magdalene and Mary the mother of Joses saw where he was laid .
41016001	When the Sabbath was past , Mary Magdalene and Mary the mother of James and Salome bought spices , so that they might go and anoint him .
41016002	And very early on the first day of the week , when the sun had risen , they went to the tomb .
41016003	And they were saying to one another , “ Who will roll away the stone for us from the entrance of the tomb ? ”
41016004	And looking up , they saw that the stone had been rolled back — it was very large .
41016005	And entering the tomb , they saw a young man sitting on the right side , dressed in a white robe , and they were alarmed .
41016006	And he said to them , “ Do not be alarmed . You seek Jesus of Nazareth , who was crucified . He has risen ; he is not here . See the place where they laid him .
41016007	But go , tell his disciples and Peter that he is going before you to Galilee . There you will see him , just as he told you . ”
41016008	And they went out and fled from the tomb , for trembling and astonishment had seized them , and they said nothing to anyone , for they were afraid .
41016009	[ [ Now when he rose early on the first day of the week , he appeared first to Mary Magdalene , from whom he had cast out seven demons .
41016010	She went and told those who had been with him , as they mourned and wept .
41016011	But when they heard that he was alive and had been seen by her , they would not believe it .
41016012	After these things he appeared in another form to two of them , as they were walking into the country .
41016013	And they went back and told the rest , but they did not believe them .
41016014	Afterward he appeared to the eleven themselves as they were reclining at table , and he rebuked them for their unbelief and hardness of heart , because they had not believed those who saw him after he had risen .
41016015	And he said to them , “ Go into all the world and proclaim the gospel to the whole creation .
41016016	Whoever believes and is baptized will be saved , but whoever does not believe will be condemned .
41016017	And these signs will accompany those who believe : in my name they will cast out demons ; they will speak in new tongues ;
41016018	they will pick up serpents with their hands ; and if they drink any deadly poison , it will not hurt them ; they will lay their hands on the sick , and they will recover . ”
41016019	So then the Lord Jesus , after he had spoken to them , was taken up into heaven and sat down at the right hand of God .
41016020	And they went out and preached everywhere , while the Lord worked with them and confirmed the message by accompanying signs . ] ]
42001001	Inasmuch as many have undertaken to compile a narrative of the things that have been accomplished among us ,
42001002	just as those who from the beginning were eyewitnesses and ministers of the word have delivered them to us ,
42001003	it seemed good to me also , having followed all things closely for some time past , to write an orderly account for you , most excellent Theophilus ,
42001004	that you may have certainty concerning the things you have been taught .
42001005	In the days of Herod , king of Judea , there was a priest named Zechariah , of the division of Abijah . And he had a wife from the daughters of Aaron , and her name was Elizabeth .
42001006	And they were both righteous before God , walking blamelessly in all the commandments and statutes of the Lord .
42001007	But they had no child , because Elizabeth was barren , and both were advanced in years .
42001008	Now while he was serving as priest before God when his division was on duty ,
42001009	according to the custom of the priesthood , he was chosen by lot to enter the temple of the Lord and burn incense .
42001010	And the whole multitude of the people were praying outside at the hour of incense .
42001011	And there appeared to him an angel of the Lord standing on the right side of the altar of incense .
42001012	And Zechariah was troubled when he saw him , and fear fell upon him .
42001013	But the angel said to him , “ Do not be afraid , Zechariah , for your prayer has been heard , and your wife Elizabeth will bear you a son , and you shall call his name John .
42001014	And you will have joy and gladness , and many will rejoice at his birth ,
42001015	for he will be great before the Lord . And he must not drink wine or strong drink , and he will be filled with the Holy Spirit , even from his mother’s womb .
42001016	And he will turn many of the children of Israel to the Lord their God ,
42001017	and he will go before him in the spirit and power of Elijah , to turn the hearts of the fathers to the children , and the disobedient to the wisdom of the just , to make ready for the Lord a people prepared . ”
42001018	And Zechariah said to the angel , “ How shall I know this ? For I am an old man , and my wife is advanced in years . ”
42001019	And the angel answered him , “ I am Gabriel . I stand in the presence of God , and I was sent to speak to you and to bring you this good news .
42001020	And behold , you will be silent and unable to speak until the day that these things take place , because you did not believe my words , which will be fulfilled in their time . ”
42001021	And the people were waiting for Zechariah , and they were wondering at his delay in the temple .
42001022	And when he came out , he was unable to speak to them , and they realized that he had seen a vision in the temple . And he kept making signs to them and remained mute .
42001023	And when his time of service was ended , he went to his home .
42001024	After these days his wife Elizabeth conceived , and for five months she kept herself hidden , saying ,
42001025	“ Thus the Lord has done for me in the days when he looked on me , to take away my reproach among people . ”
42001026	In the sixth month the angel Gabriel was sent from God to a city of Galilee named Nazareth ,
42001027	to a virgin betrothed to a man whose name was Joseph , of the house of David . And the virgin’s name was Mary .
42001028	And he came to her and said , “ Greetings , O favored one , the Lord is with you ! ”
42001029	But she was greatly troubled at the saying , and tried to discern what sort of greeting this might be .
42001030	And the angel said to her , “ Do not be afraid , Mary , for you have found favor with God .
42001031	And behold , you will conceive in your womb and bear a son , and you shall call his name Jesus .
42001032	He will be great and will be called the Son of the Most High . And the Lord God will give to him the throne of his father David ,
42001033	and he will reign over the house of Jacob forever , and of his kingdom there will be no end . ”
42001034	And Mary said to the angel , “ How will this be , since I am a virgin ? ”
42001035	And the angel answered her , “ The Holy Spirit will come upon you , and the power of the Most High will overshadow you ; therefore the child to be born will be called holy — the Son of God .
42001036	And behold , your relative Elizabeth in her old age has also conceived a son , and this is the sixth month with her who was called barren .
42001037	For nothing will be impossible with God . ”
42001038	And Mary said , “ Behold , I am the servant of the Lord ; let it be to me according to your word . ” And the angel departed from her .
42001039	In those days Mary arose and went with haste into the hill country , to a town in Judah ,
42001040	and she entered the house of Zechariah and greeted Elizabeth .
42001041	And when Elizabeth heard the greeting of Mary , the baby leaped in her womb . And Elizabeth was filled with the Holy Spirit ,
42001042	and she exclaimed with a loud cry , “ Blessed are you among women , and blessed is the fruit of your womb !
42001043	And why is this granted to me that the mother of my Lord should come to me ?
42001044	For behold , when the sound of your greeting came to my ears , the baby in my womb leaped for joy .
42001045	And blessed is she who believed that there would be a fulfillment of what was spoken to her from the Lord . ”
42001046	And Mary said , “ My soul magnifies the Lord ,
42001047	and my spirit rejoices in God my Savior ,
42001048	for he has looked on the humble estate of his servant . For behold , from now on all generations will call me blessed ;
42001049	for he who is mighty has done great things for me , and holy is his name .
42001050	And his mercy is for those who fear him from generation to generation .
42001051	He has shown strength with his arm ; he has scattered the proud in the thoughts of their hearts ;
42001052	he has brought down the mighty from their thrones and exalted those of humble estate ;
42001053	he has filled the hungry with good things , and the rich he has sent away empty .
42001054	He has helped his servant Israel , in remembrance of his mercy ,
42001055	as he spoke to our fathers , to Abraham and to his offspring forever . ”
42001056	And Mary remained with her about three months and returned to her home .
42001057	Now the time came for Elizabeth to give birth , and she bore a son .
42001058	And her neighbors and relatives heard that the Lord had shown great mercy to her , and they rejoiced with her .
42001059	And on the eighth day they came to circumcise the child . And they would have called him Zechariah after his father ,
42001060	but his mother answered , “ No ; he shall be called John . ”
42001061	And they said to her , “ None of your relatives is called by this name . ”
42001062	And they made signs to his father , inquiring what he wanted him to be called .
42001063	And he asked for a writing tablet and wrote , “ His name is John . ” And they all wondered .
42001064	And immediately his mouth was opened and his tongue loosed , and he spoke , blessing God .
42001065	And fear came on all their neighbors . And all these things were talked about through all the hill country of Judea ,
42001066	and all who heard them laid them up in their hearts , saying , “ What then will this child be ? ” For the hand of the Lord was with him .
42001067	And his father Zechariah was filled with the Holy Spirit and prophesied , saying ,
42001068	“ Blessed be the Lord God of Israel , for he has visited and redeemed his people
42001069	and has raised up a horn of salvation for us in the house of his servant David ,
42001070	as he spoke by the mouth of his holy prophets from of old ,
42001071	that we should be saved from our enemies and from the hand of all who hate us ;
42001072	to show the mercy promised to our fathers and to remember his holy covenant ,
42001073	the oath that he swore to our father Abraham , to grant us
42001074	that we , being delivered from the hand of our enemies , might serve him without fear ,
42001075	in holiness and righteousness before him all our days .
42001076	And you , child , will be called the prophet of the Most High ; for you will go before the Lord to prepare his ways ,
42001077	to give knowledge of salvation to his people in the forgiveness of their sins ,
42001078	because of the tender mercy of our God , whereby the sunrise shall visit us from on high
42001079	to give light to those who sit in darkness and in the shadow of death , to guide our feet into the way of peace . ”
42001080	And the child grew and became strong in spirit , and he was in the wilderness until the day of his public appearance to Israel .
42002001	In those days a decree went out from Caesar Augustus that all the world should be registered .
42002002	This was the first registration when Quirinius was governor of Syria .
42002003	And all went to be registered , each to his own town .
42002004	And Joseph also went up from Galilee , from the town of Nazareth , to Judea , to the city of David , which is called Bethlehem , because he was of the house and lineage of David ,
42002005	to be registered with Mary , his betrothed , who was with child .
42002006	And while they were there , the time came for her to give birth .
42002007	And she gave birth to her firstborn son and wrapped him in swaddling cloths and laid him in a manger , because there was no place for them in the inn .
42002008	And in the same region there were shepherds out in the field , keeping watch over their flock by night .
42002009	And an angel of the Lord appeared to them , and the glory of the Lord shone around them , and they were filled with fear .
42002010	And the angel said to them , “ Fear not , for behold , I bring you good news of great joy that will be for all the people .
42002011	For unto you is born this day in the city of David a Savior , who is Christ the Lord .
42002012	And this will be a sign for you : you will find a baby wrapped in swaddling cloths and lying in a manger . ”
42002013	And suddenly there was with the angel a multitude of the heavenly host praising God and saying ,
42002014	“ Glory to God in the highest , and on earth peace among those with whom he is pleased ! ”
42002015	When the angels went away from them into heaven , the shepherds said to one another , “ Let us go over to Bethlehem and see this thing that has happened , which the Lord has made known to us . ”
42002016	And they went with haste and found Mary and Joseph , and the baby lying in a manger .
42002017	And when they saw it , they made known the saying that had been told them concerning this child .
42002018	And all who heard it wondered at what the shepherds told them .
42002019	But Mary treasured up all these things , pondering them in her heart .
42002020	And the shepherds returned , glorifying and praising God for all they had heard and seen , as it had been told them .
42002021	And at the end of eight days , when he was circumcised , he was called Jesus , the name given by the angel before he was conceived in the womb .
42002022	And when the time came for their purification according to the Law of Moses , they brought him up to Jerusalem to present him to the Lord
42002023	( as it is written in the Law of the Lord , “ Every male who first opens the womb shall be called holy to the Lord ”
42002024	and to offer a sacrifice according to what is said in the Law of the Lord , “ a pair of turtledoves , or two young pigeons . ”
42002025	Now there was a man in Jerusalem , whose name was Simeon , and this man was righteous and devout , waiting for the consolation of Israel , and the Holy Spirit was upon him .
42002026	And it had been revealed to him by the Holy Spirit that he would not see death before he had seen the Lord’s Christ .
42002027	And he came in the Spirit into the temple , and when the parents brought in the child Jesus , to do for him according to the custom of the Law ,
42002028	he took him up in his arms and blessed God and said ,
42002029	“ Lord , now you are letting your servant depart in peace , according to your word ;
42002030	for my eyes have seen your salvation
42002031	that you have prepared in the presence of all peoples ,
42002032	a light for revelation to the Gentiles , and for glory to your people Israel . ”
42002033	And his father and his mother marveled at what was said about him .
42002034	And Simeon blessed them and said to Mary his mother , “ Behold , this child is appointed for the fall and rising of many in Israel , and for a sign that is opposed
42002035	( and a sword will pierce through your own soul also ) , so that thoughts from many hearts may be revealed . ”
42002036	And there was a prophetess , Anna , the daughter of Phanuel , of the tribe of Asher . She was advanced in years , having lived with her husband seven years from when she was a virgin ,
42002037	and then as a widow until she was eighty-four . She did not depart from the temple , worshiping with fasting and prayer night and day .
42002038	And coming up at that very hour she began to give thanks to God and to speak of him to all who were waiting for the redemption of Jerusalem .
42002039	And when they had performed everything according to the Law of the Lord , they returned into Galilee , to their own town of Nazareth .
42002040	And the child grew and became strong , filled with wisdom . And the favor of God was upon him .
42002041	Now his parents went to Jerusalem every year at the Feast of the Passover .
42002042	And when he was twelve years old , they went up according to custom .
42002043	And when the feast was ended , as they were returning , the boy Jesus stayed behind in Jerusalem . His parents did not know it ,
42002044	but supposing him to be in the group they went a day’s journey , but then they began to search for him among their relatives and acquaintances ,
42002045	and when they did not find him , they returned to Jerusalem , searching for him .
42002046	After three days they found him in the temple , sitting among the teachers , listening to them and asking them questions .
42002047	And all who heard him were amazed at his understanding and his answers .
42002048	And when his parents saw him , they were astonished . And his mother said to him , “ Son , why have you treated us so ? Behold , your father and I have been searching for you in great distress . ”
42002049	And he said to them , “ Why were you looking for me ? Did you not know that I must be in my Father’s house ? ”
42002050	And they did not understand the saying that he spoke to them .
42002051	And he went down with them and came to Nazareth and was submissive to them . And his mother treasured up all these things in her heart .
42002052	And Jesus increased in wisdom and in stature and in favor with God and man .
42003001	In the fifteenth year of the reign of Tiberius Caesar , Pontius Pilate being governor of Judea , and Herod being tetrarch of Galilee , and his brother Philip tetrarch of the region of Ituraea and Trachonitis , and Lysanias tetrarch of Abilene ,
42003002	during the high priesthood of Annas and Caiaphas , the word of God came to John the son of Zechariah in the wilderness .
42003003	And he went into all the region around the Jordan , proclaiming a baptism of repentance for the forgiveness of sins .
42003004	As it is written in the book of the words of Isaiah the prophet , “ The voice of one crying in the wilderness : ‘ Prepare the way of the Lord , make his paths straight .
42003005	Every valley shall be filled , and every mountain and hill shall be made low , and the crooked shall become straight , and the rough places shall become level ways ,
42003006	and all flesh shall see the salvation of God . ’ ”
42003007	He said therefore to the crowds that came out to be baptized by him , “ You brood of vipers ! Who warned you to flee from the wrath to come ?
42003008	Bear fruits in keeping with repentance . And do not begin to say to yourselves , ‘ We have Abraham as our father . ’ For I tell you , God is able from these stones to raise up children for Abraham .
42003009	Even now the axe is laid to the root of the trees . Every tree therefore that does not bear good fruit is cut down and thrown into the fire . ”
42003010	And the crowds asked him , “ What then shall we do ? ”
42003011	And he answered them , “ Whoever has two tunics is to share with him who has none , and whoever has food is to do likewise . ”
42003012	Tax collectors also came to be baptized and said to him , “ Teacher , what shall we do ? ”
42003013	And he said to them , “ Collect no more than you are authorized to do . ”
42003014	Soldiers also asked him , “ And we , what shall we do ? ” And he said to them , “ Do not extort money from anyone by threats or by false accusation , and be content with your wages . ”
42003015	As the people were in expectation , and all were questioning in their hearts concerning John , whether he might be the Christ ,
42003016	John answered them all , saying , “ I baptize you with water , but he who is mightier than I is coming , the strap of whose sandals I am not worthy to untie . He will baptize you with the Holy Spirit and with fire .
42003017	His winnowing fork is in his hand , to clear his threshing floor and to gather the wheat into his barn , but the chaff he will burn with unquenchable fire . ”
42003018	So with many other exhortations he preached good news to the people .
42003019	But Herod the tetrarch , who had been reproved by him for Herodias , his brother’s wife , and for all the evil things that Herod had done ,
42003020	added this to them all , that he locked up John in prison .
42003021	Now when all the people were baptized , and when Jesus also had been baptized and was praying , the heavens were opened ,
42003022	and the Holy Spirit descended on him in bodily form , like a dove ; and a voice came from heaven , “ You are my beloved Son ; with you I am well pleased . ”
