42004001	And Jesus , full of the Holy Spirit , returned from the Jordan and was led by the Spirit in the wilderness
42004002	for forty days , being tempted by the devil . And he ate nothing during those days . And when they were ended , he was hungry .
42004003	The devil said to him , “ If you are the Son of God , command this stone to become bread . ”
42004004	And Jesus answered him , “ It is written , ‘ Man shall not live by bread alone . ’ ”
42004005	And the devil took him up and showed him all the kingdoms of the world in a moment of time ,
42004006	and said to him , “ To you I will give all this authority and their glory , for it has been delivered to me , and I give it to whom I will .
42004007	If you , then , will worship me , it will all be yours . ”
42004008	And Jesus answered him , “ It is written , “ ‘ You shall worship the Lord your God , and him only shall you serve . ’ ”
42004009	And he took him to Jerusalem and set him on the pinnacle of the temple and said to him , “ If you are the Son of God , throw yourself down from here ,
42004010	for it is written , “ ‘ He will command his angels concerning you , to guard you , ’
42004011	and “ ‘ On their hands they will bear you up , lest you strike your foot against a stone . ’ ”
42004012	And Jesus answered him , “ It is said , ‘ You shall not put the Lord your God to the test . ’ ”
42004013	And when the devil had ended every temptation , he departed from him until an opportune time .
42004014	And Jesus returned in the power of the Spirit to Galilee , and a report about him went out through all the surrounding country .
42004015	And he taught in their synagogues , being glorified by all .
42004016	And he came to Nazareth , where he had been brought up . And as was his custom , he went to the synagogue on the Sabbath day , and he stood up to read .
42004017	And the scroll of the prophet Isaiah was given to him . He unrolled the scroll and found the place where it was written ,
42004018	“ The Spirit of the Lord is upon me , because he has anointed me to proclaim good news to the poor . He has sent me to proclaim liberty to the captives and recovering of sight to the blind , to set at liberty those who are oppressed ,
42004019	to proclaim the year of the Lord’s favor . ”
42004020	And he rolled up the scroll and gave it back to the attendant and sat down . And the eyes of all in the synagogue were fixed on him .
42004021	And he began to say to them , “ Today this Scripture has been fulfilled in your hearing . ”
42004022	And all spoke well of him and marveled at the gracious words that were coming from his mouth . And they said , “ Is not this Joseph’s son ? ”
42004023	And he said to them , “ Doubtless you will quote to me this proverb , ‘ Physician , heal yourself . ’ What we have heard you did at Capernaum , do here in your hometown as well . ”
42004024	And he said , “ Truly , I say to you , no prophet is acceptable in his hometown .
42004025	But in truth , I tell you , there were many widows in Israel in the days of Elijah , when the heavens were shut up three years and six months , and a great famine came over all the land ,
42004026	and Elijah was sent to none of them but only to Zarephath , in the land of Sidon , to a woman who was a widow .
42004027	And there were many lepers in Israel in the time of the prophet Elisha , and none of them was cleansed , but only Naaman the Syrian . ”
42004028	When they heard these things , all in the synagogue were filled with wrath .
42004029	And they rose up and drove him out of the town and brought him to the brow of the hill on which their town was built , so that they could throw him down the cliff .
42004030	But passing through their midst , he went away .
42004031	And he went down to Capernaum , a city of Galilee . And he was teaching them on the Sabbath ,
42004032	and they were astonished at his teaching , for his word possessed authority .
42004033	And in the synagogue there was a man who had the spirit of an unclean demon , and he cried out with a loud voice ,
42004034	“ Ha ! What have you to do with us , Jesus of Nazareth ? Have you come to destroy us ? I know who you are — the Holy One of God . ”
42004035	But Jesus rebuked him , saying , “ Be silent and come out of him ! ” And when the demon had thrown him down in their midst , he came out of him , having done him no harm .
42004036	And they were all amazed and said to one another , “ What is this word ? For with authority and power he commands the unclean spirits , and they come out ! ”
42004037	And reports about him went out into every place in the surrounding region .
42004038	And he arose and left the synagogue and entered Simon’s house . Now Simon’s mother-in-law was ill with a high fever , and they appealed to him on her behalf .
42004039	And he stood over her and rebuked the fever , and it left her , and immediately she rose and began to serve them .
42004040	Now when the sun was setting , all those who had any who were sick with various diseases brought them to him , and he laid his hands on every one of them and healed them .
42004041	And demons also came out of many , crying , “ You are the Son of God ! ” But he rebuked them and would not allow them to speak , because they knew that he was the Christ .
42004042	And when it was day , he departed and went into a desolate place . And the people sought him and came to him , and would have kept him from leaving them ,
42004043	but he said to them , “ I must preach the good news of the kingdom of God to the other towns as well ; for I was sent for this purpose . ”
42004044	And he was preaching in the synagogues of Judea .
42005001	On one occasion , while the crowd was pressing in on him to hear the word of God , he was standing by the lake of Gennesaret ,
42005002	and he saw two boats by the lake , but the fishermen had gone out of them and were washing their nets .
42005003	Getting into one of the boats , which was Simon’s , he asked him to put out a little from the land . And he sat down and taught the people from the boat .
42005004	And when he had finished speaking , he said to Simon , “ Put out into the deep and let down your nets for a catch . ”
42005005	And Simon answered , “ Master , we toiled all night and took nothing ! But at your word I will let down the nets . ”
42005006	And when they had done this , they enclosed a large number of fish , and their nets were breaking .
42005007	They signaled to their partners in the other boat to come and help them . And they came and filled both the boats , so that they began to sink .
42005008	But when Simon Peter saw it , he fell down at Jesus ’ knees , saying , “ Depart from me , for I am a sinful man , O Lord . ”
42005009	For he and all who were with him were astonished at the catch of fish that they had taken ,
42005010	and so also were James and John , sons of Zebedee , who were partners with Simon . And Jesus said to Simon , “ Do not be afraid ; from now on you will be catching men . ”
42005011	And when they had brought their boats to land , they left everything and followed him .
42005012	While he was in one of the cities , there came a man full of leprosy . And when he saw Jesus , he fell on his face and begged him , “ Lord , if you will , you can make me clean . ”
42005013	And Jesus stretched out his hand and touched him , saying , “ I will ; be clean . ” And immediately the leprosy left him .
42005014	And he charged him to tell no one , but “ go and show yourself to the priest , and make an offering for your cleansing , as Moses commanded , for a proof to them . ”
42005015	But now even more the report about him went abroad , and great crowds gathered to hear him and to be healed of their infirmities .
42005016	But he would withdraw to desolate places and pray .
42005017	On one of those days , as he was teaching , Pharisees and teachers of the law were sitting there , who had come from every village of Galilee and Judea and from Jerusalem . And the power of the Lord was with him to heal .
42005018	And behold , some men were bringing on a bed a man who was paralyzed , and they were seeking to bring him in and lay him before Jesus ,
42005019	but finding no way to bring him in , because of the crowd , they went up on the roof and let him down with his bed through the tiles into the midst before Jesus .
42005020	And when he saw their faith , he said , “ Man , your sins are forgiven you . ”
42005021	And the scribes and the Pharisees began to question , saying , “ Who is this who speaks blasphemies ? Who can forgive sins but God alone ? ”
42005022	When Jesus perceived their thoughts , he answered them , “ Why do you question in your hearts ?
42005023	Which is easier , to say , ‘ Your sins are forgiven you , ’ or to say , ‘ Rise and walk ’ ?
42005024	But that you may know that the Son of Man has authority on earth to forgive sins ” — he said to the man who was paralyzed — “ I say to you , rise , pick up your bed and go home . ”
42005025	And immediately he rose up before them and picked up what he had been lying on and went home , glorifying God .
42005026	And amazement seized them all , and they glorified God and were filled with awe , saying , “ We have seen extraordinary things today . ”
42005027	After this he went out and saw a tax collector named Levi , sitting at the tax booth . And he said to him , “ Follow me . ”
42005028	And leaving everything , he rose and followed him .
42005029	And Levi made him a great feast in his house , and there was a large company of tax collectors and others reclining at table with them .
42005030	And the Pharisees and their scribes grumbled at his disciples , saying , “ Why do you eat and drink with tax collectors and sinners ? ”
42005031	And Jesus answered them , “ Those who are well have no need of a physician , but those who are sick .
42005032	I have not come to call the righteous but sinners to repentance . ”
42005033	And they said to him , “ The disciples of John fast often and offer prayers , and so do the disciples of the Pharisees , but yours eat and drink . ”
42005034	And Jesus said to them , “ Can you make wedding guests fast while the bridegroom is with them ?
42005035	The days will come when the bridegroom is taken away from them , and then they will fast in those days . ”
42005036	He also told them a parable : “ No one tears a piece from a new garment and puts it on an old garment . If he does , he will tear the new , and the piece from the new will not match the old .
42005037	And no one puts new wine into old wineskins . If he does , the new wine will burst the skins and it will be spilled , and the skins will be destroyed .
42005038	But new wine must be put into fresh wineskins .
42005039	And no one after drinking old wine desires new , for he says , ‘ The old is good . ’ ”
42006001	On a Sabbath , while he was going through the grainfields , his disciples plucked and ate some heads of grain , rubbing them in their hands .
42006002	But some of the Pharisees said , “ Why are you doing what is not lawful to do on the Sabbath ? ”
42006003	And Jesus answered them , “ Have you not read what David did when he was hungry , he and those who were with him :
42006004	how he entered the house of God and took and ate the bread of the Presence , which is not lawful for any but the priests to eat , and also gave it to those with him ? ”
42006005	And he said to them , “ The Son of Man is lord of the Sabbath . ”
42006006	On another Sabbath , he entered the synagogue and was teaching , and a man was there whose right hand was withered .
42006007	And the scribes and the Pharisees watched him , to see whether he would heal on the Sabbath , so that they might find a reason to accuse him .
42006008	But he knew their thoughts , and he said to the man with the withered hand , “ Come and stand here . ” And he rose and stood there .
42006009	And Jesus said to them , “ I ask you , is it lawful on the Sabbath to do good or to do harm , to save life or to destroy it ? ”
42006010	And after looking around at them all he said to him , “ Stretch out your hand . ” And he did so , and his hand was restored .
42006011	But they were filled with fury and discussed with one another what they might do to Jesus .
42006012	In these days he went out to the mountain to pray , and all night he continued in prayer to God .
42006013	And when day came , he called his disciples and chose from them twelve , whom he named apostles :
42006014	Simon , whom he named Peter , and Andrew his brother , and James and John , and Philip , and Bartholomew ,
42006015	and Matthew , and Thomas , and James the son of Alphaeus , and Simon who was called the Zealot ,
42006016	and Judas the son of James , and Judas Iscariot , who became a traitor .
42006017	And he came down with them and stood on a level place , with a great crowd of his disciples and a great multitude of people from all Judea and Jerusalem and the seacoast of Tyre and Sidon ,
42006018	who came to hear him and to be healed of their diseases . And those who were troubled with unclean spirits were cured .
42006019	And all the crowd sought to touch him , for power came out from him and healed them all .
42006020	And he lifted up his eyes on his disciples , and said : “ Blessed are you who are poor , for yours is the kingdom of God .
42006021	“ Blessed are you who are hungry now , for you shall be satisfied . “ Blessed are you who weep now , for you shall laugh .
42006022	“ Blessed are you when people hate you and when they exclude you and revile you and spurn your name as evil , on account of the Son of Man !
42006023	Rejoice in that day , and leap for joy , for behold , your reward is great in heaven ; for so their fathers did to the prophets .
42006024	“ But woe to you who are rich , for you have received your consolation .
42006025	“ Woe to you who are full now , for you shall be hungry . “ Woe to you who laugh now , for you shall mourn and weep .
42006026	“ Woe to you , when all people speak well of you , for so their fathers did to the false prophets .
42006027	“ But I say to you who hear , Love your enemies , do good to those who hate you ,
42006028	bless those who curse you , pray for those who abuse you .
42006029	To one who strikes you on the cheek , offer the other also , and from one who takes away your cloak do not withhold your tunic either .
42006030	Give to everyone who begs from you , and from one who takes away your goods do not demand them back .
42006031	And as you wish that others would do to you , do so to them .
42006032	“ If you love those who love you , what benefit is that to you ? For even sinners love those who love them .
42006033	And if you do good to those who do good to you , what benefit is that to you ? For even sinners do the same .
42006034	And if you lend to those from whom you expect to receive , what credit is that to you ? Even sinners lend to sinners , to get back the same amount .
42006035	But love your enemies , and do good , and lend , expecting nothing in return , and your reward will be great , and you will be sons of the Most High , for he is kind to the ungrateful and the evil .
42006036	Be merciful , even as your Father is merciful .
42006037	“ Judge not , and you will not be judged ; condemn not , and you will not be condemned ; forgive , and you will be forgiven ;
42006038	give , and it will be given to you . Good measure , pressed down , shaken together , running over , will be put into your lap . For with the measure you use it will be measured back to you . ”
42006039	He also told them a parable : “ Can a blind man lead a blind man ? Will they not both fall into a pit ?
42006040	A disciple is not above his teacher , but everyone when he is fully trained will be like his teacher .
42006041	Why do you see the speck that is in your brother’s eye , but do not notice the log that is in your own eye ?
42006042	How can you say to your brother , ‘ Brother , let me take out the speck that is in your eye , ’ when you yourself do not see the log that is in your own eye ? You hypocrite , first take the log out of your own eye , and then you will see clearly to take out the speck that is in your brother’s eye .
42006043	“ For no good tree bears bad fruit , nor again does a bad tree bear good fruit ,
42006044	for each tree is known by its own fruit . For figs are not gathered from thornbushes , nor are grapes picked from a bramble bush .
42006045	The good person out of the good treasure of his heart produces good , and the evil person out of his evil treasure produces evil , for out of the abundance of the heart his mouth speaks .
42006046	“ Why do you call me ‘ Lord , Lord , ’ and not do what I tell you ?
42006047	Everyone who comes to me and hears my words and does them , I will show you what he is like :
42006048	he is like a man building a house , who dug deep and laid the foundation on the rock . And when a flood arose , the stream broke against that house and could not shake it , because it had been well built .
42006049	But the one who hears and does not do them is like a man who built a house on the ground without a foundation . When the stream broke against it , immediately it fell , and the ruin of that house was great . ”
42007001	After he had finished all his sayings in the hearing of the people , he entered Capernaum .
42007002	Now a centurion had a servant who was sick and at the point of death , who was highly valued by him .
42007003	When the centurion heard about Jesus , he sent to him elders of the Jews , asking him to come and heal his servant .
42007004	And when they came to Jesus , they pleaded with him earnestly , saying , “ He is worthy to have you do this for him ,
42007005	for he loves our nation , and he is the one who built us our synagogue . ”
42007006	And Jesus went with them . When he was not far from the house , the centurion sent friends , saying to him , “ Lord , do not trouble yourself , for I am not worthy to have you come under my roof .
42007007	Therefore I did not presume to come to you . But say the word , and let my servant be healed .
42007008	For I too am a man set under authority , with soldiers under me : and I say to one , ‘ Go , ’ and he goes ; and to another , ‘ Come , ’ and he comes ; and to my servant , ‘ Do this , ’ and he does it . ”
42007009	When Jesus heard these things , he marveled at him , and turning to the crowd that followed him , said , “ I tell you , not even in Israel have I found such faith . ”
42007010	And when those who had been sent returned to the house , they found the servant well .
42007011	Soon afterward he went to a town called Nain , and his disciples and a great crowd went with him .
42007012	As he drew near to the gate of the town , behold , a man who had died was being carried out , the only son of his mother , and she was a widow , and a considerable crowd from the town was with her .
42007013	And when the Lord saw her , he had compassion on her and said to her , “ Do not weep . ”
42007014	Then he came up and touched the bier , and the bearers stood still . And he said , “ Young man , I say to you , arise . ”
42007015	And the dead man sat up and began to speak , and Jesus gave him to his mother .
42007016	Fear seized them all , and they glorified God , saying , “ A great prophet has arisen among us ! ” and “ God has visited his people ! ”
42007017	And this report about him spread through the whole of Judea and all the surrounding country .
42007018	The disciples of John reported all these things to him . And John ,
42007019	calling two of his disciples to him , sent them to the Lord , saying , “ Are you the one who is to come , or shall we look for another ? ”
42007020	And when the men had come to him , they said , “ John the Baptist has sent us to you , saying , ‘ Are you the one who is to come , or shall we look for another ? ’ ”
42007021	In that hour he healed many people of diseases and plagues and evil spirits , and on many who were blind he bestowed sight .
42007022	And he answered them , “ Go and tell John what you have seen and heard : the blind receive their sight , the lame walk , lepers are cleansed , and the deaf hear , the dead are raised up , the poor have good news preached to them .
42007023	And blessed is the one who is not offended by me . ”
42007024	When John’s messengers had gone , Jesus began to speak to the crowds concerning John : “ What did you go out into the wilderness to see ? A reed shaken by the wind ?
42007025	What then did you go out to see ? A man dressed in soft clothing ? Behold , those who are dressed in splendid clothing and live in luxury are in kings ’ courts .
42007026	What then did you go out to see ? A prophet ? Yes , I tell you , and more than a prophet .
42007027	This is he of whom it is written , “ ‘ Behold , I send my messenger before your face , who will prepare your way before you . ’
42007028	I tell you , among those born of women none is greater than John . Yet the one who is least in the kingdom of God is greater than he . ”
42007029	( When all the people heard this , and the tax collectors too , they declared God just , having been baptized with the baptism of John ,
42007030	but the Pharisees and the lawyers rejected the purpose of God for themselves , not having been baptized by him .
42007031	“ To what then shall I compare the people of this generation , and what are they like ?
42007032	They are like children sitting in the marketplace and calling to one another , “ ‘ We played the flute for you , and you did not dance ; we sang a dirge , and you did not weep . ’
42007033	For John the Baptist has come eating no bread and drinking no wine , and you say , ‘ He has a demon . ’
42007034	The Son of Man has come eating and drinking , and you say , ‘ Look at him ! A glutton and a drunkard , a friend of tax collectors and sinners ! ’
42007035	Yet wisdom is justified by all her children . ”
42007036	One of the Pharisees asked him to eat with him , and he went into the Pharisee’s house and took his place at the table .
42007037	And behold , a woman of the city , who was a sinner , when she learned that he was reclining at table in the Pharisee’s house , brought an alabaster flask of ointment ,
42007038	and standing behind him at his feet , weeping , she began to wet his feet with her tears and wiped them with the hair of her head and kissed his feet and anointed them with the ointment .
42007039	Now when the Pharisee who had invited him saw this , he said to himself , “ If this man were a prophet , he would have known who and what sort of woman this is who is touching him , for she is a sinner . ”
42007040	And Jesus answering said to him , “ Simon , I have something to say to you . ” And he answered , “ Say it , Teacher . ”
42007041	“ A certain moneylender had two debtors . One owed five hundred denarii , and the other fifty .
42007042	When they could not pay , he cancelled the debt of both . Now which of them will love him more ? ”
42007043	Simon answered , “ The one , I suppose , for whom he cancelled the larger debt . ” And he said to him , “ You have judged rightly . ”
42007044	Then turning toward the woman he said to Simon , “ Do you see this woman ? I entered your house ; you gave me no water for my feet , but she has wet my feet with her tears and wiped them with her hair .
42007045	You gave me no kiss , but from the time I came in she has not ceased to kiss my feet .
42007046	You did not anoint my head with oil , but she has anointed my feet with ointment .
42007047	Therefore I tell you , her sins , which are many , are forgiven — for she loved much . But he who is forgiven little , loves little . ”
42007048	And he said to her , “ Your sins are forgiven . ”
42007049	Then those who were at table with him began to say among themselves , “ Who is this , who even forgives sins ? ”
42007050	And he said to the woman , “ Your faith has saved you ; go in peace . ”
42008001	Soon afterward he went on through cities and villages , proclaiming and bringing the good news of the kingdom of God . And the twelve were with him ,
42008002	and also some women who had been healed of evil spirits and infirmities : Mary , called Magdalene , from whom seven demons had gone out ,
42008003	and Joanna , the wife of Chuza , Herod’s household manager , and Susanna , and many others , who provided for them out of their means .
42008004	And when a great crowd was gathering and people from town after town came to him , he said in a parable :
42008005	“ A sower went out to sow his seed . And as he sowed , some fell along the path and was trampled underfoot , and the birds of the air devoured it .
42008006	And some fell on the rock , and as it grew up , it withered away , because it had no moisture .
42008007	And some fell among thorns , and the thorns grew up with it and choked it .
42008008	And some fell into good soil and grew and yielded a hundredfold . ” As he said these things , he called out , “ He who has ears to hear , let him hear . ”
42008009	And when his disciples asked him what this parable meant ,
42008010	he said , “ To you it has been given to know the secrets of the kingdom of God , but for others they are in parables , so that ‘ seeing they may not see , and hearing they may not understand . ’
42008011	Now the parable is this : The seed is the word of God .
42008012	The ones along the path are those who have heard ; then the devil comes and takes away the word from their hearts , so that they may not believe and be saved .
42008013	And the ones on the rock are those who , when they hear the word , receive it with joy . But these have no root ; they believe for a while , and in time of testing fall away .
42008014	And as for what fell among the thorns , they are those who hear , but as they go on their way they are choked by the cares and riches and pleasures of life , and their fruit does not mature .
42008015	As for that in the good soil , they are those who , hearing the word , hold it fast in an honest and good heart , and bear fruit with patience .
42008016	“ No one after lighting a lamp covers it with a jar or puts it under a bed , but puts it on a stand , so that those who enter may see the light .
42008017	For nothing is hidden that will not be made manifest , nor is anything secret that will not be known and come to light .
42008018	Take care then how you hear , for to the one who has , more will be given , and from the one who has not , even what he thinks that he has will be taken away . ”
42008019	Then his mother and his brothers came to him , but they could not reach him because of the crowd .
42008020	And he was told , “ Your mother and your brothers are standing outside , desiring to see you . ”
42008021	But he answered them , “ My mother and my brothers are those who hear the word of God and do it . ”
42008022	One day he got into a boat with his disciples , and he said to them , “ Let us go across to the other side of the lake . ” So they set out ,
42008023	and as they sailed he fell asleep . And a windstorm came down on the lake , and they were filling with water and were in danger .
42008024	And they went and woke him , saying , “ Master , Master , we are perishing ! ” And he awoke and rebuked the wind and the raging waves , and they ceased , and there was a calm .
42008025	He said to them , “ Where is your faith ? ” And they were afraid , and they marveled , saying to one another , “ Who then is this , that he commands even winds and water , and they obey him ? ”
42008026	Then they sailed to the country of the Gerasenes , which is opposite Galilee .
42008027	When Jesus had stepped out on land , there met him a man from the city who had demons . For a long time he had worn no clothes , and he had not lived in a house but among the tombs .
42008028	When he saw Jesus , he cried out and fell down before him and said with a loud voice , “ What have you to do with me , Jesus , Son of the Most High God ? I beg you , do not torment me . ”
42008029	For he had commanded the unclean spirit to come out of the man . ( For many a time it had seized him . He was kept under guard and bound with chains and shackles , but he would break the bonds and be driven by the demon into the desert .
42008030	Jesus then asked him , “ What is your name ? ” And he said , “ Legion , ” for many demons had entered him .
42008031	And they begged him not to command them to depart into the abyss .
42008032	Now a large herd of pigs was feeding there on the hillside , and they begged him to let them enter these . So he gave them permission .
42008033	Then the demons came out of the man and entered the pigs , and the herd rushed down the steep bank into the lake and were drowned .
42008034	When the herdsmen saw what had happened , they fled and told it in the city and in the country .
42008035	Then people went out to see what had happened , and they came to Jesus and found the man from whom the demons had gone , sitting at the feet of Jesus , clothed and in his right mind , and they were afraid .
42008036	And those who had seen it told them how the demon-possessed man had been healed .
42008037	Then all the people of the surrounding country of the Gerasenes asked him to depart from them , for they were seized with great fear . So he got into the boat and returned .
42008038	The man from whom the demons had gone begged that he might be with him , but Jesus sent him away , saying ,
42008039	“ Return to your home , and declare how much God has done for you . ” And he went away , proclaiming throughout the whole city how much Jesus had done for him .
42008040	Now when Jesus returned , the crowd welcomed him , for they were all waiting for him .
42008041	And there came a man named Jairus , who was a ruler of the synagogue . And falling at Jesus ’ feet , he implored him to come to his house ,
42008042	for he had an only daughter , about twelve years of age , and she was dying . As Jesus went , the people pressed around him .
42008043	And there was a woman who had had a discharge of blood for twelve years , and though she had spent all her living on physicians , she could not be healed by anyone .
42008044	She came up behind him and touched the fringe of his garment , and immediately her discharge of blood ceased .
42008045	And Jesus said , “ Who was it that touched me ? ” When all denied it , Peter said , “ Master , the crowds surround you and are pressing in on you ! ”
42008046	But Jesus said , “ Someone touched me , for I perceive that power has gone out from me . ”
42008047	And when the woman saw that she was not hidden , she came trembling , and falling down before him declared in the presence of all the people why she had touched him , and how she had been immediately healed .
42008048	And he said to her , “ Daughter , your faith has made you well ; go in peace . ”
42008049	While he was still speaking , someone from the ruler’s house came and said , “ Your daughter is dead ; do not trouble the Teacher any more . ”
42008050	But Jesus on hearing this answered him , “ Do not fear ; only believe , and she will be well . ”
42008051	And when he came to the house , he allowed no one to enter with him , except Peter and John and James , and the father and mother of the child .
42008052	And all were weeping and mourning for her , but he said , “ Do not weep , for she is not dead but sleeping . ”
42008053	And they laughed at him , knowing that she was dead .
42008054	But taking her by the hand he called , saying , “ Child , arise . ”
42008055	And her spirit returned , and she got up at once . And he directed that something should be given her to eat .
42008056	And her parents were amazed , but he charged them to tell no one what had happened .
42009001	And he called the twelve together and gave them power and authority over all demons and to cure diseases ,
42009002	and he sent them out to proclaim the kingdom of God and to heal .
42009003	And he said to them , “ Take nothing for your journey , no staff , nor bag , nor bread , nor money ; and do not have two tunics .
42009004	And whatever house you enter , stay there , and from there depart .
42009005	And wherever they do not receive you , when you leave that town shake off the dust from your feet as a testimony against them . ”
42009006	And they departed and went through the villages , preaching the gospel and healing everywhere .
42009007	Now Herod the tetrarch heard about all that was happening , and he was perplexed , because it was said by some that John had been raised from the dead ,
42009008	by some that Elijah had appeared , and by others that one of the prophets of old had risen .
42009009	Herod said , “ John I beheaded , but who is this about whom I hear such things ? ” And he sought to see him .
42009010	On their return the apostles told him all that they had done . And he took them and withdrew apart to a town called Bethsaida .
42009011	When the crowds learned it , they followed him , and he welcomed them and spoke to them of the kingdom of God and cured those who had need of healing .
42009012	Now the day began to wear away , and the twelve came and said to him , “ Send the crowd away to go into the surrounding villages and countryside to find lodging and get provisions , for we are here in a desolate place . ”
42009013	But he said to them , “ You give them something to eat . ” They said , “ We have no more than five loaves and two fish — unless we are to go and buy food for all these people . ”
42009014	For there were about five thousand men . And he said to his disciples , “ Have them sit down in groups of about fifty each . ”
42009015	And they did so , and had them all sit down .
42009016	And taking the five loaves and the two fish , he looked up to heaven and said a blessing over them . Then he broke the loaves and gave them to the disciples to set before the crowd .
42009017	And they all ate and were satisfied . And what was left over was picked up , twelve baskets of broken pieces .
42009018	Now it happened that as he was praying alone , the disciples were with him . And he asked them , “ Who do the crowds say that I am ? ”
42009019	And they answered , “ John the Baptist . But others say , Elijah , and others , that one of the prophets of old has risen . ”
42009020	Then he said to them , “ But who do you say that I am ? ” And Peter answered , “ The Christ of God . ”
42009021	And he strictly charged and commanded them to tell this to no one ,
42009022	saying , “ The Son of Man must suffer many things and be rejected by the elders and chief priests and scribes , and be killed , and on the third day be raised . ”
42009023	And he said to all , “ If anyone would come after me , let him deny himself and take up his cross daily and follow me .
42009024	For whoever would save his life will lose it , but whoever loses his life for my sake will save it .
42009025	For what does it profit a man if he gains the whole world and loses or forfeits himself ?
42009026	For whoever is ashamed of me and of my words , of him will the Son of Man be ashamed when he comes in his glory and the glory of the Father and of the holy angels .
42009027	But I tell you truly , there are some standing here who will not taste death until they see the kingdom of God . ”
42009028	Now about eight days after these sayings he took with him Peter and John and James and went up on the mountain to pray .
42009029	And as he was praying , the appearance of his face was altered , and his clothing became dazzling white .
42009030	And behold , two men were talking with him , Moses and Elijah ,
42009031	who appeared in glory and spoke of his departure , which he was about to accomplish at Jerusalem .
42009032	Now Peter and those who were with him were heavy with sleep , but when they became fully awake they saw his glory and the two men who stood with him .
42009033	And as the men were parting from him , Peter said to Jesus , “ Master , it is good that we are here . Let us make three tents , one for you and one for Moses and one for Elijah ” — not knowing what he said .
42009034	As he was saying these things , a cloud came and overshadowed them , and they were afraid as they entered the cloud .
42009035	And a voice came out of the cloud , saying , “ This is my Son , my Chosen One ; listen to him ! ”
42009036	And when the voice had spoken , Jesus was found alone . And they kept silent and told no one in those days anything of what they had seen .
42009037	On the next day , when they had come down from the mountain , a great crowd met him .
42009038	And behold , a man from the crowd cried out , “ Teacher , I beg you to look at my son , for he is my only child .
42009039	And behold , a spirit seizes him , and he suddenly cries out . It convulses him so that he foams at the mouth , and shatters him , and will hardly leave him .
42009040	And I begged your disciples to cast it out , but they could not . ”
42009041	Jesus answered , “ O faithless and twisted generation , how long am I to be with you and bear with you ? Bring your son here . ”
42009042	While he was coming , the demon threw him to the ground and convulsed him . But Jesus rebuked the unclean spirit and healed the boy , and gave him back to his father .
42009043	And all were astonished at the majesty of God . But while they were all marveling at everything he was doing , Jesus said to his disciples ,
42009044	“ Let these words sink into your ears : The Son of Man is about to be delivered into the hands of men . ”
42009045	But they did not understand this saying , and it was concealed from them , so that they might not perceive it . And they were afraid to ask him about this saying .
42009046	An argument arose among them as to which of them was the greatest .
42009047	But Jesus , knowing the reasoning of their hearts , took a child and put him by his side
42009048	and said to them , “ Whoever receives this child in my name receives me , and whoever receives me receives him who sent me . For he who is least among you all is the one who is great . ”
42009049	John answered , “ Master , we saw someone casting out demons in your name , and we tried to stop him , because he does not follow with us . ”
42009050	But Jesus said to him , “ Do not stop him , for the one who is not against you is for you . ”
42009051	When the days drew near for him to be taken up , he set his face to go to Jerusalem .
42009052	And he sent messengers ahead of him , who went and entered a village of the Samaritans , to make preparations for him .
42009053	But the people did not receive him , because his face was set toward Jerusalem .
42009054	And when his disciples James and John saw it , they said , “ Lord , do you want us to tell fire to come down from heaven and consume them ? ”
42009055	But he turned and rebuked them .
42009056	And they went on to another village .
42009057	As they were going along the road , someone said to him , “ I will follow you wherever you go . ”
42009058	And Jesus said to him , “ Foxes have holes , and birds of the air have nests , but the Son of Man has nowhere to lay his head . ”
42009059	To another he said , “ Follow me . ” But he said , “ Lord , let me first go and bury my father . ”
42009060	And Jesus said to him , “ Leave the dead to bury their own dead . But as for you , go and proclaim the kingdom of God . ”
42009061	Yet another said , “ I will follow you , Lord , but let me first say farewell to those at my home . ”
42009062	Jesus said to him , “ No one who puts his hand to the plow and looks back is fit for the kingdom of God . ”
42010001	After this the Lord appointed seventy-two others and sent them on ahead of him , two by two , into every town and place where he himself was about to go .
42010002	And he said to them , “ The harvest is plentiful , but the laborers are few . Therefore pray earnestly to the Lord of the harvest to send out laborers into his harvest .
42010003	Go your way ; behold , I am sending you out as lambs in the midst of wolves .
42010004	Carry no moneybag , no knapsack , no sandals , and greet no one on the road .
42010005	Whatever house you enter , first say , ‘ Peace be to this house ! ’
42010006	And if a son of peace is there , your peace will rest upon him . But if not , it will return to you .
42010007	And remain in the same house , eating and drinking what they provide , for the laborer deserves his wages . Do not go from house to house .
42010008	Whenever you enter a town and they receive you , eat what is set before you .
42010009	Heal the sick in it and say to them , ‘ The kingdom of God has come near to you . ’
42010010	But whenever you enter a town and they do not receive you , go into its streets and say ,
42010011	‘ Even the dust of your town that clings to our feet we wipe off against you . Nevertheless know this , that the kingdom of God has come near . ’
42010012	I tell you , it will be more bearable on that day for Sodom than for that town .
42010013	“ Woe to you , Chorazin ! Woe to you , Bethsaida ! For if the mighty works done in you had been done in Tyre and Sidon , they would have repented long ago , sitting in sackcloth and ashes .
42010014	But it will be more bearable in the judgment for Tyre and Sidon than for you .
42010015	And you , Capernaum , will you be exalted to heaven ? You shall be brought down to Hades .
42010016	“ The one who hears you hears me , and the one who rejects you rejects me , and the one who rejects me rejects him who sent me . ”
42010017	The seventy-two returned with joy , saying , “ Lord , even the demons are subject to us in your name ! ”
42010018	And he said to them , “ I saw Satan fall like lightning from heaven .
42010019	Behold , I have given you authority to tread on serpents and scorpions , and over all the power of the enemy , and nothing shall hurt you .
42010020	Nevertheless , do not rejoice in this , that the spirits are subject to you , but rejoice that your names are written in heaven . ”
42010021	In that same hour he rejoiced in the Holy Spirit and said , “ I thank you , Father , Lord of heaven and earth , that you have hidden these things from the wise and understanding and revealed them to little children ; yes , Father , for such was your gracious will .
42010022	All things have been handed over to me by my Father , and no one knows who the Son is except the Father , or who the Father is except the Son and anyone to whom the Son chooses to reveal him . ”
42010023	Then turning to the disciples he said privately , “ Blessed are the eyes that see what you see !
42010024	For I tell you that many prophets and kings desired to see what you see , and did not see it , and to hear what you hear , and did not hear it . ”
42010025	And behold , a lawyer stood up to put him to the test , saying , “ Teacher , what shall I do to inherit eternal life ? ”
42010026	He said to him , “ What is written in the Law ? How do you read it ? ”
42010027	And he answered , “ You shall love the Lord your God with all your heart and with all your soul and with all your strength and with all your mind , and your neighbor as yourself . ”
42010028	And he said to him , “ You have answered correctly ; do this , and you will live . ”
42010029	But he , desiring to justify himself , said to Jesus , “ And who is my neighbor ? ”
42010030	Jesus replied , “ A man was going down from Jerusalem to Jericho , and he fell among robbers , who stripped him and beat him and departed , leaving him half dead .
42010031	Now by chance a priest was going down that road , and when he saw him he passed by on the other side .
42010032	So likewise a Levite , when he came to the place and saw him , passed by on the other side .
42010033	But a Samaritan , as he journeyed , came to where he was , and when he saw him , he had compassion .
42010034	He went to him and bound up his wounds , pouring on oil and wine . Then he set him on his own animal and brought him to an inn and took care of him .
42010035	And the next day he took out two denarii and gave them to the innkeeper , saying , ‘ Take care of him , and whatever more you spend , I will repay you when I come back . ’
42010036	Which of these three , do you think , proved to be a neighbor to the man who fell among the robbers ? ”
42010037	He said , “ The one who showed him mercy . ” And Jesus said to him , “ You go , and do likewise . ”
42010038	Now as they went on their way , Jesus entered a village . And a woman named Martha welcomed him into her house .
42010039	And she had a sister called Mary , who sat at the Lord’s feet and listened to his teaching .
42010040	But Martha was distracted with much serving . And she went up to him and said , “ Lord , do you not care that my sister has left me to serve alone ? Tell her then to help me . ”
42010041	But the Lord answered her , “ Martha , Martha , you are anxious and troubled about many things ,
42010042	but one thing is necessary . Mary has chosen the good portion , which will not be taken away from her . ”
42011001	Now Jesus was praying in a certain place , and when he finished , one of his disciples said to him , “ Lord , teach us to pray , as John taught his disciples . ”
42011002	And he said to them , “ When you pray , say : “ Father , hallowed be your name . Your kingdom come .
42011003	Give us each day our daily bread ,
42011004	and forgive us our sins , for we ourselves forgive everyone who is indebted to us . And lead us not into temptation . ”
42011005	And he said to them , “ Which of you who has a friend will go to him at midnight and say to him , ‘ Friend , lend me three loaves ,
42011006	for a friend of mine has arrived on a journey , and I have nothing to set before him ’ ;
42011007	and he will answer from within , ‘ Do not bother me ; the door is now shut , and my children are with me in bed . I cannot get up and give you anything ’ ?
42011008	I tell you , though he will not get up and give him anything because he is his friend , yet because of his impudence he will rise and give him whatever he needs .
42011009	And I tell you , ask , and it will be given to you ; seek , and you will find ; knock , and it will be opened to you .
42011010	For everyone who asks receives , and the one who seeks finds , and to the one who knocks it will be opened .
42011011	What father among you , if his son asks for a fish , will instead of a fish give him a serpent ;
42011012	or if he asks for an egg , will give him a scorpion ?
42011013	If you then , who are evil , know how to give good gifts to your children , how much more will the heavenly Father give the Holy Spirit to those who ask him ! ”
42011014	Now he was casting out a demon that was mute . When the demon had gone out , the mute man spoke , and the people marveled .
42011015	But some of them said , “ He casts out demons by Beelzebul , the prince of demons , ”
42011016	while others , to test him , kept seeking from him a sign from heaven .
42011017	But he , knowing their thoughts , said to them , “ Every kingdom divided against itself is laid waste , and a divided household falls .
42011018	And if Satan also is divided against himself , how will his kingdom stand ? For you say that I cast out demons by Beelzebul .
42011019	And if I cast out demons by Beelzebul , by whom do your sons cast them out ? Therefore they will be your judges .
42011020	But if it is by the finger of God that I cast out demons , then the kingdom of God has come upon you .
42011021	When a strong man , fully armed , guards his own palace , his goods are safe ;
42011022	but when one stronger than he attacks him and overcomes him , he takes away his armor in which he trusted and divides his spoil .
42011023	Whoever is not with me is against me , and whoever does not gather with me scatters .
42011024	“ When the unclean spirit has gone out of a person , it passes through waterless places seeking rest , and finding none it says , ‘ I will return to my house from which I came . ’
42011025	And when it comes , it finds the house swept and put in order .
42011026	Then it goes and brings seven other spirits more evil than itself , and they enter and dwell there . And the last state of that person is worse than the first . ”
42011027	As he said these things , a woman in the crowd raised her voice and said to him , “ Blessed is the womb that bore you , and the breasts at which you nursed ! ”
42011028	But he said , “ Blessed rather are those who hear the word of God and keep it ! ”
42011029	When the crowds were increasing , he began to say , “ This generation is an evil generation . It seeks for a sign , but no sign will be given to it except the sign of Jonah .
42011030	For as Jonah became a sign to the people of Nineveh , so will the Son of Man be to this generation .
42011031	The queen of the South will rise up at the judgment with the men of this generation and condemn them , for she came from the ends of the earth to hear the wisdom of Solomon , and behold , something greater than Solomon is here .
42011032	The men of Nineveh will rise up at the judgment with this generation and condemn it , for they repented at the preaching of Jonah , and behold , something greater than Jonah is here .
42011033	“ No one after lighting a lamp puts it in a cellar or under a basket , but on a stand , so that those who enter may see the light .
42011034	Your eye is the lamp of your body . When your eye is healthy , your whole body is full of light , but when it is bad , your body is full of darkness .
42011035	Therefore be careful lest the light in you be darkness .
42011036	If then your whole body is full of light , having no part dark , it will be wholly bright , as when a lamp with its rays gives you light . ”
42011037	While Jesus was speaking , a Pharisee asked him to dine with him , so he went in and reclined at table .
42011038	The Pharisee was astonished to see that he did not first wash before dinner .
42011039	And the Lord said to him , “ Now you Pharisees cleanse the outside of the cup and of the dish , but inside you are full of greed and wickedness .
42011040	You fools ! Did not he who made the outside make the inside also ?
42011041	But give as alms those things that are within , and behold , everything is clean for you .
42011042	“ But woe to you Pharisees ! For you tithe mint and rue and every herb , and neglect justice and the love of God . These you ought to have done , without neglecting the others .
42011043	Woe to you Pharisees ! For you love the best seat in the synagogues and greetings in the marketplaces .
42011044	Woe to you ! For you are like unmarked graves , and people walk over them without knowing it . ”
42011045	One of the lawyers answered him , “ Teacher , in saying these things you insult us also . ”
42011046	And he said , “ Woe to you lawyers also ! For you load people with burdens hard to bear , and you yourselves do not touch the burdens with one of your fingers .
42011047	Woe to you ! For you build the tombs of the prophets whom your fathers killed .
42011048	So you are witnesses and you consent to the deeds of your fathers , for they killed them , and you build their tombs .
42011049	Therefore also the Wisdom of God said , ‘ I will send them prophets and apostles , some of whom they will kill and persecute , ’
42011050	so that the blood of all the prophets , shed from the foundation of the world , may be charged against this generation ,
42011051	from the blood of Abel to the blood of Zechariah , who perished between the altar and the sanctuary . Yes , I tell you , it will be required of this generation .
42011052	Woe to you lawyers ! For you have taken away the key of knowledge . You did not enter yourselves , and you hindered those who were entering . ”
42011053	As he went away from there , the scribes and the Pharisees began to press him hard and to provoke him to speak about many things ,
42011054	lying in wait for him , to catch him in something he might say .
42012001	In the meantime , when so many thousands of the people had gathered together that they were trampling one another , he began to say to his disciples first , “ Beware of the leaven of the Pharisees , which is hypocrisy .
42012002	Nothing is covered up that will not be revealed , or hidden that will not be known .
42012003	Therefore whatever you have said in the dark shall be heard in the light , and what you have whispered in private rooms shall be proclaimed on the housetops .
42012004	“ I tell you , my friends , do not fear those who kill the body , and after that have nothing more that they can do .
42012005	But I will warn you whom to fear : fear him who , after he has killed , has authority to cast into hell . Yes , I tell you , fear him !
42012006	Are not five sparrows sold for two pennies ? And not one of them is forgotten before God .
42012007	Why , even the hairs of your head are all numbered . Fear not ; you are of more value than many sparrows .
42012008	“ And I tell you , everyone who acknowledges me before men , the Son of Man also will acknowledge before the angels of God ,
42012009	but the one who denies me before men will be denied before the angels of God .
42012010	And everyone who speaks a word against the Son of Man will be forgiven , but the one who blasphemes against the Holy Spirit will not be forgiven .
42012011	And when they bring you before the synagogues and the rulers and the authorities , do not be anxious about how you should defend yourself or what you should say ,
42012012	for the Holy Spirit will teach you in that very hour what you ought to say . ”
42012013	Someone in the crowd said to him , “ Teacher , tell my brother to divide the inheritance with me . ”
42012014	But he said to him , “ Man , who made me a judge or arbitrator over you ? ”
42012015	And he said to them , “ Take care , and be on your guard against all covetousness , for one’s life does not consist in the abundance of his possessions . ”
42012016	And he told them a parable , saying , “ The land of a rich man produced plentifully ,
42012017	and he thought to himself , ‘ What shall I do , for I have nowhere to store my crops ? ’
42012018	And he said , ‘ I will do this : I will tear down my barns and build larger ones , and there I will store all my grain and my goods .
42012019	And I will say to my soul , Soul , you have ample goods laid up for many years ; relax , eat , drink , be merry . ’
42012020	But God said to him , ‘ Fool ! This night your soul is required of you , and the things you have prepared , whose will they be ? ’
42012021	So is the one who lays up treasure for himself and is not rich toward God . ”
42012022	And he said to his disciples , “ Therefore I tell you , do not be anxious about your life , what you will eat , nor about your body , what you will put on .
42012023	For life is more than food , and the body more than clothing .
42012024	Consider the ravens : they neither sow nor reap , they have neither storehouse nor barn , and yet God feeds them . Of how much more value are you than the birds !
42012025	And which of you by being anxious can add a single hour to his span of life ?
42012026	If then you are not able to do as small a thing as that , why are you anxious about the rest ?
42012027	Consider the lilies , how they grow : they neither toil nor spin , yet I tell you , even Solomon in all his glory was not arrayed like one of these .
42012028	But if God so clothes the grass , which is alive in the field today , and tomorrow is thrown into the oven , how much more will he clothe you , O you of little faith !
42012029	And do not seek what you are to eat and what you are to drink , nor be worried .
42012030	For all the nations of the world seek after these things , and your Father knows that you need them .
42012031	Instead , seek his kingdom , and these things will be added to you .
42012032	“ Fear not , little flock , for it is your Father’s good pleasure to give you the kingdom .
42012033	Sell your possessions , and give to the needy . Provide yourselves with moneybags that do not grow old , with a treasure in the heavens that does not fail , where no thief approaches and no moth destroys .
42012034	For where your treasure is , there will your heart be also .
42012035	“ Stay dressed for action and keep your lamps burning ,
42012036	and be like men who are waiting for their master to come home from the wedding feast , so that they may open the door to him at once when he comes and knocks .
42012037	Blessed are those servants whom the master finds awake when he comes . Truly , I say to you , he will dress himself for service and have them recline at table , and he will come and serve them .
42012038	If he comes in the second watch , or in the third , and finds them awake , blessed are those servants !
42012039	But know this , that if the master of the house had known at what hour the thief was coming , he would not have left his house to be broken into .
42012040	You also must be ready , for the Son of Man is coming at an hour you do not expect . ”
42012041	Peter said , “ Lord , are you telling this parable for us or for all ? ”
42012042	And the Lord said , “ Who then is the faithful and wise manager , whom his master will set over his household , to give them their portion of food at the proper time ?
42012043	Blessed is that servant whom his master will find so doing when he comes .
42012044	Truly , I say to you , he will set him over all his possessions .
42012045	But if that servant says to himself , ‘ My master is delayed in coming , ’ and begins to beat the male and female servants , and to eat and drink and get drunk ,
42012046	the master of that servant will come on a day when he does not expect him and at an hour he does not know , and will cut him in pieces and put him with the unfaithful .
42012047	And that servant who knew his master’s will but did not get ready or act according to his will , will receive a severe beating .
42012048	But the one who did not know , and did what deserved a beating , will receive a light beating . Everyone to whom much was given , of him much will be required , and from him to whom they entrusted much , they will demand the more .
42012049	“ I came to cast fire on the earth , and would that it were already kindled !
42012050	I have a baptism to be baptized with , and how great is my distress until it is accomplished !
42012051	Do you think that I have come to give peace on earth ? No , I tell you , but rather division .
42012052	For from now on in one house there will be five divided , three against two and two against three .
42012053	They will be divided , father against son and son against father , mother against daughter and daughter against mother , mother-in-law against her daughter-in-law and daughter-in-law against mother-in-law . ”
42012054	He also said to the crowds , “ When you see a cloud rising in the west , you say at once , ‘ A shower is coming . ’ And so it happens .
42012055	And when you see the south wind blowing , you say , ‘ There will be scorching heat , ’ and it happens .
42012056	You hypocrites ! You know how to interpret the appearance of earth and sky , but why do you not know how to interpret the present time ?
42012057	“ And why do you not judge for yourselves what is right ?
42012058	As you go with your accuser before the magistrate , make an effort to settle with him on the way , lest he drag you to the judge , and the judge hand you over to the officer , and the officer put you in prison .
42012059	I tell you , you will never get out until you have paid the very last penny . ”
42013001	There were some present at that very time who told him about the Galileans whose blood Pilate had mingled with their sacrifices .
42013002	And he answered them , “ Do you think that these Galileans were worse sinners than all the other Galileans , because they suffered in this way ?
42013003	No , I tell you ; but unless you repent , you will all likewise perish .
42013004	Or those eighteen on whom the tower in Siloam fell and killed them : do you think that they were worse offenders than all the others who lived in Jerusalem ?
42013005	No , I tell you ; but unless you repent , you will all likewise perish . ”
42013006	And he told this parable : “ A man had a fig tree planted in his vineyard , and he came seeking fruit on it and found none .
42013007	And he said to the vinedresser , ‘ Look , for three years now I have come seeking fruit on this fig tree , and I find none . Cut it down . Why should it use up the ground ? ’
42013008	And he answered him , ‘ Sir , let it alone this year also , until I dig around it and put on manure .
42013009	Then if it should bear fruit next year , well and good ; but if not , you can cut it down . ’ ”
42013010	Now he was teaching in one of the synagogues on the Sabbath .
42013011	And there was a woman who had had a disabling spirit for eighteen years . She was bent over and could not fully straighten herself .
42013012	When Jesus saw her , he called her over and said to her , “ Woman , you are freed from your disability . ”
42013013	And he laid his hands on her , and immediately she was made straight , and she glorified God .
42013014	But the ruler of the synagogue , indignant because Jesus had healed on the Sabbath , said to the people , “ There are six days in which work ought to be done . Come on those days and be healed , and not on the Sabbath day . ”
42013015	Then the Lord answered him , “ You hypocrites ! Does not each of you on the Sabbath untie his ox or his donkey from the manger and lead it away to water it ?
42013016	And ought not this woman , a daughter of Abraham whom Satan bound for eighteen years , be loosed from this bond on the Sabbath day ? ”
42013017	As he said these things , all his adversaries were put to shame , and all the people rejoiced at all the glorious things that were done by him .
42013018	He said therefore , “ What is the kingdom of God like ? And to what shall I compare it ?
42013019	It is like a grain of mustard seed that a man took and sowed in his garden , and it grew and became a tree , and the birds of the air made nests in its branches . ”
42013020	And again he said , “ To what shall I compare the kingdom of God ?
42013021	It is like leaven that a woman took and hid in three measures of flour , until it was all leavened . ”
42013022	He went on his way through towns and villages , teaching and journeying toward Jerusalem .
42013023	And someone said to him , “ Lord , will those who are saved be few ? ” And he said to them ,
42013024	“ Strive to enter through the narrow door . For many , I tell you , will seek to enter and will not be able .
42013025	When once the master of the house has risen and shut the door , and you begin to stand outside and to knock at the door , saying , ‘ Lord , open to us , ’ then he will answer you , ‘ I do not know where you come from . ’
42013026	Then you will begin to say , ‘ We ate and drank in your presence , and you taught in our streets . ’
42013027	But he will say , ‘ I tell you , I do not know where you come from . Depart from me , all you workers of evil ! ’
42013028	In that place there will be weeping and gnashing of teeth , when you see Abraham and Isaac and Jacob and all the prophets in the kingdom of God but you yourselves cast out .
42013029	And people will come from east and west , and from north and south , and recline at table in the kingdom of God .
42013030	And behold , some are last who will be first , and some are first who will be last . ”
42013031	At that very hour some Pharisees came and said to him , “ Get away from here , for Herod wants to kill you . ”
42013032	And he said to them , “ Go and tell that fox , ‘ Behold , I cast out demons and perform cures today and tomorrow , and the third day I finish my course .
42013033	Nevertheless , I must go on my way today and tomorrow and the day following , for it cannot be that a prophet should perish away from Jerusalem . ’
42013034	O Jerusalem , Jerusalem , the city that kills the prophets and stones those who are sent to it ! How often would I have gathered your children together as a hen gathers her brood under her wings , and you would not !
42013035	Behold , your house is forsaken . And I tell you , you will not see me until you say , ‘ Blessed is he who comes in the name of the Lord ! ’ ”
42014001	One Sabbath , when he went to dine at the house of a ruler of the Pharisees , they were watching him carefully .
42014002	And behold , there was a man before him who had dropsy .
42014003	And Jesus responded to the lawyers and Pharisees , saying , “ Is it lawful to heal on the Sabbath , or not ? ”
42014004	But they remained silent . Then he took him and healed him and sent him away .
42014005	And he said to them , “ Which of you , having a son or an ox that has fallen into a well on a Sabbath day , will not immediately pull him out ? ”
42014006	And they could not reply to these things .
42014007	Now he told a parable to those who were invited , when he noticed how they chose the places of honor , saying to them ,
42014008	“ When you are invited by someone to a wedding feast , do not sit down in a place of honor , lest someone more distinguished than you be invited by him ,
42014009	and he who invited you both will come and say to you , ‘ Give your place to this person , ’ and then you will begin with shame to take the lowest place .
42014010	But when you are invited , go and sit in the lowest place , so that when your host comes he may say to you , ‘ Friend , move up higher . ’ Then you will be honored in the presence of all who sit at table with you .
42014011	For everyone who exalts himself will be humbled , and he who humbles himself will be exalted . ”
42014012	He said also to the man who had invited him , “ When you give a dinner or a banquet , do not invite your friends or your brothers or your relatives or rich neighbors , lest they also invite you in return and you be repaid .
42014013	But when you give a feast , invite the poor , the crippled , the lame , the blind ,
42014014	and you will be blessed , because they cannot repay you . For you will be repaid at the resurrection of the just . ”
42014015	When one of those who reclined at table with him heard these things , he said to him , “ Blessed is everyone who will eat bread in the kingdom of God ! ”
42014016	But he said to him , “ A man once gave a great banquet and invited many .
42014017	And at the time for the banquet he sent his servant to say to those who had been invited , ‘ Come , for everything is now ready . ’
42014018	But they all alike began to make excuses . The first said to him , ‘ I have bought a field , and I must go out and see it . Please have me excused . ’
42014019	And another said , ‘ I have bought five yoke of oxen , and I go to examine them . Please have me excused . ’
42014020	And another said , ‘ I have married a wife , and therefore I cannot come . ’
42014021	So the servant came and reported these things to his master . Then the master of the house became angry and said to his servant , ‘ Go out quickly to the streets and lanes of the city , and bring in the poor and crippled and blind and lame . ’
42014022	And the servant said , ‘ Sir , what you commanded has been done , and still there is room . ’
42014023	And the master said to the servant , ‘ Go out to the highways and hedges and compel people to come in , that my house may be filled .
42014024	For I tell you , none of those men who were invited shall taste my banquet . ’ ”
42014025	Now great crowds accompanied him , and he turned and said to them ,
42014026	“ If anyone comes to me and does not hate his own father and mother and wife and children and brothers and sisters , yes , and even his own life , he cannot be my disciple .
42014027	Whoever does not bear his own cross and come after me cannot be my disciple .
42014028	For which of you , desiring to build a tower , does not first sit down and count the cost , whether he has enough to complete it ?
42014029	Otherwise , when he has laid a foundation and is not able to finish , all who see it begin to mock him ,
42014030	saying , ‘ This man began to build and was not able to finish . ’
42014031	Or what king , going out to encounter another king in war , will not sit down first and deliberate whether he is able with ten thousand to meet him who comes against him with twenty thousand ?
42014032	And if not , while the other is yet a great way off , he sends a delegation and asks for terms of peace .
42014033	So therefore , any one of you who does not renounce all that he has cannot be my disciple .
42014034	“ Salt is good , but if salt has lost its taste , how shall its saltiness be restored ?
42014035	It is of no use either for the soil or for the manure pile . It is thrown away . He who has ears to hear , let him hear . ”
42015001	Now the tax collectors and sinners were all drawing near to hear him .
42015002	And the Pharisees and the scribes grumbled , saying , “ This man receives sinners and eats with them . ”
42015003	So he told them this parable :
42015004	“ What man of you , having a hundred sheep , if he has lost one of them , does not leave the ninety-nine in the open country , and go after the one that is lost , until he finds it ?
42015005	And when he has found it , he lays it on his shoulders , rejoicing .
42015006	And when he comes home , he calls together his friends and his neighbors , saying to them , ‘ Rejoice with me , for I have found my sheep that was lost . ’
42015007	Just so , I tell you , there will be more joy in heaven over one sinner who repents than over ninety-nine righteous persons who need no repentance .
42015008	“ Or what woman , having ten silver coins , if she loses one coin , does not light a lamp and sweep the house and seek diligently until she finds it ?
42015009	And when she has found it , she calls together her friends and neighbors , saying , ‘ Rejoice with me , for I have found the coin that I had lost . ’
42015010	Just so , I tell you , there is joy before the angels of God over one sinner who repents . ”
42015011	And he said , “ There was a man who had two sons .
42015012	And the younger of them said to his father , ‘ Father , give me the share of property that is coming to me . ’ And he divided his property between them .
42015013	Not many days later , the younger son gathered all he had and took a journey into a far country , and there he squandered his property in reckless living .
42015014	And when he had spent everything , a severe famine arose in that country , and he began to be in need .
42015015	So he went and hired himself out to one of the citizens of that country , who sent him into his fields to feed pigs .
42015016	And he was longing to be fed with the pods that the pigs ate , and no one gave him anything .
42015017	“ But when he came to himself , he said , ‘ How many of my father’s hired servants have more than enough bread , but I perish here with hunger !
42015018	I will arise and go to my father , and I will say to him , “ Father , I have sinned against heaven and before you .
42015019	I am no longer worthy to be called your son . Treat me as one of your hired servants . ” ’
42015020	And he arose and came to his father . But while he was still a long way off , his father saw him and felt compassion , and ran and embraced him and kissed him .
42015021	And the son said to him , ‘ Father , I have sinned against heaven and before you . I am no longer worthy to be called your son . ’
42015022	But the father said to his servants , ‘ Bring quickly the best robe , and put it on him , and put a ring on his hand , and shoes on his feet .
42015023	And bring the fattened calf and kill it , and let us eat and celebrate .
42015024	For this my son was dead , and is alive again ; he was lost , and is found . ’ And they began to celebrate .
42015025	“ Now his older son was in the field , and as he came and drew near to the house , he heard music and dancing .
42015026	And he called one of the servants and asked what these things meant .
42015027	And he said to him , ‘ Your brother has come , and your father has killed the fattened calf , because he has received him back safe and sound . ’
42015028	But he was angry and refused to go in . His father came out and entreated him ,
42015029	but he answered his father , ‘ Look , these many years I have served you , and I never disobeyed your command , yet you never gave me a young goat , that I might celebrate with my friends .
42015030	But when this son of yours came , who has devoured your property with prostitutes , you killed the fattened calf for him ! ’
42015031	And he said to him , ‘ Son , you are always with me , and all that is mine is yours .
42015032	It was fitting to celebrate and be glad , for this your brother was dead , and is alive ; he was lost , and is found . ’ ”
42016001	He also said to the disciples , “ There was a rich man who had a manager , and charges were brought to him that this man was wasting his possessions .
42016002	And he called him and said to him , ‘ What is this that I hear about you ? Turn in the account of your management , for you can no longer be manager . ’
42016003	And the manager said to himself , ‘ What shall I do , since my master is taking the management away from me ? I am not strong enough to dig , and I am ashamed to beg .
42016004	I have decided what to do , so that when I am removed from management , people may receive me into their houses . ’
42016005	So , summoning his master’s debtors one by one , he said to the first , ‘ How much do you owe my master ? ’
42016006	He said , ‘ A hundred measures of oil . ’ He said to him , ‘ Take your bill , and sit down quickly and write fifty . ’
42016007	Then he said to another , ‘ And how much do you owe ? ’ He said , ‘ A hundred measures of wheat . ’ He said to him , ‘ Take your bill , and write eighty . ’
42016008	The master commended the dishonest manager for his shrewdness . For the sons of this world are more shrewd in dealing with their own generation than the sons of light .
42016009	And I tell you , make friends for yourselves by means of unrighteous wealth , so that when it fails they may receive you into the eternal dwellings .
42016010	“ One who is faithful in a very little is also faithful in much , and one who is dishonest in a very little is also dishonest in much .
42016011	If then you have not been faithful in the unrighteous wealth , who will entrust to you the true riches ?
42016012	And if you have not been faithful in that which is another’s , who will give you that which is your own ?
42016013	No servant can serve two masters , for either he will hate the one and love the other , or he will be devoted to the one and despise the other . You cannot serve God and money . ”
42016014	The Pharisees , who were lovers of money , heard all these things , and they ridiculed him .
42016015	And he said to them , “ You are those who justify yourselves before men , but God knows your hearts . For what is exalted among men is an abomination in the sight of God .
42016016	“ The Law and the Prophets were until John ; since then the good news of the kingdom of God is preached , and everyone forces his way into it .
42016017	But it is easier for heaven and earth to pass away than for one dot of the Law to become void .
42016018	“ Everyone who divorces his wife and marries another commits adultery , and he who marries a woman divorced from her husband commits adultery .
42016019	“ There was a rich man who was clothed in purple and fine linen and who feasted sumptuously every day .
42016020	And at his gate was laid a poor man named Lazarus , covered with sores ,
42016021	who desired to be fed with what fell from the rich man’s table . Moreover , even the dogs came and licked his sores .
42016022	The poor man died and was carried by the angels to Abraham’s side . The rich man also died and was buried ,
42016023	and in Hades , being in torment , he lifted up his eyes and saw Abraham far off and Lazarus at his side .
42016024	And he called out , ‘ Father Abraham , have mercy on me , and send Lazarus to dip the end of his finger in water and cool my tongue , for I am in anguish in this flame . ’
42016025	But Abraham said , ‘ Child , remember that you in your lifetime received your good things , and Lazarus in like manner bad things ; but now he is comforted here , and you are in anguish .
42016026	And besides all this , between us and you a great chasm has been fixed , in order that those who would pass from here to you may not be able , and none may cross from there to us . ’
42016027	And he said , ‘ Then I beg you , father , to send him to my father’s house —
42016028	for I have five brothers — so that he may warn them , lest they also come into this place of torment . ’
42016029	But Abraham said , ‘ They have Moses and the Prophets ; let them hear them . ’
42016030	And he said , ‘ No , father Abraham , but if someone goes to them from the dead , they will repent . ’
42016031	He said to him , ‘ If they do not hear Moses and the Prophets , neither will they be convinced if someone should rise from the dead . ’ ”
42017001	And he said to his disciples , “ Temptations to sin are sure to come , but woe to the one through whom they come !
42017002	It would be better for him if a millstone were hung around his neck and he were cast into the sea than that he should cause one of these little ones to sin .
42017003	Pay attention to yourselves ! If your brother sins , rebuke him , and if he repents , forgive him ,
42017004	and if he sins against you seven times in the day , and turns to you seven times , saying , ‘ I repent , ’ you must forgive him . ”
42017005	The apostles said to the Lord , “ Increase our faith ! ”
42017006	And the Lord said , “ If you had faith like a grain of mustard seed , you could say to this mulberry tree , ‘ Be uprooted and planted in the sea , ’ and it would obey you .
42017007	“ Will any one of you who has a servant plowing or keeping sheep say to him when he has come in from the field , ‘ Come at once and recline at table ’ ?
42017008	Will he not rather say to him , ‘ Prepare supper for me , and dress properly , and serve me while I eat and drink , and afterward you will eat and drink ’ ?
42017009	Does he thank the servant because he did what was commanded ?
42017010	So you also , when you have done all that you were commanded , say , ‘ We are unworthy servants ; we have only done what was our duty . ’ ”
42017011	On the way to Jerusalem he was passing along between Samaria and Galilee .
42017012	And as he entered a village , he was met by ten lepers , who stood at a distance
42017013	and lifted up their voices , saying , “ Jesus , Master , have mercy on us . ”
