42017015	Then one of them , when he saw that he was healed , turned back , praising God with a loud voice ;
42017016	and he fell on his face at Jesus ’ feet , giving him thanks . Now he was a Samaritan .
42017017	Then Jesus answered , “ Were not ten cleansed ? Where are the nine ?
42017018	Was no one found to return and give praise to God except this foreigner ? ”
42017019	And he said to him , “ Rise and go your way ; your faith has made you well . ”
42017020	Being asked by the Pharisees when the kingdom of God would come , he answered them , “ The kingdom of God is not coming with signs to be observed ,
42017021	nor will they say , ‘ Look , here it is ! ’ or ‘ There ! ’ for behold , the kingdom of God is in the midst of you . ”
42017022	And he said to the disciples , “ The days are coming when you will desire to see one of the days of the Son of Man , and you will not see it .
42017023	And they will say to you , ‘ Look , there ! ’ or ‘ Look , here ! ’ Do not go out or follow them .
42017024	For as the lightning flashes and lights up the sky from one side to the other , so will the Son of Man be in his day .
42017025	But first he must suffer many things and be rejected by this generation .
42017026	Just as it was in the days of Noah , so will it be in the days of the Son of Man .
42017027	They were eating and drinking and marrying and being given in marriage , until the day when Noah entered the ark , and the flood came and destroyed them all .
42017028	Likewise , just as it was in the days of Lot — they were eating and drinking , buying and selling , planting and building ,
42017029	but on the day when Lot went out from Sodom , fire and sulfur rained from heaven and destroyed them all —
42017030	so will it be on the day when the Son of Man is revealed .
42017031	On that day , let the one who is on the housetop , with his goods in the house , not come down to take them away , and likewise let the one who is in the field not turn back .
42017032	Remember Lot’s wife .
42017033	Whoever seeks to preserve his life will lose it , but whoever loses his life will keep it .
42017034	I tell you , in that night there will be two in one bed . One will be taken and the other left .
42017035	There will be two women grinding together . One will be taken and the other left . ”
42017037	And they said to him , “ Where , Lord ? ” He said to them , “ Where the corpse is , there the vultures will gather . ”
42018001	And he told them a parable to the effect that they ought always to pray and not lose heart .
42018002	He said , “ In a certain city there was a judge who neither feared God nor respected man .
42018003	And there was a widow in that city who kept coming to him and saying , ‘ Give me justice against my adversary . ’
42018004	For a while he refused , but afterward he said to himself , ‘ Though I neither fear God nor respect man ,
42018005	yet because this widow keeps bothering me , I will give her justice , so that she will not beat me down by her continual coming . ’ ”
42018006	And the Lord said , “ Hear what the unrighteous judge says .
42018007	And will not God give justice to his elect , who cry to him day and night ? Will he delay long over them ?
42018008	I tell you , he will give justice to them speedily . Nevertheless , when the Son of Man comes , will he find faith on earth ? ”
42018009	He also told this parable to some who trusted in themselves that they were righteous , and treated others with contempt :
42018010	“ Two men went up into the temple to pray , one a Pharisee and the other a tax collector .

42018012	I fast twice a week ; I give tithes of all that I get . ’

42018014	I tell you , this man went down to his house justified , rather than the other . For everyone who exalts himself will be humbled , but the one who humbles himself will be exalted . ”
42018015	Now they were bringing even infants to him that he might touch them . And when the disciples saw it , they rebuked them .

42018018	And a ruler asked him , “ Good Teacher , what must I do to inherit eternal life ? ”

42018020	You know the commandments : ‘ Do not commit adultery , Do not murder , Do not steal , Do not bear false witness , Honor your father and mother . ’ ”
42018021	And he said , “ All these I have kept from my youth . ”

42018023	But when he heard these things , he became very sad , for he was extremely rich .

42018037	They told him , “ Jesus of Nazareth is passing by . ”

42019001	He entered Jericho and was passing through .
42019002	And there was a man named Zacchaeus . He was a chief tax collector and was rich .
42019003	And he was seeking to see who Jesus was , but on account of the crowd he could not , because he was small of stature .
42019004	So he ran on ahead and climbed up into a sycamore tree to see him , for he was about to pass that way .
42019005	And when Jesus came to the place , he looked up and said to him , “ Zacchaeus , hurry and come down , for I must stay at your house today . ”
42019006	So he hurried and came down and received him joyfully .

42019011	As they heard these things , he proceeded to tell a parable , because he was near to Jerusalem , and because they supposed that the kingdom of God was to appear immediately .
42019012	He said therefore , “ A nobleman went into a far country to receive for himself a kingdom and then return .
42019013	Calling ten of his servants , he gave them ten minas , and said to them , ‘ Engage in business until I come . ’
42019014	But his citizens hated him and sent a delegation after him , saying , ‘ We do not want this man to reign over us . ’
42019015	When he returned , having received the kingdom , he ordered these servants to whom he had given the money to be called to him , that he might know what they had gained by doing business .
42019016	The first came before him , saying , ‘ Lord , your mina has made ten minas more . ’
42019017	And he said to him , ‘ Well done , good servant ! Because you have been faithful in a very little , you shall have authority over ten cities . ’
42019018	And the second came , saying , ‘ Lord , your mina has made five minas . ’
42019019	And he said to him , ‘ And you are to be over five cities . ’
42019020	Then another came , saying , ‘ Lord , here is your mina , which I kept laid away in a handkerchief ;
42019021	for I was afraid of you , because you are a severe man . You take what you did not deposit , and reap what you did not sow . ’
42019022	He said to him , ‘ I will condemn you with your own words , you wicked servant ! You knew that I was a severe man , taking what I did not deposit and reaping what I did not sow ?
42019023	Why then did you not put my money in the bank , and at my coming I might have collected it with interest ? ’
42019024	And he said to those who stood by , ‘ Take the mina from him , and give it to the one who has the ten minas . ’
42019025	And they said to him , ‘ Lord , he has ten minas ! ’
42019026	‘ I tell you that to everyone who has , more will be given , but from the one who has not , even what he has will be taken away .
42019027	But as for these enemies of mine , who did not want me to reign over them , bring them here and slaughter them before me . ’ ”
42019028	And when he had said these things , he went on ahead , going up to Jerusalem .

42019031	If anyone asks you , ‘ Why are you untying it ? ’ you shall say this : ‘ The Lord has need of it . ’ ”
42019032	So those who were sent went away and found it just as he had told them .

42020001	One day , as Jesus was teaching the people in the temple and preaching the gospel , the chief priests and the scribes with the elders came up
42020002	and said to him , “ Tell us by what authority you do these things , or who it is that gave you this authority . ”
42020003	He answered them , “ I also will ask you a question . Now tell me ,
42020004	was the baptism of John from heaven or from man ? ”
42020005	And they discussed it with one another , saying , “ If we say , ‘ From heaven , ’ he will say , ‘ Why did you not believe him ? ’
42020006	But if we say , ‘ From man , ’ all the people will stone us to death , for they are convinced that John was a prophet . ”
42020007	So they answered that they did not know where it came from .
42020008	And Jesus said to them , “ Neither will I tell you by what authority I do these things . ”
42020009	And he began to tell the people this parable : “ A man planted a vineyard and let it out to tenants and went into another country for a long while .
42020010	When the time came , he sent a servant to the tenants , so that they would give him some of the fruit of the vineyard . But the tenants beat him and sent him away empty-handed .
42020011	And he sent another servant . But they also beat and treated him shamefully , and sent him away empty-handed .
42020012	And he sent yet a third . This one also they wounded and cast out .
42020013	Then the owner of the vineyard said , ‘ What shall I do ? I will send my beloved son ; perhaps they will respect him . ’
42020014	But when the tenants saw him , they said to themselves , ‘ This is the heir . Let us kill him , so that the inheritance may be ours . ’
42020015	And they threw him out of the vineyard and killed him . What then will the owner of the vineyard do to them ?
42020016	He will come and destroy those tenants and give the vineyard to others . ” When they heard this , they said , “ Surely not ! ”
42020017	But he looked directly at them and said , “ What then is this that is written : “ ‘ The stone that the builders rejected has become the cornerstone ’ ?
42020018	Everyone who falls on that stone will be broken to pieces , and when it falls on anyone , it will crush him . ”
42020019	The scribes and the chief priests sought to lay hands on him at that very hour , for they perceived that he had told this parable against them , but they feared the people .
42020020	So they watched him and sent spies , who pretended to be sincere , that they might catch him in something he said , so as to deliver him up to the authority and jurisdiction of the governor .
42020021	So they asked him , “ Teacher , we know that you speak and teach rightly , and show no partiality , but truly teach the way of God .
42020022	Is it lawful for us to give tribute to Caesar , or not ? ”
42020023	But he perceived their craftiness , and said to them ,
42020024	“ Show me a denarius . Whose likeness and inscription does it have ? ” They said , “ Caesar’s . ”
42020025	He said to them , “ Then render to Caesar the things that are Caesar’s , and to God the things that are God’s . ”
42020026	And they were not able in the presence of the people to catch him in what he said , but marveling at his answer they became silent .
42020027	There came to him some Sadducees , those who deny that there is a resurrection ,
42020028	and they asked him a question , saying , “ Teacher , Moses wrote for us that if a man’s brother dies , having a wife but no children , the man must take the widow and raise up offspring for his brother .
42020029	Now there were seven brothers . The first took a wife , and died without children .
42020030	And the second
42020031	and the third took her , and likewise all seven left no children and died .
42020032	Afterward the woman also died .
42020033	In the resurrection , therefore , whose wife will the woman be ? For the seven had her as wife . ”
42020034	And Jesus said to them , “ The sons of this age marry and are given in marriage ,
42020035	but those who are considered worthy to attain to that age and to the resurrection from the dead neither marry nor are given in marriage ,
42020036	for they cannot die anymore , because they are equal to angels and are sons of God , being sons of the resurrection .
42020037	But that the dead are raised , even Moses showed , in the passage about the bush , where he calls the Lord the God of Abraham and the God of Isaac and the God of Jacob .
42020038	Now he is not God of the dead , but of the living , for all live to him . ”
42020039	Then some of the scribes answered , “ Teacher , you have spoken well . ”
42020040	For they no longer dared to ask him any question .
42020041	But he said to them , “ How can they say that the Christ is David’s son ?
42020042	For David himself says in the Book of Psalms , “ ‘ The Lord said to my Lord , Sit at my right hand ,
42020043	until I make your enemies your footstool . ’
42020044	David thus calls him Lord , so how is he his son ? ”
42020045	And in the hearing of all the people he said to his disciples ,
42020046	“ Beware of the scribes , who like to walk around in long robes , and love greetings in the marketplaces and the best seats in the synagogues and the places of honor at feasts ,
42020047	who devour widows ’ houses and for a pretense make long prayers . They will receive the greater condemnation . ”
42021001	Jesus looked up and saw the rich putting their gifts into the offering box ,
42021002	and he saw a poor widow put in two small copper coins .
42021003	And he said , “ Truly , I tell you , this poor widow has put in more than all of them .
42021004	For they all contributed out of their abundance , but she out of her poverty put in all she had to live on . ”
42021005	And while some were speaking of the temple , how it was adorned with noble stones and offerings , he said ,
42021006	“ As for these things that you see , the days will come when there will not be left here one stone upon another that will not be thrown down . ”
42021007	And they asked him , “ Teacher , when will these things be , and what will be the sign when these things are about to take place ? ”
42021008	And he said , “ See that you are not led astray . For many will come in my name , saying , ‘ I am he ! ’ and , ‘ The time is at hand ! ’ Do not go after them .
42021009	And when you hear of wars and tumults , do not be terrified , for these things must first take place , but the end will not be at once . ”
42021010	Then he said to them , “ Nation will rise against nation , and kingdom against kingdom .
42021011	There will be great earthquakes , and in various places famines and pestilences . And there will be terrors and great signs from heaven .
42021012	But before all this they will lay their hands on you and persecute you , delivering you up to the synagogues and prisons , and you will be brought before kings and governors for my name’s sake .
42021013	This will be your opportunity to bear witness .
42021014	Settle it therefore in your minds not to meditate beforehand how to answer ,
42021015	for I will give you a mouth and wisdom , which none of your adversaries will be able to withstand or contradict .
42021016	You will be delivered up even by parents and brothers and relatives and friends , and some of you they will put to death .
42021017	You will be hated by all for my name’s sake .
42021018	But not a hair of your head will perish .
42021019	By your endurance you will gain your lives .
42021020	“ But when you see Jerusalem surrounded by armies , then know that its desolation has come near .
42021021	Then let those who are in Judea flee to the mountains , and let those who are inside the city depart , and let not those who are out in the country enter it ,
42021022	for these are days of vengeance , to fulfill all that is written .
42021023	Alas for women who are pregnant and for those who are nursing infants in those days ! For there will be great distress upon the earth and wrath against this people .
42021024	They will fall by the edge of the sword and be led captive among all nations , and Jerusalem will be trampled underfoot by the Gentiles , until the times of the Gentiles are fulfilled .
42021025	“ And there will be signs in sun and moon and stars , and on the earth distress of nations in perplexity because of the roaring of the sea and the waves ,
42021026	people fainting with fear and with foreboding of what is coming on the world . For the powers of the heavens will be shaken .
42021027	And then they will see the Son of Man coming in a cloud with power and great glory .
42021028	Now when these things begin to take place , straighten up and raise your heads , because your redemption is drawing near . ”
42021029	And he told them a parable : “ Look at the fig tree , and all the trees .
42021030	As soon as they come out in leaf , you see for yourselves and know that the summer is already near .
42021031	So also , when you see these things taking place , you know that the kingdom of God is near .
42021032	Truly , I say to you , this generation will not pass away until all has taken place .
42021033	Heaven and earth will pass away , but my words will not pass away .
42021034	“ But watch yourselves lest your hearts be weighed down with dissipation and drunkenness and cares of this life , and that day come upon you suddenly like a trap .
42021035	For it will come upon all who dwell on the face of the whole earth .
42021036	But stay awake at all times , praying that you may have strength to escape all these things that are going to take place , and to stand before the Son of Man . ”
42021037	And every day he was teaching in the temple , but at night he went out and lodged on the mount called Olivet .
42021038	And early in the morning all the people came to him in the temple to hear him .
42022001	Now the Feast of Unleavened Bread drew near , which is called the Passover .
42022002	And the chief priests and the scribes were seeking how to put him to death , for they feared the people .
42022003	Then Satan entered into Judas called Iscariot , who was of the number of the twelve .
42022004	He went away and conferred with the chief priests and officers how he might betray him to them .
42022005	And they were glad , and agreed to give him money .
42022006	So he consented and sought an opportunity to betray him to them in the absence of a crowd .
42022007	Then came the day of Unleavened Bread , on which the Passover lamb had to be sacrificed .
42022008	So Jesus sent Peter and John , saying , “ Go and prepare the Passover for us , that we may eat it . ”
42022009	They said to him , “ Where will you have us prepare it ? ”
42022010	He said to them , “ Behold , when you have entered the city , a man carrying a jar of water will meet you . Follow him into the house that he enters
42022011	and tell the master of the house , ‘ The Teacher says to you , Where is the guest room , where I may eat the Passover with my disciples ? ’
42022012	And he will show you a large upper room furnished ; prepare it there . ”
42022013	And they went and found it just as he had told them , and they prepared the Passover .
42022014	And when the hour came , he reclined at table , and the apostles with him .
42022015	And he said to them , “ I have earnestly desired to eat this Passover with you before I suffer .
42022016	For I tell you I will not eat it until it is fulfilled in the kingdom of God . ”
42022017	And he took a cup , and when he had given thanks he said , “ Take this , and divide it among yourselves .
42022018	For I tell you that from now on I will not drink of the fruit of the vine until the kingdom of God comes . ”
42022019	And he took bread , and when he had given thanks , he broke it and gave it to them , saying , “ This is my body , which is given for you . Do this in remembrance of me . ”
42022020	And likewise the cup after they had eaten , saying , “ This cup that is poured out for you is the new covenant in my blood .
42022021	But behold , the hand of him who betrays me is with me on the table .
42022022	For the Son of Man goes as it has been determined , but woe to that man by whom he is betrayed ! ”
42022023	And they began to question one another , which of them it could be who was going to do this .
42022024	A dispute also arose among them , as to which of them was to be regarded as the greatest .
42022025	And he said to them , “ The kings of the Gentiles exercise lordship over them , and those in authority over them are called benefactors .
42022026	But not so with you . Rather , let the greatest among you become as the youngest , and the leader as one who serves .
42022027	For who is the greater , one who reclines at table or one who serves ? Is it not the one who reclines at table ? But I am among you as the one who serves .
42022028	“ You are those who have stayed with me in my trials ,
42022029	and I assign to you , as my Father assigned to me , a kingdom ,
42022030	that you may eat and drink at my table in my kingdom and sit on thrones judging the twelve tribes of Israel .
42022031	“ Simon , Simon , behold , Satan demanded to have you , that he might sift you like wheat ,
42022032	but I have prayed for you that your faith may not fail . And when you have turned again , strengthen your brothers . ”
42022033	Peter said to him , “ Lord , I am ready to go with you both to prison and to death . ”
42022034	Jesus said , “ I tell you , Peter , the rooster will not crow this day , until you deny three times that you know me . ”
42022035	And he said to them , “ When I sent you out with no moneybag or knapsack or sandals , did you lack anything ? ” They said , “ Nothing . ”
42022036	He said to them , “ But now let the one who has a moneybag take it , and likewise a knapsack . And let the one who has no sword sell his cloak and buy one .
42022037	For I tell you that this Scripture must be fulfilled in me : ‘ And he was numbered with the transgressors . ’ For what is written about me has its fulfillment . ”
42022038	And they said , “ Look , Lord , here are two swords . ” And he said to them , “ It is enough . ”
42022039	And he came out and went , as was his custom , to the Mount of Olives , and the disciples followed him .
42022040	And when he came to the place , he said to them , “ Pray that you may not enter into temptation . ”
42022041	And he withdrew from them about a stone’s throw , and knelt down and prayed ,
42022042	saying , “ Father , if you are willing , remove this cup from me . Nevertheless , not my will , but yours , be done . ”
42022043	And there appeared to him an angel from heaven , strengthening him .
42022044	And being in an agony he prayed more earnestly ; and his sweat became like great drops of blood falling down to the ground .
42022045	And when he rose from prayer , he came to the disciples and found them sleeping for sorrow ,
42022046	and he said to them , “ Why are you sleeping ? Rise and pray that you may not enter into temptation . ”
42022047	While he was still speaking , there came a crowd , and the man called Judas , one of the twelve , was leading them . He drew near to Jesus to kiss him ,
42022048	but Jesus said to him , “ Judas , would you betray the Son of Man with a kiss ? ”
42022049	And when those who were around him saw what would follow , they said , “ Lord , shall we strike with the sword ? ”
42022050	And one of them struck the servant of the high priest and cut off his right ear .
42022051	But Jesus said , “ No more of this ! ” And he touched his ear and healed him .
42022052	Then Jesus said to the chief priests and officers of the temple and elders , who had come out against him , “ Have you come out as against a robber , with swords and clubs ?
42022053	When I was with you day after day in the temple , you did not lay hands on me . But this is your hour , and the power of darkness . ”
42022054	Then they seized him and led him away , bringing him into the high priest’s house , and Peter was following at a distance .
42022055	And when they had kindled a fire in the middle of the courtyard and sat down together , Peter sat down among them .
42022056	Then a servant girl , seeing him as he sat in the light and looking closely at him , said , “ This man also was with him . ”
42022057	But he denied it , saying , “ Woman , I do not know him . ”
42022058	And a little later someone else saw him and said , “ You also are one of them . ” But Peter said , “ Man , I am not . ”
42022059	And after an interval of about an hour still another insisted , saying , “ Certainly this man also was with him , for he too is a Galilean . ”
42022060	But Peter said , “ Man , I do not know what you are talking about . ” And immediately , while he was still speaking , the rooster crowed .
42022061	And the Lord turned and looked at Peter . And Peter remembered the saying of the Lord , how he had said to him , “ Before the rooster crows today , you will deny me three times . ”
42022062	And he went out and wept bitterly .
42022063	Now the men who were holding Jesus in custody were mocking him as they beat him .

42022065	And they said many other things against him , blaspheming him .
42022066	When day came , the assembly of the elders of the people gathered together , both chief priests and scribes . And they led him away to their council , and they said ,
42022067	“ If you are the Christ , tell us . ” But he said to them , “ If I tell you , you will not believe ,
42022068	and if I ask you , you will not answer .
42022069	But from now on the Son of Man shall be seated at the right hand of the power of God . ”
42022070	So they all said , “ Are you the Son of God , then ? ” And he said to them , “ You say that I am . ”
42022071	Then they said , “ What further testimony do we need ? We have heard it ourselves from his own lips . ”
42023001	Then the whole company of them arose and brought him before Pilate .
42023002	And they began to accuse him , saying , “ We found this man misleading our nation and forbidding us to give tribute to Caesar , and saying that he himself is Christ , a king . ”
42023003	And Pilate asked him , “ Are you the King of the Jews ? ” And he answered him , “ You have said so . ”
42023004	Then Pilate said to the chief priests and the crowds , “ I find no guilt in this man . ”
42023005	But they were urgent , saying , “ He stirs up the people , teaching throughout all Judea , from Galilee even to this place . ”
42023006	When Pilate heard this , he asked whether the man was a Galilean .
42023007	And when he learned that he belonged to Herod’s jurisdiction , he sent him over to Herod , who was himself in Jerusalem at that time .
42023008	When Herod saw Jesus , he was very glad , for he had long desired to see him , because he had heard about him , and he was hoping to see some sign done by him .
42023009	So he questioned him at some length , but he made no answer .
42023010	The chief priests and the scribes stood by , vehemently accusing him .
42023011	And Herod with his soldiers treated him with contempt and mocked him . Then , arraying him in splendid clothing , he sent him back to Pilate .
42023012	And Herod and Pilate became friends with each other that very day , for before this they had been at enmity with each other .
42023013	Pilate then called together the chief priests and the rulers and the people ,
42023014	and said to them , “ You brought me this man as one who was misleading the people . And after examining him before you , behold , I did not find this man guilty of any of your charges against him .
42023015	Neither did Herod , for he sent him back to us . Look , nothing deserving death has been done by him .
42023016	I will therefore punish and release him . ”
42023018	But they all cried out together , “ Away with this man , and release to us Barabbas ” —
42023019	a man who had been thrown into prison for an insurrection started in the city and for murder .
42023020	Pilate addressed them once more , desiring to release Jesus ,
42023021	but they kept shouting , “ Crucify , crucify him ! ”
42023022	A third time he said to them , “ Why , what evil has he done ? I have found in him no guilt deserving death . I will therefore punish and release him . ”
42023023	But they were urgent , demanding with loud cries that he should be crucified . And their voices prevailed .
42023024	So Pilate decided that their demand should be granted .
42023025	He released the man who had been thrown into prison for insurrection and murder , for whom they asked , but he delivered Jesus over to their will .
42023026	And as they led him away , they seized one Simon of Cyrene , who was coming in from the country , and laid on him the cross , to carry it behind Jesus .
42023027	And there followed him a great multitude of the people and of women who were mourning and lamenting for him .
42023028	But turning to them Jesus said , “ Daughters of Jerusalem , do not weep for me , but weep for yourselves and for your children .
42023029	For behold , the days are coming when they will say , ‘ Blessed are the barren and the wombs that never bore and the breasts that never nursed ! ’
42023030	Then they will begin to say to the mountains , ‘ Fall on us , ’ and to the hills , ‘ Cover us . ’
42023031	For if they do these things when the wood is green , what will happen when it is dry ? ”
42023032	Two others , who were criminals , were led away to be put to death with him .
42023033	And when they came to the place that is called The Skull , there they crucified him , and the criminals , one on his right and one on his left .
42023034	And Jesus said , “ Father , forgive them , for they know not what they do . ” And they cast lots to divide his garments .
42023035	And the people stood by , watching , but the rulers scoffed at him , saying , “ He saved others ; let him save himself , if he is the Christ of God , his Chosen One ! ”
42023036	The soldiers also mocked him , coming up and offering him sour wine
42023037	and saying , “ If you are the King of the Jews , save yourself ! ”
42023038	There was also an inscription over him , “ This is the King of the Jews . ”
42023039	One of the criminals who were hanged railed at him , saying , “ Are you not the Christ ? Save yourself and us ! ”
42023040	But the other rebuked him , saying , “ Do you not fear God , since you are under the same sentence of condemnation ?
42023041	And we indeed justly , for we are receiving the due reward of our deeds ; but this man has done nothing wrong . ”
42023042	And he said , “ Jesus , remember me when you come into your kingdom . ”
42023043	And he said to him , “ Truly , I say to you , today you will be with me in Paradise . ”
42023044	It was now about the sixth hour , and there was darkness over the whole land until the ninth hour ,
42023045	while the sun’s light failed . And the curtain of the temple was torn in two .

42023047	Now when the centurion saw what had taken place , he praised God , saying , “ Certainly this man was innocent ! ”
42023048	And all the crowds that had assembled for this spectacle , when they saw what had taken place , returned home beating their breasts .

42023050	Now there was a man named Joseph , from the Jewish town of Arimathea . He was a member of the council , a good and righteous man ,
42023051	who had not consented to their decision and action ; and he was looking for the kingdom of God .

42023053	Then he took it down and wrapped it in a linen shroud and laid him in a tomb cut in stone , where no one had ever yet been laid .
42023054	It was the day of Preparation , and the Sabbath was beginning .
42023055	The women who had come with him from Galilee followed and saw the tomb and how his body was laid .

42024001	But on the first day of the week , at early dawn , they went to the tomb , taking the spices they had prepared .
42024002	And they found the stone rolled away from the tomb ,
42024003	but when they went in they did not find the body of the Lord Jesus .
42024004	While they were perplexed about this , behold , two men stood by them in dazzling apparel .
42024005	And as they were frightened and bowed their faces to the ground , the men said to them , “ Why do you seek the living among the dead ?
42024006	He is not here , but has risen . Remember how he told you , while he was still in Galilee ,
42024007	that the Son of Man must be delivered into the hands of sinful men and be crucified and on the third day rise . ”

42024009	and returning from the tomb they told all these things to the eleven and to all the rest .

42024011	but these words seemed to them an idle tale , and they did not believe them .

42024013	That very day two of them were going to a village named Emmaus , about seven miles from Jerusalem ,
42024014	and they were talking with each other about all these things that had happened .
42024015	While they were talking and discussing together , Jesus himself drew near and went with them .
42024016	But their eyes were kept from recognizing him .
42024017	And he said to them , “ What is this conversation that you are holding with each other as you walk ? ” And they stood still , looking sad .
42024018	Then one of them , named Cleopas , answered him , “ Are you the only visitor to Jerusalem who does not know the things that have happened there in these days ? ”
42024019	And he said to them , “ What things ? ” And they said to him , “ Concerning Jesus of Nazareth , a man who was a prophet mighty in deed and word before God and all the people ,
42024020	and how our chief priests and rulers delivered him up to be condemned to death , and crucified him .
42024021	But we had hoped that he was the one to redeem Israel . Yes , and besides all this , it is now the third day since these things happened .

42024023	and when they did not find his body , they came back saying that they had even seen a vision of angels , who said that he was alive .
42024024	Some of those who were with us went to the tomb and found it just as the women had said , but him they did not see . ”

42024028	So they drew near to the village to which they were going . He acted as if he were going farther ,
42024029	but they urged him strongly , saying , “ Stay with us , for it is toward evening and the day is now far spent . ” So he went in to stay with them .
42024030	When he was at table with them , he took the bread and blessed and broke it and gave it to them .
42024031	And their eyes were opened , and they recognized him . And he vanished from their sight .

42024033	And they rose that same hour and returned to Jerusalem . And they found the eleven and those who were with them gathered together ,
42024034	saying , “ The Lord has risen indeed , and has appeared to Simon ! ”
42024035	Then they told what had happened on the road , and how he was known to them in the breaking of the bread .
42024036	As they were talking about these things , Jesus himself stood among them , and said to them , “ Peace to you ! ”
42024037	But they were startled and frightened and thought they saw a spirit .
42024038	And he said to them , “ Why are you troubled , and why do doubts arise in your hearts ?
42024039	See my hands and my feet , that it is I myself . Touch me , and see . For a spirit does not have flesh and bones as you see that I have . ”
42024040	And when he had said this , he showed them his hands and his feet .

42024042	They gave him a piece of broiled fish ,
42024043	and he took it and ate before them .

42024046	and said to them , “ Thus it is written , that the Christ should suffer and on the third day rise from the dead ,
