43001001	In the beginning was the Word , and the Word was with God , and the Word was God .
43001002	He was in the beginning with God .
43001003	All things were made through him , and without him was not any thing made that was made .
43001004	In him was life , and the life was the light of men .
43001005	The light shines in the darkness , and the darkness has not overcome it .
43001006	There was a man sent from God , whose name was John .
43001007	He came as a witness , to bear witness about the light , that all might believe through him .
43001008	He was not the light , but came to bear witness about the light .
43001009	The true light , which enlightens everyone , was coming into the world .
43001010	He was in the world , and the world was made through him , yet the world did not know him .
43001011	He came to his own , and his own people did not receive him .
43001012	But to all who did receive him , who believed in his name , he gave the right to become children of God ,
43001013	who were born , not of blood nor of the will of the flesh nor of the will of man , but of God .
43001014	And the Word became flesh and dwelt among us , and we have seen his glory , glory as of the only Son from the Father , full of grace and truth .
43001015	( John bore witness about him , and cried out , “ This was he of whom I said , ‘ He who comes after me ranks before me , because he was before me . ’ ”
43001016	And from his fullness we have all received , grace upon grace .
43001017	For the law was given through Moses ; grace and truth came through Jesus Christ .
43001018	No one has ever seen God ; the only God , who is at the Father’s side , he has made him known .
43001019	And this is the testimony of John , when the Jews sent priests and Levites from Jerusalem to ask him , “ Who are you ? ”
43001020	He confessed , and did not deny , but confessed , “ I am not the Christ . ”
43001021	And they asked him , “ What then ? Are you Elijah ? ” He said , “ I am not . ” “ Are you the Prophet ? ” And he answered , “ No . ”
43001022	So they said to him , “ Who are you ? We need to give an answer to those who sent us . What do you say about yourself ? ”
43001023	He said , “ I am the voice of one crying out in the wilderness , ‘ Make straight the way of the Lord , ’ as the prophet Isaiah said . ”
43001024	( Now they had been sent from the Pharisees .
43001025	They asked him , “ Then why are you baptizing , if you are neither the Christ , nor Elijah , nor the Prophet ? ”
43001026	John answered them , “ I baptize with water , but among you stands one you do not know ,
43001027	even he who comes after me , the strap of whose sandal I am not worthy to untie . ”
43001028	These things took place in Bethany across the Jordan , where John was baptizing .
43001029	The next day he saw Jesus coming toward him , and said , “ Behold , the Lamb of God , who takes away the sin of the world !
43001030	This is he of whom I said , ‘ After me comes a man who ranks before me , because he was before me . ’
43001031	I myself did not know him , but for this purpose I came baptizing with water , that he might be revealed to Israel . ”
43001032	And John bore witness : “ I saw the Spirit descend from heaven like a dove , and it remained on him .
43001033	I myself did not know him , but he who sent me to baptize with water said to me , ‘ He on whom you see the Spirit descend and remain , this is he who baptizes with the Holy Spirit . ’
43001034	And I have seen and have borne witness that this is the Son of God . ”
43001035	The next day again John was standing with two of his disciples ,
43001036	and he looked at Jesus as he walked by and said , “ Behold , the Lamb of God ! ”
43001037	The two disciples heard him say this , and they followed Jesus .
43001038	Jesus turned and saw them following and said to them , “ What are you seeking ? ” And they said to him , “ Rabbi ” ( which means Teacher ) , “ where are you staying ? ”
43001039	He said to them , “ Come and you will see . ” So they came and saw where he was staying , and they stayed with him that day , for it was about the tenth hour .
43001040	One of the two who heard John speak and followed Jesus was Andrew , Simon Peter’s brother .
43001041	He first found his own brother Simon and said to him , “ We have found the Messiah ” ( which means Christ ) .
43001042	He brought him to Jesus . Jesus looked at him and said , “ So you are Simon the son of John ? You shall be called Cephas ” ( which means Peter ) .
43001043	The next day Jesus decided to go to Galilee . He found Philip and said to him , “ Follow me . ”
43001044	Now Philip was from Bethsaida , the city of Andrew and Peter .
43001045	Philip found Nathanael and said to him , “ We have found him of whom Moses in the Law and also the prophets wrote , Jesus of Nazareth , the son of Joseph . ”
43001046	Nathanael said to him , “ Can anything good come out of Nazareth ? ” Philip said to him , “ Come and see . ”
43001047	Jesus saw Nathanael coming toward him and said of him , “ Behold , an Israelite indeed , in whom there is no deceit ! ”
43001048	Nathanael said to him , “ How do you know me ? ” Jesus answered him , “ Before Philip called you , when you were under the fig tree , I saw you . ”
43001049	Nathanael answered him , “ Rabbi , you are the Son of God ! You are the King of Israel ! ”
43001050	Jesus answered him , “ Because I said to you , ‘ I saw you under the fig tree , ’ do you believe ? You will see greater things than these . ”
43001051	And he said to him , “ Truly , truly , I say to you , you will see heaven opened , and the angels of God ascending and descending on the Son of Man . ”
43002001	On the third day there was a wedding at Cana in Galilee , and the mother of Jesus was there .
43002002	Jesus also was invited to the wedding with his disciples .
43002003	When the wine ran out , the mother of Jesus said to him , “ They have no wine . ”
43002004	And Jesus said to her , “ Woman , what does this have to do with me ? My hour has not yet come . ”
43002005	His mother said to the servants , “ Do whatever he tells you . ”
43002006	Now there were six stone water jars there for the Jewish rites of purification , each holding twenty or thirty gallons .
43002007	Jesus said to the servants , “ Fill the jars with water . ” And they filled them up to the brim .
43002008	And he said to them , “ Now draw some out and take it to the master of the feast . ” So they took it .
43002009	When the master of the feast tasted the water now become wine , and did not know where it came from ( though the servants who had drawn the water knew ) , the master of the feast called the bridegroom
43002010	and said to him , “ Everyone serves the good wine first , and when people have drunk freely , then the poor wine . But you have kept the good wine until now . ”
43002011	This , the first of his signs , Jesus did at Cana in Galilee , and manifested his glory . And his disciples believed in him .
43002012	After this he went down to Capernaum , with his mother and his brothers and his disciples , and they stayed there for a few days .
43002013	The Passover of the Jews was at hand , and Jesus went up to Jerusalem .
43002014	In the temple he found those who were selling oxen and sheep and pigeons , and the money-changers sitting there .
43002015	And making a whip of cords , he drove them all out of the temple , with the sheep and oxen . And he poured out the coins of the money-changers and overturned their tables .
43002016	And he told those who sold the pigeons , “ Take these things away ; do not make my Father’s house a house of trade . ”
43002017	His disciples remembered that it was written , “ Zeal for your house will consume me . ”
43002018	So the Jews said to him , “ What sign do you show us for doing these things ? ”
43002019	Jesus answered them , “ Destroy this temple , and in three days I will raise it up . ”
43002020	The Jews then said , “ It has taken forty-six years to build this temple , and will you raise it up in three days ? ”
43002021	But he was speaking about the temple of his body .
43002022	When therefore he was raised from the dead , his disciples remembered that he had said this , and they believed the Scripture and the word that Jesus had spoken .
43002023	Now when he was in Jerusalem at the Passover Feast , many believed in his name when they saw the signs that he was doing .
43002024	But Jesus on his part did not entrust himself to them , because he knew all people
43002025	and needed no one to bear witness about man , for he himself knew what was in man .
43003001	Now there was a man of the Pharisees named Nicodemus , a ruler of the Jews .
43003002	This man came to Jesus by night and said to him , “ Rabbi , we know that you are a teacher come from God , for no one can do these signs that you do unless God is with him . ”
43003003	Jesus answered him , “ Truly , truly , I say to you , unless one is born again he cannot see the kingdom of God . ”
43003004	Nicodemus said to him , “ How can a man be born when he is old ? Can he enter a second time into his mother’s womb and be born ? ”
43003005	Jesus answered , “ Truly , truly , I say to you , unless one is born of water and the Spirit , he cannot enter the kingdom of God .
43003006	That which is born of the flesh is flesh , and that which is born of the Spirit is spirit .
43003007	Do not marvel that I said to you , ‘ You must be born again . ’
43003008	The wind blows where it wishes , and you hear its sound , but you do not know where it comes from or where it goes . So it is with everyone who is born of the Spirit . ”
43003009	Nicodemus said to him , “ How can these things be ? ”
43003010	Jesus answered him , “ Are you the teacher of Israel and yet you do not understand these things ?
43003011	Truly , truly , I say to you , we speak of what we know , and bear witness to what we have seen , but you do not receive our testimony .
43003012	If I have told you earthly things and you do not believe , how can you believe if I tell you heavenly things ?
43003013	No one has ascended into heaven except he who descended from heaven , the Son of Man .
43003014	And as Moses lifted up the serpent in the wilderness , so must the Son of Man be lifted up ,
43003015	that whoever believes in him may have eternal life .
43003016	“ For God so loved the world , that he gave his only Son , that whoever believes in him should not perish but have eternal life .
43003017	For God did not send his Son into the world to condemn the world , but in order that the world might be saved through him .
43003018	Whoever believes in him is not condemned , but whoever does not believe is condemned already , because he has not believed in the name of the only Son of God .
43003019	And this is the judgment : the light has come into the world , and people loved the darkness rather than the light because their works were evil .
43003020	For everyone who does wicked things hates the light and does not come to the light , lest his works should be exposed .
43003021	But whoever does what is true comes to the light , so that it may be clearly seen that his works have been carried out in God . ”
43003022	After this Jesus and his disciples went into the Judean countryside , and he remained there with them and was baptizing .
43003023	John also was baptizing at Aenon near Salim , because water was plentiful there , and people were coming and being baptized
43003024	( for John had not yet been put in prison ) .
43003025	Now a discussion arose between some of John’s disciples and a Jew over purification .
43003026	And they came to John and said to him , “ Rabbi , he who was with you across the Jordan , to whom you bore witness — look , he is baptizing , and all are going to him . ”
43003027	John answered , “ A person cannot receive even one thing unless it is given him from heaven .
43003028	You yourselves bear me witness , that I said , ‘ I am not the Christ , but I have been sent before him . ’
43003029	The one who has the bride is the bridegroom . The friend of the bridegroom , who stands and hears him , rejoices greatly at the bridegroom’s voice . Therefore this joy of mine is now complete .
43003030	He must increase , but I must decrease . ”
43003031	He who comes from above is above all . He who is of the earth belongs to the earth and speaks in an earthly way . He who comes from heaven is above all .
43003032	He bears witness to what he has seen and heard , yet no one receives his testimony .
43003033	Whoever receives his testimony sets his seal to this , that God is true .
43003034	For he whom God has sent utters the words of God , for he gives the Spirit without measure .
43003035	The Father loves the Son and has given all things into his hand .
43003036	Whoever believes in the Son has eternal life ; whoever does not obey the Son shall not see life , but the wrath of God remains on him .
43004001	Now when Jesus learned that the Pharisees had heard that Jesus was making and baptizing more disciples than John
43004002	( although Jesus himself did not baptize , but only his disciples ) ,
43004003	he left Judea and departed again for Galilee .
43004004	And he had to pass through Samaria .
43004005	So he came to a town of Samaria called Sychar , near the field that Jacob had given to his son Joseph .
43004006	Jacob’s well was there ; so Jesus , wearied as he was from his journey , was sitting beside the well . It was about the sixth hour .
43004007	A woman from Samaria came to draw water . Jesus said to her , “ Give me a drink . ”
43004008	( For his disciples had gone away into the city to buy food .
43004009	The Samaritan woman said to him , “ How is it that you , a Jew , ask for a drink from me , a woman of Samaria ? ” ( For Jews have no dealings with Samaritans .
43004010	Jesus answered her , “ If you knew the gift of God , and who it is that is saying to you , ‘ Give me a drink , ’ you would have asked him , and he would have given you living water . ”
43004011	The woman said to him , “ Sir , you have nothing to draw water with , and the well is deep . Where do you get that living water ?
43004012	Are you greater than our father Jacob ? He gave us the well and drank from it himself , as did his sons and his livestock . ”
43004013	Jesus said to her , “ Everyone who drinks of this water will be thirsty again ,
43004014	but whoever drinks of the water that I will give him will never be thirsty again . The water that I will give him will become in him a spring of water welling up to eternal life . ”
43004015	The woman said to him , “ Sir , give me this water , so that I will not be thirsty or have to come here to draw water . ”
43004016	Jesus said to her , “ Go , call your husband , and come here . ”
43004017	The woman answered him , “ I have no husband . ” Jesus said to her , “ You are right in saying , ‘ I have no husband ’ ;
43004018	for you have had five husbands , and the one you now have is not your husband . What you have said is true . ”
43004019	The woman said to him , “ Sir , I perceive that you are a prophet .
43004020	Our fathers worshiped on this mountain , but you say that in Jerusalem is the place where people ought to worship . ”
43004021	Jesus said to her , “ Woman , believe me , the hour is coming when neither on this mountain nor in Jerusalem will you worship the Father .
43004022	You worship what you do not know ; we worship what we know , for salvation is from the Jews .
43004023	But the hour is coming , and is now here , when the true worshipers will worship the Father in spirit and truth , for the Father is seeking such people to worship him .
43004024	God is spirit , and those who worship him must worship in spirit and truth . ”
43004025	The woman said to him , “ I know that Messiah is coming ( he who is called Christ ) . When he comes , he will tell us all things . ”
43004026	Jesus said to her , “ I who speak to you am he . ”
43004027	Just then his disciples came back . They marveled that he was talking with a woman , but no one said , “ What do you seek ? ” or , “ Why are you talking with her ? ”
43004028	So the woman left her water jar and went away into town and said to the people ,
43004029	“ Come , see a man who told me all that I ever did . Can this be the Christ ? ”
43004030	They went out of the town and were coming to him .
43004031	Meanwhile the disciples were urging him , saying , “ Rabbi , eat . ”
43004032	But he said to them , “ I have food to eat that you do not know about . ”
43004033	So the disciples said to one another , “ Has anyone brought him something to eat ? ”
43004034	Jesus said to them , “ My food is to do the will of him who sent me and to accomplish his work .
43004035	Do you not say , ‘ There are yet four months , then comes the harvest ’ ? Look , I tell you , lift up your eyes , and see that the fields are white for harvest .
43004036	Already the one who reaps is receiving wages and gathering fruit for eternal life , so that sower and reaper may rejoice together .
43004037	For here the saying holds true , ‘ One sows and another reaps . ’
43004038	I sent you to reap that for which you did not labor . Others have labored , and you have entered into their labor . ”
43004039	Many Samaritans from that town believed in him because of the woman’s testimony , “ He told me all that I ever did . ”
43004040	So when the Samaritans came to him , they asked him to stay with them , and he stayed there two days .
43004041	And many more believed because of his word .
43004042	They said to the woman , “ It is no longer because of what you said that we believe , for we have heard for ourselves , and we know that this is indeed the Savior of the world . ”
43004043	After the two days he departed for Galilee .
43004044	( For Jesus himself had testified that a prophet has no honor in his own hometown .
43004045	So when he came to Galilee , the Galileans welcomed him , having seen all that he had done in Jerusalem at the feast . For they too had gone to the feast .
43004046	So he came again to Cana in Galilee , where he had made the water wine . And at Capernaum there was an official whose son was ill .
43004047	When this man heard that Jesus had come from Judea to Galilee , he went to him and asked him to come down and heal his son , for he was at the point of death .
43004048	So Jesus said to him , “ Unless you see signs and wonders you will not believe . ”
43004049	The official said to him , “ Sir , come down before my child dies . ”
43004050	Jesus said to him , “ Go ; your son will live . ” The man believed the word that Jesus spoke to him and went on his way .
43004051	As he was going down , his servants met him and told him that his son was recovering .
43004052	So he asked them the hour when he began to get better , and they said to him , “ Yesterday at the seventh hour the fever left him . ”
43004053	The father knew that was the hour when Jesus had said to him , “ Your son will live . ” And he himself believed , and all his household .
43004054	This was now the second sign that Jesus did when he had come from Judea to Galilee .
43005001	After this there was a feast of the Jews , and Jesus went up to Jerusalem .
43005002	Now there is in Jerusalem by the Sheep Gate a pool , in Aramaic called Bethesda , which has five roofed colonnades .
43005003	In these lay a multitude of invalids — blind , lame , and paralyzed .
43005005	One man was there who had been an invalid for thirty-eight years .
43005006	When Jesus saw him lying there and knew that he had already been there a long time , he said to him , “ Do you want to be healed ? ”
43005007	The sick man answered him , “ Sir , I have no one to put me into the pool when the water is stirred up , and while I am going another steps down before me . ”
43005008	Jesus said to him , “ Get up , take up your bed , and walk . ”
43005009	And at once the man was healed , and he took up his bed and walked . Now that day was the Sabbath .
43005010	So the Jews said to the man who had been healed , “ It is the Sabbath , and it is not lawful for you to take up your bed . ”
43005011	But he answered them , “ The man who healed me , that man said to me , ‘ Take up your bed , and walk . ’ ”
43005012	They asked him , “ Who is the man who said to you , ‘ Take up your bed and walk ’ ? ”
43005013	Now the man who had been healed did not know who it was , for Jesus had withdrawn , as there was a crowd in the place .
43005014	Afterward Jesus found him in the temple and said to him , “ See , you are well ! Sin no more , that nothing worse may happen to you . ”
43005015	The man went away and told the Jews that it was Jesus who had healed him .
43005016	And this was why the Jews were persecuting Jesus , because he was doing these things on the Sabbath .
43005017	But Jesus answered them , “ My Father is working until now , and I am working . ”
43005018	This was why the Jews were seeking all the more to kill him , because not only was he breaking the Sabbath , but he was even calling God his own Father , making himself equal with God .
43005019	So Jesus said to them , “ Truly , truly , I say to you , the Son can do nothing of his own accord , but only what he sees the Father doing . For whatever the Father does , that the Son does likewise .
43005020	For the Father loves the Son and shows him all that he himself is doing . And greater works than these will he show him , so that you may marvel .
43005021	For as the Father raises the dead and gives them life , so also the Son gives life to whom he will .
43005022	The Father judges no one , but has given all judgment to the Son ,
43005023	that all may honor the Son , just as they honor the Father . Whoever does not honor the Son does not honor the Father who sent him .
43005024	Truly , truly , I say to you , whoever hears my word and believes him who sent me has eternal life . He does not come into judgment , but has passed from death to life .
43005025	“ Truly , truly , I say to you , an hour is coming , and is now here , when the dead will hear the voice of the Son of God , and those who hear will live .
43005026	For as the Father has life in himself , so he has granted the Son also to have life in himself .
43005027	And he has given him authority to execute judgment , because he is the Son of Man .
43005028	Do not marvel at this , for an hour is coming when all who are in the tombs will hear his voice
43005029	and come out , those who have done good to the resurrection of life , and those who have done evil to the resurrection of judgment .
43005030	“ I can do nothing on my own . As I hear , I judge , and my judgment is just , because I seek not my own will but the will of him who sent me .
43005031	If I alone bear witness about myself , my testimony is not deemed true .
43005032	There is another who bears witness about me , and I know that the testimony that he bears about me is true .
43005033	You sent to John , and he has borne witness to the truth .
43005034	Not that the testimony that I receive is from man , but I say these things so that you may be saved .
43005035	He was a burning and shining lamp , and you were willing to rejoice for a while in his light .
43005036	But the testimony that I have is greater than that of John . For the works that the Father has given me to accomplish , the very works that I am doing , bear witness about me that the Father has sent me .
43005037	And the Father who sent me has himself borne witness about me . His voice you have never heard , his form you have never seen ,
43005038	and you do not have his word abiding in you , for you do not believe the one whom he has sent .
43005039	You search the Scriptures because you think that in them you have eternal life ; and it is they that bear witness about me ,
43005040	yet you refuse to come to me that you may have life .
43005041	I do not receive glory from people .
43005042	But I know that you do not have the love of God within you .
43005043	I have come in my Father’s name , and you do not receive me . If another comes in his own name , you will receive him .
43005044	How can you believe , when you receive glory from one another and do not seek the glory that comes from the only God ?
43005045	Do not think that I will accuse you to the Father . There is one who accuses you : Moses , on whom you have set your hope .
43005046	For if you believed Moses , you would believe me ; for he wrote of me .
43005047	But if you do not believe his writings , how will you believe my words ? ”
43006001	After this Jesus went away to the other side of the Sea of Galilee , which is the Sea of Tiberias .
43006002	And a large crowd was following him , because they saw the signs that he was doing on the sick .
43006003	Jesus went up on the mountain , and there he sat down with his disciples .
43006004	Now the Passover , the feast of the Jews , was at hand .
43006005	Lifting up his eyes , then , and seeing that a large crowd was coming toward him , Jesus said to Philip , “ Where are we to buy bread , so that these people may eat ? ”
43006006	He said this to test him , for he himself knew what he would do .
43006007	Philip answered him , “ Two hundred denarii would not buy enough bread for each of them to get a little . ”
43006008	One of his disciples , Andrew , Simon Peter’s brother , said to him ,
43006009	“ There is a boy here who has five barley loaves and two fish , but what are they for so many ? ”
43006010	Jesus said , “ Have the people sit down . ” Now there was much grass in the place . So the men sat down , about five thousand in number .
43006011	Jesus then took the loaves , and when he had given thanks , he distributed them to those who were seated . So also the fish , as much as they wanted .
43006012	And when they had eaten their fill , he told his disciples , “ Gather up the leftover fragments , that nothing may be lost . ”
43006013	So they gathered them up and filled twelve baskets with fragments from the five barley loaves left by those who had eaten .
43006014	When the people saw the sign that he had done , they said , “ This is indeed the Prophet who is to come into the world ! ”
43006015	Perceiving then that they were about to come and take him by force to make him king , Jesus withdrew again to the mountain by himself .
43006016	When evening came , his disciples went down to the sea ,
43006017	got into a boat , and started across the sea to Capernaum . It was now dark , and Jesus had not yet come to them .
43006018	The sea became rough because a strong wind was blowing .
43006019	When they had rowed about three or four miles , they saw Jesus walking on the sea and coming near the boat , and they were frightened .
43006020	But he said to them , “ It is I ; do not be afraid . ”
43006021	Then they were glad to take him into the boat , and immediately the boat was at the land to which they were going .
43006022	On the next day the crowd that remained on the other side of the sea saw that there had been only one boat there , and that Jesus had not entered the boat with his disciples , but that his disciples had gone away alone .
43006023	Other boats from Tiberias came near the place where they had eaten the bread after the Lord had given thanks .
43006024	So when the crowd saw that Jesus was not there , nor his disciples , they themselves got into the boats and went to Capernaum , seeking Jesus .
43006025	When they found him on the other side of the sea , they said to him , “ Rabbi , when did you come here ? ”
43006026	Jesus answered them , “ Truly , truly , I say to you , you are seeking me , not because you saw signs , but because you ate your fill of the loaves .
43006027	Do not labor for the food that perishes , but for the food that endures to eternal life , which the Son of Man will give to you . For on him God the Father has set his seal . ”
43006028	Then they said to him , “ What must we do , to be doing the works of God ? ”
43006029	Jesus answered them , “ This is the work of God , that you believe in him whom he has sent . ”
43006030	So they said to him , “ Then what sign do you do , that we may see and believe you ? What work do you perform ?
43006031	Our fathers ate the manna in the wilderness ; as it is written , ‘ He gave them bread from heaven to eat . ’ ”
43006032	Jesus then said to them , “ Truly , truly , I say to you , it was not Moses who gave you the bread from heaven , but my Father gives you the true bread from heaven .
43006033	For the bread of God is he who comes down from heaven and gives life to the world . ”
43006034	They said to him , “ Sir , give us this bread always . ”
43006035	Jesus said to them , “ I am the bread of life ; whoever comes to me shall not hunger , and whoever believes in me shall never thirst .
43006036	But I said to you that you have seen me and yet do not believe .
43006037	All that the Father gives me will come to me , and whoever comes to me I will never cast out .
43006038	For I have come down from heaven , not to do my own will but the will of him who sent me .
43006039	And this is the will of him who sent me , that I should lose nothing of all that he has given me , but raise it up on the last day .
43006040	For this is the will of my Father , that everyone who looks on the Son and believes in him should have eternal life , and I will raise him up on the last day . ”
43006041	So the Jews grumbled about him , because he said , “ I am the bread that came down from heaven . ”
43006042	They said , “ Is not this Jesus , the son of Joseph , whose father and mother we know ? How does he now say , ‘ I have come down from heaven ’ ? ”
43006043	Jesus answered them , “ Do not grumble among yourselves .
43006044	No one can come to me unless the Father who sent me draws him . And I will raise him up on the last day .
43006045	It is written in the Prophets , ‘ And they will all be taught by God . ’ Everyone who has heard and learned from the Father comes to me —
43006046	not that anyone has seen the Father except he who is from God ; he has seen the Father .
43006047	Truly , truly , I say to you , whoever believes has eternal life .
43006048	I am the bread of life .
43006049	Your fathers ate the manna in the wilderness , and they died .
43006050	This is the bread that comes down from heaven , so that one may eat of it and not die .
43006051	I am the living bread that came down from heaven . If anyone eats of this bread , he will live forever . And the bread that I will give for the life of the world is my flesh . ”
43006052	The Jews then disputed among themselves , saying , “ How can this man give us his flesh to eat ? ”
43006053	So Jesus said to them , “ Truly , truly , I say to you , unless you eat the flesh of the Son of Man and drink his blood , you have no life in you .
43006054	Whoever feeds on my flesh and drinks my blood has eternal life , and I will raise him up on the last day .
43006055	For my flesh is true food , and my blood is true drink .
43006056	Whoever feeds on my flesh and drinks my blood abides in me , and I in him .
43006057	As the living Father sent me , and I live because of the Father , so whoever feeds on me , he also will live because of me .
43006058	This is the bread that came down from heaven , not like the bread the fathers ate and died . Whoever feeds on this bread will live forever . ”
43006059	Jesus said these things in the synagogue , as he taught at Capernaum .
43006060	When many of his disciples heard it , they said , “ This is a hard saying ; who can listen to it ? ”
43006061	But Jesus , knowing in himself that his disciples were grumbling about this , said to them , “ Do you take offense at this ?
43006062	Then what if you were to see the Son of Man ascending to where he was before ?
43006063	It is the Spirit who gives life ; the flesh is no help at all . The words that I have spoken to you are spirit and life .
43006064	But there are some of you who do not believe . ” ( For Jesus knew from the beginning who those were who did not believe , and who it was who would betray him .
43006065	And he said , “ This is why I told you that no one can come to me unless it is granted him by the Father . ”
43006066	After this many of his disciples turned back and no longer walked with him .
43006067	So Jesus said to the Twelve , “ Do you want to go away as well ? ”
43006068	Simon Peter answered him , “ Lord , to whom shall we go ? You have the words of eternal life ,
43006069	and we have believed , and have come to know , that you are the Holy One of God . ”
43006070	Jesus answered them , “ Did I not choose you , the Twelve ? And yet one of you is a devil . ”
43006071	He spoke of Judas the son of Simon Iscariot , for he , one of the Twelve , was going to betray him .
43007001	After this Jesus went about in Galilee . He would not go about in Judea , because the Jews were seeking to kill him .
43007002	Now the Jews ’ Feast of Booths was at hand .
43007003	So his brothers said to him , “ Leave here and go to Judea , that your disciples also may see the works you are doing .
43007004	For no one works in secret if he seeks to be known openly . If you do these things , show yourself to the world . ”
43007005	For not even his brothers believed in him .
43007006	Jesus said to them , “ My time has not yet come , but your time is always here .
43007007	The world cannot hate you , but it hates me because I testify about it that its works are evil .
43007008	You go up to the feast . I am not going up to this feast , for my time has not yet fully come . ”
43007009	After saying this , he remained in Galilee .
43007010	But after his brothers had gone up to the feast , then he also went up , not publicly but in private .
43007011	The Jews were looking for him at the feast , and saying , “ Where is he ? ”
43007012	And there was much muttering about him among the people . While some said , “ He is a good man , ” others said , “ No , he is leading the people astray . ”
43007013	Yet for fear of the Jews no one spoke openly of him .
43007014	About the middle of the feast Jesus went up into the temple and began teaching .
43007015	The Jews therefore marveled , saying , “ How is it that this man has learning , when he has never studied ? ”
43007016	So Jesus answered them , “ My teaching is not mine , but his who sent me .
43007017	If anyone’s will is to do God’s will , he will know whether the teaching is from God or whether I am speaking on my own authority .
43007018	The one who speaks on his own authority seeks his own glory ; but the one who seeks the glory of him who sent him is true , and in him there is no falsehood .
43007019	Has not Moses given you the law ? Yet none of you keeps the law . Why do you seek to kill me ? ”
43007020	The crowd answered , “ You have a demon ! Who is seeking to kill you ? ”
43007021	Jesus answered them , “ I did one work , and you all marvel at it .
43007022	Moses gave you circumcision ( not that it is from Moses , but from the fathers ) , and you circumcise a man on the Sabbath .
43007023	If on the Sabbath a man receives circumcision , so that the law of Moses may not be broken , are you angry with me because on the Sabbath I made a man’s whole body well ?
43007024	Do not judge by appearances , but judge with right judgment . ”
43007025	Some of the people of Jerusalem therefore said , “ Is not this the man whom they seek to kill ?
43007026	And here he is , speaking openly , and they say nothing to him ! Can it be that the authorities really know that this is the Christ ?
43007027	But we know where this man comes from , and when the Christ appears , no one will know where he comes from . ”
43007028	So Jesus proclaimed , as he taught in the temple , “ You know me , and you know where I come from ? But I have not come of my own accord . He who sent me is true , and him you do not know .
43007029	I know him , for I come from him , and he sent me . ”
43007030	So they were seeking to arrest him , but no one laid a hand on him , because his hour had not yet come .
43007031	Yet many of the people believed in him . They said , “ When the Christ appears , will he do more signs than this man has done ? ”
43007032	The Pharisees heard the crowd muttering these things about him , and the chief priests and Pharisees sent officers to arrest him .
43007033	Jesus then said , “ I will be with you a little longer , and then I am going to him who sent me .
43007034	You will seek me and you will not find me . Where I am you cannot come . ”
43007035	The Jews said to one another , “ Where does this man intend to go that we will not find him ? Does he intend to go to the Dispersion among the Greeks and teach the Greeks ?
43007036	What does he mean by saying , ‘ You will seek me and you will not find me , ’ and , ‘ Where I am you cannot come ’ ? ”
43007037	On the last day of the feast , the great day , Jesus stood up and cried out , “ If anyone thirsts , let him come to me and drink .
43007038	Whoever believes in me , as the Scripture has said , ‘ Out of his heart will flow rivers of living water . ’ ”
43007039	Now this he said about the Spirit , whom those who believed in him were to receive , for as yet the Spirit had not been given , because Jesus was not yet glorified .
43007040	When they heard these words , some of the people said , “ This really is the Prophet . ”
43007041	Others said , “ This is the Christ . ” But some said , “ Is the Christ to come from Galilee ?
43007042	Has not the Scripture said that the Christ comes from the offspring of David , and comes from Bethlehem , the village where David was ? ”
43007043	So there was a division among the people over him .
43007044	Some of them wanted to arrest him , but no one laid hands on him .
43007045	The officers then came to the chief priests and Pharisees , who said to them , “ Why did you not bring him ? ”
43007046	The officers answered , “ No one ever spoke like this man ! ”
43007047	The Pharisees answered them , “ Have you also been deceived ?
43007048	Have any of the authorities or the Pharisees believed in him ?
43007049	But this crowd that does not know the law is accursed . ”
43007050	Nicodemus , who had gone to him before , and who was one of them , said to them ,
43007051	“ Does our law judge a man without first giving him a hearing and learning what he does ? ”
43007052	They replied , “ Are you from Galilee too ? Search and see that no prophet arises from Galilee . ”
43007053	[ [ They went each to his own house ,
43008001	but Jesus went to the Mount of Olives .
43008002	Early in the morning he came again to the temple . All the people came to him , and he sat down and taught them .
43008003	The scribes and the Pharisees brought a woman who had been caught in adultery , and placing her in the midst
43008004	they said to him , “ Teacher , this woman has been caught in the act of adultery .
43008005	Now in the Law Moses commanded us to stone such women . So what do you say ? ”
43008006	This they said to test him , that they might have some charge to bring against him . Jesus bent down and wrote with his finger on the ground .
43008007	And as they continued to ask him , he stood up and said to them , “ Let him who is without sin among you be the first to throw a stone at her . ”
43008008	And once more he bent down and wrote on the ground .
43008009	But when they heard it , they went away one by one , beginning with the older ones , and Jesus was left alone with the woman standing before him .
43008010	Jesus stood up and said to her , “ Woman , where are they ? Has no one condemned you ? ”
43008011	She said , “ No one , Lord . ” And Jesus said , “ Neither do I condemn you ; go , and from now on sin no more . ” ] ]
43008012	Again Jesus spoke to them , saying , “ I am the light of the world . Whoever follows me will not walk in darkness , but will have the light of life . ”
43008013	So the Pharisees said to him , “ You are bearing witness about yourself ; your testimony is not true . ”
43008014	Jesus answered , “ Even if I do bear witness about myself , my testimony is true , for I know where I came from and where I am going , but you do not know where I come from or where I am going .
43008015	You judge according to the flesh ; I judge no one .
43008016	Yet even if I do judge , my judgment is true , for it is not I alone who judge , but I and the Father who sent me .
43008017	In your Law it is written that the testimony of two people is true .
43008018	I am the one who bears witness about myself , and the Father who sent me bears witness about me . ”
43008019	They said to him therefore , “ Where is your Father ? ” Jesus answered , “ You know neither me nor my Father . If you knew me , you would know my Father also . ”
43008020	These words he spoke in the treasury , as he taught in the temple ; but no one arrested him , because his hour had not yet come .
43008021	So he said to them again , “ I am going away , and you will seek me , and you will die in your sin . Where I am going , you cannot come . ”
43008022	So the Jews said , “ Will he kill himself , since he says , ‘ Where I am going , you cannot come ’ ? ”
43008023	He said to them , “ You are from below ; I am from above . You are of this world ; I am not of this world .
43008024	I told you that you would die in your sins , for unless you believe that I am he you will die in your sins . ”
43008025	So they said to him , “ Who are you ? ” Jesus said to them , “ Just what I have been telling you from the beginning .
43008026	I have much to say about you and much to judge , but he who sent me is true , and I declare to the world what I have heard from him . ”
43008027	They did not understand that he had been speaking to them about the Father .
43008028	So Jesus said to them , “ When you have lifted up the Son of Man , then you will know that I am he , and that I do nothing on my own authority , but speak just as the Father taught me .
43008029	And he who sent me is with me . He has not left me alone , for I always do the things that are pleasing to him . ”
43008030	As he was saying these things , many believed in him .
43008031	So Jesus said to the Jews who had believed in him , “ If you abide in my word , you are truly my disciples ,
43008032	and you will know the truth , and the truth will set you free . ”
43008033	They answered him , “ We are offspring of Abraham and have never been enslaved to anyone . How is it that you say , ‘ You will become free ’ ? ”
43008034	Jesus answered them , “ Truly , truly , I say to you , everyone who commits sin is a slave to sin .
43008035	The slave does not remain in the house forever ; the son remains forever .
43008036	So if the Son sets you free , you will be free indeed .
43008037	I know that you are offspring of Abraham ; yet you seek to kill me because my word finds no place in you .
43008038	I speak of what I have seen with my Father , and you do what you have heard from your father . ”
43008039	They answered him , “ Abraham is our father . ” Jesus said to them , “ If you were Abraham’s children , you would be doing the works Abraham did ,
43008040	but now you seek to kill me , a man who has told you the truth that I heard from God . This is not what Abraham did .
43008041	You are doing the works your father did . ” They said to him , “ We were not born of sexual immorality . We have one Father — even God . ”
43008042	Jesus said to them , “ If God were your Father , you would love me , for I came from God and I am here . I came not of my own accord , but he sent me .
43008043	Why do you not understand what I say ? It is because you cannot bear to hear my word .
43008044	You are of your father the devil , and your will is to do your father’s desires . He was a murderer from the beginning , and has nothing to do with the truth , because there is no truth in him . When he lies , he speaks out of his own character , for he is a liar and the father of lies .
43008045	But because I tell the truth , you do not believe me .
43008046	Which one of you convicts me of sin ? If I tell the truth , why do you not believe me ?
43008047	Whoever is of God hears the words of God . The reason why you do not hear them is that you are not of God . ”
43008048	The Jews answered him , “ Are we not right in saying that you are a Samaritan and have a demon ? ”
43008049	Jesus answered , “ I do not have a demon , but I honor my Father , and you dishonor me .
43008050	Yet I do not seek my own glory ; there is One who seeks it , and he is the judge .
43008051	Truly , truly , I say to you , if anyone keeps my word , he will never see death . ”
43008052	The Jews said to him , “ Now we know that you have a demon ! Abraham died , as did the prophets , yet you say , ‘ If anyone keeps my word , he will never taste death . ’
43008053	Are you greater than our father Abraham , who died ? And the prophets died ! Who do you make yourself out to be ? ”
43008054	Jesus answered , “ If I glorify myself , my glory is nothing . It is my Father who glorifies me , of whom you say , ‘ He is our God . ’
43008055	But you have not known him . I know him . If I were to say that I do not know him , I would be a liar like you , but I do know him and I keep his word .
43008056	Your father Abraham rejoiced that he would see my day . He saw it and was glad . ”
43008057	So the Jews said to him , “ You are not yet fifty years old , and have you seen Abraham ? ”
43008058	Jesus said to them , “ Truly , truly , I say to you , before Abraham was , I am . ”
43008059	So they picked up stones to throw at him , but Jesus hid himself and went out of the temple .
43009001	As he passed by , he saw a man blind from birth .
43009002	And his disciples asked him , “ Rabbi , who sinned , this man or his parents , that he was born blind ? ”
43009003	Jesus answered , “ It was not that this man sinned , or his parents , but that the works of God might be displayed in him .
43009004	We must work the works of him who sent me while it is day ; night is coming , when no one can work .
43009005	As long as I am in the world , I am the light of the world . ”
43009006	Having said these things , he spat on the ground and made mud with the saliva . Then he anointed the man’s eyes with the mud
43009007	and said to him , “ Go , wash in the pool of Siloam ” ( which means Sent ) . So he went and washed and came back seeing .
43009008	The neighbors and those who had seen him before as a beggar were saying , “ Is this not the man who used to sit and beg ? ”
43009009	Some said , “ It is he . ” Others said , “ No , but he is like him . ” He kept saying , “ I am the man . ”
43009010	So they said to him , “ Then how were your eyes opened ? ”
43009011	He answered , “ The man called Jesus made mud and anointed my eyes and said to me , ‘ Go to Siloam and wash . ’ So I went and washed and received my sight . ”
43009012	They said to him , “ Where is he ? ” He said , “ I do not know . ”
43009013	They brought to the Pharisees the man who had formerly been blind .
43009014	Now it was a Sabbath day when Jesus made the mud and opened his eyes .
43009015	So the Pharisees again asked him how he had received his sight . And he said to them , “ He put mud on my eyes , and I washed , and I see . ”
43009016	Some of the Pharisees said , “ This man is not from God , for he does not keep the Sabbath . ” But others said , “ How can a man who is a sinner do such signs ? ” And there was a division among them .
43009017	So they said again to the blind man , “ What do you say about him , since he has opened your eyes ? ” He said , “ He is a prophet . ”
43009018	The Jews did not believe that he had been blind and had received his sight , until they called the parents of the man who had received his sight
43009019	and asked them , “ Is this your son , who you say was born blind ? How then does he now see ? ”
43009020	His parents answered , “ We know that this is our son and that he was born blind .
43009021	But how he now sees we do not know , nor do we know who opened his eyes . Ask him ; he is of age . He will speak for himself . ”
43009022	( His parents said these things because they feared the Jews , for the Jews had already agreed that if anyone should confess Jesus to be Christ , he was to be put out of the synagogue .
43009023	Therefore his parents said , “ He is of age ; ask him . ”
43009024	So for the second time they called the man who had been blind and said to him , “ Give glory to God . We know that this man is a sinner . ”
43009025	He answered , “ Whether he is a sinner I do not know . One thing I do know , that though I was blind , now I see . ”
43009026	They said to him , “ What did he do to you ? How did he open your eyes ? ”
43009027	He answered them , “ I have told you already , and you would not listen . Why do you want to hear it again ? Do you also want to become his disciples ? ”
43009028	And they reviled him , saying , “ You are his disciple , but we are disciples of Moses .
43009029	We know that God has spoken to Moses , but as for this man , we do not know where he comes from . ”
43009030	The man answered , “ Why , this is an amazing thing ! You do not know where he comes from , and yet he opened my eyes .
43009031	We know that God does not listen to sinners , but if anyone is a worshiper of God and does his will , God listens to him .
43009032	Never since the world began has it been heard that anyone opened the eyes of a man born blind .
43009033	If this man were not from God , he could do nothing . ”
43009034	They answered him , “ You were born in utter sin , and would you teach us ? ” And they cast him out .
43009035	Jesus heard that they had cast him out , and having found him he said , “ Do you believe in the Son of Man ? ”
43009036	He answered , “ And who is he , sir , that I may believe in him ? ”
43009037	Jesus said to him , “ You have seen him , and it is he who is speaking to you . ”
43009038	He said , “ Lord , I believe , ” and he worshiped him .
43009039	Jesus said , “ For judgment I came into this world , that those who do not see may see , and those who see may become blind . ”
43009040	Some of the Pharisees near him heard these things , and said to him , “ Are we also blind ? ”
43009041	Jesus said to them , “ If you were blind , you would have no guilt ; but now that you say , ‘ We see , ’ your guilt remains .
43010001	“ Truly , truly , I say to you , he who does not enter the sheepfold by the door but climbs in by another way , that man is a thief and a robber .
43010002	But he who enters by the door is the shepherd of the sheep .
43010003	To him the gatekeeper opens . The sheep hear his voice , and he calls his own sheep by name and leads them out .
43010004	When he has brought out all his own , he goes before them , and the sheep follow him , for they know his voice .
43010005	A stranger they will not follow , but they will flee from him , for they do not know the voice of strangers . ”
43010006	This figure of speech Jesus used with them , but they did not understand what he was saying to them .
43010007	So Jesus again said to them , “ Truly , truly , I say to you , I am the door of the sheep .
43010008	All who came before me are thieves and robbers , but the sheep did not listen to them .
43010009	I am the door . If anyone enters by me , he will be saved and will go in and out and find pasture .
43010010	The thief comes only to steal and kill and destroy . I came that they may have life and have it abundantly .
43010011	I am the good shepherd . The good shepherd lays down his life for the sheep .
43010012	He who is a hired hand and not a shepherd , who does not own the sheep , sees the wolf coming and leaves the sheep and flees , and the wolf snatches them and scatters them .
43010013	He flees because he is a hired hand and cares nothing for the sheep .
43010014	I am the good shepherd . I know my own and my own know me ,
43010015	just as the Father knows me and I know the Father ; and I lay down my life for the sheep .
43010016	And I have other sheep that are not of this fold . I must bring them also , and they will listen to my voice . So there will be one flock , one shepherd .
43010017	For this reason the Father loves me , because I lay down my life that I may take it up again .
43010018	No one takes it from me , but I lay it down of my own accord . I have authority to lay it down , and I have authority to take it up again . This charge I have received from my Father . ”
43010019	There was again a division among the Jews because of these words .
43010020	Many of them said , “ He has a demon , and is insane ; why listen to him ? ”
43010021	Others said , “ These are not the words of one who is oppressed by a demon . Can a demon open the eyes of the blind ? ”

43010023	and Jesus was walking in the temple , in the colonnade of Solomon .

43010035	If he called them gods to whom the word of God came — and Scripture cannot be broken —

43010037	If I am not doing the works of my Father , then do not believe me ;
43010038	but if I do them , even though you do not believe me , believe the works , that you may know and understand that the Father is in me and I am in the Father . ”
43010039	Again they sought to arrest him , but he escaped from their hands .
43010040	He went away again across the Jordan to the place where John had been baptizing at first , and there he remained .
43010041	And many came to him . And they said , “ John did no sign , but everything that John said about this man was true . ”
43010042	And many believed in him there .
43011001	Now a certain man was ill , Lazarus of Bethany , the village of Mary and her sister Martha .
43011002	It was Mary who anointed the Lord with ointment and wiped his feet with her hair , whose brother Lazarus was ill .
43011003	So the sisters sent to him , saying , “ Lord , he whom you love is ill . ”
43011004	But when Jesus heard it he said , “ This illness does not lead to death . It is for the glory of God , so that the Son of God may be glorified through it . ”
43011005	Now Jesus loved Martha and her sister and Lazarus .
43011006	So , when he heard that Lazarus was ill , he stayed two days longer in the place where he was .
43011007	Then after this he said to the disciples , “ Let us go to Judea again . ”
43011008	The disciples said to him , “ Rabbi , the Jews were just now seeking to stone you , and are you going there again ? ”
43011009	Jesus answered , “ Are there not twelve hours in the day ? If anyone walks in the day , he does not stumble , because he sees the light of this world .
43011010	But if anyone walks in the night , he stumbles , because the light is not in him . ”
43011011	After saying these things , he said to them , “ Our friend Lazarus has fallen asleep , but I go to awaken him . ”
43011012	The disciples said to him , “ Lord , if he has fallen asleep , he will recover . ”
43011013	Now Jesus had spoken of his death , but they thought that he meant taking rest in sleep .
43011014	Then Jesus told them plainly , “ Lazarus has died ,
43011015	and for your sake I am glad that I was not there , so that you may believe . But let us go to him . ”
43011016	So Thomas , called the Twin , said to his fellow disciples , “ Let us also go , that we may die with him . ”
43011017	Now when Jesus came , he found that Lazarus had already been in the tomb four days .
43011018	Bethany was near Jerusalem , about two miles off ,
43011019	and many of the Jews had come to Martha and Mary to console them concerning their brother .
43011020	So when Martha heard that Jesus was coming , she went and met him , but Mary remained seated in the house .
43011021	Martha said to Jesus , “ Lord , if you had been here , my brother would not have died .
43011022	But even now I know that whatever you ask from God , God will give you . ”
43011023	Jesus said to her , “ Your brother will rise again . ”
43011024	Martha said to him , “ I know that he will rise again in the resurrection on the last day . ”
43011025	Jesus said to her , “ I am the resurrection and the life . Whoever believes in me , though he die , yet shall he live ,
43011026	and everyone who lives and believes in me shall never die . Do you believe this ? ”
43011027	She said to him , “ Yes , Lord ; I believe that you are the Christ , the Son of God , who is coming into the world . ”
43011028	When she had said this , she went and called her sister Mary , saying in private , “ The Teacher is here and is calling for you . ”
43011029	And when she heard it , she rose quickly and went to him .
43011030	Now Jesus had not yet come into the village , but was still in the place where Martha had met him .
43011031	When the Jews who were with her in the house , consoling her , saw Mary rise quickly and go out , they followed her , supposing that she was going to the tomb to weep there .
43011032	Now when Mary came to where Jesus was and saw him , she fell at his feet , saying to him , “ Lord , if you had been here , my brother would not have died . ”
43011033	When Jesus saw her weeping , and the Jews who had come with her also weeping , he was deeply moved in his spirit and greatly troubled .
43011034	And he said , “ Where have you laid him ? ” They said to him , “ Lord , come and see . ”
43011035	Jesus wept .
43011036	So the Jews said , “ See how he loved him ! ”
43011037	But some of them said , “ Could not he who opened the eyes of the blind man also have kept this man from dying ? ”
43011038	Then Jesus , deeply moved again , came to the tomb . It was a cave , and a stone lay against it .
43011039	Jesus said , “ Take away the stone . ” Martha , the sister of the dead man , said to him , “ Lord , by this time there will be an odor , for he has been dead four days . ”
43011040	Jesus said to her , “ Did I not tell you that if you believed you would see the glory of God ? ”

43011043	When he had said these things , he cried out with a loud voice , “ Lazarus , come out . ”

43011045	Many of the Jews therefore , who had come with Mary and had seen what he did , believed in him ,

43011048	If we let him go on like this , everyone will believe in him , and the Romans will come and take away both our place and our nation . ”
43011049	But one of them , Caiaphas , who was high priest that year , said to them , “ You know nothing at all .
43011050	Nor do you understand that it is better for you that one man should die for the people , not that the whole nation should perish . ”
43011051	He did not say this of his own accord , but being high priest that year he prophesied that Jesus would die for the nation ,
43011052	and not for the nation only , but also to gather into one the children of God who are scattered abroad .
43011053	So from that day on they made plans to put him to death .
43011054	Jesus therefore no longer walked openly among the Jews , but went from there to the region near the wilderness , to a town called Ephraim , and there he stayed with the disciples .
43011055	Now the Passover of the Jews was at hand , and many went up from the country to Jerusalem before the Passover to purify themselves .
43011056	They were looking for Jesus and saying to one another as they stood in the temple , “ What do you think ? That he will not come to the feast at all ? ”
43011057	Now the chief priests and the Pharisees had given orders that if anyone knew where he was , he should let them know , so that they might arrest him .
43012001	Six days before the Passover , Jesus therefore came to Bethany , where Lazarus was , whom Jesus had raised from the dead .
43012002	So they gave a dinner for him there . Martha served , and Lazarus was one of those reclining with him at table .
43012003	Mary therefore took a pound of expensive ointment made from pure nard , and anointed the feet of Jesus and wiped his feet with her hair . The house was filled with the fragrance of the perfume .
43012004	But Judas Iscariot , one of his disciples ( he who was about to betray him ) , said ,
43012005	“ Why was this ointment not sold for three hundred denarii and given to the poor ? ”
43012006	He said this , not because he cared about the poor , but because he was a thief , and having charge of the moneybag he used to help himself to what was put into it .
43012007	Jesus said , “ Leave her alone , so that she may keep it for the day of my burial .
43012008	For the poor you always have with you , but you do not always have me . ”
43012009	When the large crowd of the Jews learned that Jesus was there , they came , not only on account of him but also to see Lazarus , whom he had raised from the dead .
43012010	So the chief priests made plans to put Lazarus to death as well ,
43012011	because on account of him many of the Jews were going away and believing in Jesus .
43012012	The next day the large crowd that had come to the feast heard that Jesus was coming to Jerusalem .
43012013	So they took branches of palm trees and went out to meet him , crying out , “ Hosanna ! Blessed is he who comes in the name of the Lord , even the King of Israel ! ”
43012014	And Jesus found a young donkey and sat on it , just as it is written ,
43012015	“ Fear not , daughter of Zion ; behold , your king is coming , sitting on a donkey’s colt ! ”
43012016	His disciples did not understand these things at first , but when Jesus was glorified , then they remembered that these things had been written about him and had been done to him .
43012017	The crowd that had been with him when he called Lazarus out of the tomb and raised him from the dead continued to bear witness .
43012018	The reason why the crowd went to meet him was that they heard he had done this sign .
43012019	So the Pharisees said to one another , “ You see that you are gaining nothing . Look , the world has gone after him . ”
43012020	Now among those who went up to worship at the feast were some Greeks .
43012021	So these came to Philip , who was from Bethsaida in Galilee , and asked him , “ Sir , we wish to see Jesus . ”
43012022	Philip went and told Andrew ; Andrew and Philip went and told Jesus .
43012023	And Jesus answered them , “ The hour has come for the Son of Man to be glorified .
43012024	Truly , truly , I say to you , unless a grain of wheat falls into the earth and dies , it remains alone ; but if it dies , it bears much fruit .
43012025	Whoever loves his life loses it , and whoever hates his life in this world will keep it for eternal life .
43012026	If anyone serves me , he must follow me ; and where I am , there will my servant be also . If anyone serves me , the Father will honor him .
43012027	“ Now is my soul troubled . And what shall I say ? ‘ Father , save me from this hour ’ ? But for this purpose I have come to this hour .
43012028	Father , glorify your name . ” Then a voice came from heaven : “ I have glorified it , and I will glorify it again . ”
43012029	The crowd that stood there and heard it said that it had thundered . Others said , “ An angel has spoken to him . ”
43012030	Jesus answered , “ This voice has come for your sake , not mine .
43012031	Now is the judgment of this world ; now will the ruler of this world be cast out .
43012032	And I , when I am lifted up from the earth , will draw all people to myself . ”
43012033	He said this to show by what kind of death he was going to die .
43012034	So the crowd answered him , “ We have heard from the Law that the Christ remains forever . How can you say that the Son of Man must be lifted up ? Who is this Son of Man ? ”
43012035	So Jesus said to them , “ The light is among you for a little while longer . Walk while you have the light , lest darkness overtake you . The one who walks in the darkness does not know where he is going .
43012036	While you have the light , believe in the light , that you may become sons of light . ” When Jesus had said these things , he departed and hid himself from them .
43012037	Though he had done so many signs before them , they still did not believe in him ,
43012038	so that the word spoken by the prophet Isaiah might be fulfilled : “ Lord , who has believed what he heard from us , and to whom has the arm of the Lord been revealed ? ”
43012039	Therefore they could not believe . For again Isaiah said ,
43012040	“ He has blinded their eyes and hardened their heart , lest they see with their eyes , and understand with their heart , and turn , and I would heal them . ”
43012041	Isaiah said these things because he saw his glory and spoke of him .
43012042	Nevertheless , many even of the authorities believed in him , but for fear of the Pharisees they did not confess it , so that they would not be put out of the synagogue ;
43012043	for they loved the glory that comes from man more than the glory that comes from God .
43012044	And Jesus cried out and said , “ Whoever believes in me , believes not in me but in him who sent me .
43012045	And whoever sees me sees him who sent me .
43012046	I have come into the world as light , so that whoever believes in me may not remain in darkness .
43012047	If anyone hears my words and does not keep them , I do not judge him ; for I did not come to judge the world but to save the world .
43012048	The one who rejects me and does not receive my words has a judge ; the word that I have spoken will judge him on the last day .
43012049	For I have not spoken on my own authority , but the Father who sent me has himself given me a commandment — what to say and what to speak .
43012050	And I know that his commandment is eternal life . What I say , therefore , I say as the Father has told me . ”
43013001	Now before the Feast of the Passover , when Jesus knew that his hour had come to depart out of this world to the Father , having loved his own who were in the world , he loved them to the end .
43013002	During supper , when the devil had already put it into the heart of Judas Iscariot , Simon’s son , to betray him ,
43013003	Jesus , knowing that the Father had given all things into his hands , and that he had come from God and was going back to God ,
43013004	rose from supper . He laid aside his outer garments , and taking a towel , tied it around his waist .
43013005	Then he poured water into a basin and began to wash the disciples ’ feet and to wipe them with the towel that was wrapped around him .
43013006	He came to Simon Peter , who said to him , “ Lord , do you wash my feet ? ”
43013007	Jesus answered him , “ What I am doing you do not understand now , but afterward you will understand . ”
43013008	Peter said to him , “ You shall never wash my feet . ” Jesus answered him , “ If I do not wash you , you have no share with me . ”
43013009	Simon Peter said to him , “ Lord , not my feet only but also my hands and my head ! ”
43013010	Jesus said to him , “ The one who has bathed does not need to wash , except for his feet , but is completely clean . And you are clean , but not every one of you . ”
43013011	For he knew who was to betray him ; that was why he said , “ Not all of you are clean . ”
43013012	When he had washed their feet and put on his outer garments and resumed his place , he said to them , “ Do you understand what I have done to you ?
43013013	You call me Teacher and Lord , and you are right , for so I am .
43013014	If I then , your Lord and Teacher , have washed your feet , you also ought to wash one another’s feet .
43013015	For I have given you an example , that you also should do just as I have done to you .
43013016	Truly , truly , I say to you , a servant is not greater than his master , nor is a messenger greater than the one who sent him .
43013017	If you know these things , blessed are you if you do them .
43013018	I am not speaking of all of you ; I know whom I have chosen . But the Scripture will be fulfilled , ‘ He who ate my bread has lifted his heel against me . ’
43013019	I am telling you this now , before it takes place , that when it does take place you may believe that I am he .
43013020	Truly , truly , I say to you , whoever receives the one I send receives me , and whoever receives me receives the one who sent me . ”
43013021	After saying these things , Jesus was troubled in his spirit , and testified , “ Truly , truly , I say to you , one of you will betray me . ”
43013022	The disciples looked at one another , uncertain of whom he spoke .
43013023	One of his disciples , whom Jesus loved , was reclining at table close to Jesus ,
43013024	so Simon Peter motioned to him to ask Jesus of whom he was speaking .
43013025	So that disciple , leaning back against Jesus , said to him , “ Lord , who is it ? ”
43013026	Jesus answered , “ It is he to whom I will give this morsel of bread when I have dipped it . ” So when he had dipped the morsel , he gave it to Judas , the son of Simon Iscariot .
43013027	Then after he had taken the morsel , Satan entered into him . Jesus said to him , “ What you are going to do , do quickly . ”
43013028	Now no one at the table knew why he said this to him .
43013029	Some thought that , because Judas had the moneybag , Jesus was telling him , “ Buy what we need for the feast , ” or that he should give something to the poor .
43013030	So , after receiving the morsel of bread , he immediately went out . And it was night .
43013031	When he had gone out , Jesus said , “ Now is the Son of Man glorified , and God is glorified in him .
43013032	If God is glorified in him , God will also glorify him in himself , and glorify him at once .
43013033	Little children , yet a little while I am with you . You will seek me , and just as I said to the Jews , so now I also say to you , ‘ Where I am going you cannot come . ’
43013034	A new commandment I give to you , that you love one another : just as I have loved you , you also are to love one another .
43013035	By this all people will know that you are my disciples , if you have love for one another . ”
43013036	Simon Peter said to him , “ Lord , where are you going ? ” Jesus answered him , “ Where I am going you cannot follow me now , but you will follow afterward . ”
43013037	Peter said to him , “ Lord , why can I not follow you now ? I will lay down my life for you . ”
43013038	Jesus answered , “ Will you lay down your life for me ? Truly , truly , I say to you , the rooster will not crow till you have denied me three times .
43014001	“ Let not your hearts be troubled . Believe in God ; believe also in me .
43014002	In my Father’s house are many rooms . If it were not so , would I have told you that I go to prepare a place for you ?
43014003	And if I go and prepare a place for you , I will come again and will take you to myself , that where I am you may be also .
43014004	And you know the way to where I am going . ”
43014005	Thomas said to him , “ Lord , we do not know where you are going . How can we know the way ? ”
43014006	Jesus said to him , “ I am the way , and the truth , and the life . No one comes to the Father except through me .
43014007	If you had known me , you would have known my Father also . From now on you do know him and have seen him . ”
43014008	Philip said to him , “ Lord , show us the Father , and it is enough for us . ”
43014009	Jesus said to him , “ Have I been with you so long , and you still do not know me , Philip ? Whoever has seen me has seen the Father . How can you say , ‘ Show us the Father ’ ?
43014010	Do you not believe that I am in the Father and the Father is in me ? The words that I say to you I do not speak on my own authority , but the Father who dwells in me does his works .
43014011	Believe me that I am in the Father and the Father is in me , or else believe on account of the works themselves .
43014012	“ Truly , truly , I say to you , whoever believes in me will also do the works that I do ; and greater works than these will he do , because I am going to the Father .
43014013	Whatever you ask in my name , this I will do , that the Father may be glorified in the Son .
43014014	If you ask me anything in my name , I will do it .
43014015	“ If you love me , you will keep my commandments .
43014016	And I will ask the Father , and he will give you another Helper , to be with you forever ,
43014017	even the Spirit of truth , whom the world cannot receive , because it neither sees him nor knows him . You know him , for he dwells with you and will be in you .
43014018	“ I will not leave you as orphans ; I will come to you .
43014019	Yet a little while and the world will see me no more , but you will see me . Because I live , you also will live .
43014020	In that day you will know that I am in my Father , and you in me , and I in you .
43014021	Whoever has my commandments and keeps them , he it is who loves me . And he who loves me will be loved by my Father , and I will love him and manifest myself to him . ”
43014022	Judas ( not Iscariot
43014023	Jesus answered him , “ If anyone loves me , he will keep my word , and my Father will love him , and we will come to him and make our home with him .
43014024	Whoever does not love me does not keep my words . And the word that you hear is not mine but the Father’s who sent me .
43014025	“ These things I have spoken to you while I am still with you .
43014026	But the Helper , the Holy Spirit , whom the Father will send in my name , he will teach you all things and bring to your remembrance all that I have said to you .
43014027	Peace I leave with you ; my peace I give to you . Not as the world gives do I give to you . Let not your hearts be troubled , neither let them be afraid .
43014028	You heard me say to you , ‘ I am going away , and I will come to you . ’ If you loved me , you would have rejoiced , because I am going to the Father , for the Father is greater than I .
43014029	And now I have told you before it takes place , so that when it does take place you may believe .
43014030	I will no longer talk much with you , for the ruler of this world is coming . He has no claim on me ,
43014031	but I do as the Father has commanded me , so that the world may know that I love the Father . Rise , let us go from here .
43015001	“ I am the true vine , and my Father is the vinedresser .
43015002	Every branch in me that does not bear fruit he takes away , and every branch that does bear fruit he prunes , that it may bear more fruit .
43015003	Already you are clean because of the word that I have spoken to you .
43015004	Abide in me , and I in you . As the branch cannot bear fruit by itself , unless it abides in the vine , neither can you , unless you abide in me .
43015005	I am the vine ; you are the branches . Whoever abides in me and I in him , he it is that bears much fruit , for apart from me you can do nothing .
43015006	If anyone does not abide in me he is thrown away like a branch and withers ; and the branches are gathered , thrown into the fire , and burned .
43015007	If you abide in me , and my words abide in you , ask whatever you wish , and it will be done for you .
43015008	By this my Father is glorified , that you bear much fruit and so prove to be my disciples .
43015009	As the Father has loved me , so have I loved you . Abide in my love .
43015010	If you keep my commandments , you will abide in my love , just as I have kept my Father’s commandments and abide in his love .
43015011	These things I have spoken to you , that my joy may be in you , and that your joy may be full .
43015012	“ This is my commandment , that you love one another as I have loved you .
43015013	Greater love has no one than this , that someone lay down his life for his friends .
43015014	You are my friends if you do what I command you .
43015015	No longer do I call you servants , for the servant does not know what his master is doing ; but I have called you friends , for all that I have heard from my Father I have made known to you .
43015016	You did not choose me , but I chose you and appointed you that you should go and bear fruit and that your fruit should abide , so that whatever you ask the Father in my name , he may give it to you .
43015017	These things I command you , so that you will love one another .
43015018	“ If the world hates you , know that it has hated me before it hated you .
43015019	If you were of the world , the world would love you as its own ; but because you are not of the world , but I chose you out of the world , therefore the world hates you .
43015020	Remember the word that I said to you : ‘ A servant is not greater than his master . ’ If they persecuted me , they will also persecute you . If they kept my word , they will also keep yours .
43015021	But all these things they will do to you on account of my name , because they do not know him who sent me .
43015022	If I had not come and spoken to them , they would not have been guilty of sin , but now they have no excuse for their sin .
43015023	Whoever hates me hates my Father also .
43015024	If I had not done among them the works that no one else did , they would not be guilty of sin , but now they have seen and hated both me and my Father .
43015025	But the word that is written in their Law must be fulfilled : ‘ They hated me without a cause . ’
43015026	“ But when the Helper comes , whom I will send to you from the Father , the Spirit of truth , who proceeds from the Father , he will bear witness about me .
43015027	And you also will bear witness , because you have been with me from the beginning .
43016001	“ I have said all these things to you to keep you from falling away .
43016002	They will put you out of the synagogues . Indeed , the hour is coming when whoever kills you will think he is offering service to God .
43016003	And they will do these things because they have not known the Father , nor me .
43016004	But I have said these things to you , that when their hour comes you may remember that I told them to you . “ I did not say these things to you from the beginning , because I was with you .
43016005	But now I am going to him who sent me , and none of you asks me , ‘ Where are you going ? ’
43016006	But because I have said these things to you , sorrow has filled your heart .
43016007	Nevertheless , I tell you the truth : it is to your advantage that I go away , for if I do not go away , the Helper will not come to you . But if I go , I will send him to you .
43016008	And when he comes , he will convict the world concerning sin and righteousness and judgment :
43016009	concerning sin , because they do not believe in me ;
43016010	concerning righteousness , because I go to the Father , and you will see me no longer ;
43016011	concerning judgment , because the ruler of this world is judged .
43016012	“ I still have many things to say to you , but you cannot bear them now .
43016013	When the Spirit of truth comes , he will guide you into all the truth , for he will not speak on his own authority , but whatever he hears he will speak , and he will declare to you the things that are to come .
43016014	He will glorify me , for he will take what is mine and declare it to you .
43016015	All that the Father has is mine ; therefore I said that he will take what is mine and declare it to you .
43016016	“ A little while , and you will see me no longer ; and again a little while , and you will see me . ”
43016017	So some of his disciples said to one another , “ What is this that he says to us , ‘ A little while , and you will not see me , and again a little while , and you will see me ’ ; and , ‘ because I am going to the Father ’ ? ”
43016018	So they were saying , “ What does he mean by ‘ a little while ’ ? We do not know what he is talking about . ”
43016019	Jesus knew that they wanted to ask him , so he said to them , “ Is this what you are asking yourselves , what I meant by saying , ‘ A little while and you will not see me , and again a little while and you will see me ’ ?
43016020	Truly , truly , I say to you , you will weep and lament , but the world will rejoice . You will be sorrowful , but your sorrow will turn into joy .
43016021	When a woman is giving birth , she has sorrow because her hour has come , but when she has delivered the baby , she no longer remembers the anguish , for joy that a human being has been born into the world .
