43016022	So also you have sorrow now , but I will see you again , and your hearts will rejoice , and no one will take your joy from you .
43016023	In that day you will ask nothing of me . Truly , truly , I say to you , whatever you ask of the Father in my name , he will give it to you .
43016024	Until now you have asked nothing in my name . Ask , and you will receive , that your joy may be full .
43016025	“ I have said these things to you in figures of speech . The hour is coming when I will no longer speak to you in figures of speech but will tell you plainly about the Father .
43016026	In that day you will ask in my name , and I do not say to you that I will ask the Father on your behalf ;
43016027	for the Father himself loves you , because you have loved me and have believed that I came from God .
43016028	I came from the Father and have come into the world , and now I am leaving the world and going to the Father . ”
43016029	His disciples said , “ Ah , now you are speaking plainly and not using figurative speech !
43016030	Now we know that you know all things and do not need anyone to question you ; this is why we believe that you came from God . ”
43016031	Jesus answered them , “ Do you now believe ?
43016032	Behold , the hour is coming , indeed it has come , when you will be scattered , each to his own home , and will leave me alone . Yet I am not alone , for the Father is with me .
43016033	I have said these things to you , that in me you may have peace . In the world you will have tribulation . But take heart ; I have overcome the world . ”
43017001	When Jesus had spoken these words , he lifted up his eyes to heaven , and said , “ Father , the hour has come ; glorify your Son that the Son may glorify you ,
43017002	since you have given him authority over all flesh , to give eternal life to all whom you have given him .
43017003	And this is eternal life , that they know you the only true God , and Jesus Christ whom you have sent .
43017004	I glorified you on earth , having accomplished the work that you gave me to do .
43017005	And now , Father , glorify me in your own presence with the glory that I had with you before the world existed .
43017006	“ I have manifested your name to the people whom you gave me out of the world . Yours they were , and you gave them to me , and they have kept your word .
43017007	Now they know that everything that you have given me is from you .
43017008	For I have given them the words that you gave me , and they have received them and have come to know in truth that I came from you ; and they have believed that you sent me .
43017009	I am praying for them . I am not praying for the world but for those whom you have given me , for they are yours .
43017010	All mine are yours , and yours are mine , and I am glorified in them .
43017011	And I am no longer in the world , but they are in the world , and I am coming to you . Holy Father , keep them in your name , which you have given me , that they may be one , even as we are one .
43017012	While I was with them , I kept them in your name , which you have given me . I have guarded them , and not one of them has been lost except the son of destruction , that the Scripture might be fulfilled .
43017013	But now I am coming to you , and these things I speak in the world , that they may have my joy fulfilled in themselves .
43017014	I have given them your word , and the world has hated them because they are not of the world , just as I am not of the world .
43017015	I do not ask that you take them out of the world , but that you keep them from the evil one .
43017016	They are not of the world , just as I am not of the world .
43017017	Sanctify them in the truth ; your word is truth .
43017018	As you sent me into the world , so I have sent them into the world .
43017019	And for their sake I consecrate myself , that they also may be sanctified in truth .
43017020	“ I do not ask for these only , but also for those who will believe in me through their word ,
43017021	that they may all be one , just as you , Father , are in me , and I in you , that they also may be in us , so that the world may believe that you have sent me .
43017022	The glory that you have given me I have given to them , that they may be one even as we are one ,
43017023	I in them and you in me , that they may become perfectly one , so that the world may know that you sent me and loved them even as you loved me .
43017024	Father , I desire that they also , whom you have given me , may be with me where I am , to see my glory that you have given me because you loved me before the foundation of the world .
43017025	O righteous Father , even though the world does not know you , I know you , and these know that you have sent me .
43017026	I made known to them your name , and I will continue to make it known , that the love with which you have loved me may be in them , and I in them . ”
43018001	When Jesus had spoken these words , he went out with his disciples across the Kidron Valley , where there was a garden , which he and his disciples entered .
43018002	Now Judas , who betrayed him , also knew the place , for Jesus often met there with his disciples .
43018003	So Judas , having procured a band of soldiers and some officers from the chief priests and the Pharisees , went there with lanterns and torches and weapons .
43018004	Then Jesus , knowing all that would happen to him , came forward and said to them , “ Whom do you seek ? ”
43018005	They answered him , “ Jesus of Nazareth . ” Jesus said to them , “ I am he . ” Judas , who betrayed him , was standing with them .
43018006	When Jesus said to them , “ I am he , ” they drew back and fell to the ground .
43018007	So he asked them again , “ Whom do you seek ? ” And they said , “ Jesus of Nazareth . ”
43018008	Jesus answered , “ I told you that I am he . So , if you seek me , let these men go . ”
43018009	This was to fulfill the word that he had spoken : “ Of those whom you gave me I have lost not one . ”
43018010	Then Simon Peter , having a sword , drew it and struck the high priest’s servant and cut off his right ear . ( The servant’s name was Malchus .
43018011	So Jesus said to Peter , “ Put your sword into its sheath ; shall I not drink the cup that the Father has given me ? ”
43018012	So the band of soldiers and their captain and the officers of the Jews arrested Jesus and bound him .
43018013	First they led him to Annas , for he was the father-in-law of Caiaphas , who was high priest that year .
43018014	It was Caiaphas who had advised the Jews that it would be expedient that one man should die for the people .
43018015	Simon Peter followed Jesus , and so did another disciple . Since that disciple was known to the high priest , he entered with Jesus into the court of the high priest ,
43018016	but Peter stood outside at the door . So the other disciple , who was known to the high priest , went out and spoke to the servant girl who kept watch at the door , and brought Peter in .
43018017	The servant girl at the door said to Peter , “ You also are not one of this man’s disciples , are you ? ” He said , “ I am not . ”
43018018	Now the servants and officers had made a charcoal fire , because it was cold , and they were standing and warming themselves . Peter also was with them , standing and warming himself .
43018019	The high priest then questioned Jesus about his disciples and his teaching .
43018020	Jesus answered him , “ I have spoken openly to the world . I have always taught in synagogues and in the temple , where all Jews come together . I have said nothing in secret .
43018021	Why do you ask me ? Ask those who have heard me what I said to them ; they know what I said . ”
43018022	When he had said these things , one of the officers standing by struck Jesus with his hand , saying , “ Is that how you answer the high priest ? ”
43018023	Jesus answered him , “ If what I said is wrong , bear witness about the wrong ; but if what I said is right , why do you strike me ? ”
43018024	Annas then sent him bound to Caiaphas the high priest .
43018025	Now Simon Peter was standing and warming himself . So they said to him , “ You also are not one of his disciples , are you ? ” He denied it and said , “ I am not . ”
43018026	One of the servants of the high priest , a relative of the man whose ear Peter had cut off , asked , “ Did I not see you in the garden with him ? ”
43018027	Peter again denied it , and at once a rooster crowed .
43018028	Then they led Jesus from the house of Caiaphas to the governor’s headquarters . It was early morning . They themselves did not enter the governor’s headquarters , so that they would not be defiled , but could eat the Passover .
43018029	So Pilate went outside to them and said , “ What accusation do you bring against this man ? ”
43018030	They answered him , “ If this man were not doing evil , we would not have delivered him over to you . ”
43018031	Pilate said to them , “ Take him yourselves and judge him by your own law . ” The Jews said to him , “ It is not lawful for us to put anyone to death . ”
43018032	This was to fulfill the word that Jesus had spoken to show by what kind of death he was going to die .
43018033	So Pilate entered his headquarters again and called Jesus and said to him , “ Are you the King of the Jews ? ”
43018034	Jesus answered , “ Do you say this of your own accord , or did others say it to you about me ? ”
43018035	Pilate answered , “ Am I a Jew ? Your own nation and the chief priests have delivered you over to me . What have you done ? ”
43018036	Jesus answered , “ My kingdom is not of this world . If my kingdom were of this world , my servants would have been fighting , that I might not be delivered over to the Jews . But my kingdom is not from the world . ”
43018037	Then Pilate said to him , “ So you are a king ? ” Jesus answered , “ You say that I am a king . For this purpose I was born and for this purpose I have come into the world — to bear witness to the truth . Everyone who is of the truth listens to my voice . ”
43018038	Pilate said to him , “ What is truth ? ” After he had said this , he went back outside to the Jews and told them , “ I find no guilt in him .
43018039	But you have a custom that I should release one man for you at the Passover . So do you want me to release to you the King of the Jews ? ”
43018040	They cried out again , “ Not this man , but Barabbas ! ” Now Barabbas was a robber .
43019001	Then Pilate took Jesus and flogged him .
43019002	And the soldiers twisted together a crown of thorns and put it on his head and arrayed him in a purple robe .
43019003	They came up to him , saying , “ Hail , King of the Jews ! ” and struck him with their hands .
43019004	Pilate went out again and said to them , “ See , I am bringing him out to you that you may know that I find no guilt in him . ”
43019005	So Jesus came out , wearing the crown of thorns and the purple robe . Pilate said to them , “ Behold the man ! ”
43019006	When the chief priests and the officers saw him , they cried out , “ Crucify him , crucify him ! ” Pilate said to them , “ Take him yourselves and crucify him , for I find no guilt in him . ”
43019007	The Jews answered him , “ We have a law , and according to that law he ought to die because he has made himself the Son of God . ”
43019008	When Pilate heard this statement , he was even more afraid .
43019009	He entered his headquarters again and said to Jesus , “ Where are you from ? ” But Jesus gave him no answer .
43019010	So Pilate said to him , “ You will not speak to me ? Do you not know that I have authority to release you and authority to crucify you ? ”
43019011	Jesus answered him , “ You would have no authority over me at all unless it had been given you from above . Therefore he who delivered me over to you has the greater sin . ”
43019012	From then on Pilate sought to release him , but the Jews cried out , “ If you release this man , you are not Caesar’s friend . Everyone who makes himself a king opposes Caesar . ”
43019013	So when Pilate heard these words , he brought Jesus out and sat down on the judgment seat at a place called The Stone Pavement , and in Aramaic Gabbatha .
43019014	Now it was the day of Preparation of the Passover . It was about the sixth hour . He said to the Jews , “ Behold your King ! ”
43019015	They cried out , “ Away with him , away with him , crucify him ! ” Pilate said to them , “ Shall I crucify your King ? ” The chief priests answered , “ We have no king but Caesar . ”
43019016	So he delivered him over to them to be crucified . So they took Jesus ,
43019017	and he went out , bearing his own cross , to the place called The Place of a Skull , which in Aramaic is called Golgotha .
43019018	There they crucified him , and with him two others , one on either side , and Jesus between them .
43019019	Pilate also wrote an inscription and put it on the cross . It read , “ Jesus of Nazareth , the King of the Jews . ”
43019020	Many of the Jews read this inscription , for the place where Jesus was crucified was near the city , and it was written in Aramaic , in Latin , and in Greek .
43019021	So the chief priests of the Jews said to Pilate , “ Do not write , ‘ The King of the Jews , ’ but rather , ‘ This man said , I am King of the Jews . ’ ”
43019022	Pilate answered , “ What I have written I have written . ”
43019023	When the soldiers had crucified Jesus , they took his garments and divided them into four parts , one part for each soldier ; also his tunic . But the tunic was seamless , woven in one piece from top to bottom ,
43019024	so they said to one another , “ Let us not tear it , but cast lots for it to see whose it shall be . ” This was to fulfill the Scripture which says , “ They divided my garments among them , and for my clothing they cast lots . ” So the soldiers did these things ,
43019025	but standing by the cross of Jesus were his mother and his mother’s sister , Mary the wife of Clopas , and Mary Magdalene .
43019026	When Jesus saw his mother and the disciple whom he loved standing nearby , he said to his mother , “ Woman , behold , your son ! ”
43019027	Then he said to the disciple , “ Behold , your mother ! ” And from that hour the disciple took her to his own home .
43019028	After this , Jesus , knowing that all was now finished , said ( to fulfill the Scripture ) , “ I thirst . ”
43019029	A jar full of sour wine stood there , so they put a sponge full of the sour wine on a hyssop branch and held it to his mouth .
43019030	When Jesus had received the sour wine , he said , “ It is finished , ” and he bowed his head and gave up his spirit .
43019031	Since it was the day of Preparation , and so that the bodies would not remain on the cross on the Sabbath ( for that Sabbath was a high day ) , the Jews asked Pilate that their legs might be broken and that they might be taken away .
43019032	So the soldiers came and broke the legs of the first , and of the other who had been crucified with him .
43019033	But when they came to Jesus and saw that he was already dead , they did not break his legs .
43019034	But one of the soldiers pierced his side with a spear , and at once there came out blood and water .
43019035	He who saw it has borne witness — his testimony is true , and he knows that he is telling the truth — that you also may believe .
43019036	For these things took place that the Scripture might be fulfilled : “ Not one of his bones will be broken . ”
43019037	And again another Scripture says , “ They will look on him whom they have pierced . ”
43019038	After these things Joseph of Arimathea , who was a disciple of Jesus , but secretly for fear of the Jews , asked Pilate that he might take away the body of Jesus , and Pilate gave him permission . So he came and took away his body .
43019039	Nicodemus also , who earlier had come to Jesus by night , came bringing a mixture of myrrh and aloes , about seventy-five pounds in weight .
43019040	So they took the body of Jesus and bound it in linen cloths with the spices , as is the burial custom of the Jews .
43019041	Now in the place where he was crucified there was a garden , and in the garden a new tomb in which no one had yet been laid .
43019042	So because of the Jewish day of Preparation , since the tomb was close at hand , they laid Jesus there .
43020001	Now on the first day of the week Mary Magdalene came to the tomb early , while it was still dark , and saw that the stone had been taken away from the tomb .
43020002	So she ran and went to Simon Peter and the other disciple , the one whom Jesus loved , and said to them , “ They have taken the Lord out of the tomb , and we do not know where they have laid him . ”
43020003	So Peter went out with the other disciple , and they were going toward the tomb .
43020004	Both of them were running together , but the other disciple outran Peter and reached the tomb first .
43020005	And stooping to look in , he saw the linen cloths lying there , but he did not go in .
43020006	Then Simon Peter came , following him , and went into the tomb . He saw the linen cloths lying there ,
43020007	and the face cloth , which had been on Jesus ’ head , not lying with the linen cloths but folded up in a place by itself .
43020008	Then the other disciple , who had reached the tomb first , also went in , and he saw and believed ;
43020009	for as yet they did not understand the Scripture , that he must rise from the dead .
43020010	Then the disciples went back to their homes .
43020011	But Mary stood weeping outside the tomb , and as she wept she stooped to look into the tomb .
43020012	And she saw two angels in white , sitting where the body of Jesus had lain , one at the head and one at the feet .
43020013	They said to her , “ Woman , why are you weeping ? ” She said to them , “ They have taken away my Lord , and I do not know where they have laid him . ”
43020014	Having said this , she turned around and saw Jesus standing , but she did not know that it was Jesus .
43020015	Jesus said to her , “ Woman , why are you weeping ? Whom are you seeking ? ” Supposing him to be the gardener , she said to him , “ Sir , if you have carried him away , tell me where you have laid him , and I will take him away . ”
43020016	Jesus said to her , “ Mary . ” She turned and said to him in Aramaic , “ Rabboni ! ” ( which means Teacher ) .
43020017	Jesus said to her , “ Do not cling to me , for I have not yet ascended to the Father ; but go to my brothers and say to them , ‘ I am ascending to my Father and your Father , to my God and your God . ’ ”
43020018	Mary Magdalene went and announced to the disciples , “ I have seen the Lord ” — and that he had said these things to her .
43020019	On the evening of that day , the first day of the week , the doors being locked where the disciples were for fear of the Jews , Jesus came and stood among them and said to them , “ Peace be with you . ”
43020020	When he had said this , he showed them his hands and his side . Then the disciples were glad when they saw the Lord .
43020021	Jesus said to them again , “ Peace be with you . As the Father has sent me , even so I am sending you . ”
43020022	And when he had said this , he breathed on them and said to them , “ Receive the Holy Spirit .
43020023	If you forgive the sins of any , they are forgiven them ; if you withhold forgiveness from any , it is withheld . ”
43020024	Now Thomas , one of the Twelve , called the Twin , was not with them when Jesus came .
43020025	So the other disciples told him , “ We have seen the Lord . ” But he said to them , “ Unless I see in his hands the mark of the nails , and place my finger into the mark of the nails , and place my hand into his side , I will never believe . ”
43020026	Eight days later , his disciples were inside again , and Thomas was with them . Although the doors were locked , Jesus came and stood among them and said , “ Peace be with you . ”
43020027	Then he said to Thomas , “ Put your finger here , and see my hands ; and put out your hand , and place it in my side . Do not disbelieve , but believe . ”
43020028	Thomas answered him , “ My Lord and my God ! ”
43020029	Jesus said to him , “ Have you believed because you have seen me ? Blessed are those who have not seen and yet have believed . ”
43020030	Now Jesus did many other signs in the presence of the disciples , which are not written in this book ;
43020031	but these are written so that you may believe that Jesus is the Christ , the Son of God , and that by believing you may have life in his name .
43021001	After this Jesus revealed himself again to the disciples by the Sea of Tiberias , and he revealed himself in this way .
43021002	Simon Peter , Thomas ( called the Twin ) , Nathanael of Cana in Galilee , the sons of Zebedee , and two others of his disciples were together .
43021003	Simon Peter said to them , “ I am going fishing . ” They said to him , “ We will go with you . ” They went out and got into the boat , but that night they caught nothing .
43021004	Just as day was breaking , Jesus stood on the shore ; yet the disciples did not know that it was Jesus .
43021005	Jesus said to them , “ Children , do you have any fish ? ” They answered him , “ No . ”
43021006	He said to them , “ Cast the net on the right side of the boat , and you will find some . ” So they cast it , and now they were not able to haul it in , because of the quantity of fish .
43021007	That disciple whom Jesus loved therefore said to Peter , “ It is the Lord ! ” When Simon Peter heard that it was the Lord , he put on his outer garment , for he was stripped for work , and threw himself into the sea .
43021008	The other disciples came in the boat , dragging the net full of fish , for they were not far from the land , but about a hundred yards off .
43021009	When they got out on land , they saw a charcoal fire in place , with fish laid out on it , and bread .
43021010	Jesus said to them , “ Bring some of the fish that you have just caught . ”
43021011	So Simon Peter went aboard and hauled the net ashore , full of large fish , 153 of them . And although there were so many , the net was not torn .
43021012	Jesus said to them , “ Come and have breakfast . ” Now none of the disciples dared ask him , “ Who are you ? ” They knew it was the Lord .
43021013	Jesus came and took the bread and gave it to them , and so with the fish .
43021014	This was now the third time that Jesus was revealed to the disciples after he was raised from the dead .
43021015	When they had finished breakfast , Jesus said to Simon Peter , “ Simon , son of John , do you love me more than these ? ” He said to him , “ Yes , Lord ; you know that I love you . ” He said to him , “ Feed my lambs . ”
43021016	He said to him a second time , “ Simon , son of John , do you love me ? ” He said to him , “ Yes , Lord ; you know that I love you . ” He said to him , “ Tend my sheep . ”
43021017	He said to him the third time , “ Simon , son of John , do you love me ? ” Peter was grieved because he said to him the third time , “ Do you love me ? ” and he said to him , “ Lord , you know everything ; you know that I love you . ” Jesus said to him , “ Feed my sheep .
43021018	Truly , truly , I say to you , when you were young , you used to dress yourself and walk wherever you wanted , but when you are old , you will stretch out your hands , and another will dress you and carry you where you do not want to go . ”
43021019	( This he said to show by what kind of death he was to glorify God .
43021020	Peter turned and saw the disciple whom Jesus loved following them , the one who had been reclining at table close to him and had said , “ Lord , who is it that is going to betray you ? ”
43021021	When Peter saw him , he said to Jesus , “ Lord , what about this man ? ”
43021022	Jesus said to him , “ If it is my will that he remain until I come , what is that to you ? You follow me ! ”
43021023	So the saying spread abroad among the brothers that this disciple was not to die ; yet Jesus did not say to him that he was not to die , but , “ If it is my will that he remain until I come , what is that to you ? ”
43021024	This is the disciple who is bearing witness about these things , and who has written these things , and we know that his testimony is true .
43021025	Now there are also many other things that Jesus did . Were every one of them to be written , I suppose that the world itself could not contain the books that would be written .
44001001	In the first book , O Theophilus , I have dealt with all that Jesus began to do and teach ,
44001002	until the day when he was taken up , after he had given commands through the Holy Spirit to the apostles whom he had chosen .
44001003	He presented himself alive to them after his suffering by many proofs , appearing to them during forty days and speaking about the kingdom of God .
44001004	And while staying with them he ordered them not to depart from Jerusalem , but to wait for the promise of the Father , which , he said , “ you heard from me ;
44001005	for John baptized with water , but you will be baptized with the Holy Spirit not many days from now . ”
44001006	So when they had come together , they asked him , “ Lord , will you at this time restore the kingdom to Israel ? ”
44001007	He said to them , “ It is not for you to know times or seasons that the Father has fixed by his own authority .
44001008	But you will receive power when the Holy Spirit has come upon you , and you will be my witnesses in Jerusalem and in all Judea and Samaria , and to the end of the earth . ”
44001009	And when he had said these things , as they were looking on , he was lifted up , and a cloud took him out of their sight .
44001010	And while they were gazing into heaven as he went , behold , two men stood by them in white robes ,
44001011	and said , “ Men of Galilee , why do you stand looking into heaven ? This Jesus , who was taken up from you into heaven , will come in the same way as you saw him go into heaven . ”
44001012	Then they returned to Jerusalem from the mount called Olivet , which is near Jerusalem , a Sabbath day’s journey away .
44001013	And when they had entered , they went up to the upper room , where they were staying , Peter and John and James and Andrew , Philip and Thomas , Bartholomew and Matthew , James the son of Alphaeus and Simon the Zealot and Judas the son of James .
44001014	All these with one accord were devoting themselves to prayer , together with the women and Mary the mother of Jesus , and his brothers .
44001015	In those days Peter stood up among the brothers ( the company of persons was in all about 120
44001016	“ Brothers , the Scripture had to be fulfilled , which the Holy Spirit spoke beforehand by the mouth of David concerning Judas , who became a guide to those who arrested Jesus .
44001017	For he was numbered among us and was allotted his share in this ministry . ”
44001018	( Now this man acquired a field with the reward of his wickedness , and falling headlong he burst open in the middle and all his bowels gushed out .
44001019	And it became known to all the inhabitants of Jerusalem , so that the field was called in their own language Akeldama , that is , Field of Blood .
44001020	“ For it is written in the Book of Psalms , “ ‘ May his camp become desolate , and let there be no one to dwell in it ’ ; and “ ‘ Let another take his office . ’
44001021	So one of the men who have accompanied us during all the time that the Lord Jesus went in and out among us ,
44001022	beginning from the baptism of John until the day when he was taken up from us — one of these men must become with us a witness to his resurrection . ”
44001023	And they put forward two , Joseph called Barsabbas , who was also called Justus , and Matthias .
44001024	And they prayed and said , “ You , Lord , who know the hearts of all , show which one of these two you have chosen
44001025	to take the place in this ministry and apostleship from which Judas turned aside to go to his own place . ”
44001026	And they cast lots for them , and the lot fell on Matthias , and he was numbered with the eleven apostles .
44002001	When the day of Pentecost arrived , they were all together in one place .
44002002	And suddenly there came from heaven a sound like a mighty rushing wind , and it filled the entire house where they were sitting .
44002003	And divided tongues as of fire appeared to them and rested on each one of them .
44002004	And they were all filled with the Holy Spirit and began to speak in other tongues as the Spirit gave them utterance .
44002005	Now there were dwelling in Jerusalem Jews , devout men from every nation under heaven .
44002006	And at this sound the multitude came together , and they were bewildered , because each one was hearing them speak in his own language .
44002007	And they were amazed and astonished , saying , “ Are not all these who are speaking Galileans ?
44002008	And how is it that we hear , each of us in his own native language ?
44002009	Parthians and Medes and Elamites and residents of Mesopotamia , Judea and Cappadocia , Pontus and Asia ,
44002010	Phrygia and Pamphylia , Egypt and the parts of Libya belonging to Cyrene , and visitors from Rome ,
44002011	both Jews and proselytes , Cretans and Arabians — we hear them telling in our own tongues the mighty works of God . ”
44002012	And all were amazed and perplexed , saying to one another , “ What does this mean ? ”
44002013	But others mocking said , “ They are filled with new wine . ”
44002014	But Peter , standing with the eleven , lifted up his voice and addressed them : “ Men of Judea and all who dwell in Jerusalem , let this be known to you , and give ear to my words .
44002015	For these people are not drunk , as you suppose , since it is only the third hour of the day .
44002016	But this is what was uttered through the prophet Joel :
44002017	“ ‘ And in the last days it shall be , God declares , that I will pour out my Spirit on all flesh , and your sons and your daughters shall prophesy , and your young men shall see visions , and your old men shall dream dreams ;
44002018	even on my male servants and female servants in those days I will pour out my Spirit , and they shall prophesy .
44002019	And I will show wonders in the heavens above and signs on the earth below , blood , and fire , and vapor of smoke ;
44002020	the sun shall be turned to darkness and the moon to blood , before the day of the Lord comes , the great and magnificent day .
44002021	And it shall come to pass that everyone who calls upon the name of the Lord shall be saved . ’
44002022	“ Men of Israel , hear these words : Jesus of Nazareth , a man attested to you by God with mighty works and wonders and signs that God did through him in your midst , as you yourselves know —
44002023	this Jesus , delivered up according to the definite plan and foreknowledge of God , you crucified and killed by the hands of lawless men .
44002024	God raised him up , loosing the pangs of death , because it was not possible for him to be held by it .
44002025	For David says concerning him , “ ‘ I saw the Lord always before me , for he is at my right hand that I may not be shaken ;
44002026	therefore my heart was glad , and my tongue rejoiced ; my flesh also will dwell in hope .
44002027	For you will not abandon my soul to Hades , or let your Holy One see corruption .
44002028	You have made known to me the paths of life ; you will make me full of gladness with your presence . ’
44002029	“ Brothers , I may say to you with confidence about the patriarch David that he both died and was buried , and his tomb is with us to this day .
44002030	Being therefore a prophet , and knowing that God had sworn with an oath to him that he would set one of his descendants on his throne ,
44002031	he foresaw and spoke about the resurrection of the Christ , that he was not abandoned to Hades , nor did his flesh see corruption .
44002032	This Jesus God raised up , and of that we all are witnesses .
44002033	Being therefore exalted at the right hand of God , and having received from the Father the promise of the Holy Spirit , he has poured out this that you yourselves are seeing and hearing .
44002034	For David did not ascend into the heavens , but he himself says , “ ‘ The Lord said to my Lord , Sit at my right hand ,
44002035	until I make your enemies your footstool . ’
44002036	Let all the house of Israel therefore know for certain that God has made him both Lord and Christ , this Jesus whom you crucified . ”
44002037	Now when they heard this they were cut to the heart , and said to Peter and the rest of the apostles , “ Brothers , what shall we do ? ”
44002038	And Peter said to them , “ Repent and be baptized every one of you in the name of Jesus Christ for the forgiveness of your sins , and you will receive the gift of the Holy Spirit .
44002039	For the promise is for you and for your children and for all who are far off , everyone whom the Lord our God calls to himself . ”
44002040	And with many other words he bore witness and continued to exhort them , saying , “ Save yourselves from this crooked generation . ”
44002041	So those who received his word were baptized , and there were added that day about three thousand souls .
44002042	And they devoted themselves to the apostles ’ teaching and the fellowship , to the breaking of bread and the prayers .
44002043	And awe came upon every soul , and many wonders and signs were being done through the apostles .
44002044	And all who believed were together and had all things in common .
44002045	And they were selling their possessions and belongings and distributing the proceeds to all , as any had need .
44002046	And day by day , attending the temple together and breaking bread in their homes , they received their food with glad and generous hearts ,
44002047	praising God and having favor with all the people . And the Lord added to their number day by day those who were being saved .
44003001	Now Peter and John were going up to the temple at the hour of prayer , the ninth hour .
44003002	And a man lame from birth was being carried , whom they laid daily at the gate of the temple that is called the Beautiful Gate to ask alms of those entering the temple .
44003003	Seeing Peter and John about to go into the temple , he asked to receive alms .
44003004	And Peter directed his gaze at him , as did John , and said , “ Look at us . ”
44003005	And he fixed his attention on them , expecting to receive something from them .
44003006	But Peter said , “ I have no silver and gold , but what I do have I give to you . In the name of Jesus Christ of Nazareth , rise up and walk ! ”
44003007	And he took him by the right hand and raised him up , and immediately his feet and ankles were made strong .
44003008	And leaping up he stood and began to walk , and entered the temple with them , walking and leaping and praising God .
44003009	And all the people saw him walking and praising God ,
44003010	and recognized him as the one who sat at the Beautiful Gate of the temple , asking for alms . And they were filled with wonder and amazement at what had happened to him .
44003011	While he clung to Peter and John , all the people , utterly astounded , ran together to them in the portico called Solomon’s .
44003012	And when Peter saw it he addressed the people : “ Men of Israel , why do you wonder at this , or why do you stare at us , as though by our own power or piety we have made him walk ?
44003013	The God of Abraham , the God of Isaac , and the God of Jacob , the God of our fathers , glorified his servant Jesus , whom you delivered over and denied in the presence of Pilate , when he had decided to release him .
44003014	But you denied the Holy and Righteous One , and asked for a murderer to be granted to you ,
44003015	and you killed the Author of life , whom God raised from the dead . To this we are witnesses .
44003016	And his name — by faith in his name — has made this man strong whom you see and know , and the faith that is through Jesus has given the man this perfect health in the presence of you all .
44003017	“ And now , brothers , I know that you acted in ignorance , as did also your rulers .
44003018	But what God foretold by the mouth of all the prophets , that his Christ would suffer , he thus fulfilled .
44003019	Repent therefore , and turn again , that your sins may be blotted out ,
44003020	that times of refreshing may come from the presence of the Lord , and that he may send the Christ appointed for you , Jesus ,
44003021	whom heaven must receive until the time for restoring all the things about which God spoke by the mouth of his holy prophets long ago .
44003022	Moses said , ‘ The Lord God will raise up for you a prophet like me from your brothers . You shall listen to him in whatever he tells you .
44003023	And it shall be that every soul who does not listen to that prophet shall be destroyed from the people . ’
44003024	And all the prophets who have spoken , from Samuel and those who came after him , also proclaimed these days .
44003025	You are the sons of the prophets and of the covenant that God made with your fathers , saying to Abraham , ‘ And in your offspring shall all the families of the earth be blessed . ’
44003026	God , having raised up his servant , sent him to you first , to bless you by turning every one of you from your wickedness . ”
44004001	And as they were speaking to the people , the priests and the captain of the temple and the Sadducees came upon them ,
44004002	greatly annoyed because they were teaching the people and proclaiming in Jesus the resurrection from the dead .
44004003	And they arrested them and put them in custody until the next day , for it was already evening .
44004004	But many of those who had heard the word believed , and the number of the men came to about five thousand .
44004005	On the next day their rulers and elders and scribes gathered together in Jerusalem ,
44004006	with Annas the high priest and Caiaphas and John and Alexander , and all who were of the high-priestly family .
44004007	And when they had set them in the midst , they inquired , “ By what power or by what name did you do this ? ”
44004008	Then Peter , filled with the Holy Spirit , said to them , “ Rulers of the people and elders ,
44004009	if we are being examined today concerning a good deed done to a crippled man , by what means this man has been healed ,
44004010	let it be known to all of you and to all the people of Israel that by the name of Jesus Christ of Nazareth , whom you crucified , whom God raised from the dead — by him this man is standing before you well .
44004011	This Jesus is the stone that was rejected by you , the builders , which has become the cornerstone .
44004012	And there is salvation in no one else , for there is no other name under heaven given among men by which we must be saved . ”
44004013	Now when they saw the boldness of Peter and John , and perceived that they were uneducated , common men , they were astonished . And they recognized that they had been with Jesus .
44004014	But seeing the man who was healed standing beside them , they had nothing to say in opposition .
44004015	But when they had commanded them to leave the council , they conferred with one another ,
44004016	saying , “ What shall we do with these men ? For that a notable sign has been performed through them is evident to all the inhabitants of Jerusalem , and we cannot deny it .
44004017	But in order that it may spread no further among the people , let us warn them to speak no more to anyone in this name . ”
44004018	So they called them and charged them not to speak or teach at all in the name of Jesus .
44004019	But Peter and John answered them , “ Whether it is right in the sight of God to listen to you rather than to God , you must judge ,
44004020	for we cannot but speak of what we have seen and heard . ”
44004021	And when they had further threatened them , they let them go , finding no way to punish them , because of the people , for all were praising God for what had happened .
44004022	For the man on whom this sign of healing was performed was more than forty years old .
44004023	When they were released , they went to their friends and reported what the chief priests and the elders had said to them .
44004024	And when they heard it , they lifted their voices together to God and said , “ Sovereign Lord , who made the heaven and the earth and the sea and everything in them ,
44004025	who through the mouth of our father David , your servant , said by the Holy Spirit , “ ‘ Why did the Gentiles rage , and the peoples plot in vain ?
44004026	The kings of the earth set themselves , and the rulers were gathered together , against the Lord and against his Anointed ’ —
44004027	for truly in this city there were gathered together against your holy servant Jesus , whom you anointed , both Herod and Pontius Pilate , along with the Gentiles and the peoples of Israel ,
44004028	to do whatever your hand and your plan had predestined to take place .
44004029	And now , Lord , look upon their threats and grant to your servants to continue to speak your word with all boldness ,
44004030	while you stretch out your hand to heal , and signs and wonders are performed through the name of your holy servant Jesus . ”
44004031	And when they had prayed , the place in which they were gathered together was shaken , and they were all filled with the Holy Spirit and continued to speak the word of God with boldness .
44004032	Now the full number of those who believed were of one heart and soul , and no one said that any of the things that belonged to him was his own , but they had everything in common .
44004033	And with great power the apostles were giving their testimony to the resurrection of the Lord Jesus , and great grace was upon them all .
44004034	There was not a needy person among them , for as many as were owners of lands or houses sold them and brought the proceeds of what was sold
44004035	and laid it at the apostles ’ feet , and it was distributed to each as any had need .
44004036	Thus Joseph , who was also called by the apostles Barnabas ( which means son of encouragement ) , a Levite , a native of Cyprus ,
44004037	sold a field that belonged to him and brought the money and laid it at the apostles ’ feet .
44005001	But a man named Ananias , with his wife Sapphira , sold a piece of property ,
44005002	and with his wife’s knowledge he kept back for himself some of the proceeds and brought only a part of it and laid it at the apostles ’ feet .
44005003	But Peter said , “ Ananias , why has Satan filled your heart to lie to the Holy Spirit and to keep back for yourself part of the proceeds of the land ?
44005004	While it remained unsold , did it not remain your own ? And after it was sold , was it not at your disposal ? Why is it that you have contrived this deed in your heart ? You have not lied to men but to God . ”
44005005	When Ananias heard these words , he fell down and breathed his last . And great fear came upon all who heard of it .
44005006	The young men rose and wrapped him up and carried him out and buried him .
44005007	After an interval of about three hours his wife came in , not knowing what had happened .
44005008	And Peter said to her , “ Tell me whether you sold the land for so much . ” And she said , “ Yes , for so much . ”
44005009	But Peter said to her , “ How is it that you have agreed together to test the Spirit of the Lord ? Behold , the feet of those who have buried your husband are at the door , and they will carry you out . ”
44005010	Immediately she fell down at his feet and breathed her last . When the young men came in they found her dead , and they carried her out and buried her beside her husband .
44005011	And great fear came upon the whole church and upon all who heard of these things .
44005012	Now many signs and wonders were regularly done among the people by the hands of the apostles . And they were all together in Solomon’s Portico .
44005013	None of the rest dared join them , but the people held them in high esteem .
44005014	And more than ever believers were added to the Lord , multitudes of both men and women ,
44005015	so that they even carried out the sick into the streets and laid them on cots and mats , that as Peter came by at least his shadow might fall on some of them .
44005016	The people also gathered from the towns around Jerusalem , bringing the sick and those afflicted with unclean spirits , and they were all healed .
44005017	But the high priest rose up , and all who were with him ( that is , the party of the Sadducees ) , and filled with jealousy
44005018	they arrested the apostles and put them in the public prison .
44005019	But during the night an angel of the Lord opened the prison doors and brought them out , and said ,
44005020	“ Go and stand in the temple and speak to the people all the words of this Life . ”
44005021	And when they heard this , they entered the temple at daybreak and began to teach . Now when the high priest came , and those who were with him , they called together the council and all the senate of the people of Israel and sent to the prison to have them brought .
44005022	But when the officers came , they did not find them in the prison , so they returned and reported ,
44005023	“ We found the prison securely locked and the guards standing at the doors , but when we opened them we found no one inside . ”
44005024	Now when the captain of the temple and the chief priests heard these words , they were greatly perplexed about them , wondering what this would come to .
44005025	And someone came and told them , “ Look ! The men whom you put in prison are standing in the temple and teaching the people . ”
44005026	Then the captain with the officers went and brought them , but not by force , for they were afraid of being stoned by the people .
44005027	And when they had brought them , they set them before the council . And the high priest questioned them ,
44005028	saying , “ We strictly charged you not to teach in this name , yet here you have filled Jerusalem with your teaching , and you intend to bring this man’s blood upon us . ”
44005029	But Peter and the apostles answered , “ We must obey God rather than men .
44005030	The God of our fathers raised Jesus , whom you killed by hanging him on a tree .
44005031	God exalted him at his right hand as Leader and Savior , to give repentance to Israel and forgiveness of sins .
44005032	And we are witnesses to these things , and so is the Holy Spirit , whom God has given to those who obey him . ”
44005033	When they heard this , they were enraged and wanted to kill them .
44005034	But a Pharisee in the council named Gamaliel , a teacher of the law held in honor by all the people , stood up and gave orders to put the men outside for a little while .
44005035	And he said to them , “ Men of Israel , take care what you are about to do with these men .
44005036	For before these days Theudas rose up , claiming to be somebody , and a number of men , about four hundred , joined him . He was killed , and all who followed him were dispersed and came to nothing .
44005037	After him Judas the Galilean rose up in the days of the census and drew away some of the people after him . He too perished , and all who followed him were scattered .
44005038	So in the present case I tell you , keep away from these men and let them alone , for if this plan or this undertaking is of man , it will fail ;
44005039	but if it is of God , you will not be able to overthrow them . You might even be found opposing God ! ” So they took his advice ,
44005040	and when they had called in the apostles , they beat them and charged them not to speak in the name of Jesus , and let them go .
44005041	Then they left the presence of the council , rejoicing that they were counted worthy to suffer dishonor for the name .
44005042	And every day , in the temple and from house to house , they did not cease teaching and preaching Jesus as the Christ .
44006001	Now in these days when the disciples were increasing in number , a complaint by the Hellenists arose against the Hebrews because their widows were being neglected in the daily distribution .
44006002	And the twelve summoned the full number of the disciples and said , “ It is not right that we should give up preaching the word of God to serve tables .
44006003	Therefore , brothers , pick out from among you seven men of good repute , full of the Spirit and of wisdom , whom we will appoint to this duty .
44006004	But we will devote ourselves to prayer and to the ministry of the word . ”
44006005	And what they said pleased the whole gathering , and they chose Stephen , a man full of faith and of the Holy Spirit , and Philip , and Prochorus , and Nicanor , and Timon , and Parmenas , and Nicolaus , a proselyte of Antioch .
44006006	These they set before the apostles , and they prayed and laid their hands on them .
44006007	And the word of God continued to increase , and the number of the disciples multiplied greatly in Jerusalem , and a great many of the priests became obedient to the faith .
44006008	And Stephen , full of grace and power , was doing great wonders and signs among the people .
44006009	Then some of those who belonged to the synagogue of the Freedmen ( as it was called ) , and of the Cyrenians , and of the Alexandrians , and of those from Cilicia and Asia , rose up and disputed with Stephen .
44006010	But they could not withstand the wisdom and the Spirit with which he was speaking .
44006011	Then they secretly instigated men who said , “ We have heard him speak blasphemous words against Moses and God . ”
44006012	And they stirred up the people and the elders and the scribes , and they came upon him and seized him and brought him before the council ,
44006013	and they set up false witnesses who said , “ This man never ceases to speak words against this holy place and the law ,
44006014	for we have heard him say that this Jesus of Nazareth will destroy this place and will change the customs that Moses delivered to us . ”
44006015	And gazing at him , all who sat in the council saw that his face was like the face of an angel .
44007001	And the high priest said , “ Are these things so ? ”
44007002	And Stephen said : “ Brothers and fathers , hear me . The God of glory appeared to our father Abraham when he was in Mesopotamia , before he lived in Haran ,
44007003	and said to him , ‘ Go out from your land and from your kindred and go into the land that I will show you . ’
44007004	Then he went out from the land of the Chaldeans and lived in Haran . And after his father died , God removed him from there into this land in which you are now living .
44007005	Yet he gave him no inheritance in it , not even a foot’s length , but promised to give it to him as a possession and to his offspring after him , though he had no child .
44007006	And God spoke to this effect — that his offspring would be sojourners in a land belonging to others , who would enslave them and afflict them four hundred years .
44007007	‘ But I will judge the nation that they serve , ’ said God , ‘ and after that they shall come out and worship me in this place . ’
44007008	And he gave him the covenant of circumcision . And so Abraham became the father of Isaac , and circumcised him on the eighth day , and Isaac became the father of Jacob , and Jacob of the twelve patriarchs .
44007009	“ And the patriarchs , jealous of Joseph , sold him into Egypt ; but God was with him
44007010	and rescued him out of all his afflictions and gave him favor and wisdom before Pharaoh , king of Egypt , who made him ruler over Egypt and over all his household .
44007011	Now there came a famine throughout all Egypt and Canaan , and great affliction , and our fathers could find no food .
44007012	But when Jacob heard that there was grain in Egypt , he sent out our fathers on their first visit .
44007013	And on the second visit Joseph made himself known to his brothers , and Joseph’s family became known to Pharaoh .
44007014	And Joseph sent and summoned Jacob his father and all his kindred , seventy-five persons in all .
44007015	And Jacob went down into Egypt , and he died , he and our fathers ,
44007016	and they were carried back to Shechem and laid in the tomb that Abraham had bought for a sum of silver from the sons of Hamor in Shechem .
44007017	“ But as the time of the promise drew near , which God had granted to Abraham , the people increased and multiplied in Egypt
44007018	until there arose over Egypt another king who did not know Joseph .
44007019	He dealt shrewdly with our race and forced our fathers to expose their infants , so that they would not be kept alive .
44007020	At this time Moses was born ; and he was beautiful in God’s sight . And he was brought up for three months in his father’s house ,
44007021	and when he was exposed , Pharaoh’s daughter adopted him and brought him up as her own son .
44007022	And Moses was instructed in all the wisdom of the Egyptians , and he was mighty in his words and deeds .
44007023	“ When he was forty years old , it came into his heart to visit his brothers , the children of Israel .
44007024	And seeing one of them being wronged , he defended the oppressed man and avenged him by striking down the Egyptian .
44007025	He supposed that his brothers would understand that God was giving them salvation by his hand , but they did not understand .
44007026	And on the following day he appeared to them as they were quarreling and tried to reconcile them , saying , ‘ Men , you are brothers . Why do you wrong each other ? ’
44007027	But the man who was wronging his neighbor thrust him aside , saying , ‘ Who made you a ruler and a judge over us ?
44007028	Do you want to kill me as you killed the Egyptian yesterday ? ’
44007029	At this retort Moses fled and became an exile in the land of Midian , where he became the father of two sons .
44007030	“ Now when forty years had passed , an angel appeared to him in the wilderness of Mount Sinai , in a flame of fire in a bush .
44007031	When Moses saw it , he was amazed at the sight , and as he drew near to look , there came the voice of the Lord :
44007032	‘ I am the God of your fathers , the God of Abraham and of Isaac and of Jacob . ’ And Moses trembled and did not dare to look .
44007033	Then the Lord said to him , ‘ Take off the sandals from your feet , for the place where you are standing is holy ground .
44007034	I have surely seen the affliction of my people who are in Egypt , and have heard their groaning , and I have come down to deliver them . And now come , I will send you to Egypt . ’
44007035	“ This Moses , whom they rejected , saying , ‘ Who made you a ruler and a judge ? ’ — this man God sent as both ruler and redeemer by the hand of the angel who appeared to him in the bush .
44007036	This man led them out , performing wonders and signs in Egypt and at the Red Sea and in the wilderness for forty years .
44007037	This is the Moses who said to the Israelites , ‘ God will raise up for you a prophet like me from your brothers . ’
44007038	This is the one who was in the congregation in the wilderness with the angel who spoke to him at Mount Sinai , and with our fathers . He received living oracles to give to us .
44007039	Our fathers refused to obey him , but thrust him aside , and in their hearts they turned to Egypt ,
44007040	saying to Aaron , ‘ Make for us gods who will go before us . As for this Moses who led us out from the land of Egypt , we do not know what has become of him . ’
44007041	And they made a calf in those days , and offered a sacrifice to the idol and were rejoicing in the works of their hands .
44007042	But God turned away and gave them over to worship the host of heaven , as it is written in the book of the prophets : “ ‘ Did you bring to me slain beasts and sacrifices , during the forty years in the wilderness , O house of Israel ?
44007043	You took up the tent of Moloch and the star of your god Rephan , the images that you made to worship ; and I will send you into exile beyond Babylon . ’
44007044	“ Our fathers had the tent of witness in the wilderness , just as he who spoke to Moses directed him to make it , according to the pattern that he had seen .
44007045	Our fathers in turn brought it in with Joshua when they dispossessed the nations that God drove out before our fathers . So it was until the days of David ,
44007046	who found favor in the sight of God and asked to find a dwelling place for the God of Jacob .
44007047	But it was Solomon who built a house for him .
44007048	Yet the Most High does not dwell in houses made by hands , as the prophet says ,
44007049	“ ‘ Heaven is my throne , and the earth is my footstool . What kind of house will you build for me , says the Lord , or what is the place of my rest ?
44007050	Did not my hand make all these things ? ’
44007051	“ You stiff-necked people , uncircumcised in heart and ears , you always resist the Holy Spirit . As your fathers did , so do you .
44007052	Which of the prophets did your fathers not persecute ? And they killed those who announced beforehand the coming of the Righteous One , whom you have now betrayed and murdered ,
44007053	you who received the law as delivered by angels and did not keep it . ”
44007054	Now when they heard these things they were enraged , and they ground their teeth at him .
44007055	But he , full of the Holy Spirit , gazed into heaven and saw the glory of God , and Jesus standing at the right hand of God .
44007056	And he said , “ Behold , I see the heavens opened , and the Son of Man standing at the right hand of God . ”
44007057	But they cried out with a loud voice and stopped their ears and rushed together at him .
44007058	Then they cast him out of the city and stoned him . And the witnesses laid down their garments at the feet of a young man named Saul .
44007059	And as they were stoning Stephen , he called out , “ Lord Jesus , receive my spirit . ”
44007060	And falling to his knees he cried out with a loud voice , “ Lord , do not hold this sin against them . ” And when he had said this , he fell asleep .
44008001	And Saul approved of his execution . And there arose on that day a great persecution against the church in Jerusalem , and they were all scattered throughout the regions of Judea and Samaria , except the apostles .
44008002	Devout men buried Stephen and made great lamentation over him .
44008003	But Saul was ravaging the church , and entering house after house , he dragged off men and women and committed them to prison .
44008004	Now those who were scattered went about preaching the word .
44008005	Philip went down to the city of Samaria and proclaimed to them the Christ .
44008006	And the crowds with one accord paid attention to what was being said by Philip when they heard him and saw the signs that he did .
44008007	For unclean spirits , crying out with a loud voice , came out of many who had them , and many who were paralyzed or lame were healed .
44008008	So there was much joy in that city .
44008009	But there was a man named Simon , who had previously practiced magic in the city and amazed the people of Samaria , saying that he himself was somebody great .
44008010	They all paid attention to him , from the least to the greatest , saying , “ This man is the power of God that is called Great . ”
44008011	And they paid attention to him because for a long time he had amazed them with his magic .
44008012	But when they believed Philip as he preached good news about the kingdom of God and the name of Jesus Christ , they were baptized , both men and women .
44008013	Even Simon himself believed , and after being baptized he continued with Philip . And seeing signs and great miracles performed , he was amazed .
44008014	Now when the apostles at Jerusalem heard that Samaria had received the word of God , they sent to them Peter and John ,
44008015	who came down and prayed for them that they might receive the Holy Spirit ,
44008016	for he had not yet fallen on any of them , but they had only been baptized in the name of the Lord Jesus .
44008017	Then they laid their hands on them and they received the Holy Spirit .
44008018	Now when Simon saw that the Spirit was given through the laying on of the apostles ’ hands , he offered them money ,
44008019	saying , “ Give me this power also , so that anyone on whom I lay my hands may receive the Holy Spirit . ”
44008020	But Peter said to him , “ May your silver perish with you , because you thought you could obtain the gift of God with money !
44008021	You have neither part nor lot in this matter , for your heart is not right before God .
44008022	Repent , therefore , of this wickedness of yours , and pray to the Lord that , if possible , the intent of your heart may be forgiven you .
44008023	For I see that you are in the gall of bitterness and in the bond of iniquity . ”
44008024	And Simon answered , “ Pray for me to the Lord , that nothing of what you have said may come upon me . ”
44008025	Now when they had testified and spoken the word of the Lord , they returned to Jerusalem , preaching the gospel to many villages of the Samaritans .
44008026	Now an angel of the Lord said to Philip , “ Rise and go toward the south to the road that goes down from Jerusalem to Gaza . ” This is a desert place .
44008027	And he rose and went . And there was an Ethiopian , a eunuch , a court official of Candace , queen of the Ethiopians , who was in charge of all her treasure . He had come to Jerusalem to worship
44008028	and was returning , seated in his chariot , and he was reading the prophet Isaiah .
44008029	And the Spirit said to Philip , “ Go over and join this chariot . ”
44008030	So Philip ran to him and heard him reading Isaiah the prophet and asked , “ Do you understand what you are reading ? ”
44008031	And he said , “ How can I , unless someone guides me ? ” And he invited Philip to come up and sit with him .
44008032	Now the passage of the Scripture that he was reading was this : “ Like a sheep he was led to the slaughter and like a lamb before its shearer is silent , so he opens not his mouth .
44008033	In his humiliation justice was denied him . Who can describe his generation ? For his life is taken away from the earth . ”
44008034	And the eunuch said to Philip , “ About whom , I ask you , does the prophet say this , about himself or about someone else ? ”
44008035	Then Philip opened his mouth , and beginning with this Scripture he told him the good news about Jesus .
44008036	And as they were going along the road they came to some water , and the eunuch said , “ See , here is water ! What prevents me from being baptized ? ”
44008038	And he commanded the chariot to stop , and they both went down into the water , Philip and the eunuch , and he baptized him .
44008039	And when they came up out of the water , the Spirit of the Lord carried Philip away , and the eunuch saw him no more , and went on his way rejoicing .
44008040	But Philip found himself at Azotus , and as he passed through he preached the gospel to all the towns until he came to Caesarea .
44009001	But Saul , still breathing threats and murder against the disciples of the Lord , went to the high priest
44009002	and asked him for letters to the synagogues at Damascus , so that if he found any belonging to the Way , men or women , he might bring them bound to Jerusalem .
44009003	Now as he went on his way , he approached Damascus , and suddenly a light from heaven flashed around him .
44009004	And falling to the ground he heard a voice saying to him , “ Saul , Saul , why are you persecuting me ? ”
44009005	And he said , “ Who are you , Lord ? ” And he said , “ I am Jesus , whom you are persecuting .
44009006	But rise and enter the city , and you will be told what you are to do . ”
44009007	The men who were traveling with him stood speechless , hearing the voice but seeing no one .
44009008	Saul rose from the ground , and although his eyes were opened , he saw nothing . So they led him by the hand and brought him into Damascus .
44009009	And for three days he was without sight , and neither ate nor drank .
44009010	Now there was a disciple at Damascus named Ananias . The Lord said to him in a vision , “ Ananias . ” And he said , “ Here I am , Lord . ”
44009011	And the Lord said to him , “ Rise and go to the street called Straight , and at the house of Judas look for a man of Tarsus named Saul , for behold , he is praying ,
44009012	and he has seen in a vision a man named Ananias come in and lay his hands on him so that he might regain his sight . ”
44009013	But Ananias answered , “ Lord , I have heard from many about this man , how much evil he has done to your saints at Jerusalem .
44009014	And here he has authority from the chief priests to bind all who call on your name . ”
44009015	But the Lord said to him , “ Go , for he is a chosen instrument of mine to carry my name before the Gentiles and kings and the children of Israel .
44009016	For I will show him how much he must suffer for the sake of my name . ”
44009017	So Ananias departed and entered the house . And laying his hands on him he said , “ Brother Saul , the Lord Jesus who appeared to you on the road by which you came has sent me so that you may regain your sight and be filled with the Holy Spirit . ”
44009018	And immediately something like scales fell from his eyes , and he regained his sight . Then he rose and was baptized ;
44009019	and taking food , he was strengthened . For some days he was with the disciples at Damascus .
44009020	And immediately he proclaimed Jesus in the synagogues , saying , “ He is the Son of God . ”
44009021	And all who heard him were amazed and said , “ Is not this the man who made havoc in Jerusalem of those who called upon this name ? And has he not come here for this purpose , to bring them bound before the chief priests ? ”
44009022	But Saul increased all the more in strength , and confounded the Jews who lived in Damascus by proving that Jesus was the Christ .
44009023	When many days had passed , the Jews plotted to kill him ,
44009024	but their plot became known to Saul . They were watching the gates day and night in order to kill him ,
44009025	but his disciples took him by night and let him down through an opening in the wall , lowering him in a basket .
44009026	And when he had come to Jerusalem , he attempted to join the disciples . And they were all afraid of him , for they did not believe that he was a disciple .
44009027	But Barnabas took him and brought him to the apostles and declared to them how on the road he had seen the Lord , who spoke to him , and how at Damascus he had preached boldly in the name of Jesus .
44009028	So he went in and out among them at Jerusalem , preaching boldly in the name of the Lord .
44009029	And he spoke and disputed against the Hellenists . But they were seeking to kill him .
44009030	And when the brothers learned this , they brought him down to Caesarea and sent him off to Tarsus .
44009031	So the church throughout all Judea and Galilee and Samaria had peace and was being built up . And walking in the fear of the Lord and in the comfort of the Holy Spirit , it multiplied .
44009032	Now as Peter went here and there among them all , he came down also to the saints who lived at Lydda .
44009033	There he found a man named Aeneas , bedridden for eight years , who was paralyzed .
44009034	And Peter said to him , “ Aeneas , Jesus Christ heals you ; rise and make your bed . ” And immediately he rose .
44009035	And all the residents of Lydda and Sharon saw him , and they turned to the Lord .
44009036	Now there was in Joppa a disciple named Tabitha , which , translated , means Dorcas . She was full of good works and acts of charity .
44009037	In those days she became ill and died , and when they had washed her , they laid her in an upper room .
44009038	Since Lydda was near Joppa , the disciples , hearing that Peter was there , sent two men to him , urging him , “ Please come to us without delay . ”
44009039	So Peter rose and went with them . And when he arrived , they took him to the upper room . All the widows stood beside him weeping and showing tunics and other garments that Dorcas made while she was with them .
44009040	But Peter put them all outside , and knelt down and prayed ; and turning to the body he said , “ Tabitha , arise . ” And she opened her eyes , and when she saw Peter she sat up .
44009041	And he gave her his hand and raised her up . Then calling the saints and widows , he presented her alive .
44009042	And it became known throughout all Joppa , and many believed in the Lord .
44009043	And he stayed in Joppa for many days with one Simon , a tanner .
44010001	At Caesarea there was a man named Cornelius , a centurion of what was known as the Italian Cohort ,
44010002	a devout man who feared God with all his household , gave alms generously to the people , and prayed continually to God .
44010003	About the ninth hour of the day he saw clearly in a vision an angel of God come in and say to him , “ Cornelius . ”
44010004	And he stared at him in terror and said , “ What is it , Lord ? ” And he said to him , “ Your prayers and your alms have ascended as a memorial before God .
44010005	And now send men to Joppa and bring one Simon who is called Peter .
44010006	He is lodging with one Simon , a tanner , whose house is by the sea . ”
44010007	When the angel who spoke to him had departed , he called two of his servants and a devout soldier from among those who attended him ,
44010008	and having related everything to them , he sent them to Joppa .
44010009	The next day , as they were on their journey and approaching the city , Peter went up on the housetop about the sixth hour to pray .
44010010	And he became hungry and wanted something to eat , but while they were preparing it , he fell into a trance
44010011	and saw the heavens opened and something like a great sheet descending , being let down by its four corners upon the earth .
44010012	In it were all kinds of animals and reptiles and birds of the air .
44010013	And there came a voice to him : “ Rise , Peter ; kill and eat . ”
44010014	But Peter said , “ By no means , Lord ; for I have never eaten anything that is common or unclean . ”
44010015	And the voice came to him again a second time , “ What God has made clean , do not call common . ”
44010016	This happened three times , and the thing was taken up at once to heaven .
44010017	Now while Peter was inwardly perplexed as to what the vision that he had seen might mean , behold , the men who were sent by Cornelius , having made inquiry for Simon’s house , stood at the gate
44010018	and called out to ask whether Simon who was called Peter was lodging there .
44010019	And while Peter was pondering the vision , the Spirit said to him , “ Behold , three men are looking for you .
44010020	Rise and go down and accompany them without hesitation , for I have sent them . ”
44010021	And Peter went down to the men and said , “ I am the one you are looking for . What is the reason for your coming ? ”
44010022	And they said , “ Cornelius , a centurion , an upright and God-fearing man , who is well spoken of by the whole Jewish nation , was directed by a holy angel to send for you to come to his house and to hear what you have to say . ”
44010023	So he invited them in to be his guests . The next day he rose and went away with them , and some of the brothers from Joppa accompanied him .
44010024	And on the following day they entered Caesarea . Cornelius was expecting them and had called together his relatives and close friends .
44010025	When Peter entered , Cornelius met him and fell down at his feet and worshiped him .
44010026	But Peter lifted him up , saying , “ Stand up ; I too am a man . ”
44010027	And as he talked with him , he went in and found many persons gathered .
44010028	And he said to them , “ You yourselves know how unlawful it is for a Jew to associate with or to visit anyone of another nation , but God has shown me that I should not call any person common or unclean .
44010029	So when I was sent for , I came without objection . I ask then why you sent for me . ”
44010030	And Cornelius said , “ Four days ago , about this hour , I was praying in my house at the ninth hour , and behold , a man stood before me in bright clothing
44010031	and said , ‘ Cornelius , your prayer has been heard and your alms have been remembered before God .
44010032	Send therefore to Joppa and ask for Simon who is called Peter . He is lodging in the house of Simon , a tanner , by the sea . ’
44010033	So I sent for you at once , and you have been kind enough to come . Now therefore we are all here in the presence of God to hear all that you have been commanded by the Lord . ”
44010034	So Peter opened his mouth and said : “ Truly I understand that God shows no partiality ,
44010035	but in every nation anyone who fears him and does what is right is acceptable to him .
44010036	As for the word that he sent to Israel , preaching good news of peace through Jesus Christ ( he is Lord of all ) ,
44010037	you yourselves know what happened throughout all Judea , beginning from Galilee after the baptism that John proclaimed :
44010038	how God anointed Jesus of Nazareth with the Holy Spirit and with power . He went about doing good and healing all who were oppressed by the devil , for God was with him .
44010039	And we are witnesses of all that he did both in the country of the Jews and in Jerusalem . They put him to death by hanging him on a tree ,
44010040	but God raised him on the third day and made him to appear ,
44010041	not to all the people but to us who had been chosen by God as witnesses , who ate and drank with him after he rose from the dead .
44010042	And he commanded us to preach to the people and to testify that he is the one appointed by God to be judge of the living and the dead .
44010043	To him all the prophets bear witness that everyone who believes in him receives forgiveness of sins through his name . ”
44010044	While Peter was still saying these things , the Holy Spirit fell on all who heard the word .
44010045	And the believers from among the circumcised who had come with Peter were amazed , because the gift of the Holy Spirit was poured out even on the Gentiles .
44010046	For they were hearing them speaking in tongues and extolling God . Then Peter declared ,
44010047	“ Can anyone withhold water for baptizing these people , who have received the Holy Spirit just as we have ? ”
44010048	And he commanded them to be baptized in the name of Jesus Christ . Then they asked him to remain for some days .
44011001	Now the apostles and the brothers who were throughout Judea heard that the Gentiles also had received the word of God .
44011002	So when Peter went up to Jerusalem , the circumcision party criticized him , saying ,
44011003	“ You went to uncircumcised men and ate with them . ”
44011004	But Peter began and explained it to them in order :
44011005	“ I was in the city of Joppa praying , and in a trance I saw a vision , something like a great sheet descending , being let down from heaven by its four corners , and it came down to me .
44011006	Looking at it closely , I observed animals and beasts of prey and reptiles and birds of the air .
44011007	And I heard a voice saying to me , ‘ Rise , Peter ; kill and eat . ’
44011008	But I said , ‘ By no means , Lord ; for nothing common or unclean has ever entered my mouth . ’
44011009	But the voice answered a second time from heaven , ‘ What God has made clean , do not call common . ’
44011010	This happened three times , and all was drawn up again into heaven .
44011011	And behold , at that very moment three men arrived at the house in which we were , sent to me from Caesarea .
44011012	And the Spirit told me to go with them , making no distinction . These six brothers also accompanied me , and we entered the man’s house .
44011013	And he told us how he had seen the angel stand in his house and say , ‘ Send to Joppa and bring Simon who is called Peter ;
44011014	he will declare to you a message by which you will be saved , you and all your household . ’
44011015	As I began to speak , the Holy Spirit fell on them just as on us at the beginning .
44011016	And I remembered the word of the Lord , how he said , ‘ John baptized with water , but you will be baptized with the Holy Spirit . ’
44011017	If then God gave the same gift to them as he gave to us when we believed in the Lord Jesus Christ , who was I that I could stand in God’s way ? ”
44011018	When they heard these things they fell silent . And they glorified God , saying , “ Then to the Gentiles also God has granted repentance that leads to life . ”
44011019	Now those who were scattered because of the persecution that arose over Stephen traveled as far as Phoenicia and Cyprus and Antioch , speaking the word to no one except Jews .
44011020	But there were some of them , men of Cyprus and Cyrene , who on coming to Antioch spoke to the Hellenists also , preaching the Lord Jesus .
44011021	And the hand of the Lord was with them , and a great number who believed turned to the Lord .
44011022	The report of this came to the ears of the church in Jerusalem , and they sent Barnabas to Antioch .
44011023	When he came and saw the grace of God , he was glad , and he exhorted them all to remain faithful to the Lord with steadfast purpose ,
44011024	for he was a good man , full of the Holy Spirit and of faith . And a great many people were added to the Lord .
44011025	So Barnabas went to Tarsus to look for Saul ,
44011026	and when he had found him , he brought him to Antioch . For a whole year they met with the church and taught a great many people . And in Antioch the disciples were first called Christians .
44011027	Now in these days prophets came down from Jerusalem to Antioch .
44011028	And one of them named Agabus stood up and foretold by the Spirit that there would be a great famine over all the world ( this took place in the days of Claudius ) .
44011029	So the disciples determined , everyone according to his ability , to send relief to the brothers living in Judea .
44011030	And they did so , sending it to the elders by the hand of Barnabas and Saul .
44012001	About that time Herod the king laid violent hands on some who belonged to the church .
44012002	He killed James the brother of John with the sword ,
44012003	and when he saw that it pleased the Jews , he proceeded to arrest Peter also . This was during the days of Unleavened Bread .
44012004	And when he had seized him , he put him in prison , delivering him over to four squads of soldiers to guard him , intending after the Passover to bring him out to the people .
44012005	So Peter was kept in prison , but earnest prayer for him was made to God by the church .
44012006	Now when Herod was about to bring him out , on that very night , Peter was sleeping between two soldiers , bound with two chains , and sentries before the door were guarding the prison .
44012007	And behold , an angel of the Lord stood next to him , and a light shone in the cell . He struck Peter on the side and woke him , saying , “ Get up quickly . ” And the chains fell off his hands .
44012008	And the angel said to him , “ Dress yourself and put on your sandals . ” And he did so . And he said to him , “ Wrap your cloak around you and follow me . ”
44012009	And he went out and followed him . He did not know that what was being done by the angel was real , but thought he was seeing a vision .
44012010	When they had passed the first and the second guard , they came to the iron gate leading into the city . It opened for them of its own accord , and they went out and went along one street , and immediately the angel left him .
