44012011	When Peter came to himself , he said , “ Now I am sure that the Lord has sent his angel and rescued me from the hand of Herod and from all that the Jewish people were expecting . ”
44012012	When he realized this , he went to the house of Mary , the mother of John whose other name was Mark , where many were gathered together and were praying .
44012013	And when he knocked at the door of the gateway , a servant girl named Rhoda came to answer .
44012014	Recognizing Peter’s voice , in her joy she did not open the gate but ran in and reported that Peter was standing at the gate .
44012015	They said to her , “ You are out of your mind . ” But she kept insisting that it was so , and they kept saying , “ It is his angel ! ”
44012016	But Peter continued knocking , and when they opened , they saw him and were amazed .
44012017	But motioning to them with his hand to be silent , he described to them how the Lord had brought him out of the prison . And he said , “ Tell these things to James and to the brothers . ” Then he departed and went to another place .
44012018	Now when day came , there was no little disturbance among the soldiers over what had become of Peter .
44012019	And after Herod searched for him and did not find him , he examined the sentries and ordered that they should be put to death . Then he went down from Judea to Caesarea and spent time there .
44012020	Now Herod was angry with the people of Tyre and Sidon , and they came to him with one accord , and having persuaded Blastus , the king’s chamberlain , they asked for peace , because their country depended on the king’s country for food .
44012021	On an appointed day Herod put on his royal robes , took his seat upon the throne , and delivered an oration to them .
44012022	And the people were shouting , “ The voice of a god , and not of a man ! ”
44012023	Immediately an angel of the Lord struck him down , because he did not give God the glory , and he was eaten by worms and breathed his last .
44012024	But the word of God increased and multiplied .
44012025	And Barnabas and Saul returned from Jerusalem when they had completed their service , bringing with them John , whose other name was Mark .
44013001	Now there were in the church at Antioch prophets and teachers , Barnabas , Simeon who was called Niger , Lucius of Cyrene , Manaen a member of the court of Herod the tetrarch , and Saul .
44013002	While they were worshiping the Lord and fasting , the Holy Spirit said , “ Set apart for me Barnabas and Saul for the work to which I have called them . ”
44013003	Then after fasting and praying they laid their hands on them and sent them off .
44013004	So , being sent out by the Holy Spirit , they went down to Seleucia , and from there they sailed to Cyprus .
44013005	When they arrived at Salamis , they proclaimed the word of God in the synagogues of the Jews . And they had John to assist them .
44013006	When they had gone through the whole island as far as Paphos , they came upon a certain magician , a Jewish false prophet named Bar-Jesus .
44013007	He was with the proconsul , Sergius Paulus , a man of intelligence , who summoned Barnabas and Saul and sought to hear the word of God .
44013008	But Elymas the magician ( for that is the meaning of his name
44013009	But Saul , who was also called Paul , filled with the Holy Spirit , looked intently at him
44013010	and said , “ You son of the devil , you enemy of all righteousness , full of all deceit and villainy , will you not stop making crooked the straight paths of the Lord ?
44013011	And now , behold , the hand of the Lord is upon you , and you will be blind and unable to see the sun for a time . ” Immediately mist and darkness fell upon him , and he went about seeking people to lead him by the hand .
44013012	Then the proconsul believed , when he saw what had occurred , for he was astonished at the teaching of the Lord .
44013013	Now Paul and his companions set sail from Paphos and came to Perga in Pamphylia . And John left them and returned to Jerusalem ,
44013014	but they went on from Perga and came to Antioch in Pisidia . And on the Sabbath day they went into the synagogue and sat down .
44013015	After the reading from the Law and the Prophets , the rulers of the synagogue sent a message to them , saying , “ Brothers , if you have any word of encouragement for the people , say it . ”
44013016	So Paul stood up , and motioning with his hand said : “ Men of Israel and you who fear God , listen .
44013017	The God of this people Israel chose our fathers and made the people great during their stay in the land of Egypt , and with uplifted arm he led them out of it .
44013018	And for about forty years he put up with them in the wilderness .
44013019	And after destroying seven nations in the land of Canaan , he gave them their land as an inheritance .
44013020	All this took about 450 years . And after that he gave them judges until Samuel the prophet .
44013021	Then they asked for a king , and God gave them Saul the son of Kish , a man of the tribe of Benjamin , for forty years .
44013022	And when he had removed him , he raised up David to be their king , of whom he testified and said , ‘ I have found in David the son of Jesse a man after my heart , who will do all my will . ’
44013023	Of this man’s offspring God has brought to Israel a Savior , Jesus , as he promised .
44013024	Before his coming , John had proclaimed a baptism of repentance to all the people of Israel .
44013025	And as John was finishing his course , he said , ‘ What do you suppose that I am ? I am not he . No , but behold , after me one is coming , the sandals of whose feet I am not worthy to untie . ’
44013026	“ Brothers , sons of the family of Abraham , and those among you who fear God , to us has been sent the message of this salvation .
44013027	For those who live in Jerusalem and their rulers , because they did not recognize him nor understand the utterances of the prophets , which are read every Sabbath , fulfilled them by condemning him .
44013028	And though they found in him no guilt worthy of death , they asked Pilate to have him executed .
44013029	And when they had carried out all that was written of him , they took him down from the tree and laid him in a tomb .
44013030	But God raised him from the dead ,
44013031	and for many days he appeared to those who had come up with him from Galilee to Jerusalem , who are now his witnesses to the people .
44013032	And we bring you the good news that what God promised to the fathers ,
44013033	this he has fulfilled to us their children by raising Jesus , as also it is written in the second Psalm , “ ‘ You are my Son , today I have begotten you . ’
44013034	And as for the fact that he raised him from the dead , no more to return to corruption , he has spoken in this way , “ ‘ I will give you the holy and sure blessings of David . ’
44013035	Therefore he says also in another psalm , “ ‘ You will not let your Holy One see corruption . ’
44013036	For David , after he had served the purpose of God in his own generation , fell asleep and was laid with his fathers and saw corruption ,
44013037	but he whom God raised up did not see corruption .
44013038	Let it be known to you therefore , brothers , that through this man forgiveness of sins is proclaimed to you ,
44013039	and by him everyone who believes is freed from everything from which you could not be freed by the law of Moses .
44013040	Beware , therefore , lest what is said in the Prophets should come about :
44013041	“ ‘ Look , you scoffers , be astounded and perish ; for I am doing a work in your days , a work that you will not believe , even if one tells it to you . ’ ”
44013042	As they went out , the people begged that these things might be told them the next Sabbath .
44013043	And after the meeting of the synagogue broke up , many Jews and devout converts to Judaism followed Paul and Barnabas , who , as they spoke with them , urged them to continue in the grace of God .
44013044	The next Sabbath almost the whole city gathered to hear the word of the Lord .
44013045	But when the Jews saw the crowds , they were filled with jealousy and began to contradict what was spoken by Paul , reviling him .
44013046	And Paul and Barnabas spoke out boldly , saying , “ It was necessary that the word of God be spoken first to you . Since you thrust it aside and judge yourselves unworthy of eternal life , behold , we are turning to the Gentiles .
44013047	For so the Lord has commanded us , saying , “ ‘ I have made you a light for the Gentiles , that you may bring salvation to the ends of the earth . ’ ”
44013048	And when the Gentiles heard this , they began rejoicing and glorifying the word of the Lord , and as many as were appointed to eternal life believed .
44013049	And the word of the Lord was spreading throughout the whole region .
44013050	But the Jews incited the devout women of high standing and the leading men of the city , stirred up persecution against Paul and Barnabas , and drove them out of their district .
44013051	But they shook off the dust from their feet against them and went to Iconium .
44013052	And the disciples were filled with joy and with the Holy Spirit .
44014001	Now at Iconium they entered together into the Jewish synagogue and spoke in such a way that a great number of both Jews and Greeks believed .
44014002	But the unbelieving Jews stirred up the Gentiles and poisoned their minds against the brothers .
44014003	So they remained for a long time , speaking boldly for the Lord , who bore witness to the word of his grace , granting signs and wonders to be done by their hands .
44014004	But the people of the city were divided ; some sided with the Jews and some with the apostles .
44014005	When an attempt was made by both Gentiles and Jews , with their rulers , to mistreat them and to stone them ,
44014006	they learned of it and fled to Lystra and Derbe , cities of Lycaonia , and to the surrounding country ,
44014007	and there they continued to preach the gospel .
44014008	Now at Lystra there was a man sitting who could not use his feet . He was crippled from birth and had never walked .
44014009	He listened to Paul speaking . And Paul , looking intently at him and seeing that he had faith to be made well ,
44014010	said in a loud voice , “ Stand upright on your feet . ” And he sprang up and began walking .
44014011	And when the crowds saw what Paul had done , they lifted up their voices , saying in Lycaonian , “ The gods have come down to us in the likeness of men ! ”
44014012	Barnabas they called Zeus , and Paul , Hermes , because he was the chief speaker .
44014013	And the priest of Zeus , whose temple was at the entrance to the city , brought oxen and garlands to the gates and wanted to offer sacrifice with the crowds .
44014014	But when the apostles Barnabas and Paul heard of it , they tore their garments and rushed out into the crowd , crying out ,
44014015	“ Men , why are you doing these things ? We also are men , of like nature with you , and we bring you good news , that you should turn from these vain things to a living God , who made the heaven and the earth and the sea and all that is in them .
44014016	In past generations he allowed all the nations to walk in their own ways .
44014017	Yet he did not leave himself without witness , for he did good by giving you rains from heaven and fruitful seasons , satisfying your hearts with food and gladness . ”
44014018	Even with these words they scarcely restrained the people from offering sacrifice to them .
44014019	But Jews came from Antioch and Iconium , and having persuaded the crowds , they stoned Paul and dragged him out of the city , supposing that he was dead .
44014020	But when the disciples gathered about him , he rose up and entered the city , and on the next day he went on with Barnabas to Derbe .
44014021	When they had preached the gospel to that city and had made many disciples , they returned to Lystra and to Iconium and to Antioch ,
44014022	strengthening the souls of the disciples , encouraging them to continue in the faith , and saying that through many tribulations we must enter the kingdom of God .
44014023	And when they had appointed elders for them in every church , with prayer and fasting they committed them to the Lord in whom they had believed .
44014024	Then they passed through Pisidia and came to Pamphylia .
44014025	And when they had spoken the word in Perga , they went down to Attalia ,
44014026	and from there they sailed to Antioch , where they had been commended to the grace of God for the work that they had fulfilled .
44014027	And when they arrived and gathered the church together , they declared all that God had done with them , and how he had opened a door of faith to the Gentiles .
44014028	And they remained no little time with the disciples .
44015001	But some men came down from Judea and were teaching the brothers , “ Unless you are circumcised according to the custom of Moses , you cannot be saved . ”
44015002	And after Paul and Barnabas had no small dissension and debate with them , Paul and Barnabas and some of the others were appointed to go up to Jerusalem to the apostles and the elders about this question .
44015003	So , being sent on their way by the church , they passed through both Phoenicia and Samaria , describing in detail the conversion of the Gentiles , and brought great joy to all the brothers .
44015004	When they came to Jerusalem , they were welcomed by the church and the apostles and the elders , and they declared all that God had done with them .
44015005	But some believers who belonged to the party of the Pharisees rose up and said , “ It is necessary to circumcise them and to order them to keep the law of Moses . ”
44015006	The apostles and the elders were gathered together to consider this matter .
44015007	And after there had been much debate , Peter stood up and said to them , “ Brothers , you know that in the early days God made a choice among you , that by my mouth the Gentiles should hear the word of the gospel and believe .
44015008	And God , who knows the heart , bore witness to them , by giving them the Holy Spirit just as he did to us ,
44015009	and he made no distinction between us and them , having cleansed their hearts by faith .
44015010	Now , therefore , why are you putting God to the test by placing a yoke on the neck of the disciples that neither our fathers nor we have been able to bear ?
44015011	But we believe that we will be saved through the grace of the Lord Jesus , just as they will . ”
44015012	And all the assembly fell silent , and they listened to Barnabas and Paul as they related what signs and wonders God had done through them among the Gentiles .
44015013	After they finished speaking , James replied , “ Brothers , listen to me .
44015014	Simeon has related how God first visited the Gentiles , to take from them a people for his name .
44015015	And with this the words of the prophets agree , just as it is written ,
44015016	“ ‘ After this I will return , and I will rebuild the tent of David that has fallen ; I will rebuild its ruins , and I will restore it ,
44015017	that the remnant of mankind may seek the Lord , and all the Gentiles who are called by my name , says the Lord , who makes these things
44015018	known from of old . ’
44015019	Therefore my judgment is that we should not trouble those of the Gentiles who turn to God ,
44015020	but should write to them to abstain from the things polluted by idols , and from sexual immorality , and from what has been strangled , and from blood .
44015021	For from ancient generations Moses has had in every city those who proclaim him , for he is read every Sabbath in the synagogues . ”
44015022	Then it seemed good to the apostles and the elders , with the whole church , to choose men from among them and send them to Antioch with Paul and Barnabas . They sent Judas called Barsabbas , and Silas , leading men among the brothers ,
44015023	with the following letter : “ The brothers , both the apostles and the elders , to the brothers who are of the Gentiles in Antioch and Syria and Cilicia , greetings .
44015024	Since we have heard that some persons have gone out from us and troubled you with words , unsettling your minds , although we gave them no instructions ,
44015025	it has seemed good to us , having come to one accord , to choose men and send them to you with our beloved Barnabas and Paul ,
44015026	men who have risked their lives for the sake of our Lord Jesus Christ .
44015027	We have therefore sent Judas and Silas , who themselves will tell you the same things by word of mouth .
44015028	For it has seemed good to the Holy Spirit and to us to lay on you no greater burden than these requirements :
44015029	that you abstain from what has been sacrificed to idols , and from blood , and from what has been strangled , and from sexual immorality . If you keep yourselves from these , you will do well . Farewell . ”
44015030	So when they were sent off , they went down to Antioch , and having gathered the congregation together , they delivered the letter .
44015031	And when they had read it , they rejoiced because of its encouragement .
44015032	And Judas and Silas , who were themselves prophets , encouraged and strengthened the brothers with many words .
44015033	And after they had spent some time , they were sent off in peace by the brothers to those who had sent them .
44015035	But Paul and Barnabas remained in Antioch , teaching and preaching the word of the Lord , with many others also .
44015036	And after some days Paul said to Barnabas , “ Let us return and visit the brothers in every city where we proclaimed the word of the Lord , and see how they are . ”
44015037	Now Barnabas wanted to take with them John called Mark .
44015038	But Paul thought best not to take with them one who had withdrawn from them in Pamphylia and had not gone with them to the work .
44015039	And there arose a sharp disagreement , so that they separated from each other . Barnabas took Mark with him and sailed away to Cyprus ,
44015040	but Paul chose Silas and departed , having been commended by the brothers to the grace of the Lord .
44015041	And he went through Syria and Cilicia , strengthening the churches .
44016001	Paul came also to Derbe and to Lystra . A disciple was there , named Timothy , the son of a Jewish woman who was a believer , but his father was a Greek .
44016002	He was well spoken of by the brothers at Lystra and Iconium .
44016003	Paul wanted Timothy to accompany him , and he took him and circumcised him because of the Jews who were in those places , for they all knew that his father was a Greek .
44016004	As they went on their way through the cities , they delivered to them for observance the decisions that had been reached by the apostles and elders who were in Jerusalem .
44016005	So the churches were strengthened in the faith , and they increased in numbers daily .
44016006	And they went through the region of Phrygia and Galatia , having been forbidden by the Holy Spirit to speak the word in Asia .
44016007	And when they had come up to Mysia , they attempted to go into Bithynia , but the Spirit of Jesus did not allow them .
44016008	So , passing by Mysia , they went down to Troas .
44016009	And a vision appeared to Paul in the night : a man of Macedonia was standing there , urging him and saying , “ Come over to Macedonia and help us . ”
44016010	And when Paul had seen the vision , immediately we sought to go on into Macedonia , concluding that God had called us to preach the gospel to them .
44016011	So , setting sail from Troas , we made a direct voyage to Samothrace , and the following day to Neapolis ,
44016012	and from there to Philippi , which is a leading city of the district of Macedonia and a Roman colony . We remained in this city some days .
44016013	And on the Sabbath day we went outside the gate to the riverside , where we supposed there was a place of prayer , and we sat down and spoke to the women who had come together .
44016014	One who heard us was a woman named Lydia , from the city of Thyatira , a seller of purple goods , who was a worshiper of God . The Lord opened her heart to pay attention to what was said by Paul .
44016015	And after she was baptized , and her household as well , she urged us , saying , “ If you have judged me to be faithful to the Lord , come to my house and stay . ” And she prevailed upon us .
44016016	As we were going to the place of prayer , we were met by a slave girl who had a spirit of divination and brought her owners much gain by fortune-telling .
44016017	She followed Paul and us , crying out , “ These men are servants of the Most High God , who proclaim to you the way of salvation . ”
44016018	And this she kept doing for many days . Paul , having become greatly annoyed , turned and said to the spirit , “ I command you in the name of Jesus Christ to come out of her . ” And it came out that very hour .
44016019	But when her owners saw that their hope of gain was gone , they seized Paul and Silas and dragged them into the marketplace before the rulers .
44016020	And when they had brought them to the magistrates , they said , “ These men are Jews , and they are disturbing our city .
44016021	They advocate customs that are not lawful for us as Romans to accept or practice . ”
44016022	The crowd joined in attacking them , and the magistrates tore the garments off them and gave orders to beat them with rods .
44016023	And when they had inflicted many blows upon them , they threw them into prison , ordering the jailer to keep them safely .
44016024	Having received this order , he put them into the inner prison and fastened their feet in the stocks .
44016025	About midnight Paul and Silas were praying and singing hymns to God , and the prisoners were listening to them ,
44016026	and suddenly there was a great earthquake , so that the foundations of the prison were shaken . And immediately all the doors were opened , and everyone’s bonds were unfastened .
44016027	When the jailer woke and saw that the prison doors were open , he drew his sword and was about to kill himself , supposing that the prisoners had escaped .
44016028	But Paul cried with a loud voice , “ Do not harm yourself , for we are all here . ”
44016029	And the jailer called for lights and rushed in , and trembling with fear he fell down before Paul and Silas .
44016030	Then he brought them out and said , “ Sirs , what must I do to be saved ? ”
44016031	And they said , “ Believe in the Lord Jesus , and you will be saved , you and your household . ”
44016032	And they spoke the word of the Lord to him and to all who were in his house .
44016033	And he took them the same hour of the night and washed their wounds ; and he was baptized at once , he and all his family .
44016034	Then he brought them up into his house and set food before them . And he rejoiced along with his entire household that he had believed in God .
44016035	But when it was day , the magistrates sent the police , saying , “ Let those men go . ”
44016036	And the jailer reported these words to Paul , saying , “ The magistrates have sent to let you go . Therefore come out now and go in peace . ”
44016037	But Paul said to them , “ They have beaten us publicly , uncondemned , men who are Roman citizens , and have thrown us into prison ; and do they now throw us out secretly ? No ! Let them come themselves and take us out . ”
44016038	The police reported these words to the magistrates , and they were afraid when they heard that they were Roman citizens .
44016039	So they came and apologized to them . And they took them out and asked them to leave the city .
44016040	So they went out of the prison and visited Lydia . And when they had seen the brothers , they encouraged them and departed .
44017001	Now when they had passed through Amphipolis and Apollonia , they came to Thessalonica , where there was a synagogue of the Jews .
44017002	And Paul went in , as was his custom , and on three Sabbath days he reasoned with them from the Scriptures ,
44017003	explaining and proving that it was necessary for the Christ to suffer and to rise from the dead , and saying , “ This Jesus , whom I proclaim to you , is the Christ . ”
44017004	And some of them were persuaded and joined Paul and Silas , as did a great many of the devout Greeks and not a few of the leading women .
44017005	But the Jews were jealous , and taking some wicked men of the rabble , they formed a mob , set the city in an uproar , and attacked the house of Jason , seeking to bring them out to the crowd .
44017006	And when they could not find them , they dragged Jason and some of the brothers before the city authorities , shouting , “ These men who have turned the world upside down have come here also ,
44017007	and Jason has received them , and they are all acting against the decrees of Caesar , saying that there is another king , Jesus . ”
44017008	And the people and the city authorities were disturbed when they heard these things .
44017009	And when they had taken money as security from Jason and the rest , they let them go .
44017010	The brothers immediately sent Paul and Silas away by night to Berea , and when they arrived they went into the Jewish synagogue .
44017011	Now these Jews were more noble than those in Thessalonica ; they received the word with all eagerness , examining the Scriptures daily to see if these things were so .
44017012	Many of them therefore believed , with not a few Greek women of high standing as well as men .
44017013	But when the Jews from Thessalonica learned that the word of God was proclaimed by Paul at Berea also , they came there too , agitating and stirring up the crowds .
44017014	Then the brothers immediately sent Paul off on his way to the sea , but Silas and Timothy remained there .
44017015	Those who conducted Paul brought him as far as Athens , and after receiving a command for Silas and Timothy to come to him as soon as possible , they departed .
44017016	Now while Paul was waiting for them at Athens , his spirit was provoked within him as he saw that the city was full of idols .
44017017	So he reasoned in the synagogue with the Jews and the devout persons , and in the marketplace every day with those who happened to be there .
44017018	Some of the Epicurean and Stoic philosophers also conversed with him . And some said , “ What does this babbler wish to say ? ” Others said , “ He seems to be a preacher of foreign divinities ” — because he was preaching Jesus and the resurrection .
44017019	And they took him and brought him to the Areopagus , saying , “ May we know what this new teaching is that you are presenting ?
44017020	For you bring some strange things to our ears . We wish to know therefore what these things mean . ”
44017021	Now all the Athenians and the foreigners who lived there would spend their time in nothing except telling or hearing something new .
44017022	So Paul , standing in the midst of the Areopagus , said : “ Men of Athens , I perceive that in every way you are very religious .
44017023	For as I passed along and observed the objects of your worship , I found also an altar with this inscription , ‘ To the unknown god . ’ What therefore you worship as unknown , this I proclaim to you .
44017024	The God who made the world and everything in it , being Lord of heaven and earth , does not live in temples made by man ,
44017025	nor is he served by human hands , as though he needed anything , since he himself gives to all mankind life and breath and everything .
44017026	And he made from one man every nation of mankind to live on all the face of the earth , having determined allotted periods and the boundaries of their dwelling place ,
44017027	that they should seek God , in the hope that they might feel their way toward him and find him . Yet he is actually not far from each one of us ,
44017028	for “ ‘ In him we live and move and have our being ’ ; as even some of your own poets have said , “ ‘ For we are indeed his offspring . ’
44017029	Being then God’s offspring , we ought not to think that the divine being is like gold or silver or stone , an image formed by the art and imagination of man .
44017030	The times of ignorance God overlooked , but now he commands all people everywhere to repent ,
44017031	because he has fixed a day on which he will judge the world in righteousness by a man whom he has appointed ; and of this he has given assurance to all by raising him from the dead . ”
44017032	Now when they heard of the resurrection of the dead , some mocked . But others said , “ We will hear you again about this . ”
44017033	So Paul went out from their midst .
44017034	But some men joined him and believed , among whom also were Dionysius the Areopagite and a woman named Damaris and others with them .
44018001	After this Paul left Athens and went to Corinth .
44018002	And he found a Jew named Aquila , a native of Pontus , recently come from Italy with his wife Priscilla , because Claudius had commanded all the Jews to leave Rome . And he went to see them ,
44018003	and because he was of the same trade he stayed with them and worked , for they were tentmakers by trade .
44018004	And he reasoned in the synagogue every Sabbath , and tried to persuade Jews and Greeks .
44018005	When Silas and Timothy arrived from Macedonia , Paul was occupied with the word , testifying to the Jews that the Christ was Jesus .
44018006	And when they opposed and reviled him , he shook out his garments and said to them , “ Your blood be on your own heads ! I am innocent . From now on I will go to the Gentiles . ”
44018007	And he left there and went to the house of a man named Titius Justus , a worshiper of God . His house was next door to the synagogue .
44018008	Crispus , the ruler of the synagogue , believed in the Lord , together with his entire household . And many of the Corinthians hearing Paul believed and were baptized .
44018009	And the Lord said to Paul one night in a vision , “ Do not be afraid , but go on speaking and do not be silent ,
44018010	for I am with you , and no one will attack you to harm you , for I have many in this city who are my people . ”
44018011	And he stayed a year and six months , teaching the word of God among them .
44018012	But when Gallio was proconsul of Achaia , the Jews made a united attack on Paul and brought him before the tribunal ,
44018013	saying , “ This man is persuading people to worship God contrary to the law . ”
44018014	But when Paul was about to open his mouth , Gallio said to the Jews , “ If it were a matter of wrongdoing or vicious crime , O Jews , I would have reason to accept your complaint .
44018015	But since it is a matter of questions about words and names and your own law , see to it yourselves . I refuse to be a judge of these things . ”
44018016	And he drove them from the tribunal .
44018017	And they all seized Sosthenes , the ruler of the synagogue , and beat him in front of the tribunal . But Gallio paid no attention to any of this .
44018018	After this , Paul stayed many days longer and then took leave of the brothers and set sail for Syria , and with him Priscilla and Aquila . At Cenchreae he had cut his hair , for he was under a vow .
44018019	And they came to Ephesus , and he left them there , but he himself went into the synagogue and reasoned with the Jews .
44018020	When they asked him to stay for a longer period , he declined .
44018021	But on taking leave of them he said , “ I will return to you if God wills , ” and he set sail from Ephesus .
44018022	When he had landed at Caesarea , he went up and greeted the church , and then went down to Antioch .
44018023	After spending some time there , he departed and went from one place to the next through the region of Galatia and Phrygia , strengthening all the disciples .
44018024	Now a Jew named Apollos , a native of Alexandria , came to Ephesus . He was an eloquent man , competent in the Scriptures .
44018025	He had been instructed in the way of the Lord . And being fervent in spirit , he spoke and taught accurately the things concerning Jesus , though he knew only the baptism of John .
44018026	He began to speak boldly in the synagogue , but when Priscilla and Aquila heard him , they took him and explained to him the way of God more accurately .
44018027	And when he wished to cross to Achaia , the brothers encouraged him and wrote to the disciples to welcome him . When he arrived , he greatly helped those who through grace had believed ,
44018028	for he powerfully refuted the Jews in public , showing by the Scriptures that the Christ was Jesus .
44019001	And it happened that while Apollos was at Corinth , Paul passed through the inland country and came to Ephesus . There he found some disciples .
44019002	And he said to them , “ Did you receive the Holy Spirit when you believed ? ” And they said , “ No , we have not even heard that there is a Holy Spirit . ”
44019003	And he said , “ Into what then were you baptized ? ” They said , “ Into John’s baptism . ”
44019004	And Paul said , “ John baptized with the baptism of repentance , telling the people to believe in the one who was to come after him , that is , Jesus . ”
44019005	On hearing this , they were baptized in the name of the Lord Jesus .
44019006	And when Paul had laid his hands on them , the Holy Spirit came on them , and they began speaking in tongues and prophesying .
44019007	There were about twelve men in all .
44019008	And he entered the synagogue and for three months spoke boldly , reasoning and persuading them about the kingdom of God .
44019009	But when some became stubborn and continued in unbelief , speaking evil of the Way before the congregation , he withdrew from them and took the disciples with him , reasoning daily in the hall of Tyrannus .
44019010	This continued for two years , so that all the residents of Asia heard the word of the Lord , both Jews and Greeks .
44019011	And God was doing extraordinary miracles by the hands of Paul ,
44019012	so that even handkerchiefs or aprons that had touched his skin were carried away to the sick , and their diseases left them and the evil spirits came out of them .
44019013	Then some of the itinerant Jewish exorcists undertook to invoke the name of the Lord Jesus over those who had evil spirits , saying , “ I adjure you by the Jesus whom Paul proclaims . ”
44019014	Seven sons of a Jewish high priest named Sceva were doing this .
44019015	But the evil spirit answered them , “ Jesus I know , and Paul I recognize , but who are you ? ”
44019016	And the man in whom was the evil spirit leaped on them , mastered all of them and overpowered them , so that they fled out of that house naked and wounded .
44019017	And this became known to all the residents of Ephesus , both Jews and Greeks . And fear fell upon them all , and the name of the Lord Jesus was extolled .
44019018	Also many of those who were now believers came , confessing and divulging their practices .
44019019	And a number of those who had practiced magic arts brought their books together and burned them in the sight of all . And they counted the value of them and found it came to fifty thousand pieces of silver .
44019020	So the word of the Lord continued to increase and prevail mightily .
44019021	Now after these events Paul resolved in the Spirit to pass through Macedonia and Achaia and go to Jerusalem , saying , “ After I have been there , I must also see Rome . ”
44019022	And having sent into Macedonia two of his helpers , Timothy and Erastus , he himself stayed in Asia for a while .
44019023	About that time there arose no little disturbance concerning the Way .
44019024	For a man named Demetrius , a silversmith , who made silver shrines of Artemis , brought no little business to the craftsmen .
44019025	These he gathered together , with the workmen in similar trades , and said , “ Men , you know that from this business we have our wealth .
44019026	And you see and hear that not only in Ephesus but in almost all of Asia this Paul has persuaded and turned away a great many people , saying that gods made with hands are not gods .
44019027	And there is danger not only that this trade of ours may come into disrepute but also that the temple of the great goddess Artemis may be counted as nothing , and that she may even be deposed from her magnificence , she whom all Asia and the world worship . ”
44019028	When they heard this they were enraged and were crying out , “ Great is Artemis of the Ephesians ! ”
44019029	So the city was filled with the confusion , and they rushed together into the theater , dragging with them Gaius and Aristarchus , Macedonians who were Paul’s companions in travel .
44019030	But when Paul wished to go in among the crowd , the disciples would not let him .
44019031	And even some of the Asiarchs , who were friends of his , sent to him and were urging him not to venture into the theater .
44019032	Now some cried out one thing , some another , for the assembly was in confusion , and most of them did not know why they had come together .
44019033	Some of the crowd prompted Alexander , whom the Jews had put forward . And Alexander , motioning with his hand , wanted to make a defense to the crowd .
44019034	But when they recognized that he was a Jew , for about two hours they all cried out with one voice , “ Great is Artemis of the Ephesians ! ”
44019035	And when the town clerk had quieted the crowd , he said , “ Men of Ephesus , who is there who does not know that the city of the Ephesians is temple keeper of the great Artemis , and of the sacred stone that fell from the sky ?
44019036	Seeing then that these things cannot be denied , you ought to be quiet and do nothing rash .
44019037	For you have brought these men here who are neither sacrilegious nor blasphemers of our goddess .
44019038	If therefore Demetrius and the craftsmen with him have a complaint against anyone , the courts are open , and there are proconsuls . Let them bring charges against one another .
44019039	But if you seek anything further , it shall be settled in the regular assembly .
44019040	For we really are in danger of being charged with rioting today , since there is no cause that we can give to justify this commotion . ”
44019041	And when he had said these things , he dismissed the assembly .
44020001	After the uproar ceased , Paul sent for the disciples , and after encouraging them , he said farewell and departed for Macedonia .
44020002	When he had gone through those regions and had given them much encouragement , he came to Greece .
44020003	There he spent three months , and when a plot was made against him by the Jews as he was about to set sail for Syria , he decided to return through Macedonia .
44020004	Sopater the Berean , son of Pyrrhus , accompanied him ; and of the Thessalonians , Aristarchus and Secundus ; and Gaius of Derbe , and Timothy ; and the Asians , Tychicus and Trophimus .
44020005	These went on ahead and were waiting for us at Troas ,
44020006	but we sailed away from Philippi after the days of Unleavened Bread , and in five days we came to them at Troas , where we stayed for seven days .
44020007	On the first day of the week , when we were gathered together to break bread , Paul talked with them , intending to depart on the next day , and he prolonged his speech until midnight .
44020008	There were many lamps in the upper room where we were gathered .
44020009	And a young man named Eutychus , sitting at the window , sank into a deep sleep as Paul talked still longer . And being overcome by sleep , he fell down from the third story and was taken up dead .
44020010	But Paul went down and bent over him , and taking him in his arms , said , “ Do not be alarmed , for his life is in him . ”
44020011	And when Paul had gone up and had broken bread and eaten , he conversed with them a long while , until daybreak , and so departed .
44020012	And they took the youth away alive , and were not a little comforted .
44020013	But going ahead to the ship , we set sail for Assos , intending to take Paul aboard there , for so he had arranged , intending himself to go by land .
44020014	And when he met us at Assos , we took him on board and went to Mitylene .
44020015	And sailing from there we came the following day opposite Chios ; the next day we touched at Samos ; and the day after that we went to Miletus .
44020016	For Paul had decided to sail past Ephesus , so that he might not have to spend time in Asia , for he was hastening to be at Jerusalem , if possible , on the day of Pentecost .
44020017	Now from Miletus he sent to Ephesus and called the elders of the church to come to him .
44020018	And when they came to him , he said to them : “ You yourselves know how I lived among you the whole time from the first day that I set foot in Asia ,
44020019	serving the Lord with all humility and with tears and with trials that happened to me through the plots of the Jews ;
44020020	how I did not shrink from declaring to you anything that was profitable , and teaching you in public and from house to house ,
44020021	testifying both to Jews and to Greeks of repentance toward God and of faith in our Lord Jesus Christ .
44020022	And now , behold , I am going to Jerusalem , constrained bythe Spirit , not knowing what will happen to me there ,
44020023	except that the Holy Spirit testifies to me in every city that imprisonment and afflictions await me .
44020024	But I do not account my life of any value nor as precious to myself , if only I may finish my course and the ministry that I received from the Lord Jesus , to testify to the gospel of the grace of God .
44020025	And now , behold , I know that none of you among whom I have gone about proclaiming the kingdom will see my face again .
44020026	Therefore I testify to you this day that I am innocent of the blood of all of you ,
44020027	for I did not shrink from declaring to you the whole counsel of God .
44020028	Pay careful attention to yourselves and to all the flock , in which the Holy Spirit has made you overseers , to care for the church of God , which he obtained with his own blood .
44020029	I know that after my departure fierce wolves will come in among you , not sparing the flock ;
44020030	and from among your own selves will arise men speaking twisted things , to draw away the disciples after them .
44020031	Therefore be alert , remembering that for three years I did not cease night or day to admonish everyone with tears .
44020032	And now I commend you to God and to the word of his grace , which is able to build you up and to give you the inheritance among all those who are sanctified .
44020033	I coveted no one’s silver or gold or apparel .
44020034	You yourselves know that these hands ministered to my necessities and to those who were with me .
44020035	In all things I have shown you that by working hard in this way we must help the weak and remember the words of the Lord Jesus , how he himself said , ‘ It is more blessed to give than to receive . ’ ”
44020036	And when he had said these things , he knelt down and prayed with them all .
44020037	And there was much weeping on the part of all ; they embraced Paul and kissed him ,
44020038	being sorrowful most of all because of the word he had spoken , that they would not see his face again . And they accompanied him to the ship .
44021001	And when we had parted from them and set sail , we came by a straight course to Cos , and the next day to Rhodes , and from there to Patara .
44021002	And having found a ship crossing to Phoenicia , we went aboard and set sail .
44021003	When we had come in sight of Cyprus , leaving it on the left we sailed to Syria and landed at Tyre , for there the ship was to unload its cargo .
44021004	And having sought out the disciples , we stayed there for seven days . And through the Spirit they were telling Paul not to go on to Jerusalem .
44021005	When our days there were ended , we departed and went on our journey , and they all , with wives and children , accompanied us until we were outside the city . And kneeling down on the beach , we prayed
44021006	and said farewell to one another . Then we went on board the ship , and they returned home .
44021007	When we had finished the voyage from Tyre , we arrived at Ptolemais , and we greeted the brothers and stayed with them for one day .
44021008	On the next day we departed and came to Caesarea , and we entered the house of Philip the evangelist , who was one of the seven , and stayed with him .
44021009	He had four unmarried daughters , who prophesied .
44021010	While we were staying for many days , a prophet named Agabus came down from Judea .
44021011	And coming to us , he took Paul’s belt and bound his own feet and hands and said , “ Thus says the Holy Spirit , ‘ This is how the Jews at Jerusalem will bind the man who owns this belt and deliver him into the hands of the Gentiles . ’ ”
44021012	When we heard this , we and the people there urged him not to go up to Jerusalem .
44021013	Then Paul answered , “ What are you doing , weeping and breaking my heart ? For I am ready not only to be imprisoned but even to die in Jerusalem for the name of the Lord Jesus . ”
44021014	And since he would not be persuaded , we ceased and said , “ Let the will of the Lord be done . ”
44021015	After these days we got ready and went up to Jerusalem .
44021016	And some of the disciples from Caesarea went with us , bringing us to the house of Mnason of Cyprus , an early disciple , with whom we should lodge .
44021017	When we had come to Jerusalem , the brothers received us gladly .
44021018	On the following day Paul went in with us to James , and all the elders were present .
44021019	After greeting them , he related one by one the things that God had done among the Gentiles through his ministry .
44021020	And when they heard it , they glorified God . And they said to him , “ You see , brother , how many thousands there are among the Jews of those who have believed . They are all zealous for the law ,
44021021	and they have been told about you that you teach all the Jews who are among the Gentiles to forsake Moses , telling them not to circumcise their children or walk according to our customs .
44021022	What then is to be done ? They will certainly hear that you have come .
44021023	Do therefore what we tell you . We have four men who are under a vow ;
44021024	take these men and purify yourself along with them and pay their expenses , so that they may shave their heads . Thus all will know that there is nothing in what they have been told about you , but that you yourself also live in observance of the law .
44021025	But as for the Gentiles who have believed , we have sent a letter with our judgment that they should abstain from what has been sacrificed to idols , and from blood , and from what has been strangled , and from sexual immorality . ”
44021026	Then Paul took the men , and the next day he purified himself along with them and went into the temple , giving notice when the days of purification would be fulfilled and the offering presented for each one of them .
44021027	When the seven days were almost completed , the Jews from Asia , seeing him in the temple , stirred up the whole crowd and laid hands on him ,
44021028	crying out , “ Men of Israel , help ! This is the man who is teaching everyone everywhere against the people and the law and this place . Moreover , he even brought Greeks into the temple and has defiled this holy place . ”
44021029	For they had previously seen Trophimus the Ephesian with him in the city , and they supposed that Paul had brought him into the temple .
44021030	Then all the city was stirred up , and the people ran together . They seized Paul and dragged him out of the temple , and at once the gates were shut .
44021031	And as they were seeking to kill him , word came to the tribune of the cohort that all Jerusalem was in confusion .
44021032	He at once took soldiers and centurions and ran down to them . And when they saw the tribune and the soldiers , they stopped beating Paul .
44021033	Then the tribune came up and arrested him and ordered him to be bound with two chains . He inquired who he was and what he had done .
44021034	Some in the crowd were shouting one thing , some another . And as he could not learn the facts because of the uproar , he ordered him to be brought into the barracks .
44021035	And when he came to the steps , he was actually carried by the soldiers because of the violence of the crowd ,
44021036	for the mob of the people followed , crying out , “ Away with him ! ”
44021037	As Paul was about to be brought into the barracks , he said to the tribune , “ May I say something to you ? ” And he said , “ Do you know Greek ?
44021038	Are you not the Egyptian , then , who recently stirred up a revolt and led the four thousand men of the Assassins out into the wilderness ? ”
44021039	Paul replied , “ I am a Jew , from Tarsus in Cilicia , a citizen of no obscure city . I beg you , permit me to speak to the people . ”
44021040	And when he had given him permission , Paul , standing on the steps , motioned with his hand to the people . And when there was a great hush , he addressed them in the Hebrew language , saying :
44022001	“ Brothers and fathers , hear the defense that I now make before you . ”
44022002	And when they heard that he was addressing them in the Hebrew language , they became even more quiet . And he said :
44022003	“ I am a Jew , born in Tarsus in Cilicia , but brought up in this city , educated at the feet of Gamaliel according to the strict manner of the law of our fathers , being zealous for God as all of you are this day .
44022004	I persecuted this Way to the death , binding and delivering to prison both men and women ,
44022005	as the high priest and the whole council of elders can bear me witness . From them I received letters to the brothers , and I journeyed toward Damascus to take those also who were there and bring them in bonds to Jerusalem to be punished .
44022006	“ As I was on my way and drew near to Damascus , about noon a great light from heaven suddenly shone around me .
44022007	And I fell to the ground and heard a voice saying to me , ‘ Saul , Saul , why are you persecuting me ? ’
44022008	And I answered , ‘ Who are you , Lord ? ’ And he said to me , ‘ I am Jesus of Nazareth , whom you are persecuting . ’
44022009	Now those who were with me saw the light but did not understand the voice of the one who was speaking to me .
44022010	And I said , ‘ What shall I do , Lord ? ’ And the Lord said to me , ‘ Rise , and go into Damascus , and there you will be told all that is appointed for you to do . ’
44022011	And since I could not see because of the brightness of that light , I was led by the hand by those who were with me , and came into Damascus .
44022012	“ And one Ananias , a devout man according to the law , well spoken of by all the Jews who lived there ,
44022013	came to me , and standing by me said to me , ‘ Brother Saul , receive your sight . ’ And at that very hour I received my sight and saw him .
44022014	And he said , ‘ The God of our fathers appointed you to know his will , to see the Righteous One and to hear a voice from his mouth ;
44022015	for you will be a witness for him to everyone of what you have seen and heard .
44022016	And now why do you wait ? Rise and be baptized and wash away your sins , calling on his name . ’
44022017	“ When I had returned to Jerusalem and was praying in the temple , I fell into a trance
44022018	and saw him saying to me , ‘ Make haste and get out of Jerusalem quickly , because they will not accept your testimony about me . ’
44022019	And I said , ‘ Lord , they themselves know that in one synagogue after another I imprisoned and beat those who believed in you .
44022020	And when the blood of Stephen your witness was being shed , I myself was standing by and approving and watching over the garments of those who killed him . ’
44022021	And he said to me , ‘ Go , for I will send you far away to the Gentiles . ’ ”
44022022	Up to this word they listened to him . Then they raised their voices and said , “ Away with such a fellow from the earth ! For he should not be allowed to live . ”
44022023	And as they were shouting and throwing off their cloaks and flinging dust into the air ,
44022024	the tribune ordered him to be brought into the barracks , saying that he should be examined by flogging , to find out why they were shouting against him like this .
44022025	But when they had stretched him out for the whips , Paul said to the centurion who was standing by , “ Is it lawful for you to flog a man who is a Roman citizen and uncondemned ? ”
44022026	When the centurion heard this , he went to the tribune and said to him , “ What are you about to do ? For this man is a Roman citizen . ”
44022027	So the tribune came and said to him , “ Tell me , are you a Roman citizen ? ” And he said , “ Yes . ”
44022028	The tribune answered , “ I bought this citizenship for a large sum . ” Paul said , “ But I am a citizen by birth . ”
44022029	So those who were about to examine him withdrew from him immediately , and the tribune also was afraid , for he realized that Paul was a Roman citizen and that he had bound him .
44022030	But on the next day , desiring to know the real reason why he was being accused by the Jews , he unbound him and commanded the chief priests and all the council to meet , and he brought Paul down and set him before them .
44023001	And looking intently at the council , Paul said , “ Brothers , I have lived my life before God in all good conscience up to this day . ”
44023002	And the high priest Ananias commanded those who stood by him to strike him on the mouth .
44023003	Then Paul said to him , “ God is going to strike you , you whitewashed wall ! Are you sitting to judge me according to the law , and yet contrary to the law you order me to be struck ? ”
44023004	Those who stood by said , “ Would you revile God’s high priest ? ”
44023005	And Paul said , “ I did not know , brothers , that he was the high priest , for it is written , ‘ You shall not speak evil of a ruler of your people . ’ ”
44023006	Now when Paul perceived that one part were Sadducees and the other Pharisees , he cried out in the council , “ Brothers , I am a Pharisee , a son of Pharisees . It is with respect to the hope and the resurrection of the dead that I am on trial . ”
44023007	And when he had said this , a dissension arose between the Pharisees and the Sadducees , and the assembly was divided .
44023008	For the Sadducees say that there is no resurrection , nor angel , nor spirit , but the Pharisees acknowledge them all .
44023009	Then a great clamor arose , and some of the scribes of the Pharisees ’ party stood up and contended sharply , “ We find nothing wrong in this man . What if a spirit or an angel spoke to him ? ”
44023010	And when the dissension became violent , the tribune , afraid that Paul would be torn to pieces by them , commanded the soldiers to go down and take him away from among them by force and bring him into the barracks .
44023011	The following night the Lord stood by him and said , “ Take courage , for as you have testified to the facts about me in Jerusalem , so you must testify also in Rome . ”
44023012	When it was day , the Jews made a plot and bound themselves by an oath neither to eat nor drink till they had killed Paul .
44023013	There were more than forty who made this conspiracy .
44023014	They went to the chief priests and elders and said , “ We have strictly bound ourselves by an oath to taste no food till we have killed Paul .
44023015	Now therefore you , along with the council , give notice to the tribune to bring him down to you , as though you were going to determine his case more exactly . And we are ready to kill him before he comes near . ”
44023016	Now the son of Paul’s sister heard of their ambush , so he went and entered the barracks and told Paul .
44023017	Paul called one of the centurions and said , “ Take this young man to the tribune , for he has something to tell him . ”
44023018	So he took him and brought him to the tribune and said , “ Paul the prisoner called me and asked me to bring this young man to you , as he has something to say to you . ”
44023019	The tribune took him by the hand , and going aside asked him privately , “ What is it that you have to tell me ? ”
44023020	And he said , “ The Jews have agreed to ask you to bring Paul down to the council tomorrow , as though they were going to inquire somewhat more closely about him .
44023021	But do not be persuaded by them , for more than forty of their men are lying in ambush for him , who have bound themselves by an oath neither to eat nor drink till they have killed him . And now they are ready , waiting for your consent . ”
44023022	So the tribune dismissed the young man , charging him , “ Tell no one that you have informed me of these things . ”
44023023	Then he called two of the centurions and said , “ Get ready two hundred soldiers , with seventy horsemen and two hundred spearmen to go as far as Caesarea at the third hour of the night .
44023024	Also provide mounts for Paul to ride and bring him safely to Felix the governor . ”
44023025	And he wrote a letter to this effect :
44023026	“ Claudius Lysias , to his Excellency the governor Felix , greetings .
44023027	This man was seized by the Jews and was about to be killed by them when I came upon them with the soldiers and rescued him , having learned that he was a Roman citizen .
44023028	And desiring to know the charge for which they were accusing him , I brought him down to their council .
44023029	I found that he was being accused about questions of their law , but charged with nothing deserving death or imprisonment .
44023030	And when it was disclosed to me that there would be a plot against the man , I sent him to you at once , ordering his accusers also to state before you what they have against him . ”
44023031	So the soldiers , according to their instructions , took Paul and brought him by night to Antipatris .
44023032	And on the next day they returned to the barracks , letting the horsemen go on with him .
44023033	When they had come to Caesarea and delivered the letter to the governor , they presented Paul also before him .
44023034	On reading the letter , he asked what province he was from . And when he learned that he was from Cilicia ,
44023035	he said , “ I will give you a hearing when your accusers arrive . ” And he commanded him to be guarded in Herod’s praetorium .
44024001	And after five days the high priest Ananias came down with some elders and a spokesman , one Tertullus . They laid before the governor their case against Paul .
44024002	And when he had been summoned , Tertullus began to accuse him , saying : “ Since through you we enjoy much peace , and since by your foresight , most excellent Felix , reforms are being made for this nation ,
44024003	in every way and everywhere we accept this with all gratitude .
44024004	But , to detainyou no further , I beg you in your kindness to hear us briefly .
44024005	For we have found this man a plague , one who stirs up riots among all the Jews throughout the world and is a ringleader of the sect of the Nazarenes .
44024006	He even tried to profane the temple , but we seized him .
44024008	By examining him yourself you will be able to find out from him about everything of which we accuse him . ”
44024009	The Jews also joined in the charge , affirming that all these things were so .
44024010	And when the governor had nodded to him to speak , Paul replied : “ Knowing that for many years you have been a judge over this nation , I cheerfully make my defense .
44024011	You can verify that it is not more than twelve days since I went up to worship in Jerusalem ,
44024012	and they did not find me disputing with anyone or stirring up a crowd , either in the temple or in the synagogues or in the city .
44024013	Neither can they prove to you what they now bring up against me .
44024014	But this I confess to you , that according to the Way , which they call a sect , I worship the God of our fathers , believing everything laid down by the Law and written in the Prophets ,
44024015	having a hope in God , which these men themselves accept , that there will be a resurrection of both the just and the unjust .
44024016	So I always take pains to have a clear conscience toward both God and man .
44024017	Now after several years I came to bring alms to my nation and to present offerings .
44024018	While I was doing this , they found me purified in the temple , without any crowd or tumult . But some Jews from Asia —
44024019	they ought to be here before you and to make an accusation , should they have anything against me .
44024020	Or else let these men themselves say what wrongdoing they found when I stood before the council ,
44024021	other than this one thing that I cried out while standing among them : ‘ It is with respect to the resurrection of the dead that I am on trial before you this day . ’ ”
44024022	But Felix , having a rather accurate knowledge of the Way , put them off , saying , “ When Lysias the tribune comes down , I will decide your case . ”
44024023	Then he gave orders to the centurion that he should be kept in custody but have some liberty , and that none of his friends should be prevented from attending to his needs .
44024024	After some days Felix came with his wife Drusilla , who was Jewish , and he sent for Paul and heard him speak about faith in Christ Jesus .
44024025	And as he reasoned about righteousness and self-control and the coming judgment , Felix was alarmed and said , “ Go away for the present . When I get an opportunity I will summon you . ”
44024026	At the same time he hoped that money would be given him by Paul . So he sent for him often and conversed with him .
44024027	When two years had elapsed , Felix was succeeded by Porcius Festus . And desiring to do the Jews a favor , Felix left Paul in prison .
44025001	Now three days after Festus had arrived in the province , he went up to Jerusalem from Caesarea .
44025002	And the chief priests and the principal men of the Jews laid out their case against Paul , and they urged him ,
44025003	asking as a favor against Paul that he summon him to Jerusalem — because they were planning an ambush to kill him on the way .
44025004	Festus replied that Paul was being kept at Caesarea and that he himself intended to go there shortly .
44025005	“ So , ” said he , “ let the men of authority among you go down with me , and if there is anything wrong about the man , let them bring charges against him . ”
44025006	After he stayed among them not more than eight or ten days , he went down to Caesarea . And the next day he took his seat on the tribunal and ordered Paul to be brought .
44025007	When he had arrived , the Jews who had come down from Jerusalem stood around him , bringing many and serious charges against him that they could not prove .
44025008	Paul argued in his defense , “ Neither against the law of the Jews , nor against the temple , nor against Caesar have I committed any offense . ”
44025009	But Festus , wishing to do the Jews a favor , said to Paul , “ Do you wish to go up to Jerusalem and there be tried on these charges before me ? ”
44025010	But Paul said , “ I am standing before Caesar’s tribunal , where I ought to be tried . To the Jews I have done no wrong , as you yourself know very well .
44025011	If then I am a wrongdoer and have committed anything for which I deserve to die , I do not seek to escape death . But if there is nothing to their charges against me , no one can give me up to them . I appeal to Caesar . ”
44025012	Then Festus , when he had conferred with his council , answered , “ To Caesar you have appealed ; to Caesar you shall go . ”
44025013	Now when some days had passed , Agrippa the king and Bernice arrived at Caesarea and greeted Festus .
44025014	And as they stayed there many days , Festus laid Paul’s case before the king , saying , “ There is a man left prisoner by Felix ,
44025015	and when I was at Jerusalem , the chief priests and the elders of the Jews laid out their case against him , asking for a sentence of condemnation against him .
44025016	I answered them that it was not the custom of the Romans to give up anyone before the accused met the accusers face to face and had opportunity to make his defense concerning the charge laid against him .
44025017	So when they came together here , I made no delay , but on the next day took my seat on the tribunal and ordered the man to be brought .
44025018	When the accusers stood up , they brought no charge in his case of such evils as I supposed .
44025019	Rather they had certain points of dispute with him about their own religion and about a certain Jesus , who was dead , but whom Paul asserted to be alive .
44025020	Being at a loss how to investigate these questions , I asked whether he wanted to go to Jerusalem and be tried there regarding them .
44025021	But when Paul had appealed to be kept in custody for the decision of the emperor , I ordered him to be held until I could send him to Caesar . ”
44025022	Then Agrippa said to Festus , “ I would like to hear the man myself . ” “ Tomorrow , ” said he , “ you will hear him . ”
44025023	So on the next day Agrippa and Bernice came with great pomp , and they entered the audience hall with the military tribunes and the prominent men of the city . Then , at the command of Festus , Paul was brought in .
44025024	And Festus said , “ King Agrippa and all who are present with us , you see this man about whom the whole Jewish people petitioned me , both in Jerusalem and here , shouting that he ought not to live any longer .
44025025	But I found that he had done nothing deserving death . And as he himself appealed to the emperor , I decided to go ahead and send him .
44025026	But I have nothing definite to write to my lord about him . Therefore I have brought him before you all , and especially before you , King Agrippa , so that , after we have examined him , I may have something to write .
44025027	For it seems to me unreasonable , in sending a prisoner , not to indicate the charges against him . ”
44026001	So Agrippa said to Paul , “ You have permission to speak for yourself . ” Then Paul stretched out his hand and made his defense :
44026002	“ I consider myself fortunate that it is before you , King Agrippa , I am going to make my defense today against all the accusations of the Jews ,
44026003	especially because you are familiar with all the customs and controversies of the Jews . Therefore I beg you to listen to me patiently .
44026004	“ My manner of life from my youth , spent from the beginning among my own nation and in Jerusalem , is known by all the Jews .
44026005	They have known for a long time , if they are willing to testify , that according to the strictest party of our religion I have lived as a Pharisee .
44026006	And now I stand here on trial because of my hope in the promise made by God to our fathers ,
44026007	to which our twelve tribes hope to attain , as they earnestly worship night and day . And for this hope I am accused by Jews , O king !
44026008	Why is it thought incredible by any of you that God raises the dead ?
44026009	“ I myself was convinced that I ought to do many things in opposing the name of Jesus of Nazareth .
44026010	And I did so in Jerusalem . I not only locked up many of the saints in prison after receiving authority from the chief priests , but when they were put to death I cast my vote against them .
44026011	And I punished them often in all the synagogues and tried to make them blaspheme , and in raging fury against them I persecuted them even to foreign cities .
44026012	“ In this connection I journeyed to Damascus with the authority and commission of the chief priests .
44026013	At midday , O king , I saw on the way a light from heaven , brighter than the sun , that shone around me and those who journeyed with me .
44026014	And when we had all fallen to the ground , I heard a voice saying to me in the Hebrew language , ‘ Saul , Saul , why are you persecuting me ? It is hard for you to kick against the goads . ’
44026015	And I said , ‘ Who are you , Lord ? ’ And the Lord said , ‘ I am Jesus whom you are persecuting .
44026016	But rise and stand upon your feet , for I have appeared to you for this purpose , to appoint you as a servant and witness to the things in which you have seen me and to those in which I will appear to you ,
44026017	delivering you from your people and from the Gentiles — to whom I am sending you
44026018	to open their eyes , so that they may turn from darkness to light and from the power of Satan to God , that they may receive forgiveness of sins and a place among those who are sanctified by faith in me . ’
44026019	“ Therefore , O King Agrippa , I was not disobedient to the heavenly vision ,
44026020	but declared first to those in Damascus , then in Jerusalem and throughout all the region of Judea , and also to the Gentiles , that they should repent and turn to God , performing deeds in keeping with their repentance .
44026021	For this reason the Jews seized me in the temple and tried to kill me .
44026022	To this day I have had the help that comes from God , and so I stand here testifying both to small and great , saying nothing but what the prophets and Moses said would come to pass :
44026023	that the Christ must suffer and that , by being the first to rise from the dead , he would proclaim light both to our people and to the Gentiles . ”
44026024	And as he was saying these things in his defense , Festus said with a loud voice , “ Paul , you are out of your mind ; your great learning is driving you out of your mind . ”
44026025	But Paul said , “ I am not out of my mind , most excellent Festus , but I am speaking true and rational words .
44026026	For the king knows about these things , and to him I speak boldly . For I am persuaded that none of these things has escaped his notice , for this has not been done in a corner .
44026027	King Agrippa , do you believe the prophets ? I know that you believe . ”
44026028	And Agrippa said to Paul , “ In a short time would you persuade me to be a Christian ? ”
44026029	And Paul said , “ Whether short or long , I would to God that not only you but also all who hear me this day might become such as I am — except for these chains . ”
44026030	Then the king rose , and the governor and Bernice and those who were sitting with them .
44026031	And when they had withdrawn , they said to one another , “ This man is doing nothing to deserve death or imprisonment . ”
44026032	And Agrippa said to Festus , “ This man could have been set free if he had not appealed to Caesar . ”
44027001	And when it was decided that we should sail for Italy , they delivered Paul and some other prisoners to a centurion of the Augustan Cohort named Julius .
44027002	And embarking in a ship of Adramyttium , which was about to sail to the ports along the coast of Asia , we put to sea , accompanied by Aristarchus , a Macedonian from Thessalonica .
44027003	The next day we put in at Sidon . And Julius treated Paul kindly and gave him leave to go to his friends and be cared for .
44027004	And putting out to sea from there we sailed under the lee of Cyprus , because the winds were against us .
44027005	And when we had sailed across the open sea along the coast of Cilicia and Pamphylia , we came to Myra in Lycia .
44027006	There the centurion found a ship of Alexandria sailing for Italy and put us on board .
44027007	We sailed slowly for a number of days and arrived with difficulty off Cnidus , and as the wind did not allow us to go farther , we sailed under the lee of Crete off Salmone .
44027008	Coasting along it with difficulty , we came to a place called Fair Havens , near which was the city of Lasea .
44027009	Since much time had passed , and the voyage was now dangerous because even the Fast was already over , Paul advised them ,
44027010	saying , “ Sirs , I perceive that the voyage will be with injury and much loss , not only of the cargo and the ship , but also of our lives . ”
44027011	But the centurion paid more attention to the pilot and to the owner of the ship than to what Paul said .
44027012	And because the harbor was not suitable to spend the winter in , the majority decided to put out to sea from there , on the chance that somehow they could reach Phoenix , a harbor of Crete , facing both southwest and northwest , and spend the winter there .
44027013	Now when the south wind blew gently , supposing that they had obtained their purpose , they weighed anchor and sailed along Crete , close to the shore .
44027014	But soon a tempestuous wind , called the northeaster , struck down from the land .
44027015	And when the ship was caught and could not face the wind , we gave way to it and were driven along .
44027016	Running under the lee of a small island called Cauda , we managed with difficulty to secure the ship’s boat .
44027017	After hoisting it up , they used supports to undergird the ship . Then , fearing that they would run aground on the Syrtis , they lowered the gear , and thus they were driven along .
44027018	Since we were violently storm-tossed , they began the next day to jettison the cargo .
44027019	And on the third day they threw the ship’s tackle overboard with their own hands .
44027020	When neither sun nor stars appeared for many days , and no small tempest lay on us , all hope of our being saved was at last abandoned .
44027021	Since they had been without food for a long time , Paul stood up among them and said , “ Men , you should have listened to me and not have set sail from Crete and incurred this injury and loss .
44027022	Yet now I urge you to take heart , for there will be no loss of life among you , but only of the ship .
44027023	For this very night there stood before me an angel of the God to whom I belong and whom I worship ,
44027024	and he said , ‘ Do not be afraid , Paul ; you must stand before Caesar . And behold , God has granted you all those who sail with you . ’
44027025	So take heart , men , for I have faith in God that it will be exactly as I have been told .
44027026	But we must run aground on some island . ”
44027027	When the fourteenth night had come , as we were being driven across the Adriatic Sea , about midnight the sailors suspected that they were nearing land .
44027028	So they took a sounding and found twenty fathoms . A little farther on they took a sounding again and found fifteen fathoms .
44027029	And fearing that we might run on the rocks , they let down four anchors from the stern and prayed for day to come .
44027030	And as the sailors were seeking to escape from the ship , and had lowered the ship’s boat into the sea under pretense of laying out anchors from the bow ,
44027031	Paul said to the centurion and the soldiers , “ Unless these men stay in the ship , you cannot be saved . ”
44027032	Then the soldiers cut away the ropes of the ship’s boat and let it go .
44027033	As day was about to dawn , Paul urged them all to take some food , saying , “ Today is the fourteenth day that you have continued in suspense and without food , having taken nothing .
44027034	Therefore I urge you to take some food . For it will give you strength , for not a hair is to perish from the head of any of you . ”
44027035	And when he had said these things , he took bread , and giving thanks to God in the presence of all he broke it and began to eat .
44027036	Then they all were encouraged and ate some food themselves .
44027037	( We were in all 276 persons in the ship .
44027038	And when they had eaten enough , they lightened the ship , throwing out the wheat into the sea .
44027039	Now when it was day , they did not recognize the land , but they noticed a bay with a beach , on which they planned if possible to run the ship ashore .
44027040	So they cast off the anchors and left them in the sea , at the same time loosening the ropes that tied the rudders . Then hoisting the foresail to the wind they made for the beach .
44027041	But striking a reef , they ran the vessel aground . The bow stuck and remained immovable , and the stern was being broken up by the surf .
44027042	The soldiers ’ plan was to kill the prisoners , lest any should swim away and escape .
44027043	But the centurion , wishing to save Paul , kept them from carrying out their plan . He ordered those who could swim to jump overboard first and make for the land ,
44027044	and the rest on planks or on pieces of the ship . And so it was that all were brought safely to land .
44028001	After we were brought safely through , we then learned that the island was called Malta .
44028002	The native people showed us unusual kindness , for they kindled a fire and welcomed us all , because it had begun to rain and was cold .
44028003	When Paul had gathered a bundle of sticks and put them on the fire , a viper came out because of the heat and fastened on his hand .
44028004	When the native people saw the creature hanging from his hand , they said to one another , “ No doubt this man is a murderer . Though he has escaped from the sea , Justice has not allowed him to live . ”
44028005	He , however , shook off the creature into the fire and suffered no harm .
44028006	They were waiting for him to swell up or suddenly fall down dead . But when they had waited a long time and saw no misfortune come to him , they changed their minds and said that he was a god .
44028007	Now in the neighborhood of that place were lands belonging to the chief man of the island , named Publius , who received us and entertained us hospitably for three days .
44028008	It happened that the father of Publius lay sick with fever and dysentery . And Paul visited him and prayed , and putting his hands on him healed him .
44028009	And when this had taken place , the rest of the people on the island who had diseases also came and were cured .
44028010	They also honored us greatly , and when we were about to sail , they put on board whatever we needed .
44028011	After three months we set sail in a ship that had wintered in the island , a ship of Alexandria , with the twin gods as a figurehead .
44028012	Putting in at Syracuse , we stayed there for three days .
44028013	And from there we made a circuit and arrived at Rhegium . And after one day a south wind sprang up , and on the second day we came to Puteoli .
44028014	There we found brothers and were invited to stay with them for seven days . And so we came to Rome .
44028015	And the brothers there , when they heard about us , came as far as the Forum of Appius and Three Taverns to meet us . On seeing them , Paul thanked God and took courage .
44028016	And when we came into Rome , Paul was allowed to stay by himself , with the soldier that guarded him .
44028017	After three days he called together the local leaders of the Jews , and when they had gathered , he said to them , “ Brothers , though I had done nothing against our people or the customs of our fathers , yet I was delivered as a prisoner from Jerusalem into the hands of the Romans .
44028018	When they had examined me , they wished to set me at liberty , because there was no reason for the death penalty in my case .
44028019	But because the Jews objected , I was compelled to appeal to Caesar — though I had no charge to bring against my nation .
44028020	For this reason , therefore , I have asked to see you and speak with you , since it is because of the hope of Israel that I am wearing this chain . ”
