44028021	And they said to him , “ We have received no letters from Judea about you , and none of the brothers coming here has reported or spoken any evil about you .
44028022	But we desire to hear from you what your views are , for with regard to this sect we know that everywhere it is spoken against . ”
44028023	When they had appointed a day for him , they came to him at his lodging in greater numbers . From morning till evening he expounded to them , testifying to the kingdom of God and trying to convince them about Jesus both from the Law of Moses and from the Prophets .
44028024	And some were convinced by what he said , but others disbelieved .
44028025	And disagreeing among themselves , they departed after Paul had made one statement : “ The Holy Spirit was right in saying to your fathers through Isaiah the prophet :
44028026	“ ‘ Go to this people , and say , You will indeed hear but never understand , and you will indeed see but never perceive .
44028027	For this people’s heart has grown dull , and with their ears they can barely hear , and their eyes they have closed ; lest they should see with their eyes and hear with their ears and understand with their heart and turn , and I would heal them . ’
44028028	Therefore let it be known to you that this salvation of God has been sent to the Gentiles ; they will listen . ”
44028030	He lived there two whole years at his own expense , and welcomed all who came to him ,
44028031	proclaiming the kingdom of God and teaching about the Lord Jesus Christ with all boldness and without hindrance .
45001001	Paul , a servant of Christ Jesus , called to be an apostle , set apart for the gospel of God ,
45001002	which he promised beforehand through his prophets in the holy Scriptures ,
45001003	concerning his Son , who was descended from David according to the flesh
45001004	and was declared to be the Son of God in power according to the Spirit of holiness by his resurrection from the dead , Jesus Christ our Lord ,
45001005	through whom we have received grace and apostleship to bring about the obedience of faith for the sake of his name among all the nations ,
45001006	including you who are called to belong to Jesus Christ ,
45001007	To all those in Rome who are loved by God and called to be saints : Grace to you and peace from God our Father and the Lord Jesus Christ .
45001008	First , I thank my God through Jesus Christ for all of you , because your faith is proclaimed in all the world .
45001009	For God is my witness , whom I serve with my spirit in the gospel of his Son , that without ceasing I mention you
45001010	always in my prayers , asking that somehow by God’s will I may now at last succeed in coming to you .
45001011	For I long to see you , that I may impart to you some spiritual gift to strengthen you —
45001012	that is , that we may be mutually encouraged by each other’s faith , both yours and mine .
45001013	I want you to know , brothers , that I have often intended to come to you ( but thus far have been prevented ) , in order that I may reap some harvest among you as well as among the rest of the Gentiles .
45001014	I am under obligation both to Greeks and to barbarians , both to the wise and to the foolish .
45001015	So I am eager to preach the gospel to you also who are in Rome .
45001016	For I am not ashamed of the gospel , for it is the power of God for salvation to everyone who believes , to the Jew first and also to the Greek .
45001017	For in it the righteousness of God is revealed from faith for faith , as it is written , “ The righteous shall live by faith . ”
45001018	For the wrath of God is revealed from heaven against all ungodliness and unrighteousness of men , who by their unrighteousness suppress the truth .
45001019	For what can be known about God is plain to them , because God has shown it to them .
45001020	For his invisible attributes , namely , his eternal power and divine nature , have been clearly perceived , ever since the creation of the world , in the things that have been made . So they are without excuse .
45001021	For although they knew God , they did not honor him as God or give thanks to him , but they became futile in their thinking , and their foolish hearts were darkened .
45001022	Claiming to be wise , they became fools ,
45001023	and exchanged the glory of the immortal God for images resembling mortal man and birds and animals and creeping things .
45001024	Therefore God gave them up in the lusts of their hearts to impurity , to the dishonoring of their bodies among themselves ,
45001025	because they exchanged the truth about God for a lie and worshiped and served the creature rather than the Creator , who is blessed forever ! Amen .
45001026	For this reason God gave them up to dishonorable passions . For their women exchanged natural relations for those that are contrary to nature ;
45001027	and the men likewise gave up natural relations with women and were consumed with passion for one another , men committing shameless acts with men and receiving in themselves the due penalty for their error .
45001028	And since they did not see fit to acknowledge God , God gave them up to a debased mind to do what ought not to be done .
45001029	They were filled with all manner of unrighteousness , evil , covetousness , malice . They are full of envy , murder , strife , deceit , maliciousness . They are gossips ,
45001030	slanderers , haters of God , insolent , haughty , boastful , inventors of evil , disobedient to parents ,
45001031	foolish , faithless , heartless , ruthless .
45001032	Though they know God’s decree that those who practice such things deserve to die , they not only do them but give approval to those who practice them .
45002001	Therefore you have no excuse , O man , every one of you who judges . For in passing judgment on another you condemn yourself , because you , the judge , practice the very same things .
45002002	We know that the judgment of God rightly falls on those who practice such things .
45002003	Do you suppose , O man — you who judge those who practice such things and yet do them yourself — that you will escape the judgment of God ?
45002004	Or do you presume on the riches of his kindness and forbearance and patience , not knowing that God’s kindness is meant to lead you to repentance ?
45002005	But because of your hard and impenitent heart you are storing up wrath for yourself on the day of wrath when God’s righteous judgment will be revealed .
45002006	He will render to each one according to his works :
45002007	to those who by patience in well-doing seek for glory and honor and immortality , he will give eternal life ;
45002008	but for those who are self-seeking and do not obey the truth , but obey unrighteousness , there will be wrath and fury .
45002009	There will be tribulation and distress for every human being who does evil , the Jew first and also the Greek ,
45002010	but glory and honor and peace for everyone who does good , the Jew first and also the Greek .
45002011	For God shows no partiality .
45002012	For all who have sinned without the law will also perish without the law , and all who have sinned under the law will be judged by the law .
45002013	For it is not the hearers of the law who are righteous before God , but the doers of the law who will be justified .
45002014	For when Gentiles , who do not have the law , by nature do what the law requires , they are a law to themselves , even though they do not have the law .
45002015	They show that the work of the law is written on their hearts , while their conscience also bears witness , and their conflicting thoughts accuse or even excuse them
45002016	on that day when , according to my gospel , God judges the secrets of men by Christ Jesus .
45002017	But if you call yourself a Jew and rely on the law and boast in God
45002018	and know his will and approve what is excellent , because you are instructed from the law ;
45002019	and if you are sure that you yourself are a guide to the blind , a light to those who are in darkness ,
45002020	an instructor of the foolish , a teacher of children , having in the law the embodiment of knowledge and truth —
45002021	you then who teach others , do you not teach yourself ? While you preach against stealing , do you steal ?
45002022	You who say that one must not commit adultery , do you commit adultery ? You who abhor idols , do you rob temples ?
45002023	You who boast in the law dishonor God by breaking the law .
45002024	For , as it is written , “ The name of God is blasphemed among the Gentiles because of you . ”
45002025	For circumcision indeed is of value if you obey the law , but if you break the law , your circumcision becomes uncircumcision .
45002026	So , if a man who is uncircumcised keeps the precepts of the law , will not his uncircumcision be regarded as circumcision ?
45002027	Then he who is physically uncircumcised but keeps the law will condemn you who have the written code and circumcision but break the law .
45002028	For no one is a Jew who is merely one outwardly , nor is circumcision outward and physical .
45002029	But a Jew is one inwardly , and circumcision is a matter of the heart , by the Spirit , not by the letter . His praise is not from man but from God .
45003001	Then what advantage has the Jew ? Or what is the value of circumcision ?
45003002	Much in every way . To begin with , the Jews were entrusted with the oracles of God .
45003003	What if some were unfaithful ? Does their faithlessness nullify the faithfulness of God ?
45003004	By no means ! Let God be true though every one were a liar , as it is written , “ That you may be justified in your words , and prevail when you are judged . ”
45003005	But if our unrighteousness serves to show the righteousness of God , what shall we say ? That God is unrighteous to inflict wrath on us ? ( I speak in a human way .
45003006	By no means ! For then how could God judge the world ?
45003007	But if through my lie God’s truth abounds to his glory , why am I still being condemned as a sinner ?
45003008	And why not do evil that good may come ? — as some people slanderously charge us with saying . Their condemnation is just .
45003009	What then ? Are we Jews any better off ? No , not at all . For we have already charged that all , both Jews and Greeks , are under sin ,
45003010	as it is written : “ None is righteous , no , not one ;
45003011	no one understands ; no one seeks for God .
45003012	All have turned aside ; together they have become worthless ; no one does good , not even one . ”
45003013	“ Their throat is an open grave ; they use their tongues to deceive . ” “ The venom of asps is under their lips . ”
45003014	“ Their mouth is full of curses and bitterness . ”
45003015	“ Their feet are swift to shed blood ;
45003016	in their paths are ruin and misery ,
45003017	and the way of peace they have not known . ”
45003018	“ There is no fear of God before their eyes . ”
45003019	Now we know that whatever the law says it speaks to those who are under the law , so that every mouth may be stopped , and the whole world may be held accountable to God .
45003020	For by works of the law no human being will be justified in his sight , since through the law comes knowledge of sin .
45003021	But now the righteousness of God has been manifested apart from the law , although the Law and the Prophets bear witness to it —
45003022	the righteousness of God through faith in Jesus Christ for all who believe . For there is no distinction :
45003023	for all have sinned and fall short of the glory of God ,
45003024	and are justified by his grace as a gift , through the redemption that is in Christ Jesus ,
45003025	whom God put forward as a propitiation by his blood , to be received by faith . This was to show God’s righteousness , because in his divine forbearance he had passed over former sins .
45003026	It was to show his righteousness at the present time , so that he might be just and the justifier of the one who has faith in Jesus .
45003027	Then what becomes of our boasting ? It is excluded . By what kind of law ? By a law of works ? No , but by the law of faith .
45003028	For we hold that one is justified by faith apart from works of the law .
45003029	Or is God the God of Jews only ? Is he not the God of Gentiles also ? Yes , of Gentiles also ,
45003030	since God is one — who will justify the circumcised by faith and the uncircumcised through faith .
45003031	Do we then overthrow the law by this faith ? By no means ! On the contrary , we uphold the law .
45004001	What then shall we say was gained by Abraham , our forefather according to the flesh ?
45004002	For if Abraham was justified by works , he has something to boast about , but not before God .
45004003	For what does the Scripture say ? “ Abraham believed God , and it was counted to him as righteousness . ”
45004004	Now to the one who works , his wages are not counted as a gift but as his due .
45004005	And to the one who does not work but believes in him who justifies the ungodly , his faith is counted as righteousness ,
45004006	just as David also speaks of the blessing of the one to whom God counts righteousness apart from works :
45004007	“ Blessed are those whose lawless deeds are forgiven , and whose sins are covered ;
45004008	blessed is the man against whom the Lord will not count his sin . ”
45004009	Is this blessing then only for the circumcised , or also for the uncircumcised ? We say that faith was counted to Abraham as righteousness .
45004010	How then was it counted to him ? Was it before or after he had been circumcised ? It was not after , but before he was circumcised .
45004011	He received the sign of circumcision as a seal of the righteousness that he had by faith while he was still uncircumcised . The purpose was to make him the father of all who believe without being circumcised , so that righteousness would be counted to them as well ,
45004012	and to make him the father of the circumcised who are not merely circumcised but who also walk in the footsteps of the faith that our father Abraham had before he was circumcised .
45004013	For the promise to Abraham and his offspring that he would be heir of the world did not come through the law but through the righteousness of faith .
45004014	For if it is the adherents of the law who are to be the heirs , faith is null and the promise is void .
45004015	For the law brings wrath , but where there is no law there is no transgression .
45004016	That is why it depends on faith , in order that the promise may rest on grace and be guaranteed to all his offspring — not only to the adherent of the law but also to the one who shares the faith of Abraham , who is the father of us all ,
45004017	as it is written , “ I have made you the father of many nations ” — in the presence of the God in whom he believed , who gives life to the dead and calls into existence the things that do not exist .
45004018	In hope he believed against hope , that he should become the father of many nations , as he had been told , “ So shall your offspring be . ”
45004019	He did not weaken in faith when he considered his own body , which was as good as dead ( since he was about a hundred years old ) , or when he considered the barrenness of Sarah’s womb .
45004020	No distrust made him waver concerning the promise of God , but he grew strong in his faith as he gave glory to God ,
45004021	fully convinced that God was able to do what he had promised .
45004022	That is why his faith was “ counted to him as righteousness . ”
45004023	But the words “ it was counted to him ” were not written for his sake alone ,
45004024	but for ours also . It will be counted to us who believe in him who raised from the dead Jesus our Lord ,
45004025	who was delivered up for our trespasses and raised for our justification .
45005001	Therefore , since we have been justified by faith , we have peace with God through our Lord Jesus Christ .
45005002	Through him we have also obtained access by faith into this grace in which we stand , and we rejoice in hope of the glory of God .
45005003	More than that , we rejoice in our sufferings , knowing that suffering produces endurance ,
45005004	and endurance produces character , and character produces hope ,
45005005	and hope does not put us to shame , because God’s love has been poured into our hearts through the Holy Spirit who has been given to us .
45005006	For while we were still weak , at the right time Christ died for the ungodly .
45005007	For one will scarcely die for a righteous person — though perhaps for a good person one would dare even to die —
45005008	but God shows his love for us in that while we were still sinners , Christ died for us .
45005009	Since , therefore , we have now been justified by his blood , much more shall we be saved by him from the wrath of God .
45005010	For if while we were enemies we were reconciled to God by the death of his Son , much more , now that we are reconciled , shall we be saved by his life .
45005011	More than that , we also rejoice in God through our Lord Jesus Christ , through whom we have now received reconciliation .
45005012	Therefore , just as sin came into the world through one man , and death through sin , and so death spread to all men because all sinned —
45005013	for sin indeed was in the world before the law was given , but sin is not counted where there is no law .
45005014	Yet death reigned from Adam to Moses , even over those whose sinning was not like the transgression of Adam , who was a type of the one who was to come .
45005015	But the free gift is not like the trespass . For if many died through one man’s trespass , much more have the grace of God and the free gift by the grace of that one man Jesus Christ abounded for many .
45005016	And the free gift is not like the result of that one man’s sin . For the judgment following one trespass brought condemnation , but the free gift following many trespasses brought justification .
45005017	For if , because of one man’s trespass , death reigned through that one man , much more will those who receive the abundance of grace and the free gift of righteousness reign in life through the one man Jesus Christ .
45005018	Therefore , as one trespass led to condemnation for all men , so one act of righteousness leads to justification and life for all men .
45005019	For as by the one man’s disobedience the many were made sinners , so by the one man’s obedience the many will be made righteous .
45005020	Now the law came in to increase the trespass , but where sin increased , grace abounded all the more ,
45005021	so that , as sin reigned in death , grace also might reign through righteousness leading to eternal life through Jesus Christ our Lord .
45006001	What shall we say then ? Are we to continue in sin that grace may abound ?
45006002	By no means ! How can we who died to sin still live in it ?
45006003	Do you not know that all of us who have been baptized into Christ Jesus were baptized into his death ?
45006004	We were buried therefore with him by baptism into death , in order that , just as Christ was raised from the dead by the glory of the Father , we too might walk in newness of life .
45006005	For if we have been united with him in a death like his , we shall certainly be united with him in a resurrection like his .
45006006	We know that our old self was crucified with him in order that the body of sin might be brought to nothing , so that we would no longer be enslaved to sin .
45006007	For one who has died has been set free from sin .
45006008	Now if we have died with Christ , we believe that we will also live with him .
45006009	We know that Christ , being raised from the dead , will never die again ; death no longer has dominion over him .
45006010	For the death he died he died to sin , once for all , but the life he lives he lives to God .
45006011	So you also must consider yourselves dead to sin and alive to God in Christ Jesus .
45006012	Let not sin therefore reign in your mortal body , to make you obey its passions .
45006013	Do not present your members to sin as instruments for unrighteousness , but present yourselves to God as those who have been brought from death to life , and your members to God as instruments for righteousness .
45006014	For sin will have no dominion over you , since you are not under law but under grace .
45006015	What then ? Are we to sin because we are not under law but under grace ? By no means !
45006016	Do you not know that if you present yourselves to anyone as obedient slaves , you are slaves of the one whom you obey , either of sin , which leads to death , or of obedience , which leads to righteousness ?
45006017	But thanks be to God , that you who were once slaves of sin have become obedient from the heart to the standard of teaching to which you were committed ,
45006018	and , having been set free from sin , have become slaves of righteousness .
45006019	I am speaking in human terms , because of your natural limitations . For just as you once presented your members as slaves to impurity and to lawlessness leading to more lawlessness , so now present your members as slaves to righteousness leading to sanctification .
45006020	For when you were slaves of sin , you were free in regard to righteousness .
45006021	But what fruit were you getting at that time from the things of which you are now ashamed ? For the end of those things is death .
45006022	But now that you have been set free from sin and have become slaves of God , the fruit you get leads to sanctification and its end , eternal life .
45006023	For the wages of sin is death , but the free gift of God is eternal life in Christ Jesus our Lord .
45007001	Or do you not know , brothers — for I am speaking to those who know the law — that the law is binding on a person only as long as he lives ?
45007002	For a married woman is bound by law to her husband while he lives , but if her husband dies she is released from the law of marriage .
45007003	Accordingly , she will be called an adulteress if she lives with another man while her husband is alive . But if her husband dies , she is free from that law , and if she marries another man she is not an adulteress .
45007004	Likewise , my brothers , you also have died to the law through the body of Christ , so that you may belong to another , to him who has been raised from the dead , in order that we may bear fruit for God .
45007005	For while we were living in the flesh , our sinful passions , aroused by the law , were at work in our members to bear fruit for death .
45007006	But now we are released from the law , having died to that which held us captive , so that we serve in the new way of the Spirit and not in the old way of the written code .
45007007	What then shall we say ? That the law is sin ? By no means ! Yet if it had not been for the law , I would not have known sin . For I would not have known what it is to covet if the law had not said , “ You shall not covet . ”
45007008	But sin , seizing an opportunity through the commandment , produced in me all kinds of covetousness . For apart from the law , sin lies dead .
45007009	I was once alive apart from the law , but when the commandment came , sin came alive and I died .
45007010	The very commandment that promised life proved to be death to me .
45007011	For sin , seizing an opportunity through the commandment , deceived me and through it killed me .
45007012	So the law is holy , and the commandment is holy and righteous and good .
45007013	Did that which is good , then , bring death to me ? By no means ! It was sin , producing death in me through what is good , in order that sin might be shown to be sin , and through the commandment might become sinful beyond measure .
45007014	For we know that the law is spiritual , but I am of the flesh , sold under sin .
45007015	For I do not understand my own actions . For I do not do what I want , but I do the very thing I hate .
45007016	Now if I do what I do not want , I agree with the law , that it is good .
45007017	So now it is no longer I who do it , but sin that dwells within me .
45007018	For I know that nothing good dwells in me , that is , in my flesh . For I have the desire to do what is right , but not the ability to carry it out .
45007019	For I do not do the good I want , but the evil I do not want is what I keep on doing .
45007020	Now if I do what I do not want , it is no longer I who do it , but sin that dwells within me .
45007021	So I find it to be a law that when I want to do right , evil lies close at hand .
45007022	For I delight in the law of God , in my inner being ,
45007023	but I see in my members another law waging war against the law of my mind and making me captive to the law of sin that dwells in my members .
45007024	Wretched man that I am ! Who will deliver me from this body of death ?
45007025	Thanks be to God through Jesus Christ our Lord ! So then , I myself serve the law of God with my mind , but with my flesh I serve the law of sin .
45008001	There is therefore now no condemnation for those who are in Christ Jesus .
45008002	For the law of the Spirit of life has set you free in Christ Jesus from the law of sin and death .
45008003	For God has done what the law , weakened by the flesh , could not do . By sending his own Son in the likeness of sinful flesh and for sin , he condemned sin in the flesh ,
45008004	in order that the righteous requirement of the law might be fulfilled in us , who walk not according to the flesh but according to the Spirit .
45008005	For those who live according to the flesh set their minds on the things of the flesh , but those who live according to the Spirit set their minds on the things of the Spirit .
45008006	For to set the mind on the flesh is death , but to set the mind on the Spirit is life and peace .
45008007	For the mind that is set on the flesh is hostile to God , for it does not submit to God’s law ; indeed , it cannot .
45008008	Those who are in the flesh cannot please God .
45008009	You , however , are not in the flesh but in the Spirit , if in fact the Spirit of God dwells in you . Anyone who does not have the Spirit of Christ does not belong to him .
45008010	But if Christ is in you , although the body is dead because of sin , the Spirit is life because of righteousness .
45008011	If the Spirit of him who raised Jesus from the dead dwells in you , he who raised Christ Jesus from the dead will also give life to your mortal bodies through his Spirit who dwells in you .
45008012	So then , brothers , we are debtors , not to the flesh , to live according to the flesh .
45008013	For if you live according to the flesh you will die , but if by the Spirit you put to death the deeds of the body , you will live .
45008014	For all who are led by the Spirit of God are sons of God .
45008015	For you did not receive the spirit of slavery to fall back into fear , but you have received the Spirit of adoption as sons , by whom we cry , “ Abba ! Father ! ”
45008016	The Spirit himself bears witness with our spirit that we are children of God ,
45008017	and if children , then heirs — heirs of God and fellow heirs with Christ , provided we suffer with him in order that we may also be glorified with him .
45008018	For I consider that the sufferings of this present time are not worth comparing with the glory that is to be revealed to us .
45008019	For the creation waits with eager longing for the revealing of the sons of God .
45008020	For the creation was subjected to futility , not willingly , but because of him who subjected it , in hope
45008021	that the creation itself will be set free from its bondage to corruption and obtain the freedom of the glory of the children of God .
45008022	For we know that the whole creation has been groaning together in the pains of childbirth until now .
45008023	And not only the creation , but we ourselves , who have the firstfruits of the Spirit , groan inwardly as we wait eagerly for adoption as sons , the redemption of our bodies .
45008024	For in this hope we were saved . Now hope that is seen is not hope . For who hopes for what he sees ?
45008025	But if we hope for what we do not see , we wait for it with patience .
45008026	Likewise the Spirit helps us in our weakness . For we do not know what to pray for as we ought , but the Spirit himself intercedes for us with groanings too deep for words .
45008027	And he who searches hearts knows what is the mind of the Spirit , because the Spirit intercedes for the saints according to the will of God .
45008028	And we know that for those who love God all things work together for good , for those who are called according to his purpose .
45008029	For those whom he foreknew he also predestined to be conformed to the image of his Son , in order that he might be the firstborn among many brothers .
45008030	And those whom he predestined he also called , and those whom he called he also justified , and those whom he justified he also glorified .
45008031	What then shall we say to these things ? If God is for us , who can be against us ?
45008032	He who did not spare his own Son but gave him up for us all , how will he not also with him graciously give us all things ?
45008033	Who shall bring any charge against God’s elect ? It is God who justifies .
45008034	Who is to condemn ? Christ Jesus is the one who died — more than that , who was raised — who is at the right hand of God , who indeed is interceding for us .
45008035	Who shall separate us from the love of Christ ? Shall tribulation , or distress , or persecution , or famine , or nakedness , or danger , or sword ?
45008036	As it is written , “ For your sake we are being killed all the day long ; we are regarded as sheep to be slaughtered . ”
45008037	No , in all these things we are more than conquerors through him who loved us .
45008038	For I am sure that neither death nor life , nor angels nor rulers , nor things present nor things to come , nor powers ,
45008039	nor height nor depth , nor anything else in all creation , will be able to separate us from the love of God in Christ Jesus our Lord .
45009001	I am speaking the truth in Christ — I am not lying ; my conscience bears me witness in the Holy Spirit —
45009002	that I have great sorrow and unceasing anguish in my heart .
45009003	For I could wish that I myself were accursed and cut off from Christ for the sake of my brothers , my kinsmen according to the flesh .
45009004	They are Israelites , and to them belong the adoption , the glory , the covenants , the giving of the law , the worship , and the promises .
45009005	To them belong the patriarchs , and from their race , according to the flesh , is the Christ who is God over all , blessed forever . Amen .
45009006	But it is not as though the word of God has failed . For not all who are descended from Israel belong to Israel ,
45009007	and not all are children of Abraham because they are his offspring , but “ Through Isaac shall your offspring be named . ”
45009008	This means that it is not the children of the flesh who are the children of God , but the children of the promise are counted as offspring .
45009009	For this is what the promise said : “ About this time next year I will return , and Sarah shall have a son . ”
45009010	And not only so , but also when Rebekah had conceived children by one man , our forefather Isaac ,
45009011	though they were not yet born and had done nothing either good or bad — in order that God’s purpose of election might continue , not because of works but because of him who calls —
45009012	she was told , “ The older will serve the younger . ”
45009013	As it is written , “ Jacob I loved , but Esau I hated . ”
45009014	What shall we say then ? Is there injustice on God’s part ? By no means !
45009015	For he says to Moses , “ I will have mercy on whom I have mercy , and I will have compassion on whom I have compassion . ”
45009016	So then it depends not on human will or exertion , but on God , who has mercy .
45009017	For the Scripture says to Pharaoh , “ For this very purpose I have raised you up , that I might show my power in you , and that my name might be proclaimed in all the earth . ”
45009018	So then he has mercy on whomever he wills , and he hardens whomever he wills .
45009019	You will say to me then , “ Why does he still find fault ? For who can resist his will ? ”
45009020	But who are you , O man , to answer back to God ? Will what is molded say to its molder , “ Why have you made me like this ? ”
45009021	Has the potter no right over the clay , to make out of the same lump one vessel for honorable use and another for dishonorable use ?
45009022	What if God , desiring to show his wrath and to make known his power , has endured with much patience vessels of wrath prepared for destruction ,
45009023	in order to make known the riches of his glory for vessels of mercy , which he has prepared beforehand for glory —
45009024	even us whom he has called , not from the Jews only but also from the Gentiles ?
45009025	As indeed he says in Hosea , “ Those who were not my people I will call ‘ my people , ’ and her who was not beloved I will call ‘ beloved . ’ ”
45009026	“ And in the very place where it was said to them , ‘ You are not my people , ’ there they will be called ‘ sons of the living God . ’ ”
45009027	And Isaiah cries out concerning Israel : “ Though the number of the sons of Israel be as the sand of the sea , only a remnant of them will be saved ,
45009028	for the Lord will carry out his sentence upon the earth fully and without delay . ”
45009029	And as Isaiah predicted , “ If the Lord of hosts had not left us offspring , we would have been like Sodom and become like Gomorrah . ”
45009030	What shall we say , then ? That Gentiles who did not pursue righteousness have attained it , that is , a righteousness that is by faith ;
45009031	but that Israel who pursued a law that would lead to righteousness did not succeed in reaching that law .
45009032	Why ? Because they did not pursue it by faith , but as if it were based on works . They have stumbled over the stumbling stone ,
45009033	as it is written , “ Behold , I am laying in Zion a stone of stumbling , and a rock of offense ; and whoever believes in him will not be put to shame . ”
45010001	Brothers , my heart’s desire and prayer to God for them is that they may be saved .
45010002	For I bear them witness that they have a zeal for God , but not according to knowledge .
45010003	For , being ignorant of the righteousness of God , and seeking to establish their own , they did not submit to God’s righteousness .
45010004	For Christ is the end of the law for righteousness to everyone who believes .
45010005	For Moses writes about the righteousness that is based on the law , that the person who does the commandments shall live by them .
45010006	But the righteousness based on faith says , “ Do not say in your heart , ‘ Who will ascend into heaven ? ’ ” ( that is , to bring Christ down
45010007	or “ ‘ Who will descend into the abyss ? ’ ” ( that is , to bring Christ up from the dead ) .
45010008	But what does it say ? “ The word is near you , in your mouth and in your heart ” ( that is , the word of faith that we proclaim ) ;
45010009	because , if you confess with your mouth that Jesus is Lord and believe in your heart that God raised him from the dead , you will be saved .
45010010	For with the heart one believes and is justified , and with the mouth one confesses and is saved .
45010011	For the Scripture says , “ Everyone who believes in him will not be put to shame . ”
45010012	For there is no distinction between Jew and Greek ; for the same Lord is Lord of all , bestowing his riches on all who call on him .
45010013	For “ everyone who calls on the name of the Lord will be saved . ”
45010014	How then will they call on him in whom they have not believed ? And how are they to believe in him of whom they have never heard ? And how are they to hear without someone preaching ?
45010015	And how are they to preach unless they are sent ? As it is written , “ How beautiful are the feet of those who preach the good news ! ”
45010016	But they have not all obeyed the gospel . For Isaiah says , “ Lord , who has believed what he has heard from us ? ”
45010017	So faith comes from hearing , and hearing through the word of Christ .
45010018	But I ask , have they not heard ? Indeed they have , for “ Their voice has gone out to all the earth , and their words to the ends of the world . ”
45010019	But I ask , did Israel not understand ? First Moses says , “ I will make you jealous of those who are not a nation ; with a foolish nation I will make you angry . ”
45010020	Then Isaiah is so bold as to say , “ I have been found by those who did not seek me ; I have shown myself to those who did not ask for me . ”
45010021	But of Israel he says , “ All day long I have held out my hands to a disobedient and contrary people . ”
45011001	I ask , then , has God rejected his people ? By no means ! For I myself am an Israelite , a descendant of Abraham , a member of the tribe of Benjamin .
45011002	God has not rejected his people whom he foreknew . Do you not know what the Scripture says of Elijah , how he appeals to God against Israel ?
45011003	“ Lord , they have killed your prophets , they have demolished your altars , and I alone am left , and they seek my life . ”
45011004	But what is God’s reply to him ? “ I have kept for myself seven thousand men who have not bowed the knee to Baal . ”
45011005	So too at the present time there is a remnant , chosen by grace .
45011006	But if it is by grace , it is no longer on the basis of works ; otherwise grace would no longer be grace .
45011007	What then ? Israel failed to obtain what it was seeking . The elect obtained it , but the rest were hardened ,
45011008	as it is written , “ God gave them a spirit of stupor , eyes that would not see and ears that would not hear , down to this very day . ”
45011009	And David says , “ Let their table become a snare and a trap , a stumbling block and a retribution for them ;
45011010	let their eyes be darkened so that they cannot see , and bend their backs forever . ”
45011011	So I ask , did they stumble in order that they might fall ? By no means ! Rather through their trespass salvation has come to the Gentiles , so as to make Israel jealous .
45011012	Now if their trespass means riches for the world , and if their failure means riches for the Gentiles , how much more will their full inclusion mean !
45011013	Now I am speaking to you Gentiles . Inasmuch then as I am an apostle to the Gentiles , I magnify my ministry
45011014	in order somehow to make my fellow Jews jealous , and thus save some of them .
45011015	For if their rejection means the reconciliation of the world , what will their acceptance mean but life from the dead ?
45011016	If the dough offered as firstfruits is holy , so is the whole lump , and if the root is holy , so are the branches .
45011017	But if some of the branches were broken off , and you , although a wild olive shoot , were grafted in among the others and now share in the nourishing root of the olive tree ,
45011018	do not be arrogant toward the branches . If you are , remember it is not you who support the root , but the root that supports you .
45011019	Then you will say , “ Branches were broken off so that I might be grafted in . ”
45011020	That is true . They were broken off because of their unbelief , but you stand fast through faith . So do not become proud , but fear .
45011021	For if God did not spare the natural branches , neither will he spare you .
45011022	Note then the kindness and the severity of God : severity toward those who have fallen , but God’s kindness to you , provided you continue in his kindness . Otherwise you too will be cut off .
45011023	And even they , if they do not continue in their unbelief , will be grafted in , for God has the power to graft them in again .
45011024	For if you were cut from what is by nature a wild olive tree , and grafted , contrary to nature , into a cultivated olive tree , how much more will these , the natural branches , be grafted back into their own olive tree .
45011025	Lest you be wise in your own sight , I want you to understand this mystery , brothers : a partial hardening has come upon Israel , until the fullness of the Gentiles has come in .
45011026	And in this way all Israel will be saved , as it is written , “ The Deliverer will come from Zion , he will banish ungodliness from Jacob ” ;
45011027	“ and this will be my covenant with them when I take away their sins . ”
45011028	As regards the gospel , they are enemies of God for your sake . But as regards election , they are beloved for the sake of their forefathers .
45011029	For the gifts and the calling of God are irrevocable .
45011030	For just as you were at one time disobedient to God but now have received mercy because of their disobedience ,
45011031	so they too have now been disobedient in order that by the mercy shown to you they also may now receive mercy .
45011032	For God has consigned all to disobedience , that he may have mercy on all .
45011033	Oh , the depth of the riches and wisdom and knowledge of God ! How unsearchable are his judgments and how inscrutable his ways !
45011034	“ For who has known the mind of the Lord , or who has been his counselor ? ”
45011035	“ Or who has given a gift to him that he might be repaid ? ”
45011036	For from him and through him and to him are all things . To him be glory forever . Amen .
45012001	I appeal to you therefore , brothers , by the mercies of God , to present your bodies as a living sacrifice , holy and acceptable to God , which is your spiritual worship .
45012002	Do not be conformed to this world , but be transformed by the renewal of your mind , that by testing you may discern what is the will of God , what is good and acceptable and perfect .
45012003	For by the grace given to me I say to everyone among you not to think of himself more highly than he ought to think , but to think with sober judgment , each according to the measure of faith that God has assigned .
45012004	For as in one body we have many members , and the members do not all have the same function ,
45012005	so we , though many , are one body in Christ , and individually members one of another .
45012006	Having gifts that differ according to the grace given to us , let us use them : if prophecy , in proportion to our faith ;
45012007	if service , in our serving ; the one who teaches , in his teaching ;
45012008	the one who exhorts , in his exhortation ; the one who contributes , in generosity ; the one who leads , with zeal ; the one who does acts of mercy , with cheerfulness .
45012009	Let love be genuine . Abhor what is evil ; hold fast to what is good .
45012010	Love one another with brotherly affection . Outdo one another in showing honor .
45012011	Do not be slothful in zeal , be fervent in spirit , serve the Lord .
45012012	Rejoice in hope , be patient in tribulation , be constant in prayer .
45012013	Contribute to the needs of the saints and seek to show hospitality .
45012014	Bless those who persecute you ; bless and do not curse them .
45012015	Rejoice with those who rejoice , weep with those who weep .
45012016	Live in harmony with one another . Do not be haughty , but associate with the lowly . Never be wise in your own sight .
45012017	Repay no one evil for evil , but give thought to do what is honorable in the sight of all .
45012018	If possible , so far as it depends on you , live peaceably with all .
45012019	Beloved , never avenge yourselves , but leave it to the wrath of God , for it is written , “ Vengeance is mine , I will repay , says the Lord . ”
45012020	To the contrary , “ if your enemy is hungry , feed him ; if he is thirsty , give him something to drink ; for by so doing you will heap burning coals on his head . ”
45012021	Do not be overcome by evil , but overcome evil with good .
45013001	Let every person be subject to the governing authorities . For there is no authority except from God , and those that exist have been instituted by God .
45013002	Therefore whoever resists the authorities resists what God has appointed , and those who resist will incur judgment .
45013003	For rulers are not a terror to good conduct , but to bad . Would you have no fear of the one who is in authority ? Then do what is good , and you will receive his approval ,
45013004	for he is God’s servant for your good . But if you do wrong , be afraid , for he does not bear the sword in vain . For he is the servant of God , an avenger who carries out God’s wrath on the wrongdoer .
45013005	Therefore one must be in subjection , not only to avoid God’s wrath but also for the sake of conscience .
45013006	For because of this you also pay taxes , for the authorities are ministers of God , attending to this very thing .
45013007	Pay to all what is owed to them : taxes to whom taxes are owed , revenue to whom revenue is owed , respect to whom respect is owed , honor to whom honor is owed .
45013008	Owe no one anything , except to love each other , for the one who loves another has fulfilled the law .
45013009	For the commandments , “ You shall not commit adultery , You shall not murder , You shall not steal , You shall not covet , ” and any other commandment , are summed up in this word : “ You shall love your neighbor as yourself . ”
45013010	Love does no wrong to a neighbor ; therefore love is the fulfilling of the law .
45013011	Besides this you know the time , that the hour has come for you to wake from sleep . For salvation is nearer to us now than when we first believed .
45013012	The night is far gone ; the day is at hand . So then let us cast off the works of darkness and put on the armor of light .
45013013	Let us walk properly as in the daytime , not in orgies and drunkenness , not in sexual immorality and sensuality , not in quarreling and jealousy .
45013014	But put on the Lord Jesus Christ , and make no provision for the flesh , to gratify its desires .
45014001	As for the one who is weak in faith , welcome him , but not to quarrel over opinions .
45014002	One person believes he may eat anything , while the weak person eats only vegetables .
45014003	Let not the one who eats despise the one who abstains , and let not the one who abstains pass judgment on the one who eats , for God has welcomed him .
45014004	Who are you to pass judgment on the servant of another ? It is before his own master that he stands or falls . And he will be upheld , for the Lord is able to make him stand .
45014005	One person esteems one day as better than another , while another esteems all days alike . Each one should be fully convinced in his own mind .
45014006	The one who observes the day , observes it in honor of the Lord . The one who eats , eats in honor of the Lord , since he gives thanks to God , while the one who abstains , abstains in honor of the Lord and gives thanks to God .
45014007	For none of us lives to himself , and none of us dies to himself .
45014008	For if we live , we live to the Lord , and if we die , we die to the Lord . So then , whether we live or whether we die , we are the Lord’s .
45014009	For to this end Christ died and lived again , that he might be Lord both of the dead and of the living .
45014010	Why do you pass judgment on your brother ? Or you , why do you despise your brother ? For we will all stand before the judgment seat of God ;
45014011	for it is written , “ As I live , says the Lord , every knee shall bow to me , and every tongue shall confess to God . ”
45014012	So then each of us will give an account of himself to God .
45014013	Therefore let us not pass judgment on one another any longer , but rather decide never to put a stumbling block or hindrance in the way of a brother .
45014014	I know and am persuaded in the Lord Jesus that nothing is unclean in itself , but it is unclean for anyone who thinks it unclean .
45014015	For if your brother is grieved by what you eat , you are no longer walking in love . By what you eat , do not destroy the one for whom Christ died .
45014016	So do not let what you regard as good be spoken of as evil .
45014017	For the kingdom of God is not a matter of eating and drinking but of righteousness and peace and joy in the Holy Spirit .
45014018	Whoever thus serves Christ is acceptable to God and approved by men .
45014019	So then let us pursue what makes for peace and for mutual upbuilding .
45014020	Do not , for the sake of food , destroy the work of God . Everything is indeed clean , but it is wrong for anyone to make another stumble by what he eats .
45014021	It is good not to eat meat or drink wine or do anything that causes your brother to stumble .
45014022	The faith that you have , keep between yourself and God . Blessed is the one who has no reason to pass judgment on himself for what he approves .
45014023	But whoever has doubts is condemned if he eats , because the eating is not from faith . For whatever does not proceed from faith is sin .
45015001	We who are strong have an obligation to bear with the failings of the weak , and not to please ourselves .
45015002	Let each of us please his neighbor for his good , to build him up .
45015003	For Christ did not please himself , but as it is written , “ The reproaches of those who reproached you fell on me . ”
45015004	For whatever was written in former days was written for our instruction , that through endurance and through the encouragement of the Scriptures we might have hope .
45015005	May the God of endurance and encouragement grant you to live in such harmony with one another , in accord with Christ Jesus ,
45015006	that together you may with one voice glorify the God and Father of our Lord Jesus Christ .
45015007	Therefore welcome one another as Christ has welcomed you , for the glory of God .
45015008	For I tell you that Christ became a servant to the circumcised to show God’s truthfulness , in order to confirm the promises given to the patriarchs ,
45015009	and in order that the Gentiles might glorify God for his mercy . As it is written , “ Therefore I will praise you among the Gentiles , and sing to your name . ”
45015010	And again it is said , “ Rejoice , O Gentiles , with his people . ”
45015011	And again , “ Praise the Lord , all you Gentiles , and let all the peoples extol him . ”
45015012	And again Isaiah says , “ The root of Jesse will come , even he who arises to rule the Gentiles ; in him will the Gentiles hope . ”
45015013	May the God of hope fill you with all joy and peace in believing , so that by the power of the Holy Spirit you may abound in hope .
45015014	I myself am satisfied about you , my brothers , that you yourselves are full of goodness , filled with all knowledge and able to instruct one another .
45015015	But on some points I have written to you very boldly by way of reminder , because of the grace given me by God
45015016	to be a minister of Christ Jesus to the Gentiles in the priestly service of the gospel of God , so that the offering of the Gentiles may be acceptable , sanctified by the Holy Spirit .
45015017	In Christ Jesus , then , I have reason to be proud of my work for God .
45015018	For I will not venture to speak of anything except what Christ has accomplished through me to bring the Gentiles to obedience — by word and deed ,
45015019	by the power of signs and wonders , by the power of the Spirit of God — so that from Jerusalem and all the way around to Illyricum I have fulfilled the ministry of the gospel of Christ ;
45015020	and thus I make it my ambition to preach the gospel , not where Christ has already been named , lest I build on someone else’s foundation ,
45015021	but as it is written , “ Those who have never been told of him will see , and those who have never heard will understand . ”
45015022	This is the reason why I have so often been hindered from coming to you .
45015023	But now , since I no longer have any room for work in these regions , and since I have longed for many years to come to you ,
45015024	I hope to see you in passing as I go to Spain , and to be helped on my journey there by you , once I have enjoyed your company for a while .
45015025	At present , however , I am going to Jerusalem bringing aid to the saints .
45015026	For Macedonia and Achaia have been pleased to make some contribution for the poor among the saints at Jerusalem .
45015027	For they were pleased to do it , and indeed they owe it to them . For if the Gentiles have come to share in their spiritual blessings , they ought also to be of service to them in material blessings .
45015028	When therefore I have completed this and have delivered to them what has been collected , I will leave for Spain by way of you .
45015029	I know that when I come to you I will come in the fullness of the blessing of Christ .
45015030	I appeal to you , brothers , by our Lord Jesus Christ and by the love of the Spirit , to strive together with me in your prayers to God on my behalf ,
45015031	that I may be delivered from the unbelievers in Judea , and that my service for Jerusalem may be acceptable to the saints ,
45015032	so that by God’s will I may come to you with joy and be refreshed in your company .
45015033	May the God of peace be with you all . Amen .
45016001	I commend to you our sister Phoebe , a servant of the church at Cenchreae ,
45016002	that you may welcome her in the Lord in a way worthy of the saints , and help her in whatever she may need from you , for she has been a patron of many and of myself as well .
45016003	Greet Prisca and Aquila , my fellow workers in Christ Jesus ,
45016004	who risked their necks for my life , to whom not only I give thanks but all the churches of the Gentiles give thanks as well .
45016005	Greet also the church in their house . Greet my beloved Epaenetus , who was the first convert to Christ in Asia .
45016006	Greet Mary , who has worked hard for you .
45016007	Greet Andronicus and Junia , my kinsmen and my fellow prisoners . They are well known to the apostles , and they were in Christ before me .
45016008	Greet Ampliatus , my beloved in the Lord .
45016009	Greet Urbanus , our fellow worker in Christ , and my beloved Stachys .
45016010	Greet Apelles , who is approved in Christ . Greet those who belong to the family of Aristobulus .
45016011	Greet my kinsman Herodion . Greet those in the Lord who belong to the family of Narcissus .
45016012	Greet those workers in the Lord , Tryphaena and Tryphosa . Greet the beloved Persis , who has worked hard in the Lord .
45016013	Greet Rufus , chosen in the Lord ; also his mother , who has been a mother to me as well .
45016014	Greet Asyncritus , Phlegon , Hermes , Patrobas , Hermas , and the brothers who are with them .
45016015	Greet Philologus , Julia , Nereus and his sister , and Olympas , and all the saints who are with them .
45016016	Greet one another with a holy kiss . All the churches of Christ greet you .
45016017	I appeal to you , brothers , to watch out for those who cause divisions and create obstacles contrary to the doctrine that you have been taught ; avoid them .
45016018	For such persons do not serve our Lord Christ , but their own appetites , and by smooth talk and flattery they deceive the hearts of the naive .
45016019	For your obedience is known to all , so that I rejoice over you , but I want you to be wise as to what is good and innocent as to what is evil .
45016020	The God of peace will soon crush Satan under your feet . The grace of our Lord Jesus Christ be with you .
45016021	Timothy , my fellow worker , greets you ; so do Lucius and Jason and Sosipater , my kinsmen .
45016022	I Tertius , who wrote this letter , greet you in the Lord .
45016023	Gaius , who is host to me and to the whole church , greets you . Erastus , the city treasurer , and our brother Quartus , greet you .
45016025	Now to him who is able to strengthen you according to my gospel and the preaching of Jesus Christ , according to the revelation of the mystery that was kept secret for long ages
45016026	but has now been disclosed and through the prophetic writings has been made known to all nations , according to the command of the eternal God , to bring about the obedience of faith —
45016027	to the only wise God be glory forevermore through Jesus Christ ! Amen .
46001001	Paul , called by the will of God to be an apostle of Christ Jesus , and our brother Sosthenes ,
46001002	To the church of God that is in Corinth , to those sanctified in Christ Jesus , called to be saints together with all those who in every place call upon the name of our Lord Jesus Christ , both their Lord and ours :
46001003	Grace to you and peace from God our Father and the Lord Jesus Christ .
46001004	I give thanks to my God always for you because of the grace of God that was given you in Christ Jesus ,
46001005	that in every way you were enriched in him in all speech and all knowledge —
46001006	even as the testimony about Christ was confirmed among you —
46001007	so that you are not lacking in any spiritual gift , as you wait for the revealing of our Lord Jesus Christ ,
46001008	who will sustain you to the end , guiltless in the day of our Lord Jesus Christ .
46001009	God is faithful , by whom you were called into the fellowship of his Son , Jesus Christ our Lord .
46001010	I appeal to you , brothers , by the name of our Lord Jesus Christ , that all of you agree , and that there be no divisions among you , but that you be united in the same mind and the same judgment .
46001011	For it has been reported to me by Chloe’s people that there is quarreling among you , my brothers .
46001012	What I mean is that each one of you says , “ I follow Paul , ” or “ I follow Apollos , ” or “ I follow Cephas , ” or “ I follow Christ . ”
46001013	Is Christ divided ? Was Paul crucified for you ? Or were you baptized in the name of Paul ?
46001014	I thank God that I baptized none of you except Crispus and Gaius ,
46001015	so that no one may say that you were baptized in my name .
46001016	( I did baptize also the household of Stephanas . Beyond that , I do not know whether I baptized anyone else .
46001017	For Christ did not send me to baptize but to preach the gospel , and not with words of eloquent wisdom , lest the cross of Christ be emptied of its power .
46001018	For the word of the cross is folly to those who are perishing , but to us who are being saved it is the power of God .
46001019	For it is written , “ I will destroy the wisdom of the wise , and the discernment of the discerning I will thwart . ”
46001020	Where is the one who is wise ? Where is the scribe ? Where is the debater of this age ? Has not God made foolish the wisdom of the world ?
46001021	For since , in the wisdom of God , the world did not know God through wisdom , it pleased God through the folly of what we preach to save those who believe .
46001022	For Jews demand signs and Greeks seek wisdom ,
46001023	but we preach Christ crucified , a stumbling block to Jews and folly to Gentiles ,
46001024	but to those who are called , both Jews and Greeks , Christ the power of God and the wisdom of God .
46001025	For the foolishness of God is wiser than men , and the weakness of God is stronger than men .
46001026	For consider your calling , brothers : not many of you were wise according to worldly standards , not many were powerful , not many were of noble birth .
46001027	But God chose what is foolish in the world to shame the wise ; God chose what is weak in the world to shame the strong ;
46001028	God chose what is low and despised in the world , even things that are not , to bring to nothing things that are ,
46001029	so that no human being might boast in the presence of God .
46001030	And because of him you are in Christ Jesus , who became to us wisdom from God , righteousness and sanctification and redemption ,
46001031	so that , as it is written , “ Let the one who boasts , boast in the Lord . ”
46002001	And I , when I came to you , brothers , did not come proclaiming to you the testimony of God with lofty speech or wisdom .
46002002	For I decided to know nothing among you except Jesus Christ and him crucified .
46002003	And I was with you in weakness and in fear and much trembling ,
46002004	and my speech and my message were not in plausible words of wisdom , but in demonstration of the Spirit and of power ,
46002005	that your faith might not rest in the wisdom of men but in the power of God .
46002006	Yet among the mature we do impart wisdom , although it is not a wisdom of this age or of the rulers of this age , who are doomed to pass away .
46002007	But we impart a secret and hidden wisdom of God , which God decreed before the ages for our glory .
46002008	None of the rulers of this age understood this , for if they had , they would not have crucified the Lord of glory .
46002009	But , as it is written , “ What no eye has seen , nor ear heard , nor the heart of man imagined , what God has prepared for those who love him ” —
46002010	these things God has revealed to us through the Spirit . For the Spirit searches everything , even the depths of God .
46002011	For who knows a person’s thoughts except the spirit of that person , which is in him ? So also no one comprehends the thoughts of God except the Spirit of God .
46002012	Now we have received not the spirit of the world , but the Spirit who is from God , that we might understand the things freely given us by God .
46002013	And we impart this in words not taught by human wisdom but taught by the Spirit , interpreting spiritual truths to those who are spiritual .
46002014	The natural person does not accept the things of the Spirit of God , for they are folly to him , and he is not able to understand them because they are spiritually discerned .
46002015	The spiritual person judges all things , but is himself to be judged by no one .
46002016	“ For who has understood the mind of the Lord so as to instruct him ? ” But we have the mind of Christ .
46003001	But I , brothers , could not address you as spiritual people , but as people of the flesh , as infants in Christ .
46003002	I fed you with milk , not solid food , for you were not ready for it . And even now you are not yet ready ,
46003003	for you are still of the flesh . For while there is jealousy and strife among you , are you not of the flesh and behaving only in a human way ?
46003004	For when one says , “ I follow Paul , ” and another , “ I follow Apollos , ” are you not being merely human ?
46003005	What then is Apollos ? What is Paul ? Servants through whom you believed , as the Lord assigned to each .
46003006	I planted , Apollos watered , but God gave the growth .
46003007	So neither he who plants nor he who waters is anything , but only God who gives the growth .
46003008	He who plants and he who waters are one , and each will receive his wages according to his labor .
46003009	For we are God’s fellow workers . You are God’s field , God’s building .
46003010	According to the grace of God given to me , like a skilled master builder I laid a foundation , and someone else is building upon it . Let each one take care how he builds upon it .
46003011	For no one can lay a foundation other than that which is laid , which is Jesus Christ .
46003012	Now if anyone builds on the foundation with gold , silver , precious stones , wood , hay , straw —
46003013	each one’s work will become manifest , for the Day will disclose it , because it will be revealed by fire , and the fire will test what sort of work each one has done .
46003014	If the work that anyone has built on the foundation survives , he will receive a reward .
46003015	If anyone’s work is burned up , he will suffer loss , though he himself will be saved , but only as through fire .
46003016	Do you not know that you are God’s temple and that God’s Spirit dwells in you ?
46003017	If anyone destroys God’s temple , God will destroy him . For God’s temple is holy , and you are that temple .
46003018	Let no one deceive himself . If anyone among you thinks that he is wise in this age , let him become a fool that he may become wise .
46003019	For the wisdom of this world is folly with God . For it is written , “ He catches the wise in their craftiness , ”
46003020	and again , “ The Lord knows the thoughts of the wise , that they are futile . ”
46003021	So let no one boast in men . For all things are yours ,
46003022	whether Paul or Apollos or Cephas or the world or life or death or the present or the future — all are yours ,
46003023	and you are Christ’s , and Christ is God’s .
46004001	This is how one should regard us , as servants of Christ and stewards of the mysteries of God .
46004002	Moreover , it is required of stewards that they be found trustworthy .
46004003	But with me it is a very small thing that I should be judged by you or by any human court . In fact , I do not even judge myself .
46004004	For I am not aware of anything against myself , but I am not thereby acquitted . It is the Lord who judges me .
46004005	Therefore do not pronounce judgment before the time , before the Lord comes , who will bring to light the things now hidden in darkness and will disclose the purposes of the heart . Then each one will receive his commendation from God .
46004006	I have applied all these things to myself and Apollos for your benefit , brothers , that you may learn by us not to go beyond what is written , that none of you may be puffed up in favor of one against another .
46004007	For who sees anything different in you ? What do you have that you did not receive ? If then you received it , why do you boast as if you did not receive it ?
46004008	Already you have all you want ! Already you have become rich ! Without us you have become kings ! And would that you did reign , so that we might share the rule with you !
46004009	For I think that God has exhibited us apostles as last of all , like men sentenced to death , because we have become a spectacle to the world , to angels , and to men .
46004010	We are fools for Christ’s sake , but you are wise in Christ . We are weak , but you are strong . You are held in honor , but we in disrepute .
46004011	To the present hour we hunger and thirst , we are poorly dressed and buffeted and homeless ,
46004012	and we labor , working with our own hands . When reviled , we bless ; when persecuted , we endure ;
46004013	when slandered , we entreat . We have become , and are still , like the scum of the world , the refuse of all things .
46004014	I do not write these things to make you ashamed , but to admonish you as my beloved children .
46004015	For though you have countless guides in Christ , you do not have many fathers . For I became your father in Christ Jesus through the gospel .
46004016	I urge you , then , be imitators of me .
46004017	That is why I sent you Timothy , my beloved and faithful child in the Lord , to remind you of my ways in Christ , as I teach them everywhere in every church .
46004018	Some are arrogant , as though I were not coming to you .
46004019	But I will come to you soon , if the Lord wills , and I will find out not the talk of these arrogant people but their power .
46004020	For the kingdom of God does not consist in talk but in power .
46004021	What do you wish ? Shall I come to you with a rod , or with love in a spirit of gentleness ?
46005001	It is actually reported that there is sexual immorality among you , and of a kind that is not tolerated even among pagans , for a man has his father’s wife .
46005002	And you are arrogant ! Ought you not rather to mourn ? Let him who has done this be removed from among you .
46005003	For though absent in body , I am present in spirit ; and as if present , I have already pronounced judgment on the one who did such a thing .
46005004	When you are assembled in the name of the Lord Jesus and my spirit is present , with the power of our Lord Jesus ,
46005005	you are to deliver this man to Satan for the destruction of the flesh , so that his spirit may be saved in the day of the Lord .
46005006	Your boasting is not good . Do you not know that a little leaven leavens the whole lump ?
46005007	Cleanse out the old leaven that you may be a new lump , as you really are unleavened . For Christ , our Passover lamb , has been sacrificed .
46005008	Let us therefore celebrate the festival , not with the old leaven , the leaven of malice and evil , but with the unleavened bread of sincerity and truth .
46005009	I wrote to you in my letter not to associate with sexually immoral people —
46005010	not at all meaning the sexually immoral of this world , or the greedy and swindlers , or idolaters , since then you would need to go out of the world .
46005011	But now I am writing to you not to associate with anyone who bears the name of brother if he is guilty of sexual immorality or greed , or is an idolater , reviler , drunkard , or swindler — not even to eat with such a one .
46005012	For what have I to do with judging outsiders ? Is it not those inside the church whom you are to judge ?
46005013	God judges those outside . “ Purge the evil person from among you . ”
46006001	When one of you has a grievance against another , does he dare go to law before the unrighteous instead of the saints ?
46006002	Or do you not know that the saints will judge the world ? And if the world is to be judged by you , are you incompetent to try trivial cases ?
46006003	Do you not know that we are to judge angels ? How much more , then , matters pertaining to this life !
46006004	So if you have such cases , why do you lay them before those who have no standing in the church ?
46006005	I say this to your shame . Can it be that there is no one among you wise enough to settle a dispute between the brothers ,
46006006	but brother goes to law against brother , and that before unbelievers ?
46006007	To have lawsuits at all with one another is already a defeat for you . Why not rather suffer wrong ? Why not rather be defrauded ?
46006008	But you yourselves wrong and defraud — even your own brothers !
46006009	Or do you not know that the unrighteous will not inherit the kingdom of God ? Do not be deceived : neither the sexually immoral , nor idolaters , nor adulterers , nor men who practice homosexuality ,
46006010	nor thieves , nor the greedy , nor drunkards , nor revilers , nor swindlers will inherit the kingdom of God .
46006011	And such were some of you . But you were washed , you were sanctified , you were justified in the name of the Lord Jesus Christ and by the Spirit of our God .
46006012	“ All things are lawful for me , ” but not all things are helpful . “ All things are lawful for me , ” but I will not be enslaved by anything .
46006013	“ Food is meant for the stomach and the stomach for food ” — and God will destroy both one and the other . The body is not meant for sexual immorality , but for the Lord , and the Lord for the body .
46006014	And God raised the Lord and will also raise us up by his power .
46006015	Do you not know that your bodies are members of Christ ? Shall I then take the members of Christ and make them members of a prostitute ? Never !
46006016	Or do you not know that he who is joined to a prostitute becomes one body with her ? For , as it is written , “ The two will become one flesh . ”
46006017	But he who is joined to the Lord becomes one spirit with him .
46006018	Flee from sexual immorality . Every other sin a person commits is outside the body , but the sexually immoral person sins against his own body .
46006019	Or do you not know that your body is a temple of the Holy Spirit within you , whom you have from God ? You are not your own ,
46006020	for you were bought with a price . So glorify God in your body .
46007001	Now concerning the matters about which you wrote : “ It is good for a man not to have sexual relations with a woman . ”
46007002	But because of the temptation to sexual immorality , each man should have his own wife and each woman her own husband .
46007003	The husband should give to his wife her conjugal rights , and likewise the wife to her husband .
46007004	For the wife does not have authority over her own body , but the husband does . Likewise the husband does not have authority over his own body , but the wife does .
46007005	Do not deprive one another , except perhaps by agreement for a limited time , that you may devote yourselves to prayer ; but then come together again , so that Satan may not tempt you because of your lack of self-control .
46007006	Now as a concession , not a command , I say this .
46007007	I wish that all were as I myself am . But each has his own gift from God , one of one kind and one of another .
46007008	To the unmarried and the widows I say that it is good for them to remain single as I am .
46007009	But if they cannot exercise self-control , they should marry . For it is better to marry than to burn with passion .
46007010	To the married I give this charge ( not I , but the Lord ) : the wife should not separate from her husband
46007011	( but if she does , she should remain unmarried or else be reconciled to her husband ) , and the husband should not divorce his wife .
46007012	To the rest I say ( I , not the Lord
46007013	If any woman has a husband who is an unbeliever , and he consents to live with her , she should not divorce him .
46007014	For the unbelieving husband is made holy because of his wife , and the unbelieving wife is made holy because of her husband . Otherwise your children would be unclean , but as it is , they are holy .
46007015	But if the unbelieving partner separates , let it be so . In such cases the brother or sister is not enslaved . God has called you to peace .
46007016	For how do you know , wife , whether you will save your husband ? Or how do you know , husband , whether you will save your wife ?
46007017	Only let each person lead the life that the Lord has assigned to him , and to which God has called him . This is my rule in all the churches .
46007018	Was anyone at the time of his call already circumcised ? Let him not seek to remove the marks of circumcision . Was anyone at the time of his call uncircumcised ? Let him not seek circumcision .
46007019	For neither circumcision counts for anything nor uncircumcision , but keeping the commandments of God .
46007020	Each one should remain in the condition in which he was called .
46007021	Were you a slave when called ? Do not be concerned about it . ( But if you can gain your freedom , avail yourself of the opportunity .
46007022	For he who was called in the Lord as a slave is a freedman of the Lord . Likewise he who was free when called is a slave of Christ .
46007023	You were bought with a price ; do not become slaves of men .
46007024	So , brothers , in whatever condition each was called , there let him remain with God .
46007025	Now concerning the betrothed , I have no command from the Lord , but I give my judgment as one who by the Lord’s mercy is trustworthy .
46007026	I think that in view of the present distress it is good for a person to remain as he is .
46007027	Are you bound to a wife ? Do not seek to be free . Are you free from a wife ? Do not seek a wife .
46007028	But if you do marry , you have not sinned , and if a betrothed woman marries , she has not sinned . Yet those who marry will have worldly troubles , and I would spare you that .
46007029	This is what I mean , brothers : the appointed time has grown very short . From now on , let those who have wives live as though they had none ,
46007030	and those who mourn as though they were not mourning , and those who rejoice as though they were not rejoicing , and those who buy as though they had no goods ,
46007031	and those who deal with the world as though they had no dealings with it . For the present form of this world is passing away .
46007032	I want you to be free from anxieties . The unmarried man is anxious about the things of the Lord , how to please the Lord .
46007033	But the married man is anxious about worldly things , how to please his wife ,
46007034	and his interests are divided . And the unmarried or betrothed woman is anxious about the things of the Lord , how to be holy in body and spirit . But the married woman is anxious about worldly things , how to please her husband .
46007035	I say this for your own benefit , not to lay any restraint upon you , but to promote good order and to secure your undivided devotion to the Lord .
46007036	If anyone thinks that he is not behaving properly toward his betrothed , if his passions are strong , and it has to be , let him do as he wishes : let them marry — it is no sin .
46007037	But whoever is firmly established in his heart , being under no necessity but having his desire under control , and has determined this in his heart , to keep her as his betrothed , he will do well .
46007038	So then he who marries his betrothed does well , and he who refrains from marriage will do even better .
46007039	A wife is bound to her husband as long as he lives . But if her husband dies , she is free to be married to whom she wishes , only in the Lord .
46007040	Yet in my judgment she is happier if she remains as she is . And I think that I too have the Spirit of God .
46008001	Now concerning food offered to idols : we know that “ all of us possess knowledge . ” This “ knowledge ” puffs up , but love builds up .
46008002	If anyone imagines that he knows something , he does not yet know as he ought to know .
46008003	But if anyone loves God , he is known by God .
46008004	Therefore , as to the eating of food offered to idols , we know that “ an idol has no real existence , ” and that “ there is no God but one . ”
46008005	For although there may be so-called gods in heaven or on earth — as indeed there are many “ gods ” and many “ lords ” —
46008006	yet for us there is one God , the Father , from whom are all things and for whom we exist , and one Lord , Jesus Christ , through whom are all things and through whom we exist .
46008007	However , not all possess this knowledge . But some , through former association with idols , eat food as really offered to an idol , and their conscience , being weak , is defiled .
46008008	Food will not commend us to God . We are no worse off if we do not eat , and no better off if we do .
46008009	But take care that this right of yours does not somehow become a stumbling block to the weak .
46008010	For if anyone sees you who have knowledge eating in an idol’s temple , will he not be encouraged , if his conscience is weak , to eat food offered to idols ?
46008011	And so by your knowledge this weak person is destroyed , the brother for whom Christ died .
46008012	Thus , sinning against your brothers and wounding their conscience when it is weak , you sin against Christ .
46008013	Therefore , if food makes my brother stumble , I will never eat meat , lest I make my brother stumble .
46009001	Am I not free ? Am I not an apostle ? Have I not seen Jesus our Lord ? Are not you my workmanship in the Lord ?
46009002	If to others I am not an apostle , at least I am to you , for you are the seal of my apostleship in the Lord .
46009003	This is my defense to those who would examine me .
46009004	Do we not have the right to eat and drink ?
46009005	Do we not have the right to take along a believing wife , as do the other apostles and the brothers of the Lord and Cephas ?
46009006	Or is it only Barnabas and I who have no right to refrain from working for a living ?
46009007	Who serves as a soldier at his own expense ? Who plants a vineyard without eating any of its fruit ? Or who tends a flock without getting some of the milk ?
46009008	Do I say these things on human authority ? Does not the Law say the same ?
