46009009	For it is written in the Law of Moses , “ You shall not muzzle an ox when it treads out the grain . ” Is it for oxen that God is concerned ?
46009010	Does he not speak entirely for our sake ? It was written for our sake , because the plowman should plow in hope and the thresher thresh in hope of sharing in the crop .
46009011	If we have sown spiritual things among you , is it too much if we reap material things from you ?
46009012	If others share this rightful claim on you , do not we even more ? Nevertheless , we have not made use of this right , but we endure anything rather than put an obstacle in the way of the gospel of Christ .
46009013	Do you not know that those who are employed in the temple service get their food from the temple , and those who serve at the altar share in the sacrificial offerings ?
46009014	In the same way , the Lord commanded that those who proclaim the gospel should get their living by the gospel .
46009015	But I have made no use of any of these rights , nor am I writing these things to secure any such provision . For I would rather die than have anyone deprive me of my ground for boasting .
46009016	For if I preach the gospel , that gives me no ground for boasting . For necessity is laid upon me . Woe to me if I do not preach the gospel !
46009017	For if I do this of my own will , I have a reward , but if not of my own will , I am still entrusted with a stewardship .
46009018	What then is my reward ? That in my preaching I may present the gospel free of charge , so as not to make full use of my right in the gospel .
46009019	For though I am free from all , I have made myself a servant to all , that I might win more of them .
46009020	To the Jews I became as a Jew , in order to win Jews . To those under the law I became as one under the law ( though not being myself under the law
46009021	To those outside the law I became as one outside the law ( not being outside the law of God but under the law of Christ
46009022	To the weak I became weak , that I might win the weak . I have become all things to all people , that by all means I might save some .
46009023	I do it all for the sake of the gospel , that I may share with them in its blessings .
46009024	Do you not know that in a race all the runners run , but only one receives the prize ? So run that you may obtain it .
46009025	Every athlete exercises self-control in all things . They do it to receive a perishable wreath , but we an imperishable .
46009026	So I do not run aimlessly ; I do not box as one beating the air .
46009027	But I discipline my body and keep it under control , lest after preaching to others I myself should be disqualified .
46010001	For I want you to know , brothers , that our fathers were all under the cloud , and all passed through the sea ,
46010002	and all were baptized into Moses in the cloud and in the sea ,
46010003	and all ate the same spiritual food ,
46010004	and all drank the same spiritual drink . For they drank from the spiritual Rock that followed them , and the Rock was Christ .
46010005	Nevertheless , with most of them God was not pleased , for they were overthrown in the wilderness .
46010006	Now these things took place as examples for us , that we might not desire evil as they did .
46010007	Do not be idolaters as some of them were ; as it is written , “ The people sat down to eat and drink and rose up to play . ”
46010008	We must not indulge in sexual immorality as some of them did , and twenty-three thousand fell in a single day .
46010009	We must not put Christ to the test , as some of them did and were destroyed by serpents ,
46010010	nor grumble , as some of them did and were destroyed by the Destroyer .
46010011	Now these things happened to them as an example , but they were written down for our instruction , on whom the end of the ages has come .
46010012	Therefore let anyone who thinks that he stands take heed lest he fall .
46010013	No temptation has overtaken you that is not common to man . God is faithful , and he will not let you be tempted beyond your ability , but with the temptation he will also provide the way of escape , that you may be able to endure it .
46010014	Therefore , my beloved , flee from idolatry .
46010015	I speak as to sensible people ; judge for yourselves what I say .
46010016	The cup of blessing that we bless , is it not a participation in the blood of Christ ? The bread that we break , is it not a participation in the body of Christ ?
46010017	Because there is one bread , we who are many are one body , for we all partake of the one bread .
46010018	Consider the people of Israel : are not those who eat the sacrifices participants in the altar ?
46010019	What do I imply then ? That food offered to idols is anything , or that an idol is anything ?
46010020	No , I imply that what pagans sacrifice they offer to demons and not to God . I do not want you to be participants with demons .
46010021	You cannot drink the cup of the Lord and the cup of demons . You cannot partake of the table of the Lord and the table of demons .
46010022	Shall we provoke the Lord to jealousy ? Are we stronger than he ?
46010023	“ All things are lawful , ” but not all things are helpful . “ All things are lawful , ” but not all things build up .
46010024	Let no one seek his own good , but the good of his neighbor .
46010025	Eat whatever is sold in the meat market without raising any question on the ground of conscience .
46010026	For “ the earth is the Lord’s , and the fullness thereof . ”
46010027	If one of the unbelievers invites you to dinner and you are disposed to go , eat whatever is set before you without raising any question on the ground of conscience .
46010028	But if someone says to you , “ This has been offered in sacrifice , ” then do not eat it , for the sake of the one who informed you , and for the sake of conscience —
46010029	I do not mean your conscience , but his . For why should my liberty be determined by someone else’s conscience ?
46010030	If I partake with thankfulness , why am I denounced because of that for which I give thanks ?
46010031	So , whether you eat or drink , or whatever you do , do all to the glory of God .
46010032	Give no offense to Jews or to Greeks or to the church of God ,
46010033	just as I try to please everyone in everything I do , not seeking my own advantage , but that of many , that they may be saved .
46011001	Be imitators of me , as I am of Christ .
46011002	Now I commend you because you remember me in everything and maintain the traditions even as I delivered them to you .
46011003	But I want you to understand that the head of every man is Christ , the head of a wife is her husband , and the head of Christ is God .
46011004	Every man who prays or prophesies with his head covered dishonors his head ,
46011005	but every wife who prays or prophesies with her head uncovered dishonors her head , since it is the same as if her head were shaven .
46011006	For if a wife will not cover her head , then she should cut her hair short . But since it is disgraceful for a wife to cut off her hair or shave her head , let her cover her head .
46011007	For a man ought not to cover his head , since he is the image and glory of God , but woman is the glory of man .
46011008	For man was not made from woman , but woman from man .
46011009	Neither was man created for woman , but woman for man .
46011010	That is why a wife ought to have a symbol of authority on her head , because of the angels .
46011011	Nevertheless , in the Lord woman is not independent of man nor man of woman ;
46011012	for as woman was made from man , so man is now born of woman . And all things are from God .
46011013	Judge for yourselves : is it proper for a wife to pray to God with her head uncovered ?
46011014	Does not nature itself teach you that if a man wears long hair it is a disgrace for him ,
46011015	but if a woman has long hair , it is her glory ? For her hair is given to her for a covering .
46011016	If anyone is inclined to be contentious , we have no such practice , nor do the churches of God .
46011017	But in the following instructions I do not commend you , because when you come together it is not for the better but for the worse .
46011018	For , in the first place , when you come together as a church , I hear that there are divisions among you . And I believe it in part ,
46011019	for there must be factions among you in order that those who are genuine among you may be recognized .
46011020	When you come together , it is not the Lord’s supper that you eat .
46011021	For in eating , each one goes ahead with his own meal . One goes hungry , another gets drunk .
46011022	What ! Do you not have houses to eat and drink in ? Or do you despise the church of God and humiliate those who have nothing ? What shall I say to you ? Shall I commend you in this ? No , I will not .
46011023	For I received from the Lord what I also delivered to you , that the Lord Jesus on the night when he was betrayed took bread ,
46011024	and when he had given thanks , he broke it , and said , “ This is my body which is for you . Do this in remembrance of me . ”
46011025	In the same way also he took the cup , after supper , saying , “ This cup is the new covenant in my blood . Do this , as often as you drink it , in remembrance of me . ”
46011026	For as often as you eat this bread and drink the cup , you proclaim the Lord’s death until he comes .
46011027	Whoever , therefore , eats the bread or drinks the cup of the Lord in an unworthy manner will be guilty concerning the body and blood of the Lord .
46011028	Let a person examine himself , then , and so eat of the bread and drink of the cup .
46011029	For anyone who eats and drinks without discerning the body eats and drinks judgment on himself .
46011030	That is why many of you are weak and ill , and some have died .
46011031	But if we judged ourselves truly , we would not be judged .
46011032	But when we are judged by the Lord , we are disciplined so that we may not be condemned along with the world .
46011033	So then , my brothers , when you come together to eat , wait for one another —
46011034	if anyone is hungry , let him eat at home — so that when you come together it will not be for judgment . About the other things I will give directions when I come .
46012001	Now concerning spiritual gifts , brothers , I do not want you to be uninformed .
46012002	You know that when you were pagans you were led astray to mute idols , however you were led .
46012003	Therefore I want you to understand that no one speaking in the Spirit of God ever says “ Jesus is accursed ! ” and no one can say “ Jesus is Lord ” except in the Holy Spirit .
46012004	Now there are varieties of gifts , but the same Spirit ;
46012005	and there are varieties of service , but the same Lord ;
46012006	and there are varieties of activities , but it is the same God who empowers them all in everyone .
46012007	To each is given the manifestation of the Spirit for the common good .
46012008	For to one is given through the Spirit the utterance of wisdom , and to another the utterance of knowledge according to the same Spirit ,
46012009	to another faith by the same Spirit , to another gifts of healing by the one Spirit ,
46012010	to another the working of miracles , to another prophecy , to another the ability to distinguish between spirits , to another various kinds of tongues , to another the interpretation of tongues .
46012011	All these are empowered by one and the same Spirit , who apportions to each one individually as he wills .
46012012	For just as the body is one and has many members , and all the members of the body , though many , are one body , so it is with Christ .
46012013	For in one Spirit we were all baptized into one body — Jews or Greeks , slaves or free — and all were made to drink of one Spirit .
46012014	For the body does not consist of one member but of many .
46012015	If the foot should say , “ Because I am not a hand , I do not belong to the body , ” that would not make it any less a part of the body .
46012016	And if the ear should say , “ Because I am not an eye , I do not belong to the body , ” that would not make it any less a part of the body .
46012017	If the whole body were an eye , where would be the sense of hearing ? If the whole body were an ear , where would be the sense of smell ?
46012018	But as it is , God arranged the members in the body , each one of them , as he chose .
46012019	If all were a single member , where would the body be ?
46012020	As it is , there are many parts , yet one body .
46012021	The eye cannot say to the hand , “ I have no need of you , ” nor again the head to the feet , “ I have no need of you . ”
46012022	On the contrary , the parts of the body that seem to be weaker are indispensable ,
46012023	and on those parts of the body that we think less honorable we bestow the greater honor , and our unpresentable parts are treated with greater modesty ,
46012024	which our more presentable parts do not require . But God has so composed the body , giving greater honor to the part that lacked it ,
46012025	that there may be no division in the body , but that the members may have the same care for one another .
46012026	If one member suffers , all suffer together ; if one member is honored , all rejoice together .
46012027	Now you are the body of Christ and individually members of it .
46012028	And God has appointed in the church first apostles , second prophets , third teachers , then miracles , then gifts of healing , helping , administrating , and various kinds of tongues .
46012029	Are all apostles ? Are all prophets ? Are all teachers ? Do all work miracles ?
46012030	Do all possess gifts of healing ? Do all speak with tongues ? Do all interpret ?
46012031	But earnestly desire the higher gifts . And I will show you a still more excellent way .
46013001	If I speak in the tongues of men and of angels , but have not love , I am a noisy gong or a clanging cymbal .
46013002	And if I have prophetic powers , and understand all mysteries and all knowledge , and if I have all faith , so as to remove mountains , but have not love , I am nothing .
46013003	If I give away all I have , and if I deliver up my body to be burned , but have not love , I gain nothing .
46013004	Love is patient and kind ; love does not envy or boast ; it is not arrogant
46013005	or rude . It does not insist on its own way ; it is not irritable or resentful ;
46013006	it does not rejoice at wrongdoing , but rejoices with the truth .
46013007	Love bears all things , believes all things , hopes all things , endures all things .
46013008	Love never ends . As for prophecies , they will pass away ; as for tongues , they will cease ; as for knowledge , it will pass away .
46013009	For we know in part and we prophesy in part ,
46013010	but when the perfect comes , the partial will pass away .
46013011	When I was a child , I spoke like a child , I thought like a child , I reasoned like a child . When I became a man , I gave up childish ways .
46013012	For now we see in a mirror dimly , but then face to face . Now I know in part ; then I shall know fully , even as I have been fully known .
46013013	So now faith , hope , and love abide , these three ; but the greatest of these is love .
46014001	Pursue love , and earnestly desire the spiritual gifts , especially that you may prophesy .
46014002	For one who speaks in a tongue speaks not to men but to God ; for no one understands him , but he utters mysteries in the Spirit .
46014003	On the other hand , the one who prophesies speaks to people for their upbuilding and encouragement and consolation .
46014004	The one who speaks in a tongue builds up himself , but the one who prophesies builds up the church .
46014005	Now I want you all to speak in tongues , but even more to prophesy . The one who prophesies is greater than the one who speaks in tongues , unless someone interprets , so that the church may be built up .
46014006	Now , brothers , if I come to you speaking in tongues , how will I benefit you unless I bring you some revelation or knowledge or prophecy or teaching ?
46014007	If even lifeless instruments , such as the flute or the harp , do not give distinct notes , how will anyone know what is played ?
46014008	And if the bugle gives an indistinct sound , who will get ready for battle ?
46014009	So with yourselves , if with your tongue you utter speech that is not intelligible , how will anyone know what is said ? For you will be speaking into the air .
46014010	There are doubtless many different languages in the world , and none is without meaning ,
46014011	but if I do not know the meaning of the language , I will be a foreigner to the speaker and the speaker a foreigner to me .
46014012	So with yourselves , since you are eager for manifestations of the Spirit , strive to excel in building up the church .
46014013	Therefore , one who speaks in a tongue should pray for the power to interpret .
46014014	For if I pray in a tongue , my spirit prays but my mind is unfruitful .
46014015	What am I to do ? I will pray with my spirit , but I will pray with my mind also ; I will sing praise with my spirit , but I will sing with my mind also .
46014016	Otherwise , if you give thanks with your spirit , how can anyone in the position of an outsider say “ Amen ” to your thanksgiving when he does not know what you are saying ?
46014017	For you may be giving thanks well enough , but the other person is not being built up .
46014018	I thank God that I speak in tongues more than all of you .
46014019	Nevertheless , in church I would rather speak five words with my mind in order to instruct others , than ten thousand words in a tongue .
46014020	Brothers , do not be children in your thinking . Be infants in evil , but in your thinking be mature .
46014021	In the Law it is written , “ By people of strange tongues and by the lips of foreigners will I speak to this people , and even then they will not listen to me , says the Lord . ”
46014022	Thus tongues are a sign not for believers but for unbelievers , while prophecy is a sign not for unbelievers but for believers .
46014023	If , therefore , the whole church comes together and all speak in tongues , and outsiders or unbelievers enter , will they not say that you are out of your minds ?
46014024	But if all prophesy , and an unbeliever or outsider enters , he is convicted by all , he is called to account by all ,
46014025	the secrets of his heart are disclosed , and so , falling on his face , he will worship God and declare that God is really among you .
46014026	What then , brothers ? When you come together , each one has a hymn , a lesson , a revelation , a tongue , or an interpretation . Let all things be done for building up .
46014027	If any speak in a tongue , let there be only two or at most three , and each in turn , and let someone interpret .
46014028	But if there is no one to interpret , let each of them keep silent in church and speak to himself and to God .
46014029	Let two or three prophets speak , and let the others weigh what is said .
46014030	If a revelation is made to another sitting there , let the first be silent .
46014031	For you can all prophesy one by one , so that all may learn and all be encouraged ,
46014032	and the spirits of prophets are subject to prophets .
46014033	For God is not a God of confusion but of peace . As in all the churches of the saints ,
46014034	the women should keep silent in the churches . For they are not permitted to speak , but should be in submission , as the Law also says .
46014035	If there is anything they desire to learn , let them ask their husbands at home . For it is shameful for a woman to speak in church .
46014036	Or was it from you that the word of God came ? Or are you the only ones it has reached ?
46014037	If anyone thinks that he is a prophet , or spiritual , he should acknowledge that the things I am writing to you are a command of the Lord .
46014038	If anyone does not recognize this , he is not recognized .
46014039	So , my brothers , earnestly desire to prophesy , and do not forbid speaking in tongues .
46014040	But all things should be done decently and in order .
46015001	Now I would remind you , brothers , of the gospel I preached to you , which you received , in which you stand ,
46015002	and by which you are being saved , if you hold fast to the word I preached to you — unless you believed in vain .
46015003	For I delivered to you as of first importance what I also received : that Christ died for our sins in accordance with the Scriptures ,
46015004	that he was buried , that he was raised on the third day in accordance with the Scriptures ,
46015005	and that he appeared to Cephas , then to the twelve .
46015006	Then he appeared to more than five hundred brothers at one time , most of whom are still alive , though some have fallen asleep .
46015007	Then he appeared to James , then to all the apostles .
46015008	Last of all , as to one untimely born , he appeared also to me .
46015009	For I am the least of the apostles , unworthy to be called an apostle , because I persecuted the church of God .
46015010	But by the grace of God I am what I am , and his grace toward me was not in vain . On the contrary , I worked harder than any of them , though it was not I , but the grace of God that is with me .
46015011	Whether then it was I or they , so we preach and so you believed .
46015012	Now if Christ is proclaimed as raised from the dead , how can some of you say that there is no resurrection of the dead ?
46015013	But if there is no resurrection of the dead , then not even Christ has been raised .
46015014	And if Christ has not been raised , then our preaching is in vain and your faith is in vain .
46015015	We are even found to be misrepresenting God , because we testified about God that he raised Christ , whom he did not raise if it is true that the dead are not raised .
46015016	For if the dead are not raised , not even Christ has been raised .
46015017	And if Christ has not been raised , your faith is futile and you are still in your sins .
46015018	Then those also who have fallen asleep in Christ have perished .
46015019	If in Christ we have hope in this life only , we are of all people most to be pitied .
46015020	But in fact Christ has been raised from the dead , the firstfruits of those who have fallen asleep .
46015021	For as by a man came death , by a man has come also the resurrection of the dead .
46015022	For as in Adam all die , so also in Christ shall all be made alive .
46015023	But each in his own order : Christ the firstfruits , then at his coming those who belong to Christ .
46015024	Then comes the end , when he delivers the kingdom to God the Father after destroying every rule and every authority and power .
46015025	For he must reign until he has put all his enemies under his feet .
46015026	The last enemy to be destroyed is death .
46015027	For “ God has put all things in subjection under his feet . ” But when it says , “ all things are put in subjection , ” it is plain that he is excepted who put all things in subjection under him .
46015028	When all things are subjected to him , then the Son himself will also be subjected to him who put all things in subjection under him , that God may be all in all .
46015029	Otherwise , what do people mean by being baptized on behalf of the dead ? If the dead are not raised at all , why are people baptized on their behalf ?
46015030	Why are we in danger every hour ?
46015031	I protest , brothers , by my pride in you , which I have in Christ Jesus our Lord , I die every day !
46015032	What do I gain if , humanly speaking , I fought with beasts at Ephesus ? If the dead are not raised , “ Let us eat and drink , for tomorrow we die . ”
46015033	Do not be deceived : “ Bad company ruins good morals . ”
46015034	Wake up from your drunken stupor , as is right , and do not go on sinning . For some have no knowledge of God . I say this to your shame .
46015035	But someone will ask , “ How are the dead raised ? With what kind of body do they come ? ”
46015036	You foolish person ! What you sow does not come to life unless it dies .
46015037	And what you sow is not the body that is to be , but a bare kernel , perhaps of wheat or of some other grain .
46015038	But God gives it a body as he has chosen , and to each kind of seed its own body .
46015039	For not all flesh is the same , but there is one kind for humans , another for animals , another for birds , and another for fish .
46015040	There are heavenly bodies and earthly bodies , but the glory of the heavenly is of one kind , and the glory of the earthly is of another .
46015041	There is one glory of the sun , and another glory of the moon , and another glory of the stars ; for star differs from star in glory .
46015042	So is it with the resurrection of the dead . What is sown is perishable ; what is raised is imperishable .
46015043	It is sown in dishonor ; it is raised in glory . It is sown in weakness ; it is raised in power .
46015044	It is sown a natural body ; it is raised a spiritual body . If there is a natural body , there is also a spiritual body .
46015045	Thus it is written , “ The first man Adam became a living being ” ; the last Adam became a life-giving spirit .
46015046	But it is not the spiritual that is first but the natural , and then the spiritual .
46015047	The first man was from the earth , a man of dust ; the second man is from heaven .
46015048	As was the man of dust , so also are those who are of the dust , and as is the man of heaven , so also are those who are of heaven .
46015049	Just as we have borne the image of the man of dust , we shall also bear the image of the man of heaven .
46015050	I tell you this , brothers : flesh and blood cannot inherit the kingdom of God , nor does the perishable inherit the imperishable .
46015051	Behold ! I tell you a mystery . We shall not all sleep , but we shall all be changed ,
46015052	in a moment , in the twinkling of an eye , at the last trumpet . For the trumpet will sound , and the dead will be raised imperishable , and we shall be changed .
46015053	For this perishable body must put on the imperishable , and this mortal body must put on immortality .
46015054	When the perishable puts on the imperishable , and the mortal puts on immortality , then shall come to pass the saying that is written : “ Death is swallowed up in victory . ”
46015055	“ O death , where is your victory ? O death , where is your sting ? ”
46015056	The sting of death is sin , and the power of sin is the law .
46015057	But thanks be to God , who gives us the victory through our Lord Jesus Christ .
46015058	Therefore , my beloved brothers , be steadfast , immovable , always abounding in the work of the Lord , knowing that in the Lord your labor is not in vain .
46016001	Now concerning the collection for the saints : as I directed the churches of Galatia , so you also are to do .
46016002	On the first day of every week , each of you is to put something aside and store it up , as he may prosper , so that there will be no collecting when I come .
46016003	And when I arrive , I will send those whom you accredit by letter to carry your gift to Jerusalem .
46016004	If it seems advisable that I should go also , they will accompany me .
46016005	I will visit you after passing through Macedonia , for I intend to pass through Macedonia ,
46016006	and perhaps I will stay with you or even spend the winter , so that you may help me on my journey , wherever I go .
46016007	For I do not want to see you now just in passing . I hope to spend some time with you , if the Lord permits .
46016008	But I will stay in Ephesus until Pentecost ,
46016009	for a wide door for effective work has opened to me , and there are many adversaries .
46016010	When Timothy comes , see that you put him at ease among you , for he is doing the work of the Lord , as I am .
46016011	So let no one despise him . Help him on his way in peace , that he may return to me , for I am expecting him with the brothers .
46016012	Now concerning our brother Apollos , I strongly urged him to visit you with the other brothers , but it was not at all his will to come now . He will come when he has opportunity .
46016013	Be watchful , stand firm in the faith , act like men , be strong .
46016014	Let all that you do be done in love .
46016015	Now I urge you , brothers — you know that the household of Stephanas were the first converts in Achaia , and that they have devoted themselves to the service of the saints —
46016016	be subject to such as these , and to every fellow worker and laborer .
46016017	I rejoice at the coming of Stephanas and Fortunatus and Achaicus , because they have made up for your absence ,
46016018	for they refreshed my spirit as well as yours . Give recognition to such men .
46016019	The churches of Asia send you greetings . Aquila and Prisca , together with the church in their house , send you hearty greetings in the Lord .
46016020	All the brothers send you greetings . Greet one another with a holy kiss .
46016021	I , Paul , write this greeting with my own hand .
46016022	If anyone has no love for the Lord , let him be accursed . Our Lord , come !
46016023	The grace of the Lord Jesus be with you .
46016024	My love be with you all in Christ Jesus . Amen .
47001001	Paul , an apostle of Christ Jesus by the will of God , and Timothy our brother , To the church of God that is at Corinth , with all the saints who are in the whole of Achaia :
47001002	Grace to you and peace from God our Father and the Lord Jesus Christ .
47001003	Blessed be the God and Father of our Lord Jesus Christ , the Father of mercies and God of all comfort ,
47001004	who comforts us in all our affliction , so that we may be able to comfort those who are in any affliction , with the comfort with which we ourselves are comforted by God .
47001005	For as we share abundantly in Christ’s sufferings , so through Christ we share abundantly in comfort too .
47001006	If we are afflicted , it is for your comfort and salvation ; and if we are comforted , it is for your comfort , which you experience when you patiently endure the same sufferings that we suffer .
47001007	Our hope for you is unshaken , for we know that as you share in our sufferings , you will also share in our comfort .
47001008	For we do not want you to be ignorant , brothers , of the affliction we experienced in Asia . For we were so utterly burdened beyond our strength that we despaired of life itself .
47001009	Indeed , we felt that we had received the sentence of death . But that was to make us rely not on ourselves but on God who raises the dead .
47001010	He delivered us from such a deadly peril , and he will deliver us . On him we have set our hope that he will deliver us again .
47001011	You also must help us by prayer , so that many will give thanks on our behalf for the blessing granted us through the prayers of many .
47001012	For our boast is this , the testimony of our conscience , that we behaved in the world with simplicity and godly sincerity , not by earthly wisdom but by the grace of God , and supremely so toward you .
47001013	For we are not writing to you anything other than what you read and acknowledge and I hope you will fully acknowledge —
47001014	just as you did partially acknowledge us — that on the day of our Lord Jesus you will boast of us as we will boast of you .
47001015	Because I was sure of this , I wanted to come to you first , so that you might have a second experience of grace .
47001016	I wanted to visit you on my way to Macedonia , and to come back to you from Macedonia and have you send me on my way to Judea .
47001017	Was I vacillating when I wanted to do this ? Do I make my plans according to the flesh , ready to say “ Yes , yes ” and “ No , no ” at the same time ?
47001018	As surely as God is faithful , our word to you has not been Yes and No .
47001019	For the Son of God , Jesus Christ , whom we proclaimed among you , Silvanus and Timothy and I , was not Yes and No , but in him it is always Yes .
47001020	For all the promises of God find their Yes in him . That is why it is through him that we utter our Amen to God for his glory .
47001021	And it is God who establishes us with you in Christ , and has anointed us ,
47001022	and who has also put his seal on us and given us his Spirit in our hearts as a guarantee .
47001023	But I call God to witness against me — it was to spare you that I refrained from coming again to Corinth .
47001024	Not that we lord it over your faith , but we work with you for your joy , for you stand firm in your faith .
47002001	For I made up my mind not to make another painful visit to you .
47002002	For if I cause you pain , who is there to make me glad but the one whom I have pained ?
47002003	And I wrote as I did , so that when I came I might not suffer pain from those who should have made me rejoice , for I felt sure of all of you , that my joy would be the joy of you all .
47002004	For I wrote to you out of much affliction and anguish of heart and with many tears , not to cause you pain but to let you know the abundant love that I have for you .
47002005	Now if anyone has caused pain , he has caused it not to me , but in some measure — not to put it too severely — to all of you .
47002006	For such a one , this punishment by the majority is enough ,
47002007	so you should rather turn to forgive and comfort him , or he may be overwhelmed by excessive sorrow .
47002008	So I beg you to reaffirm your love for him .
47002009	For this is why I wrote , that I might test you and know whether you are obedient in everything .
47002010	Anyone whom you forgive , I also forgive . Indeed , what I have forgiven , if I have forgiven anything , has been for your sake in the presence of Christ ,
47002011	so that we would not be outwitted by Satan ; for we are not ignorant of his designs .
47002012	When I came to Troas to preach the gospel of Christ , even though a door was opened for me in the Lord ,
47002013	my spirit was not at rest because I did not find my brother Titus there . So I took leave of them and went on to Macedonia .
47002014	But thanks be to God , who in Christ always leads us in triumphal procession , and through us spreads the fragrance of the knowledge of him everywhere .
47002015	For we are the aroma of Christ to God among those who are being saved and among those who are perishing ,
47002016	to one a fragrance from death to death , to the other a fragrance from life to life . Who is sufficient for these things ?
47002017	For we are not , like so many , peddlers of God’s word , but as men of sincerity , as commissioned by God , in the sight of God we speak in Christ .
47003001	Are we beginning to commend ourselves again ? Or do we need , as some do , letters of recommendation to you , or from you ?
47003002	You yourselves are our letter of recommendation , written on our hearts , to be known and read by all .
47003003	And you show that you are a letter from Christ delivered by us , written not with ink but with the Spirit of the living God , not on tablets of stone but on tablets of human hearts .
47003004	Such is the confidence that we have through Christ toward God .
47003005	Not that we are sufficient in ourselves to claim anything as coming from us , but our sufficiency is from God ,
47003006	who has made us competent to be ministers of a new covenant , not of the letter but of the Spirit . For the letter kills , but the Spirit gives life .
47003007	Now if the ministry of death , carved in letters on stone , came with such glory that the Israelites could not gaze at Moses ’ face because of its glory , which was being brought to an end ,
47003008	will not the ministry of the Spirit have even more glory ?
47003009	For if there was glory in the ministry of condemnation , the ministry of righteousness must far exceed it in glory .
47003010	Indeed , in this case , what once had glory has come to have no glory at all , because of the glory that surpasses it .
47003011	For if what was being brought to an end came with glory , much more will what is permanent have glory .
47003012	Since we have such a hope , we are very bold ,
47003013	not like Moses , who would put a veil over his face so that the Israelites might not gaze at the outcome of what was being brought to an end .
47003014	But their minds were hardened . For to this day , when they read the old covenant , that same veil remains unlifted , because only through Christ is it taken away .
47003015	Yes , to this day whenever Moses is read a veil lies over their hearts .
47003016	But when one turns to the Lord , the veil is removed .
47003017	Now the Lord is the Spirit , and where the Spirit of the Lord is , there is freedom .
47003018	And we all , with unveiled face , beholding the glory of the Lord , are being transformed into the same image from one degree of glory to another . For this comes from the Lord who is the Spirit .
47004001	Therefore , having this ministry by the mercy of God , we do not lose heart .
47004002	But we have renounced disgraceful , underhanded ways . We refuse to practice cunning or to tamper with God’s word , but by the open statement of the truth we would commend ourselves to everyone’s conscience in the sight of God .
47004003	And even if our gospel is veiled , it is veiled only to those who are perishing .
47004004	In their case the god of this world has blinded the minds of the unbelievers , to keep them from seeing the light of the gospel of the glory of Christ , who is the image of God .
47004005	For what we proclaim is not ourselves , but Jesus Christ as Lord , with ourselves as your servants for Jesus ’ sake .
47004006	For God , who said , “ Let light shine out of darkness , ” has shone in our hearts to give the light of the knowledge of the glory of God in the face of Jesus Christ .
47004007	But we have this treasure in jars of clay , to show that the surpassing power belongs to God and not to us .
47004008	We are afflicted in every way , but not crushed ; perplexed , but not driven to despair ;
47004009	persecuted , but not forsaken ; struck down , but not destroyed ;
47004010	always carrying in the body the death of Jesus , so that the life of Jesus may also be manifested in our bodies .
47004011	For we who live are always being given over to death for Jesus ’ sake , so that the life of Jesus also may be manifested in our mortal flesh .
47004012	So death is at work in us , but life in you .
47004013	Since we have the same spirit of faith according to what has been written , “ I believed , and so I spoke , ” we also believe , and so we also speak ,
47004014	knowing that he who raised the Lord Jesus will raise us also with Jesus and bring us with you into his presence .
47004015	For it is all for your sake , so that as grace extends to more and more people it may increase thanksgiving , to the glory of God .
47004016	So we do not lose heart . Though our outer self is wasting away , our inner self is being renewed day by day .
47004017	For this light momentary affliction is preparing for us an eternal weight of glory beyond all comparison ,
47004018	as we look not to the things that are seen but to the things that are unseen . For the things that are seen are transient , but the things that are unseen are eternal .
47005001	For we know that if the tent that is our earthly home is destroyed , we have a building from God , a house not made with hands , eternal in the heavens .
47005002	For in this tent we groan , longing to put on our heavenly dwelling ,
47005003	if indeed by putting it on we may not be found naked .
47005004	For while we are still in this tent , we groan , being burdened — not that we would be unclothed , but that we would be further clothed , so that what is mortal may be swallowed up by life .
47005005	He who has prepared us for this very thing is God , who has given us the Spirit as a guarantee .
47005006	So we are always of good courage . We know that while we are at home in the body we are away from the Lord ,
47005007	for we walk by faith , not by sight .
47005008	Yes , we are of good courage , and we would rather be away from the body and at home with the Lord .
47005009	So whether we are at home or away , we make it our aim to please him .
47005010	For we must all appear before the judgment seat of Christ , so that each one may receive what is due for what he has done in the body , whether good or evil .
47005011	Therefore , knowing the fear of the Lord , we persuade others . But what we are is known to God , and I hope it is known also to your conscience .
47005012	We are not commending ourselves to you again but giving you cause to boast about us , so that you may be able to answer those who boast about outward appearance and not about what is in the heart .
47005013	For if we are beside ourselves , it is for God ; if we are in our right mind , it is for you .
47005014	For the love of Christ controls us , because we have concluded this : that one has died for all , therefore all have died ;
47005015	and he died for all , that those who live might no longer live for themselves but for him who for their sake died and was raised .
47005016	From now on , therefore , we regard no one according to the flesh . Even though we once regarded Christ according to the flesh , we regard him thus no longer .
47005017	Therefore , if anyone is in Christ , he is a new creation . The old has passed away ; behold , the new has come .
47005018	All this is from God , who through Christ reconciled us to himself and gave us the ministry of reconciliation ;
47005019	that is , in Christ God was reconciling the world to himself , not counting their trespasses against them , and entrusting to us the message of reconciliation .
47005020	Therefore , we are ambassadors for Christ , God making his appeal through us . We implore you on behalf of Christ , be reconciled to God .
47005021	For our sake he made him to be sin who knew no sin , so that in him we might become the righteousness of God .
47006001	Working together with him , then , we appeal to you not to receive the grace of God in vain .
47006002	For he says , “ In a favorable time I listened to you , and in a day of salvation I have helped you . ” Behold , now is the favorable time ; behold , now is the day of salvation .
47006003	We put no obstacle in anyone’s way , so that no fault may be found with our ministry ,
47006004	but as servants of God we commend ourselves in every way : by great endurance , in afflictions , hardships , calamities ,
47006005	beatings , imprisonments , riots , labors , sleepless nights , hunger ;
47006006	by purity , knowledge , patience , kindness , the Holy Spirit , genuine love ;
47006007	by truthful speech , and the power of God ; with the weapons of righteousness for the right hand and for the left ;
47006008	through honor and dishonor , through slander and praise . We are treated as impostors , and yet are true ;
47006009	as unknown , and yet well known ; as dying , and behold , we live ; as punished , and yet not killed ;
47006010	as sorrowful , yet always rejoicing ; as poor , yet making many rich ; as having nothing , yet possessing everything .
47006011	We have spoken freely to you , Corinthians ; our heart is wide open .
47006012	You are not restricted by us , but you are restricted in your own affections .
47006013	In return ( I speak as to children
47006014	Do not be unequally yoked with unbelievers . For what partnership has righteousness with lawlessness ? Or what fellowship has light with darkness ?
47006015	What accord has Christ with Belial ? Or what portion does a believer share with an unbeliever ?
47006016	What agreement has the temple of God with idols ? For we are the temple of the living God ; as God said , “ I will make my dwelling among them and walk among them , and I will be their God , and they shall be my people .
47006017	Therefore go out from their midst , and be separate from them , says the Lord , and touch no unclean thing ; then I will welcome you ,
47006018	and I will be a father to you , and you shall be sons and daughters to me , says the Lord Almighty . ”
47007001	Since we have these promises , beloved , let us cleanse ourselves from every defilement of body and spirit , bringing holiness to completion in the fear of God .
47007002	Make room in your hearts for us . We have wronged no one , we have corrupted no one , we have taken advantage of no one .
47007003	I do not say this to condemn you , for I said before that you are in our hearts , to die together and to live together .
47007004	I am acting with great boldness toward you ; I have great pride in you ; I am filled with comfort . In all our affliction , I am overflowing with joy .
47007005	For even when we came into Macedonia , our bodies had no rest , but we were afflicted at every turn — fighting without and fear within .
47007006	But God , who comforts the downcast , comforted us by the coming of Titus ,
47007007	and not only by his coming but also by the comfort with which he was comforted by you , as he told us of your longing , your mourning , your zeal for me , so that I rejoiced still more .
47007008	For even if I made you grieve with my letter , I do not regret it — though I did regret it , for I see that that letter grieved you , though only for a while .
47007009	As it is , I rejoice , not because you were grieved , but because you were grieved into repenting . For you felt a godly grief , so that you suffered no loss through us .
47007010	For godly grief produces a repentance that leads to salvation without regret , whereas worldly grief produces death .
47007011	For see what earnestness this godly grief has produced in you , but also what eagerness to clear yourselves , what indignation , what fear , what longing , what zeal , what punishment ! At every point you have proved yourselves innocent in the matter .
47007012	So although I wrote to you , it was not for the sake of the one who did the wrong , nor for the sake of the one who suffered the wrong , but in order that your earnestness for us might be revealed to you in the sight of God .
47007013	Therefore we are comforted . And besides our own comfort , we rejoiced still more at the joy of Titus , because his spirit has been refreshed by you all .
47007014	For whatever boasts I made to him about you , I was not put to shame . But just as everything we said to you was true , so also our boasting before Titus has proved true .
47007015	And his affection for you is even greater , as he remembers the obedience of you all , how you received him with fear and trembling .
47007016	I rejoice , because I have perfect confidence in you .
47008001	We want you to know , brothers , about the grace of God that has been given among the churches of Macedonia ,
47008002	for in a severe test of affliction , their abundance of joy and their extreme poverty have overflowed in a wealth of generosity on their part .
47008003	For they gave according to their means , as I can testify , and beyond their means , of their own accord ,
47008004	begging us earnestly for the favor of taking part in the relief of the saints —
47008005	and this , not as we expected , but they gave themselves first to the Lord and then by the will of God to us .
47008006	Accordingly , we urged Titus that as he had started , so he should complete among you this act of grace .
47008007	But as you excel in everything — in faith , in speech , in knowledge , in all earnestness , and in our love for you — see that you excel in this act of grace also .
47008008	I say this not as a command , but to prove by the earnestness of others that your love also is genuine .
47008009	For you know the grace of our Lord Jesus Christ , that though he was rich , yet for your sake he became poor , so that you by his poverty might become rich .
47008010	And in this matter I give my judgment : this benefits you , who a year ago started not only to do this work but also to desire to do it .
47008011	So now finish doing it as well , so that your readiness in desiring it may be matched by your completing it out of what you have .
47008012	For if the readiness is there , it is acceptable according to what a person has , not according to what he does not have .
47008013	For I do not mean that others should be eased and you burdened , but that as a matter of fairness
47008014	your abundance at the present time should supply their need , so that their abundance may supply your need , that there may be fairness .
47008015	As it is written , “ Whoever gathered much had nothing left over , and whoever gathered little had no lack . ”
47008016	But thanks be to God , who put into the heart of Titus the same earnest care I have for you .
47008017	For he not only accepted our appeal , but being himself very earnest he is going to you of his own accord .
47008018	With him we are sending the brother who is famous among all the churches for his preaching of the gospel .
47008019	And not only that , but he has been appointed by the churches to travel with us as we carry out this act of grace that is being ministered by us , for the glory of the Lord himself and to show our good will .
47008020	We take this course so that no one should blame us about this generous gift that is being administered by us ,
47008021	for we aim at what is honorable not only in the Lord’s sight but also in the sight of man .
47008022	And with them we are sending our brother whom we have often tested and found earnest in many matters , but who is now more earnest than ever because of his great confidence in you .
47008023	As for Titus , he is my partner and fellow worker for your benefit . And as for our brothers , they are messengers of the churches , the glory of Christ .
47008024	So give proof before the churches of your love and of our boasting about you to these men .
47009001	Now it is superfluous for me to write to you about the ministry for the saints ,
47009002	for I know your readiness , of which I boast about you to the people of Macedonia , saying that Achaia has been ready since last year . And your zeal has stirred up most of them .
47009003	But I am sending the brothers so that our boasting about you may not prove empty in this matter , so that you may be ready , as I said you would be .
47009004	Otherwise , if some Macedonians come with me and find that you are not ready , we would be humiliated — to say nothing of you — for being so confident .
47009005	So I thought it necessary to urge the brothers to go on ahead to you and arrange in advance for the gift you have promised , so that it may be ready as a willing gift , not as an exaction .
47009006	The point is this : whoever sows sparingly will also reap sparingly , and whoever sows bountifully will also reap bountifully .
47009007	Each one must give as he has decided in his heart , not reluctantly or under compulsion , for God loves a cheerful giver .
47009008	And God is able to make all grace abound to you , so that having all sufficiency in all things at all times , you may abound in every good work .
47009009	As it is written , “ He has distributed freely , he has given to the poor ; his righteousness endures forever . ”
47009010	He who supplies seed to the sower and bread for food will supply and multiply your seed for sowing and increase the harvest of your righteousness .
47009011	You will be enriched in every way to be generous in every way , which through us will produce thanksgiving to God .
47009012	For the ministry of this service is not only supplying the needs of the saints but is also overflowing in many thanksgivings to God .
47009013	By their approval of this service , they will glorify God because of your submission flowing from your confession of the gospel of Christ , and the generosity of your contribution for them and for all others ,
47009014	while they long for you and pray for you , because of the surpassing grace of God upon you .
47009015	Thanks be to God for his inexpressible gift !
47010001	I , Paul , myself entreat you , by the meekness and gentleness of Christ — I who am humble when face to face with you , but bold toward you when I am away ! —
47010002	I beg of you that when I am present I may not have to show boldness with such confidence as I count on showing against some who suspect us of walking according to the flesh .
47010003	For though we walk in the flesh , we are not waging war according to the flesh .
47010004	For the weapons of our warfare are not of the flesh but have divine power to destroy strongholds .
47010005	We destroy arguments and every lofty opinion raised against the knowledge of God , and take every thought captive to obey Christ ,
47010006	being ready to punish every disobedience , when your obedience is complete .
47010007	Look at what is before your eyes . If anyone is confident that he is Christ’s , let him remind himself that just as he is Christ’s , so also are we .
47010008	For even if I boast a little too much of our authority , which the Lord gave for building you up and not for destroying you , I will not be ashamed .
47010009	I do not want to appear to be frightening you with my letters .
47010010	For they say , “ His letters are weighty and strong , but his bodily presence is weak , and his speech of no account . ”
47010011	Let such a person understand that what we say by letter when absent , we do when present .
47010012	Not that we dare to classify or compare ourselves with some of those who are commending themselves . But when they measure themselves by one another and compare themselves with one another , they are without understanding .
47010013	But we will not boast beyond limits , but will boast only with regard to the area of influence God assigned to us , to reach even to you .
47010014	For we are not overextending ourselves , as though we did not reach you . For we were the first to come all the way to you with the gospel of Christ .
47010015	We do not boast beyond limit in the labors of others . But our hope is that as your faith increases , our area of influence among you may be greatly enlarged ,
47010016	so that we may preach the gospel in lands beyond you , without boasting of work already done in another’s area of influence .
47010017	“ Let the one who boasts , boast in the Lord . ”
47010018	For it is not the one who commends himself who is approved , but the one whom the Lord commends .
47011001	I wish you would bear with me in a little foolishness . Do bear with me !
47011002	For I feel a divine jealousy for you , since I betrothed you to one husband , to present you as a pure virgin to Christ .
47011003	But I am afraid that as the serpent deceived Eve by his cunning , your thoughts will be led astray from a sincere and pure devotion to Christ .
47011004	For if someone comes and proclaims another Jesus than the one we proclaimed , or if you receive a different spirit from the one you received , or if you accept a different gospel from the one you accepted , you put up with it readily enough .
47011005	Indeed , I consider that I am not in the least inferior to these super-apostles .
47011006	Even if I am unskilled in speaking , I am not so in knowledge ; indeed , in every way we have made this plain to you in all things .
47011007	Or did I commit a sin in humbling myself so that you might be exalted , because I preached God’s gospel to you free of charge ?
47011008	I robbed other churches by accepting support from them in order to serve you .
47011009	And when I was with you and was in need , I did not burden anyone , for the brothers who came from Macedonia supplied my need . So I refrained and will refrain from burdening you in any way .
47011010	As the truth of Christ is in me , this boasting of mine will not be silenced in the regions of Achaia .
47011011	And why ? Because I do not love you ? God knows I do !
47011012	And what I do I will continue to do , in order to undermine the claim of those who would like to claim that in their boasted mission they work on the same terms as we do .
47011013	For such men are false apostles , deceitful workmen , disguising themselves as apostles of Christ .
47011014	And no wonder , for even Satan disguises himself as an angel of light .
47011015	So it is no surprise if his servants , also , disguise themselves as servants of righteousness . Their end will correspond to their deeds .
47011016	I repeat , let no one think me foolish . But even if you do , accept me as a fool , so that I too may boast a little .
47011017	What I am saying with this boastful confidence , I say not with the Lord’s authority but as a fool .
47011018	Since many boast according to the flesh , I too will boast .
47011019	For you gladly bear with fools , being wise yourselves !
47011020	For you bear it if someone makes slaves of you , or devours you , or takes advantage of you , or puts on airs , or strikes you in the face .
47011021	To my shame , I must say , we were too weak for that ! But whatever anyone else dares to boast of — I am speaking as a fool — I also dare to boast of that .
47011022	Are they Hebrews ? So am I . Are they Israelites ? So am I . Are they offspring of Abraham ? So am I .
47011023	Are they servants of Christ ? I am a better one — I am talking like a madman — with far greater labors , far more imprisonments , with countless beatings , and often near death .
47011024	Five times I received at the hands of the Jews the forty lashes less one .
47011025	Three times I was beaten with rods . Once I was stoned . Three times I was shipwrecked ; a night and a day I was adrift at sea ;
47011026	on frequent journeys , in danger from rivers , danger from robbers , danger from my own people , danger from Gentiles , danger in the city , danger in the wilderness , danger at sea , danger from false brothers ;
47011027	in toil and hardship , through many a sleepless night , in hunger and thirst , often without food , in cold and exposure .
47011028	And , apart from other things , there is the daily pressure on me of my anxiety for all the churches .
47011029	Who is weak , and I am not weak ? Who is made to fall , and I am not indignant ?
47011030	If I must boast , I will boast of the things that show my weakness .
47011031	The God and Father of the Lord Jesus , he who is blessed forever , knows that I am not lying .
47011032	At Damascus , the governor under King Aretas was guarding the city of Damascus in order to seize me ,
47011033	but I was let down in a basket through a window in the wall and escaped his hands .
47012001	I must go on boasting . Though there is nothing to be gained by it , I will go on to visions and revelations of the Lord .
47012002	I know a man in Christ who fourteen years ago was caught up to the third heaven — whether in the body or out of the body I do not know , God knows .
47012003	And I know that this man was caught up into paradise — whether in the body or out of the body I do not know , God knows —
47012004	and he heard things that cannot be told , which man may not utter .
47012005	On behalf of this man I will boast , but on my own behalf I will not boast , except of my weaknesses .
47012006	Though if I should wish to boast , I would not be a fool , for I would be speaking the truth . But I refrain from it , so that no one may think more of me than he sees in me or hears from me .
47012007	So to keep me from becoming conceited because of the surpassing greatness of the revelations , a thorn was given me in the flesh , a messenger of Satan to harass me , to keep me from becoming conceited .
47012008	Three times I pleaded with the Lord about this , that it should leave me .
47012009	But he said to me , “ My grace is sufficient for you , for my power is made perfect in weakness . ” Therefore I will boast all the more gladly of my weaknesses , so that the power of Christ may rest upon me .
47012010	For the sake of Christ , then , I am content with weaknesses , insults , hardships , persecutions , and calamities . For when I am weak , then I am strong .
47012011	I have been a fool ! You forced me to it , for I ought to have been commended by you . For I was not at all inferior to these super-apostles , even though I am nothing .
47012012	The signs of a true apostle were performed among you with utmost patience , with signs and wonders and mighty works .
47012013	For in what were you less favored than the rest of the churches , except that I myself did not burden you ? Forgive me this wrong !
47012014	Here for the third time I am ready to come to you . And I will not be a burden , for I seek not what is yours but you . For children are not obligated to save up for their parents , but parents for their children .
47012015	I will most gladly spend and be spent for your souls . If I love you more , am I to be loved less ?
47012016	But granting that I myself did not burden you , I was crafty , you say , and got the better of you by deceit .
47012017	Did I take advantage of you through any of those whom I sent to you ?
47012018	I urged Titus to go , and sent the brother with him . Did Titus take advantage of you ? Did we not act in the same spirit ? Did we not take the same steps ?
47012019	Have you been thinking all along that we have been defending ourselves to you ? It is in the sight of God that we have been speaking in Christ , and all for your upbuilding , beloved .
47012020	For I fear that perhaps when I come I may find you not as I wish , and that you may find me not as you wish — that perhaps there may be quarreling , jealousy , anger , hostility , slander , gossip , conceit , and disorder .
47012021	I fear that when I come again my God may humble me before you , and I may have to mourn over many of those who sinned earlier and have not repented of the impurity , sexual immorality , and sensuality that they have practiced .
47013001	This is the third time I am coming to you . Every charge must be established by the evidence of two or three witnesses .
47013002	I warned those who sinned before and all the others , and I warn them now while absent , as I did when present on my second visit , that if I come again I will not spare them —
47013003	since you seek proof that Christ is speaking in me . He is not weak in dealing with you , but is powerful among you .
47013004	For he was crucified in weakness , but lives by the power of God . For we also are weak in him , but in dealing with you we will live with him by the power of God .
47013005	Examine yourselves , to see whether you are in the faith . Test yourselves . Or do you not realize this about yourselves , that Jesus Christ is in you ? — unless indeed you fail to meet the test !
47013006	I hope you will find out that we have not failed the test .
47013007	But we pray to God that you may not do wrong — not that we may appear to have met the test , but that you may do what is right , though we may seem to have failed .
47013008	For we cannot do anything against the truth , but only for the truth .
47013009	For we are glad when we are weak and you are strong . Your restoration is what we pray for .
47013010	For this reason I write these things while I am away from you , that when I come I may not have to be severe in my use of the authority that the Lord has given me for building up and not for tearing down .
47013011	Finally , brothers , rejoice . Aim for restoration , comfort one another , agree with one another , live in peace ; and the God of love and peace will be with you .
47013012	Greet one another with a holy kiss .
47013013	All the saints greet you .
47013014	The grace of the Lord Jesus Christ and the love of God and the fellowship of the Holy Spirit be with you all .
48001001	Paul , an apostle — not from men nor through man , but through Jesus Christ and God the Father , who raised him from the dead —
48001002	and all the brothers who are with me , To the churches of Galatia :
48001003	Grace to you and peace from God our Father and the Lord Jesus Christ ,
48001004	who gave himself for our sins to deliver us from the present evil age , according to the will of our God and Father ,
48001005	to whom be the glory forever and ever . Amen .
48001006	I am astonished that you are so quickly deserting him who called you in the grace of Christ and are turning to a different gospel —
48001007	not that there is another one , but there are some who trouble you and want to distort the gospel of Christ .
48001008	But even if we or an angel from heaven should preach to you a gospel contrary to the one we preached to you , let him be accursed .
48001009	As we have said before , so now I say again : If anyone is preaching to you a gospel contrary to the one you received , let him be accursed .
48001010	For am I now seeking the approval of man , or of God ? Or am I trying to please man ? If I were still trying to please man , I would not be a servant of Christ .
48001011	For I would have you know , brothers , that the gospel that was preached by me is not man’s gospel .
48001012	For I did not receive it from any man , nor was I taught it , but I received it through a revelation of Jesus Christ .
48001013	For you have heard of my former life in Judaism , how I persecuted the church of God violently and tried to destroy it .
48001014	And I was advancing in Judaism beyond many of my own age among my people , so extremely zealous was I for the traditions of my fathers .
48001015	But when he who had set me apart before I was born , and who called me by his grace ,
48001016	was pleased to reveal his Son to me , in order that I might preach him among the Gentiles , I did not immediately consult with anyone ;
48001017	nor did I go up to Jerusalem to those who were apostles before me , but I went away into Arabia , and returned again to Damascus .
48001018	Then after three years I went up to Jerusalem to visit Cephas and remained with him fifteen days .
48001019	But I saw none of the other apostles except James the Lord’s brother .
48001020	( In what I am writing to you , before God , I do not lie !
48001021	Then I went into the regions of Syria and Cilicia .
48001022	And I was still unknown in person to the churches of Judea that are in Christ .
48001023	They only were hearing it said , “ He who used to persecute us is now preaching the faith he once tried to destroy . ”
48001024	And they glorified God because of me .
48002001	Then after fourteen years I went up again to Jerusalem with Barnabas , taking Titus along with me .
48002002	I went up because of a revelation and set before them ( though privately before those who seemed influential
48002003	But even Titus , who was with me , was not forced to be circumcised , though he was a Greek .
48002004	Yet because of false brothers secretly brought in — who slipped in to spy out our freedom that we have in Christ Jesus , so that they might bring us into slavery —
48002005	to them we did not yield in submission even for a moment , so that the truth of the gospel might be preserved for you .
48002006	And from those who seemed to be influential ( what they were makes no difference to me ; God shows no partiality ) — those , I say , who seemed influential added nothing to me .
48002007	On the contrary , when they saw that I had been entrusted with the gospel to the uncircumcised , just as Peter had been entrusted with the gospel to the circumcised
48002008	( for he who worked through Peter for his apostolic ministry to the circumcised worked also through me for mine to the Gentiles ) ,
48002009	and when James and Cephas and John , who seemed to be pillars , perceived the grace that was given to me , they gave the right hand of fellowship to Barnabas and me , that we should go to the Gentiles and they to the circumcised .
48002010	Only , they asked us to remember the poor , the very thing I was eager to do .
48002011	But when Cephas came to Antioch , I opposed him to his face , because he stood condemned .
48002012	For before certain men came from James , he was eating with the Gentiles ; but when they came he drew back and separated himself , fearing the circumcision party .
48002013	And the rest of the Jews acted hypocritically along with him , so that even Barnabas was led astray by their hypocrisy .
48002014	But when I saw that their conduct was not in step with the truth of the gospel , I said to Cephas before them all , “ If you , though a Jew , live like a Gentile and not like a Jew , how can you force the Gentiles to live like Jews ? ”
48002015	We ourselves are Jews by birth and not Gentile sinners ;
48002016	yet we know that a person is not justified by works of the law but through faith in Jesus Christ , so we also have believed in Christ Jesus , in order to be justified by faith in Christ and not by works of the law , because by works of the law no one will be justified .
48002017	But if , in our endeavor to be justified in Christ , we too were found to be sinners , is Christ then a servant of sin ? Certainly not !
48002018	For if I rebuild what I tore down , I prove myself to be a transgressor .
48002019	For through the law I died to the law , so that I might live to God .
48002020	I have been crucified with Christ . It is no longer I who live , but Christ who lives in me . And the life I now live in the flesh I live by faith in the Son of God , who loved me and gave himself for me .
48002021	I do not nullify the grace of God , for if righteousness were through the law , then Christ died for no purpose .
48003001	O foolish Galatians ! Who has bewitched you ? It was before your eyes that Jesus Christ was publicly portrayed as crucified .
48003002	Let me ask you only this : Did you receive the Spirit by works of the law or by hearing with faith ?
48003003	Are you so foolish ? Having begun by the Spirit , are you now being perfected by the flesh ?
48003004	Did you suffer so many things in vain — if indeed it was in vain ?
48003005	Does he who supplies the Spirit to you and works miracles among you do so by works of the law , or by hearing with faith —
48003006	just as Abraham “ believed God , and it was counted to him as righteousness ” ?
48003007	Know then that it is those of faith who are the sons of Abraham .
48003008	And the Scripture , foreseeing that God would justify the Gentiles by faith , preached the gospel beforehand to Abraham , saying , “ In you shall all the nations be blessed . ”
48003009	So then , those who are of faith are blessed along with Abraham , the man of faith .
48003010	For all who rely on works of the law are under a curse ; for it is written , “ Cursed be everyone who does not abide by all things written in the Book of the Law , and do them . ”
48003011	Now it is evident that no one is justified before God by the law , for “ The righteous shall live by faith . ”
48003012	But the law is not of faith , rather “ The one who does them shall live by them . ”
48003013	Christ redeemed us from the curse of the law by becoming a curse for us — for it is written , “ Cursed is everyone who is hanged on a tree ” —
48003014	so that in Christ Jesus the blessing of Abraham might come to the Gentiles , so that we might receive the promised Spirit through faith .
48003015	To give a human example , brothers : even with a man-made covenant , no one annuls it or adds to it once it has been ratified .
48003016	Now the promises were made to Abraham and to his offspring . It does not say , “ And to offsprings , ” referring to many , but referring to one , “ And to your offspring , ” who is Christ .
48003017	This is what I mean : the law , which came 430 years afterward , does not annul a covenant previously ratified by God , so as to make the promise void .
48003018	For if the inheritance comes by the law , it no longer comes by promise ; but God gave it to Abraham by a promise .
48003019	Why then the law ? It was added because of transgressions , until the offspring should come to whom the promise had been made , and it was put in place through angels by an intermediary .
48003020	Now an intermediary implies more than one , but God is one .
48003021	Is the law then contrary to the promises of God ? Certainly not ! For if a law had been given that could give life , then righteousness would indeed be by the law .
48003022	But the Scripture imprisoned everything under sin , so that the promise by faith in Jesus Christ might be given to those who believe .
48003023	Now before faith came , we were held captive under the law , imprisoned until the coming faith would be revealed .
48003024	So then , the law was our guardian until Christ came , in order that we might be justified by faith .
48003025	But now that faith has come , we are no longer under a guardian ,
48003026	for in Christ Jesus you are all sons of God , through faith .
48003027	For as many of you as were baptized into Christ have put on Christ .
48003028	There is neither Jew nor Greek , there is neither slave nor free , there is no male and female , for you are all one in Christ Jesus .
48003029	And if you are Christ’s , then you are Abraham’s offspring , heirs according to promise .
48004001	I mean that the heir , as long as he is a child , is no different from a slave , though he is the owner of everything ,
48004002	but he is under guardians and managers until the date set by his father .
48004003	In the same way we also , when we were children , were enslaved to the elementary principles of the world .
48004004	But when the fullness of time had come , God sent forth his Son , born of woman , born under the law ,
48004005	to redeem those who were under the law , so that we might receive adoption as sons .
48004006	And because you are sons , God has sent the Spirit of his Son into our hearts , crying , “ Abba ! Father ! ”
48004007	So you are no longer a slave , but a son , and if a son , then an heir through God .
48004008	Formerly , when you did not know God , you were enslaved to those that by nature are not gods .
48004009	But now that you have come to know God , or rather to be known by God , how can you turn back again to the weak and worthless elementary principles of the world , whose slaves you want to be once more ?
48004010	You observe days and months and seasons and years !
48004011	I am afraid I may have labored over you in vain .
48004012	Brothers , I entreat you , become as I am , for I also have become as you are . You did me no wrong .
48004013	You know it was because of a bodily ailment that I preached the gospel to you at first ,
48004014	and though my condition was a trial to you , you did not scorn or despise me , but received me as an angel of God , as Christ Jesus .
48004015	What then has become of the blessing you felt ? For I testify to you that , if possible , you would have gouged out your eyes and given them to me .
48004016	Have I then become your enemy by telling you the truth ?
48004017	They make much of you , but for no good purpose . They want to shut you out , that you may make much of them .
48004018	It is always good to be made much of for a good purpose , and not only when I am present with you ,
48004019	my little children , for whom I am again in the anguish of childbirth until Christ is formed in you !
48004020	I wish I could be present with you now and change my tone , for I am perplexed about you .
48004021	Tell me , you who desire to be under the law , do you not listen to the law ?
48004022	For it is written that Abraham had two sons , one by a slave woman and one by a free woman .
48004023	But the son of the slave was born according to the flesh , while the son of the free woman was born through promise .
48004024	Now this may be interpreted allegorically : these women are two covenants . One is from Mount Sinai , bearing children for slavery ; she is Hagar .
48004025	Now Hagar is Mount Sinai in Arabia ; she corresponds to the present Jerusalem , for she is in slavery with her children .
48004026	But the Jerusalem above is free , and she is our mother .
48004027	For it is written , “ Rejoice , O barren one who does not bear ; break forth and cry aloud , you who are not in labor ! For the children of the desolate one will be more than those of the one who has a husband . ”
48004028	Now you , brothers , like Isaac , are children of promise .
48004029	But just as at that time he who was born according to the flesh persecuted him who was born according to the Spirit , so also it is now .
48004030	But what does the Scripture say ? “ Cast out the slave woman and her son , for the son of the slave woman shall not inherit with the son of the free woman . ”
48004031	So , brothers , we are not children of the slave but of the free woman .
48005001	For freedom Christ has set us free ; stand firm therefore , and do not submit again to a yoke of slavery .
48005002	Look : I , Paul , say to you that if you accept circumcision , Christ will be of no advantage to you .
48005003	I testify again to every man who accepts circumcision that he is obligated to keep the whole law .
48005004	You are severed from Christ , you who would be justified by the law ; you have fallen away from grace .
48005005	For through the Spirit , by faith , we ourselves eagerly wait for the hope of righteousness .
48005006	For in Christ Jesus neither circumcision nor uncircumcision counts for anything , but only faith working through love .
48005007	You were running well . Who hindered you from obeying the truth ?
48005008	This persuasion is not from him who calls you .
48005009	A little leaven leavens the whole lump .
48005010	I have confidence in the Lord that you will take no other view than mine , and the one who is troubling you will bear the penalty , whoever he is .
48005011	But if I , brothers , still preach circumcision , why am I still being persecuted ? In that case the offense of the cross has been removed .
48005012	I wish those who unsettle you would emasculate themselves !
48005013	For you were called to freedom , brothers . Only do not use your freedom as an opportunity for the flesh , but through love serve one another .
48005014	For the whole law is fulfilled in one word : “ You shall love your neighbor as yourself . ”
48005015	But if you bite and devour one another , watch out that you are not consumed by one another .
48005016	But I say , walk by the Spirit , and you will not gratify the desires of the flesh .
48005017	For the desires of the flesh are against the Spirit , and the desires of the Spirit are against the flesh , for these are opposed to each other , to keep you from doing the things you want to do .
48005018	But if you are led by the Spirit , you are not under the law .
48005019	Now the works of the flesh are evident : sexual immorality , impurity , sensuality ,
48005020	idolatry , sorcery , enmity , strife , jealousy , fits of anger , rivalries , dissensions , divisions ,
48005021	envy , drunkenness , orgies , and things like these . I warn you , as I warned you before , that those who do such things will not inherit the kingdom of God .
48005022	But the fruit of the Spirit is love , joy , peace , patience , kindness , goodness , faithfulness ,
48005023	gentleness , self-control ; against such things there is no law .
48005024	And those who belong to Christ Jesus have crucified the flesh with its passions and desires .
48005025	If we live by the Spirit , let us also walk by the Spirit .
48005026	Let us not become conceited , provoking one another , envying one another .
48006001	Brothers , if anyone is caught in any transgression , you who are spiritual should restore him in a spirit of gentleness . Keep watch on yourself , lest you too be tempted .
48006002	Bear one another’s burdens , and so fulfill the law of Christ .
48006003	For if anyone thinks he is something , when he is nothing , he deceives himself .
