48006004	But let each one test his own work , and then his reason to boast will be in himself alone and not in his neighbor .
48006005	For each will have to bear his own load .
48006006	One who is taught the word must share all good things with the one who teaches .
48006007	Do not be deceived : God is not mocked , for whatever one sows , that will he also reap .
48006008	For the one who sows to his own flesh will from the flesh reap corruption , but the one who sows to the Spirit will from the Spirit reap eternal life .
48006009	And let us not grow weary of doing good , for in due season we will reap , if we do not give up .
48006010	So then , as we have opportunity , let us do good to everyone , and especially to those who are of the household of faith .
48006011	See with what large letters I am writing to you with my own hand .
48006012	It is those who want to make a good showing in the flesh who would force you to be circumcised , and only in order that they may not be persecuted for the cross of Christ .
48006013	For even those who are circumcised do not themselves keep the law , but they desire to have you circumcised that they may boast in your flesh .
48006014	But far be it from me to boast except in the cross of our Lord Jesus Christ , by which the world has been crucified to me , and I to the world .
48006015	For neither circumcision counts for anything , nor uncircumcision , but a new creation .
48006016	And as for all who walk by this rule , peace and mercy be upon them , and upon the Israel of God .
48006017	From now on let no one cause me trouble , for I bear on my body the marks of Jesus .
48006018	The grace of our Lord Jesus Christ be with your spirit , brothers . Amen .
49001001	Paul , an apostle of Christ Jesus by the will of God , To the saints who are in Ephesus , and are faithful in Christ Jesus :
49001002	Grace to you and peace from God our Father and the Lord Jesus Christ .
49001003	Blessed be the God and Father of our Lord Jesus Christ , who has blessed us in Christ with every spiritual blessing in the heavenly places ,
49001004	even as he chose us in him before the foundation of the world , that we should be holy and blameless before him . In love
49001005	he predestined us for adoption as sons through Jesus Christ , according to the purpose of his will ,
49001006	to the praise of his glorious grace , with which he has blessed us in the Beloved .
49001007	In him we have redemption through his blood , the forgiveness of our trespasses , according to the riches of his grace ,
49001008	which he lavished upon us , in all wisdom and insight
49001009	making known to us the mystery of his will , according to his purpose , which he set forth in Christ
49001010	as a plan for the fullness of time , to unite all things in him , things in heaven and things on earth .
49001011	In him we have obtained an inheritance , having been predestined according to the purpose of him who works all things according to the counsel of his will ,
49001012	so that we who were the first to hope in Christ might be to the praise of his glory .
49001013	In him you also , when you heard the word of truth , the gospel of your salvation , and believed in him , were sealed with the promised Holy Spirit ,
49001014	who is the guarantee of our inheritance until we acquire possession of it , to the praise of his glory .
49001015	For this reason , because I have heard of your faith in the Lord Jesus and your love toward all the saints ,
49001016	I do not cease to give thanks for you , remembering you in my prayers ,
49001017	that the God of our Lord Jesus Christ , the Father of glory , may give you a spirit of wisdom and of revelation in the knowledge of him ,
49001018	having the eyes of your hearts enlightened , that you may know what is the hope to which he has called you , what are the riches of his glorious inheritance in the saints ,
49001019	and what is the immeasurable greatness of his power toward us who believe , according to the working of his great might
49001020	that he worked in Christ when he raised him from the dead and seated him at his right hand in the heavenly places ,
49001021	far above all rule and authority and power and dominion , and above every name that is named , not only in this age but also in the one to come .
49001022	And he put all things under his feet and gave him as head over all things to the church ,
49001023	which is his body , the fullness of him who fills all in all .
49002001	And you were dead in the trespasses and sins
49002002	in which you once walked , following the course of this world , following the prince of the power of the air , the spirit that is now at work in the sons of disobedience —
49002003	among whom we all once lived in the passions of our flesh , carrying out the desires of the body and the mind , and were by nature children of wrath , like the rest of mankind .
49002004	But God , being rich in mercy , because of the great love with which he loved us ,
49002005	even when we were dead in our trespasses , made us alive together with Christ — by grace you have been saved —
49002006	and raised us up with him and seated us with him in the heavenly places in Christ Jesus ,
49002007	so that in the coming ages he might show the immeasurable riches of his grace in kindness toward us in Christ Jesus .
49002008	For by grace you have been saved through faith . And this is not your own doing ; it is the gift of God ,
49002009	not a result of works , so that no one may boast .
49002010	For we are his workmanship , created in Christ Jesus for good works , which God prepared beforehand , that we should walk in them .
49002011	Therefore remember that at one time you Gentiles in the flesh , called “ the uncircumcision ” by what is called the circumcision , which is made in the flesh by hands —
49002012	remember that you were at that time separated from Christ , alienated from the commonwealth of Israel and strangers to the covenants of promise , having no hope and without God in the world .
49002013	But now in Christ Jesus you who once were far off have been brought near by the blood of Christ .
49002014	For he himself is our peace , who has made us both one and has broken down in his flesh the dividing wall of hostility
49002015	by abolishing the law of commandments expressed in ordinances , that he might create in himself one new man in place of the two , so making peace ,
49002016	and might reconcile us both to God in one body through the cross , thereby killing the hostility .
49002017	And he came and preached peace to you who were far off and peace to those who were near .
49002018	For through him we both have access in one Spirit to the Father .
49002019	So then you are no longer strangers and aliens , but you are fellow citizens with the saints and members of the household of God ,
49002020	built on the foundation of the apostles and prophets , Christ Jesus himself being the cornerstone ,
49002021	in whom the whole structure , being joined together , grows into a holy temple in the Lord .
49002022	In him you also are being built together into a dwelling place for God by the Spirit .
49003001	For this reason I , Paul , a prisoner for Christ Jesus on behalf of you Gentiles —
49003002	assuming that you have heard of the stewardship of God’s grace that was given to me for you ,
49003003	how the mystery was made known to me by revelation , as I have written briefly .
49003004	When you read this , you can perceive my insight into the mystery of Christ ,
49003005	which was not made known to the sons of men in other generations as it has now been revealed to his holy apostles and prophets by the Spirit .
49003006	This mystery is that the Gentiles are fellow heirs , members of the same body , and partakers of the promise in Christ Jesus through the gospel .
49003007	Of this gospel I was made a minister according to the gift of God’s grace , which was given me by the working of his power .
49003008	To me , though I am the very least of all the saints , this grace was given , to preach to the Gentiles the unsearchable riches of Christ ,
49003009	and to bring to light for everyone what is the plan of the mystery hidden for ages in God who created all things ,
49003010	so that through the church the manifold wisdom of God might now be made known to the rulers and authorities in the heavenly places .
49003011	This was according to the eternal purpose that he has realized in Christ Jesus our Lord ,
49003012	in whom we have boldness and access with confidence through our faith in him .
49003013	So I ask you not to lose heart over what I am suffering for you , which is your glory .
49003014	For this reason I bow my knees before the Father ,
49003015	from whom every family in heaven and on earth is named ,
49003016	that according to the riches of his glory he may grant you to be strengthened with power through his Spirit in your inner being ,
49003017	so that Christ may dwell in your hearts through faith — that you , being rooted and grounded in love ,
49003018	may have strength to comprehend with all the saints what is the breadth and length and height and depth ,
49003019	and to know the love of Christ that surpasses knowledge , that you may be filled with all the fullness of God .
49003020	Now to him who is able to do far more abundantly than all that we ask or think , according to the power at work within us ,
49003021	to him be glory in the church and in Christ Jesus throughout all generations , forever and ever . Amen .
49004001	I therefore , a prisoner for the Lord , urge you to walk in a manner worthy of the calling to which you have been called ,
49004002	with all humility and gentleness , with patience , bearing with one another in love ,
49004003	eager to maintain the unity of the Spirit in the bond of peace .
49004004	There is one body and one Spirit — just as you were called to the one hope that belongs to your call —
49004005	one Lord , one faith , one baptism ,
49004006	one God and Father of all , who is over all and through all and in all .
49004007	But grace was given to each one of us according to the measure of Christ’s gift .
49004008	Therefore it says , “ When he ascended on high he led a host of captives , and he gave gifts to men . ”
49004009	( In saying , “ He ascended , ” what does it mean but that he had also descended into the lower regions , the earth ?
49004010	He who descended is the one who also ascended far above all the heavens , that he might fill all things .
49004011	And he gave the apostles , the prophets , the evangelists , the shepherds and teachers ,
49004012	to equip the saints for the work of ministry , for building up the body of Christ ,
49004013	until we all attain to the unity of the faith and of the knowledge of the Son of God , to mature manhood , to the measure of the stature of the fullness of Christ ,
49004014	so that we may no longer be children , tossed to and fro by the waves and carried about by every wind of doctrine , by human cunning , by craftiness in deceitful schemes .
49004015	Rather , speaking the truth in love , we are to grow up in every way into him who is the head , into Christ ,
49004016	from whom the whole body , joined and held together by every joint with which it is equipped , when each part is working properly , makes the body grow so that it builds itself up in love .
49004017	Now this I say and testify in the Lord , that you must no longer walk as the Gentiles do , in the futility of their minds .
49004018	They are darkened in their understanding , alienated from the life of God because of the ignorance that is in them , due to their hardness of heart .
49004019	They have become callous and have given themselves up to sensuality , greedy to practice every kind of impurity .
49004020	But that is not the way you learned Christ ! —
49004021	assuming that you have heard about him and were taught in him , as the truth is in Jesus ,
49004022	to put off your old self , which belongs to your former manner of life and is corrupt through deceitful desires ,
49004023	and to be renewed in the spirit of your minds ,
49004024	and to put on the new self , created after the likeness of God in true righteousness and holiness .
49004025	Therefore , having put away falsehood , let each one of you speak the truth with his neighbor , for we are members one of another .
49004026	Be angry and do not sin ; do not let the sun go down on your anger ,
49004027	and give no opportunity to the devil .
49004028	Let the thief no longer steal , but rather let him labor , doing honest work with his own hands , so that he may have something to share with anyone in need .
49004029	Let no corrupting talk come out of your mouths , but only such as is good for building up , as fits the occasion , that it may give grace to those who hear .
49004030	And do not grieve the Holy Spirit of God , by whom you were sealed for the day of redemption .
49004031	Let all bitterness and wrath and anger and clamor and slander be put away from you , along with all malice .
49004032	Be kind to one another , tenderhearted , forgiving one another , as God in Christ forgave you .
49005001	Therefore be imitators of God , as beloved children .
49005002	And walk in love , as Christ loved us and gave himself up for us , a fragrant offering and sacrifice to God .
49005003	But sexual immorality and all impurity or covetousness must not even be named among you , as is proper among saints .
49005004	Let there be no filthiness nor foolish talk nor crude joking , which are out of place , but instead let there be thanksgiving .
49005005	For you may be sure of this , that everyone who is sexually immoral or impure , or who is covetous ( that is , an idolater ) , has no inheritance in the kingdom of Christ and God .
49005006	Let no one deceive you with empty words , for because of these things the wrath of God comes upon the sons of disobedience .
49005007	Therefore do not become partners with them ;
49005008	for at one time you were darkness , but now you are light in the Lord . Walk as children of light
49005009	( for the fruit of light is found in all that is good and right and true ) ,
49005010	and try to discern what is pleasing to the Lord .
49005011	Take no part in the unfruitful works of darkness , but instead expose them .
49005012	For it is shameful even to speak of the things that they do in secret .
49005013	But when anything is exposed by the light , it becomes visible ,
49005014	for anything that becomes visible is light . Therefore it says , “ Awake , O sleeper , and arise from the dead , and Christ will shine on you . ”
49005015	Look carefully then how you walk , not as unwise but as wise ,
49005016	making the best use of the time , because the days are evil .
49005017	Therefore do not be foolish , but understand what the will of the Lord is .
49005018	And do not get drunk with wine , for that is debauchery , but be filled with the Spirit ,
49005019	addressing one another in psalms and hymns and spiritual songs , singing and making melody to the Lord with your heart ,
49005020	giving thanks always and for everything to God the Father in the name of our Lord Jesus Christ ,
49005021	submitting to one another out of reverence for Christ .
49005022	Wives , submit to your own husbands , as to the Lord .
49005023	For the husband is the head of the wife even as Christ is the head of the church , his body , and is himself its Savior .
49005024	Now as the church submits to Christ , so also wives should submit in everything to their husbands .
49005025	Husbands , love your wives , as Christ loved the church and gave himself up for her ,
49005026	that he might sanctify her , having cleansed her by the washing of water with the word ,
49005027	so that he might present the church to himself in splendor , without spot or wrinkle or any such thing , that she might be holy and without blemish .
49005028	In the same way husbands should love their wives as their own bodies . He who loves his wife loves himself .
49005029	For no one ever hated his own flesh , but nourishes and cherishes it , just as Christ does the church ,
49005030	because we are members of his body .
49005031	“ Therefore a man shall leave his father and mother and hold fast to his wife , and the two shall become one flesh . ”
49005032	This mystery is profound , and I am saying that it refers to Christ and the church .
49005033	However , let each one of you love his wife as himself , and let the wife see that she respects her husband .
49006001	Children , obey your parents in the Lord , for this is right .
49006002	“ Honor your father and mother ” ( this is the first commandment with a promise ) ,
49006003	“ that it may go well with you and that you may live long in the land . ”
49006004	Fathers , do not provoke your children to anger , but bring them up in the discipline and instruction of the Lord .
49006005	Slaves , obey your earthly masters with fear and trembling , with a sincere heart , as you would Christ ,
49006006	not by the way of eye-service , as people-pleasers , but as servants of Christ , doing the will of God from the heart ,
49006007	rendering service with a good will as to the Lord and not to man ,
49006008	knowing that whatever good anyone does , this he will receive back from the Lord , whether he is a slave or free .
49006009	Masters , do the same to them , and stop your threatening , knowing that he who is both their Master and yours is in heaven , and that there is no partiality with him .
49006010	Finally , be strong in the Lord and in the strength of his might .
49006011	Put on the whole armor of God , that you may be able to stand against the schemes of the devil .
49006012	For we do not wrestle against flesh and blood , but against the rulers , against the authorities , against the cosmic powers over this present darkness , against the spiritual forces of evil in the heavenly places .
49006013	Therefore take up the whole armor of God , that you may be able to withstand in the evil day , and having done all , to stand firm .
49006014	Stand therefore , having fastened on the belt of truth , and having put on the breastplate of righteousness ,
49006015	and , as shoes for your feet , having put on the readiness given by the gospel of peace .
49006016	In all circumstances take up the shield of faith , with which you can extinguish all the flaming darts of the evil one ;
49006017	and take the helmet of salvation , and the sword of the Spirit , which is the word of God ,
49006018	praying at all times in the Spirit , with all prayer and supplication . To that end keep alert with all perseverance , making supplication for all the saints ,
49006019	and also for me , that words may be given to me in opening my mouth boldly to proclaim the mystery of the gospel ,
49006020	for which I am an ambassador in chains , that I may declare it boldly , as I ought to speak .
49006021	So that you also may know how I am and what I am doing , Tychicus the beloved brother and faithful minister in the Lord will tell you everything .
49006022	I have sent him to you for this very purpose , that you may know how we are , and that he may encourage your hearts .
49006023	Peace be to the brothers , and love with faith , from God the Father and the Lord Jesus Christ .
49006024	Grace be with all who love our Lord Jesus Christ with love incorruptible .
50001001	Paul and Timothy , servants of Christ Jesus , To all the saints in Christ Jesus who are at Philippi , with the overseersand deacons :
50001002	Grace to you and peace from God our Father and the Lord Jesus Christ .
50001003	I thank my God in all my remembrance of you ,
50001004	always in every prayer of mine for you all making my prayer with joy ,
50001005	because of your partnership in the gospel from the first day until now .
50001006	And I am sure of this , that he who began a good work in you will bring it to completion at the day of Jesus Christ .
50001007	It is right for me to feel this way about you all , because I hold you in my heart , for you are all partakers with me of grace , both in my imprisonment and in the defense and confirmation of the gospel .
50001008	For God is my witness , how I yearn for you all with the affection of Christ Jesus .
50001009	And it is my prayer that your love may abound more and more , with knowledge and all discernment ,
50001010	so that you may approve what is excellent , and so be pure and blameless for the day of Christ ,
50001011	filled with the fruit of righteousness that comes through Jesus Christ , to the glory and praise of God .
50001012	I want you to know , brothers , that what has happened to me has really served to advance the gospel ,
50001013	so that it has become known throughout the whole imperial guard and to all the rest that my imprisonment is for Christ .
50001014	And most of the brothers , having become confident in the Lord by my imprisonment , are much more bold to speak the word without fear .
50001015	Some indeed preach Christ from envy and rivalry , but others from good will .
50001016	The latter do it out of love , knowing that I am put here for the defense of the gospel .
50001017	The former proclaim Christ out of rivalry , not sincerely but thinking to afflict me in my imprisonment .
50001018	What then ? Only that in every way , whether in pretense or in truth , Christ is proclaimed , and in that I rejoice . Yes , and I will rejoice ,
50001019	for I know that through your prayers and the help of the Spirit of Jesus Christ this will turn out for my deliverance ,
50001020	as it is my eager expectation and hope that I will not be at all ashamed , but that with full courage now as always Christ will be honored in my body , whether by life or by death .
50001021	For to me to live is Christ , and to die is gain .
50001022	If I am to live in the flesh , that means fruitful labor for me . Yet which I shall choose I cannot tell .
50001023	I am hard pressed between the two . My desire is to depart and be with Christ , for that is far better .
50001024	But to remain in the flesh is more necessary on your account .
50001025	Convinced of this , I know that I will remain and continue with you all , for your progress and joy in the faith ,
50001026	so that in me you may have ample cause to glory in Christ Jesus , because of my coming to you again .
50001027	Only let your manner of life be worthy of the gospel of Christ , so that whether I come and see you or am absent , I may hear of you that you are standing firm in one spirit , with one mind striving side by side for the faith of the gospel ,
50001028	and not frightened in anything by your opponents . This is a clear sign to them of their destruction , but of your salvation , and that from God .
50001029	For it has been granted to you that for the sake of Christ you should not only believe in him but also suffer for his sake ,
50001030	engaged in the same conflict that you saw I had and now hear that I still have .
50002001	So if there is any encouragement in Christ , any comfort from love , any participation in the Spirit , any affection and sympathy ,
50002002	complete my joy by being of the same mind , having the same love , being in full accord and of one mind .
50002003	Do nothing from rivalry or conceit , but in humility count others more significant than yourselves .
50002004	Let each of you look not only to his own interests , but also to the interests of others .
50002005	Have this mind among yourselves , which is yours in Christ Jesus ,
50002006	who , though he was in the form of God , did not count equality with God a thing to be grasped ,
50002007	but made himself nothing , taking the form of a servant , being born in the likeness of men .
50002008	And being found in human form , he humbled himself by becoming obedient to the point of death , even death on a cross .
50002009	Therefore God has highly exalted him and bestowed on him the name that is above every name ,
50002010	so that at the name of Jesus every knee should bow , in heaven and on earth and under the earth ,
50002011	and every tongue confess that Jesus Christ is Lord , to the glory of God the Father .
50002012	Therefore , my beloved , as you have always obeyed , so now , not only as in my presence but much more in my absence , work out your own salvation with fear and trembling ,
50002013	for it is God who works in you , both to will and to work for his good pleasure .
50002014	Do all things without grumbling or questioning ,
50002015	that you may be blameless and innocent , children of God without blemish in the midst of a crooked and twisted generation , among whom you shine as lights in the world ,
50002016	holding fast to the word of life , so that in the day of Christ I may be proud that I did not run in vain or labor in vain .
50002017	Even if I am to be poured out as a drink offering upon the sacrificial offering of your faith , I am glad and rejoice with you all .
50002018	Likewise you also should be glad and rejoice with me .
50002019	I hope in the Lord Jesus to send Timothy to you soon , so that I too may be cheered by news of you .
50002020	For I have no one like him , who will be genuinely concerned for your welfare .
50002021	For they all seek their own interests , not those of Jesus Christ .
50002022	But you know Timothy’s proven worth , how as a son with a father he has served with me in the gospel .
50002023	I hope therefore to send him just as soon as I see how it will go with me ,
50002024	and I trust in the Lord that shortly I myself will come also .
50002025	I have thought it necessary to send to you Epaphroditus my brother and fellow worker and fellow soldier , and your messenger and minister to my need ,
50002026	for he has been longing for you all and has been distressed because you heard that he was ill .
50002027	Indeed he was ill , near to death . But God had mercy on him , and not only on him but on me also , lest I should have sorrow upon sorrow .
50002028	I am the more eager to send him , therefore , that you may rejoice at seeing him again , and that I may be less anxious .
50002029	So receive him in the Lord with all joy , and honor such men ,
50002030	for he nearly died for the work of Christ , risking his life to complete what was lacking in your service to me .
50003001	Finally , my brothers , rejoice in the Lord . To write the same things to you is no trouble to me and is safe for you .
50003002	Look out for the dogs , look out for the evildoers , look out for those who mutilate the flesh .
50003003	For we are the circumcision , who worship by the Spirit of God and glory in Christ Jesus and put no confidence in the flesh —
50003004	though I myself have reason for confidence in the flesh also . If anyone else thinks he has reason for confidence in the flesh , I have more :
50003005	circumcised on the eighth day , of the people of Israel , of the tribe of Benjamin , a Hebrew of Hebrews ; as to the law , a Pharisee ;
50003006	as to zeal , a persecutor of the church ; as to righteousness under the law , blameless .
50003007	But whatever gain I had , I counted as loss for the sake of Christ .
50003008	Indeed , I count everything as loss because of the surpassing worth of knowing Christ Jesus my Lord . For his sake I have suffered the loss of all things and count them as rubbish , in order that I may gain Christ
50003009	and be found in him , not having a righteousness of my own that comes from the law , but that which comes through faith in Christ , the righteousness from God that depends on faith —
50003010	that I may know him and the power of his resurrection , and may share his sufferings , becoming like him in his death ,
50003011	that by any means possible I may attain the resurrection from the dead .
50003012	Not that I have already obtained this or am already perfect , but I press on to make it my own , because Christ Jesus has made me his own .
50003013	Brothers , I do not consider that I have made it my own . But one thing I do : forgetting what lies behind and straining forward to what lies ahead ,
50003014	I press on toward the goal for the prize of the upward call of God in Christ Jesus .
50003015	Let those of us who are mature think this way , and if in anything you think otherwise , God will reveal that also to you .
50003016	Only let us hold true to what we have attained .
50003017	Brothers , join in imitating me , and keep your eyes on those who walk according to the example you have in us .
50003018	For many , of whom I have often told you and now tell you even with tears , walk as enemies of the cross of Christ .
50003019	Their end is destruction , their god is their belly , and they glory in their shame , with minds set on earthly things .
50003020	But our citizenship is in heaven , and from it we await a Savior , the Lord Jesus Christ ,
50003021	who will transform our lowly body to be like his glorious body , by the power that enables him even to subject all things to himself .
50004001	Therefore , my brothers , whom I love and long for , my joy and crown , stand firm thus in the Lord , my beloved .
50004002	I entreat Euodia and I entreat Syntyche to agree in the Lord .
50004003	Yes , I ask you also , true companion , help these women , who have labored side by side with me in the gospel together with Clement and the rest of my fellow workers , whose names are in the book of life .
50004004	Rejoice in the Lord always ; again I will say , Rejoice .
50004005	Let your reasonableness be known to everyone . The Lord is at hand ;
50004006	do not be anxious about anything , but in everything by prayer and supplication with thanksgiving let your requests be made known to God .
50004007	And the peace of God , which surpasses all understanding , will guard your hearts and your minds in Christ Jesus .
50004008	Finally , brothers , whatever is true , whatever is honorable , whatever is just , whatever is pure , whatever is lovely , whatever is commendable , if there is any excellence , if there is anything worthy of praise , think about these things .
50004009	What you have learned and received and heard and seen in me — practice these things , and the God of peace will be with you .
50004010	I rejoiced in the Lord greatly that now at length you have revived your concern for me . You were indeed concerned for me , but you had no opportunity .
50004011	Not that I am speaking of being in need , for I have learned in whatever situation I am to be content .
50004012	I know how to be brought low , and I know how to abound . In any and every circumstance , I have learned the secret of facing plenty and hunger , abundance and need .
50004013	I can do all things through him who strengthens me .
50004014	Yet it was kind of you to share my trouble .
50004015	And you Philippians yourselves know that in the beginning of the gospel , when I left Macedonia , no church entered into partnership with me in giving and receiving , except you only .
50004016	Even in Thessalonica you sent me help for my needs once and again .
50004017	Not that I seek the gift , but I seek the fruit that increases to your credit .
50004018	I have received full payment , and more . I am well supplied , having received from Epaphroditus the gifts you sent , a fragrant offering , a sacrifice acceptable and pleasing to God .
50004019	And my God will supply every need of yours according to his riches in glory in Christ Jesus .
50004020	To our God and Father be glory forever and ever . Amen .
50004021	Greet every saint in Christ Jesus . The brothers who are with me greet you .
50004022	All the saints greet you , especially those of Caesar’s household .
50004023	The grace of the Lord Jesus Christ be with your spirit .
51001001	Paul , an apostle of Christ Jesus by the will of God , and Timothy our brother ,
51001002	To the saints and faithful brothers in Christ at Colossae : Grace to you and peace from God our Father .
51001003	We always thank God , the Father of our Lord Jesus Christ , when we pray for you ,
51001004	since we heard of your faith in Christ Jesus and of the love that you have for all the saints ,
51001005	because of the hope laid up for you in heaven . Of this you have heard before in the word of the truth , the gospel ,
51001006	which has come to you , as indeed in the whole world it is bearing fruit and growing — as it also does among you , since the day you heard it and understood the grace of God in truth ,
51001007	just as you learned it from Epaphras our beloved fellow servant . He is a faithful minister of Christ on your behalf
51001008	and has made known to us your love in the Spirit .
51001009	And so , from the day we heard , we have not ceased to pray for you , asking that you may be filled with the knowledge of his will in all spiritual wisdom and understanding ,
51001010	so as to walk in a manner worthy of the Lord , fully pleasing to him , bearing fruit in every good work and increasing in the knowledge of God .
51001011	May you be strengthened with all power , according to his glorious might , for all endurance and patience with joy ,
51001012	giving thanks to the Father , who has qualified you to share in the inheritance of the saints in light .
51001013	He has delivered us from the domain of darkness and transferred us to the kingdom of his beloved Son ,
51001014	in whom we have redemption , the forgiveness of sins .
51001015	He is the image of the invisible God , the firstborn of all creation .
51001016	For by him all things were created , in heaven and on earth , visible and invisible , whether thrones or dominions or rulers or authorities — all things were created through him and for him .
51001017	And he is before all things , and in him all things hold together .
51001018	And he is the head of the body , the church . He is the beginning , the firstborn from the dead , that in everything he might be preeminent .
51001019	For in him all the fullness of God was pleased to dwell ,
51001020	and through him to reconcile to himself all things , whether on earth or in heaven , making peace by the blood of his cross .
51001021	And you , who once were alienated and hostile in mind , doing evil deeds ,
51001022	he has now reconciled in his body of flesh by his death , in order to present you holy and blameless and above reproach before him ,
51001023	if indeed you continue in the faith , stable and steadfast , not shifting from the hope of the gospel that you heard , which has been proclaimed in all creation under heaven , and of which I , Paul , became a minister .
51001024	Now I rejoice in my sufferings for your sake , and in my flesh I am filling up what is lacking in Christ’s afflictions for the sake of his body , that is , the church ,
51001025	of which I became a minister according to the stewardship from God that was given to me for you , to make the word of God fully known ,
51001026	the mystery hidden for ages and generations but now revealed to his saints .
51001027	To them God chose to make known how great among the Gentiles are the riches of the glory of this mystery , which is Christ in you , the hope of glory .
51001028	Him we proclaim , warning everyone and teaching everyone with all wisdom , that we may present everyone mature in Christ .
51001029	For this I toil , struggling with all his energy that he powerfully works within me .
51002001	For I want you to know how great a struggle I have for you and for those at Laodicea and for all who have not seen me face to face ,
51002002	that their hearts may be encouraged , being knit together in love , to reach all the riches of full assurance of understanding and the knowledge of God’s mystery , which is Christ ,
51002003	in whom are hidden all the treasures of wisdom and knowledge .
51002004	I say this in order that no one may delude you with plausible arguments .
51002005	For though I am absent in body , yet I am with you in spirit , rejoicing to see your good order and the firmness of your faith in Christ .
51002006	Therefore , as you received Christ Jesus the Lord , so walk in him ,
51002007	rooted and built up in him and established in the faith , just as you were taught , abounding in thanksgiving .
51002008	See to it that no one takes you captive by philosophy and empty deceit , according to human tradition , according to the elemental spirits of the world , and not according to Christ .
51002009	For in him the whole fullness of deity dwells bodily ,
51002010	and you have been filled in him , who is the head of all rule and authority .
51002011	In him also you were circumcised with a circumcision made without hands , by putting off the body of the flesh , by the circumcision of Christ ,
51002012	having been buried with him in baptism , in which you were also raised with him through faith in the powerful working of God , who raised him from the dead .
51002013	And you , who were dead in your trespasses and the uncircumcision of your flesh , God made alive together with him , having forgiven us all our trespasses ,
51002014	by canceling the record of debt that stood against us with its legal demands . This he set aside , nailing it to the cross .
51002015	He disarmed the rulers and authorities and put them to open shame , by triumphing over them in him .
51002016	Therefore let no one pass judgment on you in questions of food and drink , or with regard to a festival or a new moon or a Sabbath .
51002017	These are a shadow of the things to come , but the substance belongs to Christ .
51002018	Let no one disqualify you , insisting on asceticism and worship of angels , going on in detail about visions , puffed up without reason by his sensuous mind ,
51002019	and not holding fast to the Head , from whom the whole body , nourished and knit together through its joints and ligaments , grows with a growth that is from God .
51002020	If with Christ you died to the elemental spirits of the world , why , as if you were still alive in the world , do you submit to regulations —
51002021	“ Do not handle , Do not taste , Do not touch ”
51002022	( referring to things that all perish as they are used ) — according to human precepts and teachings ?
51002023	These have indeed an appearance of wisdom in promoting self-made religion and asceticism and severity to the body , but they are of no value in stopping the indulgence of the flesh .
51003001	If then you have been raised with Christ , seek the things that are above , where Christ is , seated at the right hand of God .
51003002	Set your minds on things that are above , not on things that are on earth .
51003003	For you have died , and your life is hidden with Christ in God .
51003004	When Christ who is your life appears , then you also will appear with him in glory .
51003005	Put to death therefore what is earthly in you : sexual immorality , impurity , passion , evil desire , and covetousness , which is idolatry .
51003006	On account of these the wrath of God is coming .
51003007	In these you too once walked , when you were living in them .
51003008	But now you must put them all away : anger , wrath , malice , slander , and obscene talk from your mouth .
51003009	Do not lie to one another , seeing that you have put off the old self with its practices
51003010	and have put on the new self , which is being renewed in knowledge after the image of its creator .
51003011	Here there is not Greek and Jew , circumcised and uncircumcised , barbarian , Scythian , slave , free ; but Christ is all , and in all .
51003012	Put on then , as God’s chosen ones , holy and beloved , compassionate hearts , kindness , humility , meekness , and patience ,
51003013	bearing with one another and , if one has a complaint against another , forgiving each other ; as the Lord has forgiven you , so you also must forgive .
51003014	And above all these put on love , which binds everything together in perfect harmony .
51003015	And let the peace of Christ rule in your hearts , to which indeed you were called in one body . And be thankful .
51003016	Let the word of Christ dwell in you richly , teaching and admonishing one another in all wisdom , singing psalms and hymns and spiritual songs , with thankfulness in your hearts to God .
51003017	And whatever you do , in word or deed , do everything in the name of the Lord Jesus , giving thanks to God the Father through him .
51003018	Wives , submit to your husbands , as is fitting in the Lord .
51003019	Husbands , love your wives , and do not be harsh with them .
51003020	Children , obey your parents in everything , for this pleases the Lord .
51003021	Fathers , do not provoke your children , lest they become discouraged .
51003022	Slaves , obey in everything those who are your earthly masters , not by way of eye-service , as people-pleasers , but with sincerity of heart , fearing the Lord .
51003023	Whatever you do , work heartily , as for the Lord and not for men ,
51003024	knowing that from the Lord you will receive the inheritance as your reward . You are serving the Lord Christ .
51003025	For the wrongdoer will be paid back for the wrong he has done , and there is no partiality .
51004001	Masters , treat your slaves justly and fairly , knowing that you also have a Master in heaven .
51004002	Continue steadfastly in prayer , being watchful in it with thanksgiving .
51004003	At the same time , pray also for us , that God may open to us a door for the word , to declare the mystery of Christ , on account of which I am in prison —
51004004	that I may make it clear , which is how I ought to speak .
51004005	Walk in wisdom toward outsiders , making the best use of the time .
51004006	Let your speech always be gracious , seasoned with salt , so that you may know how you ought to answer each person .
51004007	Tychicus will tell you all about my activities . He is a beloved brother and faithful minister and fellow servant in the Lord .
51004008	I have sent him to you for this very purpose , that you may know how we are and that he may encourage your hearts ,
51004009	and with him Onesimus , our faithful and beloved brother , who is one of you . They will tell you of everything that has taken place here .
51004010	Aristarchus my fellow prisoner greets you , and Mark the cousin of Barnabas ( concerning whom you have received instructions — if he comes to you , welcome him ) ,
51004011	and Jesus who is called Justus . These are the only men of the circumcision among my fellow workers for the kingdom of God , and they have been a comfort to me .
51004012	Epaphras , who is one of you , a servant of Christ Jesus , greets you , always struggling on your behalf in his prayers , that you may stand mature and fully assured in all the will of God .
51004013	For I bear him witness that he has worked hard for you and for those in Laodicea and in Hierapolis .
51004014	Luke the beloved physician greets you , as does Demas .
51004015	Give my greetings to the brothers at Laodicea , and to Nympha and the church in her house .
51004016	And when this letter has been read among you , have it also read in the church of the Laodiceans ; and see that you also read the letter from Laodicea .
51004017	And say to Archippus , “ See that you fulfill the ministry that you have received in the Lord . ”
51004018	I , Paul , write this greeting with my own hand . Remember my chains . Grace be with you .
52001001	Paul , Silvanus , and Timothy , To the church of the Thessalonians in God the Father and the Lord Jesus Christ : Grace to you and peace .
52001002	We give thanks to God always for all of you , constantly mentioning you in our prayers ,
52001003	remembering before our God and Father your work of faith and labor of love and steadfastness of hope in our Lord Jesus Christ .
52001004	For we know , brothers loved by God , that he has chosen you ,
52001005	because our gospel came to you not only in word , but also in power and in the Holy Spirit and with full conviction . You know what kind of men we proved to be among you for your sake .
52001006	And you became imitators of us and of the Lord , for you received the word in much affliction , with the joy of the Holy Spirit ,
52001007	so that you became an example to all the believers in Macedonia and in Achaia .
52001008	For not only has the word of the Lord sounded forth from you in Macedonia and Achaia , but your faith in God has gone forth everywhere , so that we need not say anything .
52001009	For they themselves report concerning us the kind of reception we had among you , and how you turned to God from idols to serve the living and true God ,
52001010	and to wait for his Son from heaven , whom he raised from the dead , Jesus who delivers us from the wrath to come .
52002001	For you yourselves know , brothers , that our coming to you was not in vain .
52002002	But though we had already suffered and been shamefully treated at Philippi , as you know , we had boldness in our God to declare to you the gospel of God in the midst of much conflict .
52002003	For our appeal does not spring from error or impurity or any attempt to deceive ,
52002004	but just as we have been approved by God to be entrusted with the gospel , so we speak , not to please man , but to please God who tests our hearts .
52002005	For we never came with words of flattery , as you know , nor with a pretext for greed — God is witness .
52002006	Nor did we seek glory from people , whether from you or from others , though we could have made demands as apostles of Christ .
52002007	But we were gentle among you , like a nursing mother taking care of her own children .
52002008	So , being affectionately desirous of you , we were ready to share with you not only the gospel of God but also our own selves , because you had become very dear to us .
52002009	For you remember , brothers , our labor and toil : we worked night and day , that we might not be a burden to any of you , while we proclaimed to you the gospel of God .
52002010	You are witnesses , and God also , how holy and righteous and blameless was our conduct toward you believers .
52002011	For you know how , like a father with his children ,
52002012	we exhorted each one of you and encouraged you and charged you to walk in a manner worthy of God , who calls you into his own kingdom and glory .
52002013	And we also thank God constantly for this , that when you received the word of God , which you heard from us , you accepted it not as the word of men but as what it really is , the word of God , which is at work in you believers .
52002014	For you , brothers , became imitators of the churches of God in Christ Jesus that are in Judea . For you suffered the same things from your own countrymen as they did from the Jews ,
52002015	who killed both the Lord Jesus and the prophets , and drove us out , and displease God and oppose all mankind
52002016	by hindering us from speaking to the Gentiles that they might be saved — so as always to fill up the measure of their sins . But God’s wrath has come upon them at last !
52002017	But since we were torn away from you , brothers , for a short time , in person not in heart , we endeavored the more eagerly and with great desire to see you face to face ,
52002018	because we wanted to come to you — I , Paul , again and again — but Satan hindered us .
52002019	For what is our hope or joy or crown of boasting before our Lord Jesus at his coming ? Is it not you ?
52002020	For you are our glory and joy .
52003001	Therefore when we could bear it no longer , we were willing to be left behind at Athens alone ,
52003002	and we sent Timothy , our brother and God’s coworker in the gospel of Christ , to establish and exhort you in your faith ,
52003003	that no one be moved by these afflictions . For you yourselves know that we are destined for this .
52003004	For when we were with you , we kept telling you beforehand that we were to suffer affliction , just as it has come to pass , and just as you know .
52003005	For this reason , when I could bear it no longer , I sent to learn about your faith , for fear that somehow the tempter had tempted you and our labor would be in vain .
52003006	But now that Timothy has come to us from you , and has brought us the good news of your faith and love and reported that you always remember us kindly and long to see us , as we long to see you —
52003007	for this reason , brothers , in all our distress and affliction we have been comforted about you through your faith .
52003008	For now we live , if you are standing fast in the Lord .
52003009	For what thanksgiving can we return to God for you , for all the joy that we feel for your sake before our God ,
52003010	as we pray most earnestly night and day that we may see you face to face and supply what is lacking in your faith ?
52003011	Now may our God and Father himself , and our Lord Jesus , direct our way to you ,
52003012	and may the Lord make you increase and abound in love for one another and for all , as we do for you ,
52003013	so that he may establish your hearts blameless in holiness before our God and Father , at the coming of our Lord Jesus with all his saints .
52004001	Finally , then , brothers , we ask and urge you in the Lord Jesus , that as you received from us how you ought to walk and to please God , just as you are doing , that you do so more and more .
52004002	For you know what instructions we gave you through the Lord Jesus .
52004003	For this is the will of God , your sanctification : that you abstain from sexual immorality ;
52004004	that each one of you know how to control his own body in holiness and honor ,
52004005	not in the passion of lust like the Gentiles who do not know God ;
52004006	that no one transgress and wrong his brother in this matter , because the Lord is an avenger in all these things , as we told you beforehand and solemnly warned you .
52004007	For God has not called us for impurity , but in holiness .
52004008	Therefore whoever disregards this , disregards not man but God , who gives his Holy Spirit to you .
52004009	Now concerning brotherly love you have no need for anyone to write to you , for you yourselves have been taught by God to love one another ,
52004010	for that indeed is what you are doing to all the brothers throughout Macedonia . But we urge you , brothers , to do this more and more ,
52004011	and to aspire to live quietly , and to mind your own affairs , and to work with your hands , as we instructed you ,
52004012	so that you may walk properly before outsiders and be dependent on no one .
52004013	But we do not want you to be uninformed , brothers , about those who are asleep , that you may not grieve as others do who have no hope .
52004014	For since we believe that Jesus died and rose again , even so , through Jesus , God will bring with him those who have fallen asleep .
52004015	For this we declare to you by a word from the Lord , that we who are alive , who are left until the coming of the Lord , will not precede those who have fallen asleep .
52004016	For the Lord himself will descend from heaven with a cry of command , with the voice of an archangel , and with the sound of the trumpet of God . And the dead in Christ will rise first .
52004017	Then we who are alive , who are left , will be caught up together with them in the clouds to meet the Lord in the air , and so we will always be with the Lord .
52004018	Therefore encourage one another with these words .
52005001	Now concerning the times and the seasons , brothers , you have no need to have anything written to you .
52005002	For you yourselves are fully aware that the day of the Lord will come like a thief in the night .
52005003	While people are saying , “ There is peace and security , ” then sudden destruction will come upon them as labor pains come upon a pregnant woman , and they will not escape .
52005004	But you are not in darkness , brothers , for that day to surprise you like a thief .
52005005	For you are all children of light , children of the day . We are not of the night or of the darkness .
52005006	So then let us not sleep , as others do , but let us keep awake and be sober .
52005007	For those who sleep , sleep at night , and those who get drunk , are drunk at night .
52005008	But since we belong to the day , let us be sober , having put on the breastplate of faith and love , and for a helmet the hope of salvation .
52005009	For God has not destined us for wrath , but to obtain salvation through our Lord Jesus Christ ,
52005010	who died for us so that whether we are awake or asleep we might live with him .
52005011	Therefore encourage one another and build one another up , just as you are doing .
52005012	We ask you , brothers , to respect those who labor among you and are over you in the Lord and admonish you ,
52005013	and to esteem them very highly in love because of their work . Be at peace among yourselves .
52005014	And we urge you , brothers , admonish the idle , encourage the fainthearted , help the weak , be patient with them all .
52005015	See that no one repays anyone evil for evil , but always seek to do good to one another and to everyone .
52005016	Rejoice always ,
52005017	pray without ceasing ,
52005018	give thanks in all circumstances ; for this is the will of God in Christ Jesus for you .
52005019	Do not quench the Spirit .
52005020	Do not despise prophecies ,
52005021	but test everything ; hold fast what is good .
52005022	Abstain from every form of evil .
52005023	Now may the God of peace himself sanctify you completely , and may your whole spirit and soul and body be kept blameless at the coming of our Lord Jesus Christ .
52005024	He who calls you is faithful ; he will surely do it .
52005025	Brothers , pray for us .
52005026	Greet all the brothers with a holy kiss .
52005027	I put you under oath before the Lord to have this letter read to all the brothers .
52005028	The grace of our Lord Jesus Christ be with you .
53001001	Paul , Silvanus , and Timothy , To the church of the Thessalonians in God our Father and the Lord Jesus Christ :
53001002	Grace to you and peace from God our Father and the Lord Jesus Christ .
53001003	We ought always to give thanks to God for you , brothers , as is right , because your faith is growing abundantly , and the love of every one of you for one another is increasing .
53001004	Therefore we ourselves boast about you in the churches of God for your steadfastness and faith in all your persecutions and in the afflictions that you are enduring .
53001005	This is evidence of the righteous judgment of God , that you may be considered worthy of the kingdom of God , for which you are also suffering —
53001006	since indeed God considers it just to repay with affliction those who afflict you ,
53001007	and to grant relief to you who are afflicted as well as to us , when the Lord Jesus is revealed from heaven with his mighty angels
53001008	in flaming fire , inflicting vengeance on those who do not know God and on those who do not obey the gospel of our Lord Jesus .
53001009	They will suffer the punishment of eternal destruction , away from the presence of the Lord and from the glory of his might ,
53001010	when he comes on that day to be glorified in his saints , and to be marveled at among all who have believed , because our testimony to you was believed .
53001011	To this end we always pray for you , that our God may make you worthy of his calling and may fulfill every resolve for good and every work of faith by his power ,
53001012	so that the name of our Lord Jesus may be glorified in you , and you in him , according to the grace of our God and the Lord Jesus Christ .
53002001	Now concerning the coming of our Lord Jesus Christ and our being gathered together to him , we ask you , brothers ,
53002002	not to be quickly shaken in mind or alarmed , either by a spirit or a spoken word , or a letter seeming to be from us , to the effect that the day of the Lord has come .
53002003	Let no one deceive you in any way . For that day will not come , unless the rebellion comes first , and the man of lawlessness is revealed , the son of destruction ,
53002004	who opposes and exalts himself against every so-called god or object of worship , so that he takes his seat in the temple of God , proclaiming himself to be God .
53002005	Do you not remember that when I was still with you I told you these things ?
53002006	And you know what is restraining him now so that he may be revealed in his time .
53002007	For the mystery of lawlessness is already at work . Only he who now restrains it will do so until he is out of the way .
53002008	And then the lawless one will be revealed , whom the Lord Jesus will kill with the breath of his mouth and bring to nothing by the appearance of his coming .
53002009	The coming of the lawless one is by the activity of Satan with all power and false signs and wonders ,
53002010	and with all wicked deception for those who are perishing , because they refused to love the truth and so be saved .
53002011	Therefore God sends them a strong delusion , so that they may believe what is false ,
53002012	in order that all may be condemned who did not believe the truth but had pleasure in unrighteousness .
53002013	But we ought always to give thanks to God for you , brothers beloved by the Lord , because God chose you as the firstfruits to be saved , through sanctification by the Spirit and belief in the truth .
53002014	To this he called you through our gospel , so that you may obtain the glory of our Lord Jesus Christ .
53002015	So then , brothers , stand firm and hold to the traditions that you were taught by us , either by our spoken word or by our letter .
53002016	Now may our Lord Jesus Christ himself , and God our Father , who loved us and gave us eternal comfort and good hope through grace ,
53002017	comfort your hearts and establish them in every good work and word .
53003001	Finally , brothers , pray for us , that the word of the Lord may speed ahead and be honored , as happened among you ,
53003002	and that we may be delivered from wicked and evil men . For not all have faith .
53003003	But the Lord is faithful . He will establish you and guard you against the evil one .
53003004	And we have confidence in the Lord about you , that you are doing and will do the things that we command .
53003005	May the Lord direct your hearts to the love of God and to the steadfastness of Christ .
53003006	Now we command you , brothers , in the name of our Lord Jesus Christ , that you keep away from any brother who is walking in idleness and not in accord with the tradition that you received from us .
53003007	For you yourselves know how you ought to imitate us , because we were not idle when we were with you ,
53003008	nor did we eat anyone’s bread without paying for it , but with toil and labor we worked night and day , that we might not be a burden to any of you .
53003009	It was not because we do not have that right , but to give you in ourselves an example to imitate .
53003010	For even when we were with you , we would give you this command : If anyone is not willing to work , let him not eat .
53003011	For we hear that some among you walk in idleness , not busy at work , but busybodies .
53003012	Now such persons we command and encourage in the Lord Jesus Christ to do their work quietly and to earn their own living .
53003013	As for you , brothers , do not grow weary in doing good .
53003014	If anyone does not obey what we say in this letter , take note of that person , and have nothing to do with him , that he may be ashamed .
53003015	Do not regard him as an enemy , but warn him as a brother .
53003016	Now may the Lord of peace himself give you peace at all times in every way . The Lord be with you all .
53003017	I , Paul , write this greeting with my own hand . This is the sign of genuineness in every letter of mine ; it is the way I write .
53003018	The grace of our Lord Jesus Christ be with you all .
54001001	Paul , an apostle of Christ Jesus by command of God our Savior and of Christ Jesus our hope ,
54001002	To Timothy , my true child in the faith : Grace , mercy , and peace from God the Father and Christ Jesus our Lord .
54001003	As I urged you when I was going to Macedonia , remain at Ephesus so that you may charge certain persons not to teach any different doctrine ,
54001004	nor to devote themselves to myths and endless genealogies , which promote speculations rather than the stewardship from God that is by faith .
54001005	The aim of our charge is love that issues from a pure heart and a good conscience and a sincere faith .
54001006	Certain persons , by swerving from these , have wandered away into vain discussion ,
54001007	desiring to be teachers of the law , without understanding either what they are saying or the things about which they make confident assertions .
54001008	Now we know that the law is good , if one uses it lawfully ,
54001009	understanding this , that the law is not laid down for the just but for the lawless and disobedient , for the ungodly and sinners , for the unholy and profane , for those who strike their fathers and mothers , for murderers ,
54001010	the sexually immoral , men who practice homosexuality , enslavers , liars , perjurers , and whatever else is contrary to sound doctrine ,
54001011	in accordance with the gospel of the glory of the blessed God with which I have been entrusted .
54001012	I thank him who has given me strength , Christ Jesus our Lord , because he judged me faithful , appointing me to his service ,
54001013	though formerly I was a blasphemer , persecutor , and insolent opponent . But I received mercy because I had acted ignorantly in unbelief ,
54001014	and the grace of our Lord overflowed for me with the faith and love that are in Christ Jesus .
54001015	The saying is trustworthy and deserving of full acceptance , that Christ Jesus came into the world to save sinners , of whom I am the foremost .
54001016	But I received mercy for this reason , that in me , as the foremost , Jesus Christ might display his perfect patience as an example to those who were to believe in him for eternal life .
54001017	To the King of ages , immortal , invisible , the only God , be honor and glory forever and ever . Amen .
54001018	This charge I entrust to you , Timothy , my child , in accordance with the prophecies previously made about you , that by them you may wage the good warfare ,
54001019	holding faith and a good conscience . By rejecting this , some have made shipwreck of their faith ,
54001020	among whom are Hymenaeus and Alexander , whom I have handed over to Satan that they may learn not to blaspheme .
54002001	First of all , then , I urge that supplications , prayers , intercessions , and thanksgivings be made for all people ,
54002002	for kings and all who are in high positions , that we may lead a peaceful and quiet life , godly and dignified in every way .
54002003	This is good , and it is pleasing in the sight of God our Savior ,
54002004	who desires all people to be saved and to come to the knowledge of the truth .
54002005	For there is one God , and there is one mediator between God and men , the man Christ Jesus ,
54002006	who gave himself as a ransom for all , which is the testimony given at the proper time .
54002007	For this I was appointed a preacher and an apostle ( I am telling the truth , I am not lying ) , a teacher of the Gentiles in faith and truth .
54002008	I desire then that in every place the men should pray , lifting holy hands without anger or quarreling ;
54002009	likewise also that women should adorn themselves in respectable apparel , with modesty and self-control , not with braided hair and gold or pearls or costly attire ,
54002010	but with what is proper for women who profess godliness — with good works .
54002011	Let a woman learn quietly with all submissiveness .
54002012	I do not permit a woman to teach or to exercise authority over a man ; rather , she is to remain quiet .
54002013	For Adam was formed first , then Eve ;
54002014	and Adam was not deceived , but the woman was deceived and became a transgressor .
54002015	Yet she will be saved through childbearing — if they continue in faith and love and holiness , with self-control .
54003001	The saying is trustworthy : If anyone aspires to the office of overseer , he desires a noble task .
54003002	Therefore an overseer must be above reproach , the husband of one wife , sober-minded , self-controlled , respectable , hospitable , able to teach ,
54003003	not a drunkard , not violent but gentle , not quarrelsome , not a lover of money .
54003004	He must manage his own household well , with all dignity keeping his children submissive ,
54003005	for if someone does not know how to manage his own household , how will he care for God’s church ?
54003006	He must not be a recent convert , or he may become puffed up with conceit and fall into the condemnation of the devil .
54003007	Moreover , he must be well thought of by outsiders , so that he may not fall into disgrace , into a snare of the devil .
54003008	Deacons likewise must be dignified , not double-tongued , not addicted to much wine , not greedy for dishonest gain .
54003009	They must hold the mystery of the faith with a clear conscience .
54003010	And let them also be tested first ; then let them serve as deacons if they prove themselves blameless .
54003011	Their wives likewise must be dignified , not slanderers , but sober-minded , faithful in all things .
54003012	Let deacons each be the husband of one wife , managing their children and their own households well .
54003013	For those who serve well as deacons gain a good standing for themselves and also great confidence in the faith that is in Christ Jesus .
54003014	I hope to come to you soon , but I am writing these things to you so that ,
54003015	if I delay , you may know how one ought to behave in the household of God , which is the church of the living God , a pillar and buttress of the truth .
54003016	Great indeed , we confess , is the mystery of godliness : He was manifested in the flesh , vindicated by the Spirit , seen by angels , proclaimed among the nations , believed on in the world , taken up in glory .
54004001	Now the Spirit expressly says that in later times some will depart from the faith by devoting themselves to deceitful spirits and teachings of demons ,
54004002	through the insincerity of liars whose consciences are seared ,
54004003	who forbid marriage and require abstinence from foods that God created to be received with thanksgiving by those who believe and know the truth .
54004004	For everything created by God is good , and nothing is to be rejected if it is received with thanksgiving ,
54004005	for it is made holy by the word of God and prayer .
54004006	If you put these things before the brothers , you will be a good servant of Christ Jesus , being trained in the words of the faith and of the good doctrine that you have followed .
54004007	Have nothing to do with irreverent , silly myths . Rather train yourself for godliness ;
54004008	for while bodily training is of some value , godliness is of value in every way , as it holds promise for the present life and also for the life to come .
54004009	The saying is trustworthy and deserving of full acceptance .
54004010	For to this end we toil and strive , because we have our hope set on the living God , who is the Savior of all people , especially of those who believe .
54004011	Command and teach these things .
54004012	Let no one despise you for your youth , but set the believers an example in speech , in conduct , in love , in faith , in purity .
54004013	Until I come , devote yourself to the public reading of Scripture , to exhortation , to teaching .
54004014	Do not neglect the gift you have , which was given you by prophecy when the council of elders laid their hands on you .
54004015	Practice these things , immerse yourself in them , so that all may see your progress .
54004016	Keep a close watch on yourself and on the teaching . Persist in this , for by so doing you will save both yourself and your hearers .
54005001	Do not rebuke an older man but encourage him as you would a father , younger men as brothers ,
54005002	older women as mothers , younger women as sisters , in all purity .
54005003	Honor widows who are truly widows .
54005004	But if a widow has children or grandchildren , let them first learn to show godliness to their own household and to make some return to their parents , for this is pleasing in the sight of God .
54005005	She who is truly a widow , left all alone , has set her hope on God and continues in supplications and prayers night and day ,
54005006	but she who is self-indulgent is dead even while she lives .
54005007	Command these things as well , so that they may be without reproach .
54005008	But if anyone does not provide for his relatives , and especially for members of his household , he has denied the faith and is worse than an unbeliever .
54005009	Let a widow be enrolled if she is not less than sixty years of age , having been the wife of one husband ,
54005010	and having a reputation for good works : if she has brought up children , has shown hospitality , has washed the feet of the saints , has cared for the afflicted , and has devoted herself to every good work .
54005011	But refuse to enroll younger widows , for when their passions draw them away from Christ , they desire to marry
54005012	and so incur condemnation for having abandoned their former faith .
54005013	Besides that , they learn to be idlers , going about from house to house , and not only idlers , but also gossips and busybodies , saying what they should not .
54005014	So I would have younger widows marry , bear children , manage their households , and give the adversary no occasion for slander .
54005015	For some have already strayed after Satan .
54005016	If any believing woman has relatives who are widows , let her care for them . Let the church not be burdened , so that it may care for those who are truly widows .
54005017	Let the elders who rule well be considered worthy of double honor , especially those who labor in preaching and teaching .
54005018	For the Scripture says , “ You shall not muzzle an ox when it treads out the grain , ” and , “ The laborer deserves his wages . ”
54005019	Do not admit a charge against an elder except on the evidence of two or three witnesses .
54005020	As for those who persist in sin , rebuke them in the presence of all , so that the rest may stand in fear .
54005021	In the presence of God and of Christ Jesus and of the elect angels I charge you to keep these rules without prejudging , doing nothing from partiality .
54005022	Do not be hasty in the laying on of hands , nor take part in the sins of others ; keep yourself pure .
54005023	( No longer drink only water , but use a little wine for the sake of your stomach and your frequent ailments .
54005024	The sins of some men are conspicuous , going before them to judgment , but the sins of others appear later .
54005025	So also good works are conspicuous , and even those that are not cannot remain hidden .
54006001	Let all who are under a yoke as slaves regard their own masters as worthy of all honor , so that the name of God and the teaching may not be reviled .
54006002	Those who have believing masters must not be disrespectful on the ground that they are brothers ; rather they must serve all the better since those who benefit by their good service are believers and beloved . Teach and urge these things .
54006003	If anyone teaches a different doctrine and does not agree with the sound words of our Lord Jesus Christ and the teaching that accords with godliness ,
54006004	he is puffed up with conceit and understands nothing . He has an unhealthy craving for controversy and for quarrels about words , which produce envy , dissension , slander , evil suspicions ,
54006005	and constant friction among people who are depraved in mind and deprived of the truth , imagining that godliness is a means of gain .
54006006	Now there is great gain in godliness with contentment ,
54006007	for we brought nothing into the world , and we cannot take anything out of the world .
54006008	But if we have food and clothing , with these we will be content .
54006009	But those who desire to be rich fall into temptation , into a snare , into many senseless and harmful desires that plunge people into ruin and destruction .
54006010	For the love of money is a root of all kinds of evils . It is through this craving that some have wandered away from the faith and pierced themselves with many pangs .
54006011	But as for you , O man of God , flee these things . Pursue righteousness , godliness , faith , love , steadfastness , gentleness .
54006012	Fight the good fight of the faith . Take hold of the eternal life to which you were called and about which you made the good confession in the presence of many witnesses .
54006013	I charge you in the presence of God , who gives life to all things , and of Christ Jesus , who in his testimony before Pontius Pilate made the good confession ,
54006014	to keep the commandment unstained and free from reproach until the appearing of our Lord Jesus Christ ,
54006015	which he will display at the proper time — he who is the blessed and only Sovereign , the King of kings and Lord of lords ,
54006016	who alone has immortality , who dwells in unapproachable light , whom no one has ever seen or can see . To him be honor and eternal dominion . Amen .
54006017	As for the rich in this present age , charge them not to be haughty , nor to set their hopes on the uncertainty of riches , but on God , who richly provides us with everything to enjoy .
54006018	They are to do good , to be rich in good works , to be generous and ready to share ,
54006019	thus storing up treasure for themselves as a good foundation for the future , so that they may take hold of that which is truly life .
54006020	O Timothy , guard the deposit entrusted to you . Avoid the irreverent babble and contradictions of what is falsely called “ knowledge , ”
54006021	for by professing it some have swerved from the faith . Grace be with you .
55001001	Paul , an apostle of Christ Jesus by the will of God according to the promise of the life that is in Christ Jesus ,
55001002	To Timothy , my beloved child : Grace , mercy , and peace from God the Father and Christ Jesus our Lord .
55001003	I thank God whom I serve , as did my ancestors , with a clear conscience , as I remember you constantly in my prayers night and day .
55001004	As I remember your tears , I long to see you , that I may be filled with joy .
55001005	I am reminded of your sincere faith , a faith that dwelt first in your grandmother Lois and your mother Eunice and now , I am sure , dwells in you as well .
55001006	For this reason I remind you to fan into flame the gift of God , which is in you through the laying on of my hands ,
55001007	for God gave us a spirit not of fear but of power and love and self-control .
55001008	Therefore do not be ashamed of the testimony about our Lord , nor of me his prisoner , but share in suffering for the gospel by the power of God ,
55001009	who saved us and called us to a holy calling , not because of our works but because of his own purpose and grace , which he gave us in Christ Jesus before the ages began ,
55001010	and which now has been manifested through the appearing of our Savior Christ Jesus , who abolished death and brought life and immortality to light through the gospel ,
55001011	for which I was appointed a preacher and apostle and teacher ,
55001012	which is why I suffer as I do . But I am not ashamed , for I know whom I have believed , and I am convinced that he is able to guard until that Day what has been entrusted to me .
55001013	Follow the pattern of the sound words that you have heard from me , in the faith and love that are in Christ Jesus .
55001014	By the Holy Spirit who dwells within us , guard the good deposit entrusted to you .
55001015	You are aware that all who are in Asia turned away from me , among whom are Phygelus and Hermogenes .
55001016	May the Lord grant mercy to the household of Onesiphorus , for he often refreshed me and was not ashamed of my chains ,
55001017	but when he arrived in Rome he searched for me earnestly and found me —
55001018	may the Lord grant him to find mercy from the Lord on that Day ! — and you well know all the service he rendered at Ephesus .
55002001	You then , my child , be strengthened by the grace that is in Christ Jesus ,
55002002	and what you have heard from me in the presence of many witnesses entrust to faithful men who will be able to teach others also .
55002003	Share in suffering as a good soldier of Christ Jesus .
55002004	No soldier gets entangled in civilian pursuits , since his aim is to please the one who enlisted him .
55002005	An athlete is not crowned unless he competes according to the rules .
55002006	It is the hard-working farmer who ought to have the first share of the crops .
55002007	Think over what I say , for the Lord will give you understanding in everything .
55002008	Remember Jesus Christ , risen from the dead , the offspring of David , as preached in my gospel ,
55002009	for which I am suffering , bound with chains as a criminal . But the word of God is not bound !
55002010	Therefore I endure everything for the sake of the elect , that they also may obtain the salvation that is in Christ Jesus with eternal glory .
55002011	The saying is trustworthy , for : If we have died with him , we will also live with him ;
55002012	if we endure , we will also reign with him ; if we deny him , he also will deny us ;
55002013	if we are faithless , he remains faithful — for he cannot deny himself .
55002014	Remind them of these things , and charge them before God not to quarrel about words , which does no good , but only ruins the hearers .
55002015	Do your best to present yourself to God as one approved , a worker who has no need to be ashamed , rightly handling the word of truth .
55002016	But avoid irreverent babble , for it will lead people into more and more ungodliness ,
55002017	and their talk will spread like gangrene . Among them are Hymenaeus and Philetus ,
55002018	who have swerved from the truth , saying that the resurrection has already happened . They are upsetting the faith of some .
55002019	But God’s firm foundation stands , bearing this seal : “ The Lord knows those who are his , ” and , “ Let everyone who names the name of the Lord depart from iniquity . ”
55002020	Now in a great house there are not only vessels of gold and silver but also of wood and clay , some for honorable use , some for dishonorable .
55002021	Therefore , if anyone cleanses himself from what is dishonorable , he will be a vessel for honorable use , set apart as holy , useful to the master of the house , ready for every good work .
55002022	So flee youthful passions and pursue righteousness , faith , love , and peace , along with those who call on the Lord from a pure heart .
55002023	Have nothing to do with foolish , ignorant controversies ; you know that they breed quarrels .
55002024	And the Lord’s servant must not be quarrelsome but kind to everyone , able to teach , patiently enduring evil ,
55002025	correcting his opponents with gentleness . God may perhaps grant them repentance leading to a knowledge of the truth ,
55002026	and they may come to their senses and escape from the snare of the devil , after being captured by him to do his will .
55003001	But understand this , that in the last days there will come times of difficulty .
55003002	For people will be lovers of self , lovers of money , proud , arrogant , abusive , disobedient to their parents , ungrateful , unholy ,
55003003	heartless , unappeasable , slanderous , without self-control , brutal , not loving good ,
