55003004	treacherous , reckless , swollen with conceit , lovers of pleasure rather than lovers of God ,
55003005	having the appearance of godliness , but denying its power . Avoid such people .
55003006	For among them are those who creep into households and capture weak women , burdened with sins and led astray by various passions ,
55003007	always learning and never able to arrive at a knowledge of the truth .
55003008	Just as Jannes and Jambres opposed Moses , so these men also oppose the truth , men corrupted in mind and disqualified regarding the faith .
55003009	But they will not get very far , for their folly will be plain to all , as was that of those two men .
55003010	You , however , have followed my teaching , my conduct , my aim in life , my faith , my patience , my love , my steadfastness ,
55003011	my persecutions and sufferings that happened to me at Antioch , at Iconium , and at Lystra — which persecutions I endured ; yet from them all the Lord rescued me .
55003012	Indeed , all who desire to live a godly life in Christ Jesus will be persecuted ,
55003013	while evil people and impostors will go on from bad to worse , deceiving and being deceived .
55003014	But as for you , continue in what you have learned and have firmly believed , knowing from whom you learned it
55003015	and how from childhood you have been acquainted with the sacred writings , which are able to make you wise for salvation through faith in Christ Jesus .
55003016	All Scripture is breathed out by God and profitable for teaching , for reproof , for correction , and for training in righteousness ,
55003017	that the man of God may be competent , equipped for every good work .
55004001	I charge you in the presence of God and of Christ Jesus , who is to judge the living and the dead , and by his appearing and his kingdom :
55004002	preach the word ; be ready in season and out of season ; reprove , rebuke , and exhort , with complete patience and teaching .
55004003	For the time is coming when people will not endure sound teaching , but having itching ears they will accumulate for themselves teachers to suit their own passions ,
55004004	and will turn away from listening to the truth and wander off into myths .
55004005	As for you , always be sober-minded , endure suffering , do the work of an evangelist , fulfill your ministry .
55004006	For I am already being poured out as a drink offering , and the time of my departure has come .
55004007	I have fought the good fight , I have finished the race , I have kept the faith .
55004008	Henceforth there is laid up for me the crown of righteousness , which the Lord , the righteous judge , will award to me on that Day , and not only to me but also to all who have loved his appearing .
55004009	Do your best to come to me soon .
55004010	For Demas , in love with this present world , has deserted me and gone to Thessalonica . Crescens has gone to Galatia , Titus to Dalmatia .
55004011	Luke alone is with me . Get Mark and bring him with you , for he is very useful to me for ministry .
55004012	Tychicus I have sent to Ephesus .
55004013	When you come , bring the cloak that I left with Carpus at Troas , also the books , and above all the parchments .
55004014	Alexander the coppersmith did me great harm ; the Lord will repay him according to his deeds .
55004015	Beware of him yourself , for he strongly opposed our message .
55004016	At my first defense no one came to stand by me , but all deserted me . May it not be charged against them !
55004017	But the Lord stood by me and strengthened me , so that through me the message might be fully proclaimed and all the Gentiles might hear it . So I was rescued from the lion’s mouth .
55004018	The Lord will rescue me from every evil deed and bring me safely into his heavenly kingdom . To him be the glory forever and ever . Amen .
55004019	Greet Prisca and Aquila , and the household of Onesiphorus .
55004020	Erastus remained at Corinth , and I left Trophimus , who was ill , at Miletus .
55004021	Do your best to come before winter . Eubulus sends greetings to you , as do Pudens and Linus and Claudia and all the brothers .
55004022	The Lord be with your spirit . Grace be with you .
56001001	Paul , a servant of God and an apostle of Jesus Christ , for the sake of the faith of God’s elect and their knowledge of the truth , which accords with godliness ,
56001002	in hope of eternal life , which God , who never lies , promised before the ages began
56001003	and at the proper time manifested in his word through the preaching with which I have been entrusted by the command of God our Savior ;
56001004	To Titus , my true child in a common faith : Grace and peace from God the Father and Christ Jesus our Savior .
56001005	This is why I left you in Crete , so that you might put what remained into order , and appoint elders in every town as I directed you —
56001006	if anyone is above reproach , the husband of one wife , and his children are believers and not open to the charge of debauchery or insubordination .
56001007	For an overseer , as God’s steward , must be above reproach . He must not be arrogant or quick-tempered or a drunkard or violent or greedy for gain ,
56001008	but hospitable , a lover of good , self-controlled , upright , holy , and disciplined .
56001009	He must hold firm to the trustworthy word as taught , so that he may be able to give instruction in sound doctrine and also to rebuke those who contradict it .
56001010	For there are many who are insubordinate , empty talkers and deceivers , especially those of the circumcision party .
56001011	They must be silenced , since they are upsetting whole families by teaching for shameful gain what they ought not to teach .
56001012	One of the Cretans , a prophet of their own , said , “ Cretans are always liars , evil beasts , lazy gluttons . ”
56001013	This testimony is true . Therefore rebuke them sharply , that they may be sound in the faith ,
56001014	not devoting themselves to Jewish myths and the commands of people who turn away from the truth .
56001015	To the pure , all things are pure , but to the defiled and unbelieving , nothing is pure ; but both their minds and their consciences are defiled .
56001016	They profess to know God , but they deny him by their works . They are detestable , disobedient , unfit for any good work .
56002001	But as for you , teach what accords with sound doctrine .
56002002	Older men are to be sober-minded , dignified , self-controlled , sound in faith , in love , and in steadfastness .
56002003	Older women likewise are to be reverent in behavior , not slanderers or slaves to much wine . They are to teach what is good ,
56002004	and so train the young women to love their husbands and children ,
56002005	to be self-controlled , pure , working at home , kind , and submissive to their own husbands , that the word of God may not be reviled .
56002006	Likewise , urge the younger men to be self-controlled .
56002007	Show yourself in all respects to be a model of good works , and in your teaching show integrity , dignity ,
56002008	and sound speech that cannot be condemned , so that an opponent may be put to shame , having nothing evil to say about us .
56002009	Slaves are to be submissive to their own masters in everything ; they are to be well-pleasing , not argumentative ,
56002010	not pilfering , but showing all good faith , so that in everything they may adorn the doctrine of God our Savior .
56002011	For the grace of God has appeared , bringing salvation for all people ,
56002012	training us to renounce ungodliness and worldly passions , and to live self-controlled , upright , and godly lives in the present age ,
56002013	waiting for our blessed hope , the appearing of the glory of our great God and Savior Jesus Christ ,
56002014	who gave himself for us to redeem us from all lawlessness and to purify for himself a people for his own possession who are zealous for good works .
56002015	Declare these things ; exhort and rebuke with all authority . Let no one disregard you .
56003001	Remind them to be submissive to rulers and authorities , to be obedient , to be ready for every good work ,
56003002	to speak evil of no one , to avoid quarreling , to be gentle , and to show perfect courtesy toward all people .
56003003	For we ourselves were once foolish , disobedient , led astray , slaves to various passions and pleasures , passing our days in malice and envy , hated by others and hating one another .
56003004	But when the goodness and loving kindness of God our Savior appeared ,
56003005	he saved us , not because of works done by us in righteousness , but according to his own mercy , by the washing of regeneration and renewal of the Holy Spirit ,
56003006	whom he poured out on us richly through Jesus Christ our Savior ,
56003007	so that being justified by his grace we might become heirs according to the hope of eternal life .
56003008	The saying is trustworthy , and I want you to insist on these things , so that those who have believed in God may be careful to devote themselves to good works . These things are excellent and profitable for people .
56003009	But avoid foolish controversies , genealogies , dissensions , and quarrels about the law , for they are unprofitable and worthless .
56003010	As for a person who stirs up division , after warning him once and then twice , have nothing more to do with him ,
56003011	knowing that such a person is warped and sinful ; he is self-condemned .
56003012	When I send Artemas or Tychicus to you , do your best to come to me at Nicopolis , for I have decided to spend the winter there .
56003013	Do your best to speed Zenas the lawyer and Apollos on their way ; see that they lack nothing .
56003014	And let our people learn to devote themselves to good works , so as to help cases of urgent need , and not be unfruitful .
56003015	All who are with me send greetings to you . Greet those who love us in the faith . Grace be with you all .
57001001	Paul , a prisoner for Christ Jesus , and Timothy our brother , To Philemon our beloved fellow worker
57001002	and Apphia our sister and Archippus our fellow soldier , and the church in your house :
57001003	Grace to you and peace from God our Father and the Lord Jesus Christ .
57001004	I thank my God always when I remember you in my prayers ,
57001005	because I hear of your love and of the faith that you have toward the Lord Jesus and for all the saints ,
57001006	and I pray that the sharing of your faith may become effective for the full knowledge of every good thing that is in us for the sake of Christ .
57001007	For I have derived much joy and comfort from your love , my brother , because the hearts of the saints have been refreshed through you .
57001008	Accordingly , though I am bold enough in Christ to command you to do what is required ,
57001009	yet for love’s sake I prefer to appeal to you — I , Paul , an old man and now a prisoner also for Christ Jesus —
57001010	I appeal to you for my child , Onesimus , whose father I became in my imprisonment .
57001011	( Formerly he was useless to you , but now he is indeed useful to you and to me .
57001012	I am sending him back to you , sending my very heart .
57001013	I would have been glad to keep him with me , in order that he might serve me on your behalf during my imprisonment for the gospel ,
57001014	but I preferred to do nothing without your consent in order that your goodness might not be by compulsion but of your own accord .
57001015	For this perhaps is why he was parted from you for a while , that you might have him back forever ,
57001016	no longer as a slave but more than a slave , as a beloved brother — especially to me , but how much more to you , both in the flesh and in the Lord .
57001017	So if you consider me your partner , receive him as you would receive me .
57001018	If he has wronged you at all , or owes you anything , charge that to my account .
57001019	I , Paul , write this with my own hand : I will repay it — to say nothing of your owing me even your own self .
57001020	Yes , brother , I want some benefit from you in the Lord . Refresh my heart in Christ .
57001021	Confident of your obedience , I write to you , knowing that you will do even more than I say .
57001022	At the same time , prepare a guest room for me , for I am hoping that through your prayers I will be graciously given to you .
57001023	Epaphras , my fellow prisoner in Christ Jesus , sends greetings to you ,
57001024	and so do Mark , Aristarchus , Demas , and Luke , my fellow workers .
57001025	The grace of the Lord Jesus Christ be with your spirit .
58001001	Long ago , at many times and in many ways , God spoke to our fathers by the prophets ,
58001002	but in these last days he has spoken to us by his Son , whom he appointed the heir of all things , through whom also he created the world .
58001003	He is the radiance of the glory of God and the exact imprint of his nature , and he upholds the universe by the word of his power . After making purification for sins , he sat down at the right hand of the Majesty on high ,
58001004	having become as much superior to angels as the name he has inherited is more excellent than theirs .
58001005	For to which of the angels did God ever say , “ You are my Son , today I have begotten you ” ? Or again , “ I will be to him a father , and he shall be to me a son ” ?
58001006	And again , when he brings the firstborn into the world , he says , “ Let all God’s angels worship him . ”
58001007	Of the angels he says , “ He makes his angels winds , and his ministers a flame of fire . ”
58001008	But of the Son he says , “ Your throne , O God , is forever and ever , the scepter of uprightness is the scepter of your kingdom .
58001009	You have loved righteousness and hated wickedness ; therefore God , your God , has anointed you with the oil of gladness beyond your companions . ”
58001010	And , “ You , Lord , laid the foundation of the earth in the beginning , and the heavens are the work of your hands ;
58001011	they will perish , but you remain ; they will all wear out like a garment ,
58001012	like a robe you will roll them up , like a garment they will be changed . But you are the same , and your years will have no end . ”
58001013	And to which of the angels has he ever said , “ Sit at my right hand until I make your enemies a footstool for your feet ” ?
58001014	Are they not all ministering spirits sent out to serve for the sake of those who are to inherit salvation ?
58002001	Therefore we must pay much closer attention to what we have heard , lest we drift away from it .
58002002	For since the message declared by angels proved to be reliable , and every transgression or disobedience received a just retribution ,
58002003	how shall we escape if we neglect such a great salvation ? It was declared at first by the Lord , and it was attested to us by those who heard ,
58002004	while God also bore witness by signs and wonders and various miracles and by gifts of the Holy Spirit distributed according to his will .
58002005	Now it was not to angels that God subjected the world to come , of which we are speaking .
58002006	It has been testified somewhere , “ What is man , that you are mindful of him , or the son of man , that you care for him ?
58002007	You made him for a little while lower than the angels ; you have crowned him with glory and honor ,
58002008	putting everything in subjection under his feet . ” Now in putting everything in subjection to him , he left nothing outside his control . At present , we do not yet see everything in subjection to him .
58002009	But we see him who for a little while was made lower than the angels , namely Jesus , crowned with glory and honor because of the suffering of death , so that by the grace of God he might taste death for everyone .
58002010	For it was fitting that he , for whom and by whom all things exist , in bringing many sons to glory , should make the founder of their salvation perfect through suffering .
58002011	For he who sanctifies and those who are sanctified all have one source . That is why he is not ashamed to call them brothers ,
58002012	saying , “ I will tell of your name to my brothers ; in the midst of the congregation I will sing your praise . ”
58002013	And again , “ I will put my trust in him . ” And again , “ Behold , I and the children God has given me . ”
58002014	Since therefore the children share in flesh and blood , he himself likewise partook of the same things , that through death he might destroy the one who has the power of death , that is , the devil ,
58002015	and deliver all those who through fear of death were subject to lifelong slavery .
58002016	For surely it is not angels that he helps , but he helps the offspring of Abraham .
58002017	Therefore he had to be made like his brothers in every respect , so that he might become a merciful and faithful high priest in the service of God , to make propitiation for the sins of the people .
58002018	For because he himself has suffered when tempted , he is able to help those who are being tempted .
58003001	Therefore , holy brothers , you who share in a heavenly calling , consider Jesus , the apostle and high priest of our confession ,
58003002	who was faithful to him who appointed him , just as Moses also was faithful in all God’s house .
58003003	For Jesus has been counted worthy of more glory than Moses — as much more glory as the builder of a house has more honor than the house itself .
58003004	( For every house is built by someone , but the builder of all things is God .
58003005	Now Moses was faithful in all God’s house as a servant , to testify to the things that were to be spoken later ,
58003006	but Christ is faithful over God’s house as a son . And we are his house if indeed we hold fast our confidence and our boasting in our hope .
58003007	Therefore , as the Holy Spirit says , “ Today , if you hear his voice ,
58003008	do not harden your hearts as in the rebellion , on the day of testing in the wilderness ,
58003009	where your fathers put me to the test and saw my works for forty years .
58003010	Therefore I was provoked with that generation , and said , ‘ They always go astray in their heart ; they have not known my ways . ’
58003011	As I swore in my wrath , ‘ They shall not enter my rest . ’ ”
58003012	Take care , brothers , lest there be in any of you an evil , unbelieving heart , leading you to fall away from the living God .
58003013	But exhort one another every day , as long as it is called “ today , ” that none of you may be hardened by the deceitfulness of sin .
58003014	For we have come to share in Christ , if indeed we hold our original confidence firm to the end .
58003015	As it is said , “ Today , if you hear his voice , do not harden your hearts as in the rebellion . ”
58003016	For who were those who heard and yet rebelled ? Was it not all those who left Egypt led by Moses ?
58003017	And with whom was he provoked for forty years ? Was it not with those who sinned , whose bodies fell in the wilderness ?
58003018	And to whom did he swear that they would not enter his rest , but to those who were disobedient ?
58003019	So we see that they were unable to enter because of unbelief .
58004001	Therefore , while the promise of entering his rest still stands , let us fear lest any of you should seem to have failed to reach it .
58004002	For good news came to us just as to them , but the message they heard did not benefit them , because they were not united by faith with those who listened .
58004003	For we who have believed enter that rest , as he has said , “ As I swore in my wrath , ‘ They shall not enter my rest , ’ ” although his works were finished from the foundation of the world .
58004004	For he has somewhere spoken of the seventh day in this way : “ And God rested on the seventh day from all his works . ”
58004005	And again in this passage he said , “ They shall not enter my rest . ”
58004006	Since therefore it remains for some to enter it , and those who formerly received the good news failed to enter because of disobedience ,
58004007	again he appoints a certain day , “ Today , ” saying through David so long afterward , in the words already quoted , “ Today , if you hear his voice , do not harden your hearts . ”
58004008	For if Joshua had given them rest , God would not have spoken of another day later on .
58004009	So then , there remains a Sabbath rest for the people of God ,
58004010	for whoever has entered God’s rest has also rested from his works as God did from his .
58004011	Let us therefore strive to enter that rest , so that no one may fall by the same sort of disobedience .
58004012	For the word of God is living and active , sharper than any two-edged sword , piercing to the division of soul and of spirit , of joints and of marrow , and discerning the thoughts and intentions of the heart .
58004013	And no creature is hidden from his sight , but all are naked and exposed to the eyes of him to whom we must give account .
58004014	Since then we have a great high priest who has passed through the heavens , Jesus , the Son of God , let us hold fast our confession .
58004015	For we do not have a high priest who is unable to sympathize with our weaknesses , but one who in every respect has been tempted as we are , yet without sin .
58004016	Let us then with confidence draw near to the throne of grace , that we may receive mercy and find grace to help in time of need .
58005001	For every high priest chosen from among men is appointed to act on behalf of men in relation to God , to offer gifts and sacrifices for sins .
58005002	He can deal gently with the ignorant and wayward , since he himself is beset with weakness .
58005003	Because of this he is obligated to offer sacrifice for his own sins just as he does for those of the people .
58005004	And no one takes this honor for himself , but only when called by God , just as Aaron was .
58005005	So also Christ did not exalt himself to be made a high priest , but was appointed by him who said to him , “ You are my Son , today I have begotten you ” ;
58005006	as he says also in another place , “ You are a priest forever , after the order of Melchizedek . ”
58005007	In the days of his flesh , Jesus offered up prayers and supplications , with loud cries and tears , to him who was able to save him from death , and he was heard because of his reverence .
58005008	Although he was a son , he learned obedience through what he suffered .
58005009	And being made perfect , he became the source of eternal salvation to all who obey him ,
58005010	being designated by God a high priest after the order of Melchizedek .
58005011	About this we have much to say , and it is hard to explain , since you have become dull of hearing .
58005012	For though by this time you ought to be teachers , you need someone to teach you again the basic principles of the oracles of God . You need milk , not solid food ,
58005013	for everyone who lives on milk is unskilled in the word of righteousness , since he is a child .
58005014	But solid food is for the mature , for those who have their powers of discernment trained by constant practice to distinguish good from evil .
58006001	Therefore let us leave the elementary doctrine of Christ and go on to maturity , not laying again a foundation of repentance from dead works and of faith toward God ,
58006002	and of instruction about washings , the laying on of hands , the resurrection of the dead , and eternal judgment .
58006003	And this we will do if God permits .
58006004	For it is impossible , in the case of those who have once been enlightened , who have tasted the heavenly gift , and have shared in the Holy Spirit ,
58006005	and have tasted the goodness of the word of God and the powers of the age to come ,
58006006	and then have fallen away , to restore them again to repentance , since they are crucifying once again the Son of God to their own harm and holding him up to contempt .
58006007	For land that has drunk the rain that often falls on it , and produces a crop useful to those for whose sake it is cultivated , receives a blessing from God .
58006008	But if it bears thorns and thistles , it is worthless and near to being cursed , and its end is to be burned .
58006009	Though we speak in this way , yet in your case , beloved , we feel sure of better things — things that belong to salvation .
58006010	For God is not unjust so as to overlook your work and the love that you have shown for his name in serving the saints , as you still do .
58006011	And we desire each one of you to show the same earnestness to have the full assurance of hope until the end ,
58006012	so that you may not be sluggish , but imitators of those who through faith and patience inherit the promises .
58006013	For when God made a promise to Abraham , since he had no one greater by whom to swear , he swore by himself ,
58006014	saying , “ Surely I will bless you and multiply you . ”
58006015	And thus Abraham , having patiently waited , obtained the promise .
58006016	For people swear by something greater than themselves , and in all their disputes an oath is final for confirmation .
58006017	So when God desired to show more convincingly to the heirs of the promise the unchangeable character of his purpose , he guaranteed it with an oath ,
58006018	so that by two unchangeable things , in which it is impossible for God to lie , we who have fled for refuge might have strong encouragement to hold fast to the hope set before us .
58006019	We have this as a sure and steadfast anchor of the soul , a hope that enters into the inner place behind the curtain ,
58006020	where Jesus has gone as a forerunner on our behalf , having become a high priest forever after the order of Melchizedek .
58007001	For this Melchizedek , king of Salem , priest of the Most High God , met Abraham returning from the slaughter of the kings and blessed him ,
58007002	and to him Abraham apportioned a tenth part of everything . He is first , by translation of his name , king of righteousness , and then he is also king of Salem , that is , king of peace .
58007003	He is without father or mother or genealogy , having neither beginning of days nor end of life , but resembling the Son of God he continues a priest forever .
58007004	See how great this man was to whom Abraham the patriarch gave a tenth of the spoils !
58007005	And those descendants of Levi who receive the priestly office have a commandment in the law to take tithes from the people , that is , from their brothers , though these also are descended from Abraham .
58007006	But this man who does not have his descent from them received tithes from Abraham and blessed him who had the promises .
58007007	It is beyond dispute that the inferior is blessed by the superior .
58007008	In the one case tithes are received by mortal men , but in the other case , by one of whom it is testified that he lives .
58007009	One might even say that Levi himself , who receives tithes , paid tithes through Abraham ,
58007010	for he was still in the loins of his ancestor when Melchizedek met him .
58007011	Now if perfection had been attainable through the Levitical priesthood ( for under it the people received the law ) , what further need would there have been for another priest to arise after the order of Melchizedek , rather than one named after the order of Aaron ?
58007012	For when there is a change in the priesthood , there is necessarily a change in the law as well .
58007013	For the one of whom these things are spoken belonged to another tribe , from which no one has ever served at the altar .
58007014	For it is evident that our Lord was descended from Judah , and in connection with that tribe Moses said nothing about priests .
58007015	This becomes even more evident when another priest arises in the likeness of Melchizedek ,
58007016	who has become a priest , not on the basis of a legal requirement concerning bodily descent , but by the power of an indestructible life .
58007017	For it is witnessed of him , “ You are a priest forever , after the order of Melchizedek . ”
58007018	For on the one hand , a former commandment is set aside because of its weakness and uselessness
58007019	( for the law made nothing perfect ) ; but on the other hand , a better hope is introduced , through which we draw near to God .
58007020	And it was not without an oath . For those who formerly became priests were made such without an oath ,
58007021	but this one was made a priest with an oath by the one who said to him : “ The Lord has sworn and will not change his mind , ‘ You are a priest forever . ’ ”
58007022	This makes Jesus the guarantor of a better covenant .
58007023	The former priests were many in number , because they were prevented by death from continuing in office ,
58007024	but he holds his priesthood permanently , because he continues forever .
58007025	Consequently , he is able to save to the uttermost those who draw near to God through him , since he always lives to make intercession for them .
58007026	For it was indeed fitting that we should have such a high priest , holy , innocent , unstained , separated from sinners , and exalted above the heavens .
58007027	He has no need , like those high priests , to offer sacrifices daily , first for his own sins and then for those of the people , since he did this once for all when he offered up himself .
58007028	For the law appoints men in their weakness as high priests , but the word of the oath , which came later than the law , appoints a Son who has been made perfect forever .
58008001	Now the point in what we are saying is this : we have such a high priest , one who is seated at the right hand of the throne of the Majesty in heaven ,
58008002	a minister in the holy places , in the true tent that the Lord set up , not man .
58008003	For every high priest is appointed to offer gifts and sacrifices ; thus it is necessary for this priest also to have something to offer .
58008004	Now if he were on earth , he would not be a priest at all , since there are priests who offer gifts according to the law .
58008005	They serve a copy and shadow of the heavenly things . For when Moses was about to erect the tent , he was instructed by God , saying , “ See that you make everything according to the pattern that was shown you on the mountain . ”
58008006	But as it is , Christ has obtained a ministry that is as much more excellent than the old as the covenant he mediates is better , since it is enacted on better promises .
58008007	For if that first covenant had been faultless , there would have been no occasion to look for a second .
58008008	For he finds fault with them when he says : “ Behold , the days are coming , declares the Lord , when I will establish a new covenant with the house of Israel and with the house of Judah ,
58008009	not like the covenant that I made with their fathers on the day when I took them by the hand to bring them out of the land of Egypt . For they did not continue in my covenant , and so I showed no concern for them , declares the Lord .
58008010	For this is the covenant that I will make with the house of Israel after those days , declares the Lord : I will put my laws into their minds , and write them on their hearts , and I will be their God , and they shall be my people .
58008011	And they shall not teach , each one his neighbor and each one his brother , saying , ‘ Know the Lord , ’ for they shall all know me , from the least of them to the greatest .
58008012	For I will be merciful toward their iniquities , and I will remember their sins no more . ”
58008013	In speaking of a new covenant , he makes the first one obsolete . And what is becoming obsolete and growing old is ready to vanish away .
58009001	Now even the first covenant had regulations for worship and an earthly place of holiness .
58009002	For a tent was prepared , the first section , in which were the lampstand and the table and the bread of the Presence . It is called the Holy Place .
58009003	Behind the second curtain was a second section called the Most Holy Place ,
58009004	having the golden altar of incense and the ark of the covenant covered on all sides with gold , in which was a golden urn holding the manna , and Aaron’s staff that budded , and the tablets of the covenant .
58009005	Above it were the cherubim of glory overshadowing the mercy seat . Of these things we cannot now speak in detail .
58009006	These preparations having thus been made , the priests go regularly into the first section , performing their ritual duties ,
58009007	but into the second only the high priest goes , and he but once a year , and not without taking blood , which he offers for himself and for the unintentional sins of the people .
58009008	By this the Holy Spirit indicates that the way into the holy places is not yet opened as long as the first section is still standing
58009009	( which is symbolic for the present age ) . According to this arrangement , gifts and sacrifices are offered that cannot perfect the conscience of the worshiper ,
58009010	but deal only with food and drink and various washings , regulations for the body imposed until the time of reformation .
58009011	But when Christ appeared as a high priest of the good things that have come , then through the greater and more perfect tent ( not made with hands , that is , not of this creation
58009012	he entered once for all into the holy places , not by means of the blood of goats and calves but by means of his own blood , thus securing an eternal redemption .
58009013	For if the blood of goats and bulls , and the sprinkling of defiled persons with the ashes of a heifer , sanctify for the purification of the flesh ,
58009014	how much more will the blood of Christ , who through the eternal Spirit offered himself without blemish to God , purify our conscience from dead works to serve the living God .
58009015	Therefore he is the mediator of a new covenant , so that those who are called may receive the promised eternal inheritance , since a death has occurred that redeems them from the transgressions committed under the first covenant .
58009016	For where a will is involved , the death of the one who made it must be established .
58009017	For a will takes effect only at death , since it is not in force as long as the one who made it is alive .
58009018	Therefore not even the first covenant was inaugurated without blood .
58009019	For when every commandment of the law had been declared by Moses to all the people , he took the blood of calves and goats , with water and scarlet wool and hyssop , and sprinkled both the book itself and all the people ,
58009020	saying , “ This is the blood of the covenant that God commanded for you . ”
58009021	And in the same way he sprinkled with the blood both the tent and all the vessels used in worship .
58009022	Indeed , under the law almost everything is purified with blood , and without the shedding of blood there is no forgiveness of sins .
58009023	Thus it was necessary for the copies of the heavenly things to be purified with these rites , but the heavenly things themselves with better sacrifices than these .
58009024	For Christ has entered , not into holy places made with hands , which are copies of the true things , but into heaven itself , now to appear in the presence of God on our behalf .
58009025	Nor was it to offer himself repeatedly , as the high priest enters the holy places every year with blood not his own ,
58009026	for then he would have had to suffer repeatedly since the foundation of the world . But as it is , he has appeared once for all at the end of the ages to put away sin by the sacrifice of himself .
58009027	And just as it is appointed for man to die once , and after that comes judgment ,
58009028	so Christ , having been offered once to bear the sins of many , will appear a second time , not to deal with sin but to save those who are eagerly waiting for him .
58010001	For since the law has but a shadow of the good things to come instead of the true form of these realities , it can never , by the same sacrifices that are continually offered every year , make perfect those who draw near .
58010002	Otherwise , would they not have ceased to be offered , since the worshipers , having once been cleansed , would no longer have any consciousness of sins ?
58010003	But in these sacrifices there is a reminder of sins every year .
58010004	For it is impossible for the blood of bulls and goats to take away sins .
58010005	Consequently , when Christ came into the world , he said , “ Sacrifices and offerings you have not desired , but a body have you prepared for me ;
58010006	in burnt offerings and sin offerings you have taken no pleasure .
58010007	Then I said , ‘ Behold , I have come to do your will , O God , as it is written of me in the scroll of the book . ’ ”
58010008	When he said above , “ You have neither desired nor taken pleasure in sacrifices and offerings and burnt offerings and sin offerings ” ( these are offered according to the law ) ,
58010009	then he added , “ Behold , I have come to do your will . ” He does away with the first in order to establish the second .
58010010	And by that will we have been sanctified through the offering of the body of Jesus Christ once for all .
58010011	And every priest stands daily at his service , offering repeatedly the same sacrifices , which can never take away sins .
58010012	But when Christ had offered for all time a single sacrifice for sins , he sat down at the right hand of God ,
58010013	waiting from that time until his enemies should be made a footstool for his feet .
58010014	For by a single offering he has perfected for all time those who are being sanctified .
58010015	And the Holy Spirit also bears witness to us ; for after saying ,
58010016	“ This is the covenant that I will make with them after those days , declares the Lord : I will put my laws on their hearts , and write them on their minds , ”
58010017	then he adds , “ I will remember their sins and their lawless deeds no more . ”
58010018	Where there is forgiveness of these , there is no longer any offering for sin .
58010019	Therefore , brothers , since we have confidence to enter the holy places by the blood of Jesus ,
58010020	by the new and living way that he opened for us through the curtain , that is , through his flesh ,
58010021	and since we have a great priest over the house of God ,
58010022	let us draw near with a true heart in full assurance of faith , with our hearts sprinkled clean from an evil conscience and our bodies washed with pure water .
58010023	Let us hold fast the confession of our hope without wavering , for he who promised is faithful .
58010024	And let us consider how to stir up one another to love and good works ,
58010025	not neglecting to meet together , as is the habit of some , but encouraging one another , and all the more as you see the Day drawing near .
58010026	For if we go on sinning deliberately after receiving the knowledge of the truth , there no longer remains a sacrifice for sins ,
58010027	but a fearful expectation of judgment , and a fury of fire that will consume the adversaries .
58010028	Anyone who has set aside the law of Moses dies without mercy on the evidence of two or three witnesses .
58010029	How much worse punishment , do you think , will be deserved by the one who has spurned the Son of God , and has profaned the blood of the covenant by which he was sanctified , and has outraged the Spirit of grace ?
58010030	For we know him who said , “ Vengeance is mine ; I will repay . ” And again , “ The Lord will judge his people . ”
58010031	It is a fearful thing to fall into the hands of the living God .
58010032	But recall the former days when , after you were enlightened , you endured a hard struggle with sufferings ,
58010033	sometimes being publicly exposed to reproach and affliction , and sometimes being partners with those so treated .
58010034	For you had compassion on those in prison , and you joyfully accepted the plundering of your property , since you knew that you yourselves had a better possession and an abiding one .
58010035	Therefore do not throw away your confidence , which has a great reward .
58010036	For you have need of endurance , so that when you have done the will of God you may receive what is promised .
58010037	For , “ Yet a little while , and the coming one will come and will not delay ;
58010038	but my righteous one shall live by faith , and if he shrinks back , my soul has no pleasure in him . ”
58010039	But we are not of those who shrink back and are destroyed , but of those who have faith and preserve their souls .
58011001	Now faith is the assurance of things hoped for , the conviction of things not seen .
58011002	For by it the people of old received their commendation .
58011003	By faith we understand that the universe was created by the word of God , so that what is seen was not made out of things that are visible .
58011004	By faith Abel offered to God a more acceptable sacrifice than Cain , through which he was commended as righteous , God commending him by accepting his gifts . And through his faith , though he died , he still speaks .
58011005	By faith Enoch was taken up so that he should not see death , and he was not found , because God had taken him . Now before he was taken he was commended as having pleased God .
58011006	And without faith it is impossible to please him , for whoever would draw near to God must believe that he exists and that he rewards those who seek him .
58011007	By faith Noah , being warned by God concerning events as yet unseen , in reverent fear constructed an ark for the saving of his household . By this he condemned the world and became an heir of the righteousness that comes by faith .
58011008	By faith Abraham obeyed when he was called to go out to a place that he was to receive as an inheritance . And he went out , not knowing where he was going .
58011009	By faith he went to live in the land of promise , as in a foreign land , living in tents with Isaac and Jacob , heirs with him of the same promise .
58011010	For he was looking forward to the city that has foundations , whose designer and builder is God .
58011011	By faith Sarah herself received power to conceive , even when she was past the age , since she considered him faithful who had promised .
58011012	Therefore from one man , and him as good as dead , were born descendants as many as the stars of heaven and as many as the innumerable grains of sand by the seashore .
58011013	These all died in faith , not having received the things promised , but having seen them and greeted them from afar , and having acknowledged that they were strangers and exiles on the earth .
58011014	For people who speak thus make it clear that they are seeking a homeland .
58011015	If they had been thinking of that land from which they had gone out , they would have had opportunity to return .
58011016	But as it is , they desire a better country , that is , a heavenly one . Therefore God is not ashamed to be called their God , for he has prepared for them a city .
58011017	By faith Abraham , when he was tested , offered up Isaac , and he who had received the promises was in the act of offering up his only son ,
58011018	of whom it was said , “ Through Isaac shall your offspring be named . ”
58011019	He considered that God was able even to raise him from the dead , from which , figuratively speaking , he did receive him back .
58011020	By faith Isaac invoked future blessings on Jacob and Esau .
58011021	By faith Jacob , when dying , blessed each of the sons of Joseph , bowing in worship over the head of his staff .
58011022	By faith Joseph , at the end of his life , made mention of the exodus of the Israelites and gave directions concerning his bones .
58011023	By faith Moses , when he was born , was hidden for three months by his parents , because they saw that the child was beautiful , and they were not afraid of the king’s edict .
58011024	By faith Moses , when he was grown up , refused to be called the son of Pharaoh’s daughter ,
58011025	choosing rather to be mistreated with the people of God than to enjoy the fleeting pleasures of sin .
58011026	He considered the reproach of Christ greater wealth than the treasures of Egypt , for he was looking to the reward .
58011027	By faith he left Egypt , not being afraid of the anger of the king , for he endured as seeing him who is invisible .
58011028	By faith he kept the Passover and sprinkled the blood , so that the Destroyer of the firstborn might not touch them .
58011029	By faith the people crossed the Red Sea as on dry land , but the Egyptians , when they attempted to do the same , were drowned .
58011030	By faith the walls of Jericho fell down after they had been encircled for seven days .
58011031	By faith Rahab the prostitute did not perish with those who were disobedient , because she had given a friendly welcome to the spies .
58011032	And what more shall I say ? For time would fail me to tell of Gideon , Barak , Samson , Jephthah , of David and Samuel and the prophets —
58011033	who through faith conquered kingdoms , enforced justice , obtained promises , stopped the mouths of lions ,
58011034	quenched the power of fire , escaped the edge of the sword , were made strong out of weakness , became mighty in war , put foreign armies to flight .
58011035	Women received back their dead by resurrection . Some were tortured , refusing to accept release , so that they might rise again to a better life .
58011036	Others suffered mocking and flogging , and even chains and imprisonment .
58011037	They were stoned , they were sawn in two , they were killed with the sword . They went about in skins of sheep and goats , destitute , afflicted , mistreated —
58011038	of whom the world was not worthy — wandering about in deserts and mountains , and in dens and caves of the earth .
58011039	And all these , though commended through their faith , did not receive what was promised ,
58011040	since God had provided something better for us , that apart from us they should not be made perfect .
58012001	Therefore , since we are surrounded by so great a cloud of witnesses , let us also lay aside every weight , and sin which clings so closely , and let us run with endurance the race that is set before us ,
58012002	looking to Jesus , the founder and perfecter of our faith , who for the joy that was set before him endured the cross , despising the shame , and is seated at the right hand of the throne of God .
58012003	Consider him who endured from sinners such hostility against himself , so that you may not grow weary or fainthearted .
58012004	In your struggle against sin you have not yet resisted to the point of shedding your blood .
58012005	And have you forgotten the exhortation that addresses you as sons ? “ My son , do not regard lightly the discipline of the Lord , nor be weary when reproved by him .
58012006	For the Lord disciplines the one he loves , and chastises every son whom he receives . ”
58012007	It is for discipline that you have to endure . God is treating you as sons . For what son is there whom his father does not discipline ?
58012008	If you are left without discipline , in which all have participated , then you are illegitimate children and not sons .
58012009	Besides this , we have had earthly fathers who disciplined us and we respected them . Shall we not much more be subject to the Father of spirits and live ?
58012010	For they disciplined us for a short time as it seemed best to them , but he disciplines us for our good , that we may share his holiness .
58012011	For the moment all discipline seems painful rather than pleasant , but later it yields the peaceful fruit of righteousness to those who have been trained by it .
58012012	Therefore lift your drooping hands and strengthen your weak knees ,
58012013	and make straight paths for your feet , so that what is lame may not be put out of joint but rather be healed .
58012014	Strive for peace with everyone , and for the holiness without which no one will see the Lord .
58012015	See to it that no one fails to obtain the grace of God ; that no “ root of bitterness ” springs up and causes trouble , and by it many become defiled ;
58012016	that no one is sexually immoral or unholy like Esau , who sold his birthright for a single meal .
58012017	For you know that afterward , when he desired to inherit the blessing , he was rejected , for he found no chance to repent , though he sought it with tears .
58012018	For you have not come to what may be touched , a blazing fire and darkness and gloom and a tempest
58012019	and the sound of a trumpet and a voice whose words made the hearers beg that no further messages be spoken to them .
58012020	For they could not endure the order that was given , “ If even a beast touches the mountain , it shall be stoned . ”
58012021	Indeed , so terrifying was the sight that Moses said , “ I tremble with fear . ”
58012022	But you have come to Mount Zion and to the city of the living God , the heavenly Jerusalem , and to innumerable angels in festal gathering ,
58012023	and to the assembly of the firstborn who are enrolled in heaven , and to God , the judge of all , and to the spirits of the righteous made perfect ,
58012024	and to Jesus , the mediator of a new covenant , and to the sprinkled blood that speaks a better word than the blood of Abel .
58012025	See that you do not refuse him who is speaking . For if they did not escape when they refused him who warned them on earth , much less will we escape if we reject him who warns from heaven .
58012026	At that time his voice shook the earth , but now he has promised , “ Yet once more I will shake not only the earth but also the heavens . ”
58012027	This phrase , “ Yet once more , ” indicates the removal of things that are shaken — that is , things that have been made — in order that the things that cannot be shaken may remain .
58012028	Therefore let us be grateful for receiving a kingdom that cannot be shaken , and thus let us offer to God acceptable worship , with reverence and awe ,
58012029	for our God is a consuming fire .
58013001	Let brotherly love continue .
58013002	Do not neglect to show hospitality to strangers , for thereby some have entertained angels unawares .
58013003	Remember those who are in prison , as though in prison with them , and those who are mistreated , since you also are in the body .
58013004	Let marriage be held in honor among all , and let the marriage bed be undefiled , for God will judge the sexually immoral and adulterous .
58013005	Keep your life free from love of money , and be content with what you have , for he has said , “ I will never leave you nor forsake you . ”
58013006	So we can confidently say , “ The Lord is my helper ; I will not fear ; what can man do to me ? ”
58013007	Remember your leaders , those who spoke to you the word of God . Consider the outcome of their way of life , and imitate their faith .
58013008	Jesus Christ is the same yesterday and today and forever .
58013009	Do not be led away by diverse and strange teachings , for it is good for the heart to be strengthened by grace , not by foods , which have not benefited those devoted to them .
58013010	We have an altar from which those who serve the tent have no right to eat .
58013011	For the bodies of those animals whose blood is brought into the holy places by the high priest as a sacrifice for sin are burned outside the camp .
58013012	So Jesus also suffered outside the gate in order to sanctify the people through his own blood .
58013013	Therefore let us go to him outside the camp and bear the reproach he endured .
58013014	For here we have no lasting city , but we seek the city that is to come .
58013015	Through him then let us continually offer up a sacrifice of praise to God , that is , the fruit of lips that acknowledge his name .
58013016	Do not neglect to do good and to share what you have , for such sacrifices are pleasing to God .
58013017	Obey your leaders and submit to them , for they are keeping watch over your souls , as those who will have to give an account . Let them do this with joy and not with groaning , for that would be of no advantage to you .
58013018	Pray for us , for we are sure that we have a clear conscience , desiring to act honorably in all things .
58013019	I urge you the more earnestly to do this in order that I may be restored to you the sooner .
58013020	Now may the God of peace who brought again from the dead our Lord Jesus , the great shepherd of the sheep , by the blood of the eternal covenant ,
58013021	equip you with everything good that you may do his will , working in us that which is pleasing in his sight , through Jesus Christ , to whom be glory forever and ever . Amen .
58013022	I appeal to you , brothers , bear with my word of exhortation , for I have written to you briefly .
58013023	You should know that our brother Timothy has been released , with whom I shall see you if he comes soon .
58013024	Greet all your leaders and all the saints . Those who come from Italy send you greetings .
58013025	Grace be with all of you .
59001001	James , a servant of God and of the Lord Jesus Christ , To the twelve tribes in the Dispersion : Greetings .
59001002	Count it all joy , my brothers , when you meet trials of various kinds ,
59001003	for you know that the testing of your faith produces steadfastness .
59001004	And let steadfastness have its full effect , that you may be perfect and complete , lacking in nothing .
59001005	If any of you lacks wisdom , let him ask God , who gives generously to all without reproach , and it will be given him .
59001006	But let him ask in faith , with no doubting , for the one who doubts is like a wave of the sea that is driven and tossed by the wind .
59001007	For that person must not suppose that he will receive anything from the Lord ;
59001008	he is a double-minded man , unstable in all his ways .
59001009	Let the lowly brother boast in his exaltation ,
59001010	and the rich in his humiliation , because like a flower of the grass he will pass away .
59001011	For the sun rises with its scorching heat and withers the grass ; its flower falls , and its beauty perishes . So also will the rich man fade away in the midst of his pursuits .
59001012	Blessed is the man who remains steadfast under trial , for when he has stood the test he will receive the crown of life , which God has promised to those who love him .
59001013	Let no one say when he is tempted , “ I am being tempted by God , ” for God cannot be tempted with evil , and he himself tempts no one .
59001014	But each person is tempted when he is lured and enticed by his own desire .
59001015	Then desire when it has conceived gives birth to sin , and sin when it is fully grown brings forth death .
59001016	Do not be deceived , my beloved brothers .
59001017	Every good gift and every perfect gift is from above , coming down from the Father of lights with whom there is no variation or shadow due to change .
59001018	Of his own will he brought us forth by the word of truth , that we should be a kind of firstfruits of his creatures .
59001019	Know this , my beloved brothers : let every person be quick to hear , slow to speak , slow to anger ;
59001020	for the anger of man does not produce the righteousness of God .
59001021	Therefore put away all filthiness and rampant wickedness and receive with meekness the implanted word , which is able to save your souls .
59001022	But be doers of the word , and not hearers only , deceiving yourselves .
59001023	For if anyone is a hearer of the word and not a doer , he is like a man who looks intently at his natural face in a mirror .
59001024	For he looks at himself and goes away and at once forgets what he was like .
59001025	But the one who looks into the perfect law , the law of liberty , and perseveres , being no hearer who forgets but a doer who acts , he will be blessed in his doing .
59001026	If anyone thinks he is religious and does not bridle his tongue but deceives his heart , this person’s religion is worthless .
59001027	Religion that is pure and undefiled before God , the Father , is this : to visit orphans and widows in their affliction , and to keep oneself unstained from the world .
59002001	My brothers , show no partiality as you hold the faith in our Lord Jesus Christ , the Lord of glory .
59002002	For if a man wearing a gold ring and fine clothing comes into your assembly , and a poor man in shabby clothing also comes in ,
59002003	and if you pay attention to the one who wears the fine clothing and say , “ You sit here in a good place , ” while you say to the poor man , “ You stand over there , ” or , “ Sit down at my feet , ”
59002004	have you not then made distinctions among yourselves and become judges with evil thoughts ?
59002005	Listen , my beloved brothers , has not God chosen those who are poor in the world to be rich in faith and heirs of the kingdom , which he has promised to those who love him ?
59002006	But you have dishonored the poor man . Are not the rich the ones who oppress you , and the ones who drag you into court ?
59002007	Are they not the ones who blaspheme the honorable name by which you were called ?
59002008	If you really fulfill the royal law according to the Scripture , “ You shall love your neighbor as yourself , ” you are doing well .
59002009	But if you show partiality , you are committing sin and are convicted by the law as transgressors .
59002010	For whoever keeps the whole law but fails in one point has become accountable for all of it .
59002011	For he who said , “ Do not commit adultery , ” also said , “ Do not murder . ” If you do not commit adultery but do murder , you have become a transgressor of the law .
59002012	So speak and so act as those who are to be judged under the law of liberty .
59002013	For judgment is without mercy to one who has shown no mercy . Mercy triumphs over judgment .
59002014	What good is it , my brothers , if someone says he has faith but does not have works ? Can that faith save him ?
59002015	If a brother or sister is poorly clothed and lacking in daily food ,
59002016	and one of you says to them , “ Go in peace , be warmed and filled , ” without giving them the things needed for the body , what good is that ?
59002017	So also faith by itself , if it does not have works , is dead .
59002018	But someone will say , “ You have faith and I have works . ” Show me your faith apart from your works , and I will show you my faith by my works .
59002019	You believe that God is one ; you do well . Even the demons believe — and shudder !
59002020	Do you want to be shown , you foolish person , that faith apart from works is useless ?
59002021	Was not Abraham our father justified by works when he offered up his son Isaac on the altar ?
59002022	You see that faith was active along with his works , and faith was completed by his works ;
59002023	and the Scripture was fulfilled that says , “ Abraham believed God , and it was counted to him as righteousness ” — and he was called a friend of God .
59002024	You see that a person is justified by works and not by faith alone .
59002025	And in the same way was not also Rahab the prostitute justified by works when she received the messengers and sent them out by another way ?
59002026	For as the body apart from the spirit is dead , so also faith apart from works is dead .
59003001	Not many of you should become teachers , my brothers , for you know that we who teach will be judged with greater strictness .
59003002	For we all stumble in many ways . And if anyone does not stumble in what he says , he is a perfect man , able also to bridle his whole body .
59003003	If we put bits into the mouths of horses so that they obey us , we guide their whole bodies as well .
59003004	Look at the ships also : though they are so large and are driven by strong winds , they are guided by a very small rudder wherever the will of the pilot directs .
59003005	So also the tongue is a small member , yet it boasts of great things . How great a forest is set ablaze by such a small fire !
59003006	And the tongue is a fire , a world of unrighteousness . The tongue is set among our members , staining the whole body , setting on fire the entire course of life , and set on fire by hell .
59003007	For every kind of beast and bird , of reptile and sea creature , can be tamed and has been tamed by mankind ,
59003008	but no human being can tame the tongue . It is a restless evil , full of deadly poison .
59003009	With it we bless our Lord and Father , and with it we curse people who are made in the likeness of God .
59003010	From the same mouth come blessing and cursing . My brothers , these things ought not to be so .
59003011	Does a spring pour forth from the same opening both fresh and salt water ?
59003012	Can a fig tree , my brothers , bear olives , or a grapevine produce figs ? Neither can a salt pond yield fresh water .
59003013	Who is wise and understanding among you ? By his good conduct let him show his works in the meekness of wisdom .
59003014	But if you have bitter jealousy and selfish ambition in your hearts , do not boast and be false to the truth .
59003015	This is not the wisdom that comes down from above , but is earthly , unspiritual , demonic .
59003016	For where jealousy and selfish ambition exist , there will be disorder and every vile practice .
59003017	But the wisdom from above is first pure , then peaceable , gentle , open to reason , full of mercy and good fruits , impartial and sincere .
59003018	And a harvest of righteousness is sown in peace by those who make peace .
59004001	What causes quarrels and what causes fights among you ? Is it not this , that your passions are at war within you ?
59004002	You desire and do not have , so you murder . You covet and cannot obtain , so you fight and quarrel . You do not have , because you do not ask .
59004003	You ask and do not receive , because you ask wrongly , to spend it on your passions .
59004004	You adulterous people ! Do you not know that friendship with the world is enmity with God ? Therefore whoever wishes to be a friend of the world makes himself an enemy of God .
59004005	Or do you suppose it is to no purpose that the Scripture says , “ He yearns jealously over the spirit that he has made to dwell in us ” ?
59004006	But he gives more grace . Therefore it says , “ God opposes the proud , but gives grace to the humble . ”
59004007	Submit yourselves therefore to God . Resist the devil , and he will flee from you .
59004008	Draw near to God , and he will draw near to you . Cleanse your hands , you sinners , and purify your hearts , you double-minded .
59004009	Be wretched and mourn and weep . Let your laughter be turned to mourning and your joy to gloom .
59004010	Humble yourselves before the Lord , and he will exalt you .
59004011	Do not speak evil against one another , brothers . The one who speaks against a brother or judges his brother , speaks evil against the law and judges the law . But if you judge the law , you are not a doer of the law but a judge .
59004012	There is only one lawgiver and judge , he who is able to save and to destroy . But who are you to judge your neighbor ?
59004013	Come now , you who say , “ Today or tomorrow we will go into such and such a town and spend a year there and trade and make a profit ” —
59004014	yet you do not know what tomorrow will bring . What is your life ? For you are a mist that appears for a little time and then vanishes .
59004015	Instead you ought to say , “ If the Lord wills , we will live and do this or that . ”
59004016	As it is , you boast in your arrogance . All such boasting is evil .
59004017	So whoever knows the right thing to do and fails to do it , for him it is sin .
59005001	Come now , you rich , weep and howl for the miseries that are coming upon you .
59005002	Your riches have rotted and your garments are moth-eaten .
59005003	Your gold and silver have corroded , and their corrosion will be evidence against you and will eat your flesh like fire . You have laid up treasure in the last days .
59005004	Behold , the wages of the laborers who mowed your fields , which you kept back by fraud , are crying out against you , and the cries of the harvesters have reached the ears of the Lord of hosts .
59005005	You have lived on the earth in luxury and in self-indulgence . You have fattened your hearts in a day of slaughter .
59005006	You have condemned and murdered the righteous person . He does not resist you .
59005007	Be patient , therefore , brothers , until the coming of the Lord . See how the farmer waits for the precious fruit of the earth , being patient about it , until it receives the early and the late rains .
59005008	You also , be patient . Establish your hearts , for the coming of the Lord is at hand .
59005009	Do not grumble against one another , brothers , so that you may not be judged ; behold , the Judge is standing at the door .
59005010	As an example of suffering and patience , brothers , take the prophets who spoke in the name of the Lord .
59005011	Behold , we consider those blessed who remained steadfast . You have heard of the steadfastness of Job , and you have seen the purpose of the Lord , how the Lord is compassionate and merciful .
59005012	But above all , my brothers , do not swear , either by heaven or by earth or by any other oath , but let your “ yes ” be yes and your “ no ” be no , so that you may not fall under condemnation .
59005013	Is anyone among you suffering ? Let him pray . Is anyone cheerful ? Let him sing praise .
59005014	Is anyone among you sick ? Let him call for the elders of the church , and let them pray over him , anointing him with oil in the name of the Lord .
59005015	And the prayer of faith will save the one who is sick , and the Lord will raise him up . And if he has committed sins , he will be forgiven .
59005016	Therefore , confess your sins to one another and pray for one another , that you may be healed . The prayer of a righteous person has great power as it is working .
59005017	Elijah was a man with a nature like ours , and he prayed fervently that it might not rain , and for three years and six months it did not rain on the earth .
59005018	Then he prayed again , and heaven gave rain , and the earth bore its fruit .
59005019	My brothers , if anyone among you wanders from the truth and someone brings him back ,
59005020	let him know that whoever brings back a sinner from his wandering will save his soul from death and will cover a multitude of sins .
60001001	Peter , an apostle of Jesus Christ , To those who are elect exiles of the dispersion in Pontus , Galatia , Cappadocia , Asia , and Bithynia ,
60001002	according to the foreknowledge of God the Father , in the sanctification of the Spirit , for obedience to Jesus Christ and for sprinkling with his blood : May grace and peace be multiplied to you .
60001003	Blessed be the God and Father of our Lord Jesus Christ ! According to his great mercy , he has caused us to be born again to a living hope through the resurrection of Jesus Christ from the dead ,
60001004	to an inheritance that is imperishable , undefiled , and unfading , kept in heaven for you ,
60001005	who by God’s power are being guarded through faith for a salvation ready to be revealed in the last time .
60001006	In this you rejoice , though now for a little while , if necessary , you have been grieved by various trials ,
60001007	so that the tested genuineness of your faith — more precious than gold that perishes though it is tested by fire — may be found to result in praise and glory and honor at the revelation of Jesus Christ .
60001008	Though you have not seen him , you love him . Though you do not now see him , you believe in him and rejoice with joy that is inexpressible and filled with glory ,
60001009	obtaining the outcome of your faith , the salvation of your souls .
60001010	Concerning this salvation , the prophets who prophesied about the grace that was to be yours searched and inquired carefully ,
60001011	inquiring what person or time the Spirit of Christ in them was indicating when he predicted the sufferings of Christ and the subsequent glories .
60001012	It was revealed to them that they were serving not themselves but you , in the things that have now been announced to you through those who preached the good news to you by the Holy Spirit sent from heaven , things into which angels long to look .
60001013	Therefore , preparing your minds for action , and being sober-minded , set your hope fully on the grace that will be brought to you at the revelation of Jesus Christ .
60001014	As obedient children , do not be conformed to the passions of your former ignorance ,
60001015	but as he who called you is holy , you also be holy in all your conduct ,
60001016	since it is written , “ You shall be holy , for I am holy . ”
60001017	And if you call on him as Father who judges impartially according to each one’s deeds , conduct yourselves with fear throughout the time of your exile ,
60001018	knowing that you were ransomed from the futile ways inherited from your forefathers , not with perishable things such as silver or gold ,
60001019	but with the precious blood of Christ , like that of a lamb without blemish or spot .
60001020	He was foreknown before the foundation of the world but was made manifest in the last times for the sake of you
60001021	who through him are believers in God , who raised him from the dead and gave him glory , so that your faith and hope are in God .
60001022	Having purified your souls by your obedience to the truth for a sincere brotherly love , love one another earnestly from a pure heart ,
60001023	since you have been born again , not of perishable seed but of imperishable , through the living and abiding word of God ;
60001024	for “ All flesh is like grass and all its glory like the flower of grass . The grass withers , and the flower falls ,
60001025	but the word of the Lord remains forever . ” And this word is the good news that was preached to you .
60002001	So put away all malice and all deceit and hypocrisy and envy and all slander .
60002002	Like newborn infants , long for the pure spiritual milk , that by it you may grow up into salvation —
60002003	if indeed you have tasted that the Lord is good .
60002004	As you come to him , a living stone rejected by men but in the sight of God chosen and precious ,
60002005	you yourselves like living stones are being built up as a spiritual house , to be a holy priesthood , to offer spiritual sacrifices acceptable to God through Jesus Christ .
60002006	For it stands in Scripture : “ Behold , I am laying in Zion a stone , a cornerstone chosen and precious , and whoever believes in him will not be put to shame . ”
60002007	So the honor is for you who believe , but for those who do not believe , “ The stone that the builders rejected has become the cornerstone , ”
60002008	and “ A stone of stumbling , and a rock of offense . ” They stumble because they disobey the word , as they were destined to do .
60002009	But you are a chosen race , a royal priesthood , a holy nation , a people for his own possession , that you may proclaim the excellencies of him who called you out of darkness into his marvelous light .
60002010	Once you were not a people , but now you are God’s people ; once you had not received mercy , but now you have received mercy .
60002011	Beloved , I urge you as sojourners and exiles to abstain from the passions of the flesh , which wage war against your soul .
60002012	Keep your conduct among the Gentiles honorable , so that when they speak against you as evildoers , they may see your good deeds and glorify God on the day of visitation .
60002013	Be subject for the Lord’s sake to every human institution , whether it be to the emperor as supreme ,
60002014	or to governors as sent by him to punish those who do evil and to praise those who do good .
60002015	For this is the will of God , that by doing good you should put to silence the ignorance of foolish people .
60002016	Live as people who are free , not using your freedom as a cover-up for evil , but living as servants of God .
60002017	Honor everyone . Love the brotherhood . Fear God . Honor the emperor .
60002018	Servants , be subject to your masters with all respect , not only to the good and gentle but also to the unjust .
60002019	For this is a gracious thing , when , mindful of God , one endures sorrows while suffering unjustly .
60002020	For what credit is it if , when you sin and are beaten for it , you endure ? But if when you do good and suffer for it you endure , this is a gracious thing in the sight of God .
60002021	For to this you have been called , because Christ also suffered for you , leaving you an example , so that you might follow in his steps .
60002022	He committed no sin , neither was deceit found in his mouth .
60002023	When he was reviled , he did not revile in return ; when he suffered , he did not threaten , but continued entrusting himself to him who judges justly .
60002024	He himself bore our sins in his body on the tree , that we might die to sin and live to righteousness . By his wounds you have been healed .
60002025	For you were straying like sheep , but have now returned to the Shepherd and Overseer of your souls .
60003001	Likewise , wives , be subject to your own husbands , so that even if some do not obey the word , they may be won without a word by the conduct of their wives ,
60003002	when they see your respectful and pure conduct .
60003003	Do not let your adorning be external — the braiding of hair and the putting on of gold jewelry , or the clothing you wear —
60003004	but let your adorning be the hidden person of the heart with the imperishable beauty of a gentle and quiet spirit , which in God’s sight is very precious .
60003005	For this is how the holy women who hoped in God used to adorn themselves , by submitting to their own husbands ,
60003006	as Sarah obeyed Abraham , calling him lord . And you are her children , if you do good and do not fear anything that is frightening .
60003007	Likewise , husbands , live with your wives in an understanding way , showing honor to the woman as the weaker vessel , since they are heirs with you of the grace of life , so that your prayers may not be hindered .
60003008	Finally , all of you , have unity of mind , sympathy , brotherly love , a tender heart , and a humble mind .
60003009	Do not repay evil for evil or reviling for reviling , but on the contrary , bless , for to this you were called , that you may obtain a blessing .
60003010	For “ Whoever desires to love life and see good days , let him keep his tongue from evil and his lips from speaking deceit ;
60003011	let him turn away from evil and do good ; let him seek peace and pursue it .
60003012	For the eyes of the Lord are on the righteous , and his ears are open to their prayer . But the face of the Lord is against those who do evil . ”
60003013	Now who is there to harm you if you are zealous for what is good ?
60003014	But even if you should suffer for righteousness ’ sake , you will be blessed . Have no fear of them , nor be troubled ,
60003015	but in your hearts honor Christ the Lord as holy , always being prepared to make a defense to anyone who asks you for a reason for the hope that is in you ; yet do it with gentleness and respect ,
60003016	having a good conscience , so that , when you are slandered , those who revile your good behavior in Christ may be put to shame .
60003017	For it is better to suffer for doing good , if that should be God’s will , than for doing evil .
60003018	For Christ also suffered once for sins , the righteous for the unrighteous , that he might bring us to God , being put to death in the flesh but made alive in the spirit ,
60003019	in which he went and proclaimed to the spirits in prison ,
60003020	because they formerly did not obey , when God’s patience waited in the days of Noah , while the ark was being prepared , in which a few , that is , eight persons , were brought safely through water .
60003021	Baptism , which corresponds to this , now saves you , not as a removal of dirt from the body but as an appeal to God for a good conscience , through the resurrection of Jesus Christ ,
60003022	who has gone into heaven and is at the right hand of God , with angels , authorities , and powers having been subjected to him .
60004001	Since therefore Christ suffered in the flesh , arm yourselves with the same way of thinking , for whoever has suffered in the flesh has ceased from sin ,
60004002	so as to live for the rest of the time in the flesh no longer for human passions but for the will of God .
60004003	For the time that is past suffices for doing what the Gentiles want to do , living in sensuality , passions , drunkenness , orgies , drinking parties , and lawless idolatry .
60004004	With respect to this they are surprised when you do not join them in the same flood of debauchery , and they malign you ;
60004005	but they will give account to him who is ready to judge the living and the dead .
60004006	For this is why the gospel was preached even to those who are dead , that though judged in the flesh the way people are , they might live in the spirit the way God does .
60004007	The end of all things is at hand ; therefore be self-controlled and sober-minded for the sake of your prayers .
60004008	Above all , keep loving one another earnestly , since love covers a multitude of sins .
60004009	Show hospitality to one another without grumbling .
60004010	As each has received a gift , use it to serve one another , as good stewards of God’s varied grace :
60004011	whoever speaks , as one who speaks oracles of God ; whoever serves , as one who serves by the strength that God supplies — in order that in everything God may be glorified through Jesus Christ . To him belong glory and dominion forever and ever . Amen .
60004012	Beloved , do not be surprised at the fiery trial when it comes upon you to test you , as though something strange were happening to you .
60004013	But rejoice insofar as you share Christ’s sufferings , that you may also rejoice and be glad when his glory is revealed .
60004014	If you are insulted for the name of Christ , you are blessed , because the Spirit of glory and of God rests upon you .
60004015	But let none of you suffer as a murderer or a thief or an evildoer or as a meddler .
60004016	Yet if anyone suffers as a Christian , let him not be ashamed , but let him glorify God in that name .
60004017	For it is time for judgment to begin at the household of God ; and if it begins with us , what will be the outcome for those who do not obey the gospel of God ?
60004018	And “ If the righteous is scarcely saved , what will become of the ungodly and the sinner ? ”
60004019	Therefore let those who suffer according to God’s will entrust their souls to a faithful Creator while doing good .
60005001	So I exhort the elders among you , as a fellow elder and a witness of the sufferings of Christ , as well as a partaker in the glory that is going to be revealed :
60005002	shepherd the flock of God that is among you , exercising oversight , not under compulsion , but willingly , as God would have you ; not for shameful gain , but eagerly ;
60005003	not domineering over those in your charge , but being examples to the flock .
60005004	And when the chief Shepherd appears , you will receive the unfading crown of glory .
60005005	Likewise , you who are younger , be subject to the elders . Clothe yourselves , all of you , with humility toward one another , for “ God opposes the proud but gives grace to the humble . ”
