60005006	Humble yourselves , therefore , under the mighty hand of God so that at the proper time he may exalt you ,
60005007	casting all your anxieties on him , because he cares for you .
60005008	Be sober-minded ; be watchful . Your adversary the devil prowls around like a roaring lion , seeking someone to devour .
60005009	Resist him , firm in your faith , knowing that the same kinds of suffering are being experienced by your brotherhood throughout the world .
60005010	And after you have suffered a little while , the God of all grace , who has called you to his eternal glory in Christ , will himself restore , confirm , strengthen , and establish you .
60005011	To him be the dominion forever and ever . Amen .
60005012	By Silvanus , a faithful brother as I regard him , I have written briefly to you , exhorting and declaring that this is the true grace of God . Stand firm in it .
60005013	She who is at Babylon , who is likewise chosen , sends you greetings , and so does Mark , my son .
60005014	Greet one another with the kiss of love . Peace to all of you who are in Christ .
61001001	Simeon Peter , a servant and apostle of Jesus Christ , To those who have obtained a faith of equal standing with ours by the righteousness of our God and Savior Jesus Christ :
61001002	May grace and peace be multiplied to you in the knowledge of God and of Jesus our Lord .
61001003	His divine power has granted to us all things that pertain to life and godliness , through the knowledge of him who called us to his own glory and excellence ,
61001004	by which he has granted to us his precious and very great promises , so that through them you may become partakers of the divine nature , having escaped from the corruption that is in the world because of sinful desire .
61001005	For this very reason , make every effort to supplement your faith with virtue , and virtue with knowledge ,
61001006	and knowledge with self-control , and self-control with steadfastness , and steadfastness with godliness ,
61001007	and godliness with brotherly affection , and brotherly affection with love .
61001008	For if these qualities are yours and are increasing , they keep you from being ineffective or unfruitful in the knowledge of our Lord Jesus Christ .
61001009	For whoever lacks these qualities is so nearsighted that he is blind , having forgotten that he was cleansed from his former sins .
61001010	Therefore , brothers , be all the more diligent to make your calling and election sure , for if you practice these qualities you will never fall .
61001011	For in this way there will be richly provided for you an entrance into the eternal kingdom of our Lord and Savior Jesus Christ .
61001012	Therefore I intend always to remind you of these qualities , though you know them and are established in the truth that you have .
61001013	I think it right , as long as I am in this body , to stir you up by way of reminder ,
61001014	since I know that the putting off of my body will be soon , as our Lord Jesus Christ made clear to me .
61001015	And I will make every effort so that after my departure you may be able at any time to recall these things .
61001016	For we did not follow cleverly devised myths when we made known to you the power and coming of our Lord Jesus Christ , but we were eyewitnesses of his majesty .
61001017	For when he received honor and glory from God the Father , and the voice was borne to him by the Majestic Glory , “ This is my beloved Son , with whom I am well pleased , ”
61001018	we ourselves heard this very voice borne from heaven , for we were with him on the holy mountain .
61001019	And we have something more sure , the prophetic word , to which you will do well to pay attention as to a lamp shining in a dark place , until the day dawns and the morning star rises in your hearts ,
61001020	knowing this first of all , that no prophecy of Scripture comes from someone’s own interpretation .
61001021	For no prophecy was ever produced by the will of man , but men spoke from God as they were carried along by the Holy Spirit .
61002001	But false prophets also arose among the people , just as there will be false teachers among you , who will secretly bring in destructive heresies , even denying the Master who bought them , bringing upon themselves swift destruction .
61002002	And many will follow their sensuality , and because of them the way of truth will be blasphemed .
61002003	And in their greed they will exploit you with false words . Their condemnation from long ago is not idle , and their destruction is not asleep .
61002004	For if God did not spare angels when they sinned , but cast them into hell and committed them to chains of gloomy darkness to be kept until the judgment ;
61002005	if he did not spare the ancient world , but preserved Noah , a herald of righteousness , with seven others , when he brought a flood upon the world of the ungodly ;
61002006	if by turning the cities of Sodom and Gomorrah to ashes he condemned them to extinction , making them an example of what is going to happen to the ungodly ;
61002007	and if he rescued righteous Lot , greatly distressed by the sensual conduct of the wicked
61002008	( for as that righteous man lived among them day after day , he was tormenting his righteous soul over their lawless deeds that he saw and heard ) ;
61002009	then the Lord knows how to rescue the godly from trials , and to keep the unrighteous under punishment until the day of judgment ,
61002010	and especially those who indulge in the lust of defiling passion and despise authority . Bold and willful , they do not tremble as they blaspheme the glorious ones ,
61002011	whereas angels , though greater in might and power , do not pronounce a blasphemous judgment against them before the Lord .
61002012	But these , like irrational animals , creatures of instinct , born to be caught and destroyed , blaspheming about matters of which they are ignorant , will also be destroyed in their destruction ,
61002013	suffering wrong as the wage for their wrongdoing . They count it pleasure to revel in the daytime . They are blots and blemishes , reveling in their deceptions , while they feast with you .
61002014	They have eyes full of adultery , insatiable for sin . They entice unsteady souls . They have hearts trained in greed . Accursed children !
61002015	Forsaking the right way , they have gone astray . They have followed the way of Balaam , the son of Beor , who loved gain from wrongdoing ,
61002016	but was rebuked for his own transgression ; a speechless donkey spoke with human voice and restrained the prophet’s madness .
61002017	These are waterless springs and mists driven by a storm . For them the gloom of utter darkness has been reserved .
61002018	For , speaking loud boasts of folly , they entice by sensual passions of the flesh those who are barely escaping from those who live in error .
61002019	They promise them freedom , but they themselves are slaves of corruption . For whatever overcomes a person , to that he is enslaved .
61002020	For if , after they have escaped the defilements of the world through the knowledge of our Lord and Savior Jesus Christ , they are again entangled in them and overcome , the last state has become worse for them than the first .
61002021	For it would have been better for them never to have known the way of righteousness than after knowing it to turn back from the holy commandment delivered to them .
61002022	What the true proverb says has happened to them : “ The dog returns to its own vomit , and the sow , after washing herself , returns to wallow in the mire . ”
61003001	This is now the second letter that I am writing to you , beloved . In both of them I am stirring up your sincere mind by way of reminder ,
61003002	that you should remember the predictions of the holy prophets and the commandment of the Lord and Savior through your apostles ,
61003003	knowing this first of all , that scoffers will come in the last days with scoffing , following their own sinful desires .
61003004	They will say , “ Where is the promise of his coming ? For ever since the fathers fell asleep , all things are continuing as they were from the beginning of creation . ”
61003005	For they deliberately overlook this fact , that the heavens existed long ago , and the earth was formed out of water and through water by the word of God ,
61003006	and that by means of these the world that then existed was deluged with water and perished .
61003007	But by the same word the heavens and earth that now exist are stored up for fire , being kept until the day of judgment and destruction of the ungodly .
61003008	But do not overlook this one fact , beloved , that with the Lord one day is as a thousand years , and a thousand years as one day .
61003009	The Lord is not slow to fulfill his promise as some count slowness , but is patient toward you , not wishing that any should perish , but that all should reach repentance .
61003010	But the day of the Lord will come like a thief , and then the heavens will pass away with a roar , and the heavenly bodies will be burned up and dissolved , and the earth and the works that are done on it will be exposed .
61003011	Since all these things are thus to be dissolved , what sort of people ought you to be in lives of holiness and godliness ,
61003012	waiting for and hastening the coming of the day of God , because of which the heavens will be set on fire and dissolved , and the heavenly bodies will melt as they burn !
61003013	But according to his promise we are waiting for new heavens and a new earth in which righteousness dwells .
61003014	Therefore , beloved , since you are waiting for these , be diligent to be found by him without spot or blemish , and at peace .
61003015	And count the patience of our Lord as salvation , just as our beloved brother Paul also wrote to you according to the wisdom given him ,
61003016	as he does in all his letters when he speaks in them of these matters . There are some things in them that are hard to understand , which the ignorant and unstable twist to their own destruction , as they do the other Scriptures .
61003017	You therefore , beloved , knowing this beforehand , take care that you are not carried away with the error of lawless people and lose your own stability .
61003018	But grow in the grace and knowledge of our Lord and Savior Jesus Christ . To him be the glory both now and to the day of eternity . Amen .
62001001	That which was from the beginning , which we have heard , which we have seen with our eyes , which we looked upon and have touched with our hands , concerning the word of life —
62001002	the life was made manifest , and we have seen it , and testify to it and proclaim to you the eternal life , which was with the Father and was made manifest to us —
62001003	that which we have seen and heard we proclaim also to you , so that you too may have fellowship with us ; and indeed our fellowship is with the Father and with his Son Jesus Christ .
62001004	And we are writing these things so that our joy may be complete .
62001005	This is the message we have heard from him and proclaim to you , that God is light , and in him is no darkness at all .
62001006	If we say we have fellowship with him while we walk in darkness , we lie and do not practice the truth .
62001007	But if we walk in the light , as he is in the light , we have fellowship with one another , and the blood of Jesus his Son cleanses us from all sin .
62001008	If we say we have no sin , we deceive ourselves , and the truth is not in us .
62001009	If we confess our sins , he is faithful and just to forgive us our sins and to cleanse us from all unrighteousness .
62001010	If we say we have not sinned , we make him a liar , and his word is not in us .
62002001	My little children , I am writing these things to you so that you may not sin . But if anyone does sin , we have an advocate with the Father , Jesus Christ the righteous .
62002002	He is the propitiation for our sins , and not for ours only but also for the sins of the whole world .
62002003	And by this we know that we have come to know him , if we keep his commandments .
62002004	Whoever says “ I know him ” but does not keep his commandments is a liar , and the truth is not in him ,
62002005	but whoever keeps his word , in him truly the love of God is perfected . By this we may know that we are in him :
62002006	whoever says he abides in him ought to walk in the same way in which he walked .
62002007	Beloved , I am writing you no new commandment , but an old commandment that you had from the beginning . The old commandment is the word that you have heard .
62002008	At the same time , it is a new commandment that I am writing to you , which is true in him and in you , because the darkness is passing away and the true light is already shining .
62002009	Whoever says he is in the light and hates his brother is still in darkness .
62002010	Whoever loves his brother abides in the light , and in him there is no cause for stumbling .
62002011	But whoever hates his brother is in the darkness and walks in the darkness , and does not know where he is going , because the darkness has blinded his eyes .
62002012	I am writing to you , little children , because your sins are forgiven for his name’s sake .
62002013	I am writing to you , fathers , because you know him who is from the beginning . I am writing to you , young men , because you have overcome the evil one . I write to you , children , because you know the Father .
62002014	I write to you , fathers , because you know him who is from the beginning . I write to you , young men , because you are strong , and the word of God abides in you , and you have overcome the evil one .
62002015	Do not love the world or the things in the world . If anyone loves the world , the love of the Father is not in him .
62002016	For all that is in the world — the desires of the flesh and the desires of the eyes and pride in possessions — is not from the Father but is from the world .
62002017	And the world is passing away along with its desires , but whoever does the will of God abides forever .
62002018	Children , it is the last hour , and as you have heard that antichrist is coming , so now many antichrists have come . Therefore we know that it is the last hour .
62002019	They went out from us , but they were not of us ; for if they had been of us , they would have continued with us . But they went out , that it might become plain that they all are not of us .
62002020	But you have been anointed by the Holy One , and you all have knowledge .
62002021	I write to you , not because you do not know the truth , but because you know it , and because no lie is of the truth .
62002022	Who is the liar but he who denies that Jesus is the Christ ? This is the antichrist , he who denies the Father and the Son .
62002023	No one who denies the Son has the Father . Whoever confesses the Son has the Father also .
62002024	Let what you heard from the beginning abide in you . If what you heard from the beginning abides in you , then you too will abide in the Son and in the Father .
62002025	And this is the promise that he made to us — eternal life .
62002026	I write these things to you about those who are trying to deceive you .
62002027	But the anointing that you received from him abides in you , and you have no need that anyone should teach you . But as his anointing teaches you about everything , and is true , and is no lie — just as it has taught you , abide in him .
62002028	And now , little children , abide in him , so that when he appears we may have confidence and not shrink from him in shame at his coming .
62002029	If you know that he is righteous , you may be sure that everyone who practices righteousness has been born of him .
62003001	See what kind of love the Father has given to us , that we should be called children of God ; and so we are . The reason why the world does not know us is that it did not know him .
62003002	Beloved , we are God’s children now , and what we will be has not yet appeared ; but we know that when he appears we shall be like him , because we shall see him as he is .
62003003	And everyone who thus hopes in him purifies himself as he is pure .
62003004	Everyone who makes a practice of sinning also practices lawlessness ; sin is lawlessness .
62003005	You know that he appeared to take away sins , and in him there is no sin .
62003006	No one who abides in him keeps on sinning ; no one who keeps on sinning has either seen him or known him .
62003007	Little children , let no one deceive you . Whoever practices righteousness is righteous , as he is righteous .
62003008	Whoever makes a practice of sinning is of the devil , for the devil has been sinning from the beginning . The reason the Son of God appeared was to destroy the works of the devil .
62003009	No one born of God makes a practice of sinning , for God’s seed abides in him , and he cannot keep on sinning because he has been born of God .
62003010	By this it is evident who are the children of God , and who are the children of the devil : whoever does not practice righteousness is not of God , nor is the one who does not love his brother .
62003011	For this is the message that you have heard from the beginning , that we should love one another .
62003012	We should not be like Cain , who was of the evil one and murdered his brother . And why did he murder him ? Because his own deeds were evil and his brother’s righteous .
62003013	Do not be surprised , brothers , that the world hates you .
62003014	We know that we have passed out of death into life , because we love the brothers . Whoever does not love abides in death .
62003015	Everyone who hates his brother is a murderer , and you know that no murderer has eternal life abiding in him .
62003016	By this we know love , that he laid down his life for us , and we ought to lay down our lives for the brothers .
62003017	But if anyone has the world’s goods and sees his brother in need , yet closes his heart against him , how does God’s love abide in him ?
62003018	Little children , let us not love in word or talk but in deed and in truth .
62003019	By this we shall know that we are of the truth and reassure our heart before him ;
62003020	for whenever our heart condemns us , God is greater than our heart , and he knows everything .
62003021	Beloved , if our heart does not condemn us , we have confidence before God ;
62003022	and whatever we ask we receive from him , because we keep his commandments and do what pleases him .
62003023	And this is his commandment , that we believe in the name of his Son Jesus Christ and love one another , just as he has commanded us .
62003024	Whoever keeps his commandments abides in God , and God in him . And by this we know that he abides in us , by the Spirit whom he has given us .
62004001	Beloved , do not believe every spirit , but test the spirits to see whether they are from God , for many false prophets have gone out into the world .
62004002	By this you know the Spirit of God : every spirit that confesses that Jesus Christ has come in the flesh is from God ,
62004003	and every spirit that does not confess Jesus is not from God . This is the spirit of the antichrist , which you heard was coming and now is in the world already .
62004004	Little children , you are from God and have overcome them , for he who is in you is greater than he who is in the world .
62004005	They are from the world ; therefore they speak from the world , and the world listens to them .
62004006	We are from God . Whoever knows God listens to us ; whoever is not from God does not listen to us . By this we know the Spirit of truth and the spirit of error .
62004007	Beloved , let us love one another , for love is from God , and whoever loves has been born of God and knows God .
62004008	Anyone who does not love does not know God , because God is love .
62004009	In this the love of God was made manifest among us , that God sent his only Son into the world , so that we might live through him .
62004010	In this is love , not that we have loved God but that he loved us and sent his Son to be the propitiation for our sins .
62004011	Beloved , if God so loved us , we also ought to love one another .
62004012	No one has ever seen God ; if we love one another , God abides in us and his love is perfected in us .
62004013	By this we know that we abide in him and he in us , because he has given us of his Spirit .
62004014	And we have seen and testify that the Father has sent his Son to be the Savior of the world .
62004015	Whoever confesses that Jesus is the Son of God , God abides in him , and he in God .
62004016	So we have come to know and to believe the love that God has for us . God is love , and whoever abides in love abides in God , and God abides in him .
62004017	By this is love perfected with us , so that we may have confidence for the day of judgment , because as he is so also are we in this world .
62004018	There is no fear in love , but perfect love casts out fear . For fear has to do with punishment , and whoever fears has not been perfected in love .
62004019	We love because he first loved us .
62004020	If anyone says , “ I love God , ” and hates his brother , he is a liar ; for he who does not love his brother whom he has seen cannot love God whom he has not seen .
62004021	And this commandment we have from him : whoever loves God must also love his brother .
62005001	Everyone who believes that Jesus is the Christ has been born of God , and everyone who loves the Father loves whoever has been born of him .
62005002	By this we know that we love the children of God , when we love God and obey his commandments .
62005003	For this is the love of God , that we keep his commandments . And his commandments are not burdensome .
62005004	For everyone who has been born of God overcomes the world . And this is the victory that has overcome the world — our faith .
62005005	Who is it that overcomes the world except the one who believes that Jesus is the Son of God ?
62005006	This is he who came by water and blood — Jesus Christ ; not by the water only but by the water and the blood . And the Spirit is the one who testifies , because the Spirit is the truth .
62005007	For there are three that testify :
62005008	the Spirit and the water and the blood ; and these three agree .
62005009	If we receive the testimony of men , the testimony of God is greater , for this is the testimony of God that he has borne concerning his Son .
62005010	Whoever believes in the Son of God has the testimony in himself . Whoever does not believe God has made him a liar , because he has not believed in the testimony that God has borne concerning his Son .
62005011	And this is the testimony , that God gave us eternal life , and this life is in his Son .
62005012	Whoever has the Son has life ; whoever does not have the Son of God does not have life .
62005013	I write these things to you who believe in the name of the Son of God that you may know that you have eternal life .
62005014	And this is the confidence that we have toward him , that if we ask anything according to his will he hears us .
62005015	And if we know that he hears us in whatever we ask , we know that we have the requests that we have asked of him .
62005016	If anyone sees his brother committing a sin not leading to death , he shall ask , and God will give him life — to those who commit sins that do not lead to death . There is sin that leads to death ; I do not say that one should pray for that .
62005017	All wrongdoing is sin , but there is sin that does not lead to death .
62005018	We know that everyone who has been born of God does not keep on sinning , but he who was born of God protects him , and the evil one does not touch him .
62005019	We know that we are from God , and the whole world lies in the power of the evil one .
62005020	And we know that the Son of God has come and has given us understanding , so that we may know him who is true ; and we are in him who is true , in his Son Jesus Christ . He is the true God and eternal life .
62005021	Little children , keep yourselves from idols .
63001001	The elder to the elect lady and her children , whom I love in truth , and not only I , but also all who know the truth ,
63001002	because of the truth that abides in us and will be with us forever :
63001003	Grace , mercy , and peace will be with us , from God the Father and from Jesus Christ the Father’s Son , in truth and love .
63001004	I rejoiced greatly to find some of your children walking in the truth , just as we were commanded by the Father .
63001005	And now I ask you , dear lady — not as though I were writing you a new commandment , but the one we have had from the beginning — that we love one another .
63001006	And this is love , that we walk according to his commandments ; this is the commandment , just as you have heard from the beginning , so that you should walk in it .
63001007	For many deceivers have gone out into the world , those who do not confess the coming of Jesus Christ in the flesh . Such a one is the deceiver and the antichrist .
63001008	Watch yourselves , so that you may not lose what we have worked for , but may win a full reward .
63001009	Everyone who goes on ahead and does not abide in the teaching of Christ , does not have God . Whoever abides in the teaching has both the Father and the Son .
63001010	If anyone comes to you and does not bring this teaching , do not receive him into your house or give him any greeting ,
63001011	for whoever greets him takes part in his wicked works .
63001012	Though I have much to write to you , I would rather not use paper and ink . Instead I hope to come to you and talk face to face , so that our joy may be complete .
63001013	The children of your elect sister greet you .
64001001	The elder to the beloved Gaius , whom I love in truth .
64001002	Beloved , I pray that all may go well with you and that you may be in good health , as it goes well with your soul .
64001003	For I rejoiced greatly when the brothers came and testified to your truth , as indeed you are walking in the truth .
64001004	I have no greater joy than to hear that my children are walking in the truth .
64001005	Beloved , it is a faithful thing you do in all your efforts for these brothers , strangers as they are ,
64001006	who testified to your love before the church . You will do well to send them on their journey in a manner worthy of God .
64001007	For they have gone out for the sake of the name , accepting nothing from the Gentiles .
64001008	Therefore we ought to support people like these , that we may be fellow workers for the truth .
64001009	I have written something to the church , but Diotrephes , who likes to put himself first , does not acknowledge our authority .
64001010	So if I come , I will bring up what he is doing , talking wicked nonsense against us . And not content with that , he refuses to welcome the brothers , and also stops those who want to and puts them out of the church .
64001011	Beloved , do not imitate evil but imitate good . Whoever does good is from God ; whoever does evil has not seen God .
64001012	Demetrius has received a good testimony from everyone , and from the truth itself . We also add our testimony , and you know that our testimony is true .
64001013	I had much to write to you , but I would rather not write with pen and ink .
64001014	I hope to see you soon , and we will talk face to face .
64001015	Peace be to you . The friends greet you . Greet the friends , every one of them .
65001001	Jude , a servant of Jesus Christ and brother of James , To those who are called , beloved in God the Father and kept forJesus Christ :
65001002	May mercy , peace , and love be multiplied to you .
65001003	Beloved , although I was very eager to write to you about our common salvation , I found it necessary to write appealing to you to contend for the faith that was once for all delivered to the saints .
65001004	For certain people have crept in unnoticed who long ago were designated for this condemnation , ungodly people , who pervert the grace of our God into sensuality and deny our only Master and Lord , Jesus Christ .
65001005	Now I want to remind you , although you once fully knew it , that Jesus , who saved a people out of the land of Egypt , afterward destroyed those who did not believe .
65001006	And the angels who did not stay within their own position of authority , but left their proper dwelling , he has kept in eternal chains under gloomy darkness until the judgment of the great day —
65001007	just as Sodom and Gomorrah and the surrounding cities , which likewise indulged in sexual immorality and pursued unnatural desire , serve as an example by undergoing a punishment of eternal fire .
65001008	Yet in like manner these people also , relying on their dreams , defile the flesh , reject authority , and blaspheme the glorious ones .
65001009	But when the archangel Michael , contending with the devil , was disputing about the body of Moses , he did not presume to pronounce a blasphemous judgment , but said , “ The Lord rebuke you . ”
65001010	But these people blaspheme all that they do not understand , and they are destroyed by all that they , like unreasoning animals , understand instinctively .
65001011	Woe to them ! For they walked in the way of Cain and abandoned themselves for the sake of gain to Balaam’s error and perished in Korah’s rebellion .
65001012	These are hidden reefs at your love feasts , as they feast with you without fear , shepherds feeding themselves ; waterless clouds , swept along by winds ; fruitless trees in late autumn , twice dead , uprooted ;
65001013	wild waves of the sea , casting up the foam of their own shame ; wandering stars , for whom the gloom of utter darkness has been reserved forever .
65001014	It was also about these that Enoch , the seventh from Adam , prophesied , saying , “ Behold , the Lord comes with ten thousands of his holy ones ,
65001015	to execute judgment on all and to convict all the ungodly of all their deeds of ungodliness that they have committed in such an ungodly way , and of all the harsh things that ungodly sinners have spoken against him . ”
65001016	These are grumblers , malcontents , following their own sinful desires ; they are loud-mouthed boasters , showing favoritism to gain advantage .
65001017	But you must remember , beloved , the predictions of the apostles of our Lord Jesus Christ .
65001018	They said to you , “ In the last time there will be scoffers , following their own ungodly passions . ”
65001019	It is these who cause divisions , worldly people , devoid of the Spirit .
65001020	But you , beloved , building yourselves up in your most holy faith and praying in the Holy Spirit ,
65001021	keep yourselves in the love of God , waiting for the mercy of our Lord Jesus Christ that leads to eternal life .
65001022	And have mercy on those who doubt ;
65001023	save others by snatching them out of the fire ; to others show mercy with fear , hating even the garment stained by the flesh .
65001024	Now to him who is able to keep you from stumbling and to present you blameless before the presence of his glory with great joy ,
65001025	to the only God , our Savior , through Jesus Christ our Lord , be glory , majesty , dominion , and authority , before all time and now and forever . Amen .
